bhavantu vighnabhaṅgāya bhavasya caraṇāmbujāḥ ।। viṣṇormatsyāvatāre sakalavasumatīmaṇḍalaṃ vyaśnuvānās tasyāsyodīritānāṃ dhvanir apaharatād aśriyaṃ vaḥ śrutīnām ।। devīṃ sarasvatīṃ caiva tato jayam udīrayet ।। triguṇāya trivedāya namas tasmai svayambhuve ।।
munayo dīrghasattrānte papracchur dīrghasaṃhitām ।। kathāsu śaunakādyās tu abhinandya muhurmuhuḥ ।। tānyevāmṛtakalpāni śrotum icchāmahe punaḥ ।। kasmācca bhagavān viṣṇur matsyarūpatvam āśritaḥ ।।
kasya hetoḥ kapālitvaṃ jagāma vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ ।। tvadvākyenāmṛtasyeva na tṛptiriha jāyate ।। mātsyaṃ purāṇamakhilaṃ yajjagāda gadādharaḥ ।। putre rājyaṃ samāropya kṣamāvān ravinandanaḥ ।।
samaduḥkhasukho vīraḥ prāptavān yogam uttamam ।। varaṃ vṛṇīṣva provāca prītaḥ sa kamalāsanaḥ ।। ekam evāham icchāmi tvatto varamanuttamam ।। bhaveyaṃ rakṣaṇāyālaṃ pralaye samupasthite ।।
puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ sumahatī khātpapāta surārpitā ।। papāta pāṇyor upari śapharī jalasaṃyutā ।। rakṣaṇāyākarodyatnaṃ sa tasminkarakodare ।। so abhavanmatsyarūpeṇa pāhi pāhīti cābravīt ।।
tatrāpi caikarātreṇa hastatrayam avardhata ।। sa matsyaḥ pāhi pāhīti tvāmahaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।। yadā na māti tatrāpi kūpe matsyaḥ sarovare ।। tatrāpyāha punar dīnaḥ pāhi pāhi nṛpottama ।।
yadā tadā samudre taṃ prākṣipanmedinīpatiḥ ।। tadā prāha manurbhītaḥ ko api tvamasureśvaraḥ ।। yojanāyutaviṃśatyā kasya tulyaṃ bhavedvapuḥ ।। hṛṣīkeśa jagannātha jagaddhāma namo astu te ।।
sādhu sādhviti covāca samyagjñātas tvayānagha ।। bhaviṣyati jale magnā saśailavanakānanā ।। mahājīvanikāyasya rakṣaṇārthaṃ mahīpate ।। asyāṃ nidhāya sarvāṃs tān anāthān pāhi suvrata ।।
śṛṅge asminmama rājendra tademāṃ saṃyamiṣyasi ।। prajāpatistvaṃ bhavitā jagataḥ pṛthivīpate ।। manvantarādhipaścāpi devapūjyo bhaviṣyasi ।। bhagavankiyadbhirvarṣair bhaviṣyatyantarakṣayaḥ ।।
tvayā saha punaryogaḥ kathaṃ vā bhavitā mama ।। yāvadvarṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ durbhikṣam aśubhāvaham ।। saptasapterbhaviṣyanti prataptāṅgāravarṣiṇaḥ ।। bhavasyāpi lalāṭotthas tṛtīyanayanānalaḥ ।।
evaṃ dagdhā mahī sarvā yadā syādbhasmasaṃnibhā ।। tataḥ sadevanakṣatraṃ jagadyāsyati saṃkṣayam ।। vidyutpatākaḥ śoṇastu saptaite layavāridāḥ ।। samudrāḥ kṣobhamāgatya caikatvena vyavasthitāḥ ।।
vedanāvamimāṃ gṛhya sattvabījāni sarvaśaḥ ।। saṃyamya nāvaṃ macchṛṅge matsyabhāvābhirakṣitaḥ ।। somasūryāvahaṃ brahmā caturlokasamanvitaḥ ।। bhavo vedāḥ purāṇāni vidyābhiḥ sarvatovṛtam ।।
evamekārṇave jāte cākṣuṣāntarasaṃkṣaye ।। evamuktvā sa bhagavāṃs tatraivāntaradhīyata ।। abhyasan yāvad ābhūtasamplavaṃ pūrvasūcitam ।। śṛṅgī prādurbabhūvātha matsyarūpī janārdanaḥ ।।
bhūtānsarvānsamākṛṣya yogenāropya dharmavit ।। uparyupasthitastasyāḥ praṇipatya janārdanam ।। tadidānīṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvamṛṣisattamāḥ ।। tad evaikārṇave tasmin manuḥ papraccha keśavam ।।
vaṃśyānucaritaṃ caiva bhuvanasya ca vistaram ।। varṇāśramavibhāgaṃ ca tatheṣṭāpūrtasaṃjñitam ।। tatsarvaṃ vistareṇa tvaṃ dharmaṃ vyākhyātumarhasi ।। prasuptamiva cātarkyam aprajñātamalakṣaṇam ।।
tataḥ svayambhūr avyaktaḥ prabhavaḥ puṇyakarmaṇām ।। nārāyaṇa iti khyātaḥ sa ekaḥ svayam udbabhau ।। apa eva sasarjādau tāsu vīryam avāsṛjat ।। saṃvatsarasahasreṇa sūryāyutasamaprabham ।।
prabhāvād api tadvyāptyā viṣṇutvam agamat punaḥ ।। ādityaścādibhūtatvād brahmā brahma paṭhann abhūt ।। sa cākaroddiśaḥ sarvā madhye vyoma ca śāśvatam ।। jarāyurmerumukhyāś ca śailās tasyābhavaṃs tadā ।
yad aulbaṃ tad abhūn meghas taḍitsaṅghātamaṇḍalam ।। lavaṇekṣusurādyāś ca nānāratnasamanvitāḥ ।। tattejasaś ca tatraiṣa mārtaṇḍaḥ samajāyata ।। caturmukhaḥ sa bhagavān abhūl lokapitāmahaḥ ।।
tamavehi rajorūpaṃ mahat sattvam udāhṛtam ।। kathaṃ tu lokān asṛjad brahmā brahmavidāṃ varaḥ ।। āvibhūtās tathā vedāḥ sāṅgopāṅgapadakramāḥ ।। nityaṃ śabdamayaṃ puṇyaṃ śatakoṭipravistaram ।।
mīmāṃsānyāyavidyāś ca pramāṇāṣṭakasaṃyutāḥ ।। manasaḥ pūrvasṛṣṭā vai jātā yat tena mānasāḥ ।। aṅgiraś cābhavat paścāt pulastyas tadanantaram ।। pracetāś ca tataḥ putro vasiṣṭhaś cābhavat punaḥ ।।
daśemān mānasān brahmā munīn putrān ajijanat ।। aṅguṣṭhād dakṣiṇād dakṣaḥ prajāpatir ajāyata ।। bhrūmadhyād abhavat krodho lobhaś cādharasaṃbhavaḥ ।। bharataḥ karamadhyāt tu brahmasūnur abhūt tataḥ ।।
aṅgajā iti vikhyātā daśamī brahmaṇaḥ sutā ।। ahaṃkāraḥ smṛtaḥ krodho buddhir nāma kim ucyate ।। sāmyāvasthitir eteṣāṃ prakṛtiḥ parikīrtitā ।। etad eva prajāsṛṣṭiṃ karoti vikaroti ca ।।
ekā mūrtis trayo bhāgā brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ ।। mahān iti yataḥ khyātir lokānāṃ jāyate sadā ।। prādur bhavanti cānyāni tathā karmavaśāni tu ।। pāyūpasthaṃ hastapādaṃ vākka cendriyasaṃgrahaḥ ।।
utsargānandanādānagatyālāpāś ca tatkriyāḥ ।। indriyāvayavāḥ sūkṣmās tasya mūrtiṃ manīṣiṇaḥ ।। śarīrayogāj jīvo api śarīrī gadyate budhaiḥ ।। ākāśaṃ śabdatanmātrād abhūc chabdaguṇātmakam ।।
vāyoś ca sparśatanmātrāt tejaś cāvir abhūt tataḥ ।। tejovikārād abhavad vāri rājaṃś caturguṇam ।। bhūmis tu gandhatanmātrād abhūt pañcaguṇānvitā ।। ebhiḥ saṃpāditaṃ bhuṅkte puruṣaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ ।।
evaṃ ṣaḍviṃśakaṃ proktaṃ śarīram iha mānave ।। etat tattvātmakaṃ kṛtvā jagad vedhā ajījanat ।। tataḥ saṃjapatas tasya bhitvā deham akalmaṣam ।। śatarūpā ca sā khyātā sāvitrī ca nigadyate ।।
tataḥ svadehasaṃbhūtām ātmajām ity akalpayat ।। aho rūpam aho rūpam iti cāha prajāpatiḥ ।। brahmā na kiṃcid dadṛśe tanmukhālokanād ṛte ।। tataḥ praṇāmanamrāṃ tāṃ punar evābhyalokayat ।।
putrebhyo lajjitasyāsya tadrūpālokanecchayā ।। vismayasphuradoṣṭhaṃ ca pāścātyam udagāt tataḥ ।। tato anyad abhavat tasya kāmāturatayā tathā ।। sṛṣṭyarthaṃ yat kṛtaṃ tena tapaḥ paramadāruṇam ।।
āvirbhavajjaṭābhiś ca tad vaktraṃ cāvṛṇot prabhuḥ ।। prajāḥ sṛjadhvam abhitaḥ sadevāsuramānuṣīḥ ।। gateṣu teṣu sṛṣṭyarthaṃ praṇāmāvanatām imām ।। salajjāṃ cakame devaḥ kamalodaramandire ।।
tataḥkālena mahatā tasyāḥ putro abhavan manuḥ ।। tadrūpaguṇasāmānyād adhipuruṣa ucyate ।। svāyaṃbhuvā mahābhāgāḥ sapta sapta tathāpare ।। auttamipramukhās tadvad yesāṃ tvaṃ saptamo adhunā ।।
kathaṃ na doṣamagamat karmaṇānena padmabhūḥ ।। vaivāhikastatsutānāṃ chinddhi me saṃśayaṃ vibho ।। atīndriyendriyā tadvad atīndriyaśarīrikā ।। na martyairabhitaḥ śakyā vaktuṃ vai māṃsacakṣubhiḥ ।।
vidanti mārgaṃ divyānāṃ divyā eva na mānavāḥ ।। yasmāttasmānna rājendra tadvicāro nṛṇāṃ śubhaḥ ।। gāyatrī brahmaṇastadvad aṅgabhūtā nigadyate ।। bhāratī yatra yatraiva tatra tatra prajāpatiḥ ।।
gāyatrī brahmaṇaḥpārśvaṃ tathaiva na vimuñcati ।। tasmānna kaściddoṣaḥ syāt sāvitrīgamane vibho ।। svasutopagamād brahmā śaśāpa kusumāyudham ।। tasmāttvaddehamacirād rudro bhasmīkariṣyati ।।
na māmakāraṇe śaptuṃ tvamihārhasi mānada ।। indriyakṣobhajanakaḥ sarveṣāmeva dehinām ।। kṣobhyaṃ manaḥ prayatnena tvayaivoktaṃ purā vibho ।। kuru prasādaṃ bhagavan svaśarīrāptaye punaḥ ।।
rāmo nāma yadā martyo matsattvabalamāśritaḥ ।। tadbhrātustatsamasya tvaṃ tadā putratvameṣyasi ।। tato bharatavaṃśānte bhūtvā vatsanṛpātmajaḥ ।। sukhāni dharmataḥ prāpya matsamīpaṃ gamiṣyasi ।।
śokapramodābhiyuto jagāma sa yathāgatam ।। kathaṃ ca dagdho rudreṇa kimatha kusumāyudhaḥ ।। etatsarvaṃ samācakṣva mūlataḥ saṃśayo hi me ।। jananī yā manordevī śatarūpā śatendriyā ।।
tataḥ sa śatarūpāyāṃ saptāpatyānyajījanat ।। teṣāmayamabhūllokaḥ sarvajñānātmakaḥ purā ।। sanatkumāraṃ ca vibhuṃ pūrveṣāmapi pūrvajam ।। rājanyān asṛjadbāhvor viṭchūdrān ūrupādayoḥ ।।
chandāṃsi ca sasarjādau parjanyaṃ ca tataḥ param ।। koṭīśca caturaśītiṃ jarāmaraṇavarjitāḥ ।। naivaṃvidhā bhavetsṛṣṭir jarāmaraṇavarjitā ।। evaṃ sthitaḥ sa tenādau sṛṣṭeḥ sthāṇurato abhavat ।।
patnīmevāpa rūpāḍhyām anantā nāma nāmataḥ ।। dharmasya kanyā caturā sūnṛtā nāma bhāminī ।। apasyatim apasyantaṃ kīrtimantaṃ dhruvaṃ tathā ।। dhruvo varṣasahasrāṇi trīṇi kṛtvā tapaḥ purā ।।
tameva purataḥ kṛtvā dhruvaṃ saptarṣayaḥ sthitāḥ ।। agnikanyā tu succhāyā śiṣṭātsā suṣuve sutān ।। cakṣuṣaṃ brahmadauhitryāṃ vīriṇyāṃ sa ripuṃjayaḥ ।। manur vai rājakanyāyāṃ naḍvalāyāṃ sa cākṣuṣaḥ ।।
ūruḥ pūruḥ śatadyumnas tapasvī satyavāgghaviḥ ।। abhimanyustu daśamo naḍvalāyām ajāyata ।। agniṃ sumanasaṃ khyātiṃ kratumaṅgirasaṃ gayam ।। pṛthurnāma mahātejāḥ sa putrau dvāv ajījanat ।।
prācīnabarhiṣaṃ sāṅgaṃ yamaṃ śukraṃ balaṃ śubham ।। havirdhānāḥ prajās tena bahavaḥ sampravartitāḥ ।। sarve pracetaso nāma dhanurvedasya pāragāḥ ।। devādeśācca tānagnir adahadravinandana ।।
tebhyastu dakṣamekaṃ sā putram agryam ajījanat ।। ajījanatsomakanyā nadīṃ candravatīṃ tathā ।। vakṣye tāsāṃ tu vistāraṃ loke yaḥ supratiṣṭhitaḥ ।। valīmukhāḥ śaṅkukarṇāḥ karṇaprāvaraṇās tathā ।।
śvasūkaramukhāḥ kecit keciduṣṭramukhās tathā ।। sa sṛṣṭvā manasā dakṣaḥ striyaḥ paścādajījanat ।। devāsuramanuṣyādi tābhyaḥ sarvamabhūjjagat ।। utpattiṃ vistareṇaiva sūta brūhi yathātatham ।।
dakṣātprācetasād ūrdhvaṃ sṛṣṭir maithunasambhavā ।। yathā sasarja caivādau tathaiva śṛṇuta dvijāḥ ।। dakṣaḥ putrasahasrāṇi pāñcajanyāmajījanat ।। nāradaḥ prāha haryaśvān dakṣaputrānsamāgatān ।।
tataḥ sṛṣṭiṃ viśeṣeṇa kurudhvamṛṣisattamāḥ ।। adyāpi na nivartante samudrādiva sindhavaḥ ।। vairiṇyāmeva putrāṇāṃ sahasramasṛjatprabhuḥ ।। nārado anugatānprāha punastānpūrvavatsa tān ।।
āgatya cātha sṛṣṭiṃ ca kariṣyatha viśeṣataḥ ।। anviṣyanduḥkhamāpnoti tena tatparivarjayet ।। vairiṇyāṃ janayāmāsa dakṣaḥ prācetasastathā ।। saptaviṃśatiṃ somāya catasro ariṣṭanemaye ।।
dve caivāṅgirase tadvat tāsāṃ nāmāni vistarāt ।। marutvatī vasur yāmī lambā bhānur arundhatī ।। dharmapatnyaḥ samākhyātās tāsāṃ putrān nibodhata ।। marutvatyāṃ marutvanto vasos tu vasavastathā ।।
lambāyāṃ ghoṣanāmāno nāgavīthī tu yāmijā ।। saṃkalpāyāstu saṃkalpo vasusṛṣṭiṃ nibodhata ।। vasavaste samākhyātās teṣāṃ sargaṃ nibodhata ।। pratyūṣaśca prabhāsaśca vasavo aṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ ।।
śāmbo atha maṇivaktraśca yajñarakṣādhikāriṇaḥ ।। draviṇo havyavāhaśca dharaputrāv ubhau smṛtau ।। manoharā dharātputrān avāpātha hareḥ sutā ।। avāpa cānalāt putrāv agniprāyaguṇau punaḥ ।।
tasya śākho viśākhaśca naigameyaś ca pṛṣṭhajāḥ ।। viśvakarmā prabhāsasya putraḥ śilpī prajāpatiḥ ।। taḍāgārāmakūpeṣu smṛtaḥ so amaravardhakiḥ ।। haraśca bahurūpaśca tryambakaśca sureśvaraḥ ।।
ete rudrāḥ samākhyātā ekādaśa gaṇeśvarāḥ ।। koṭayaścaturaśītis tatputrāś cākṣayā matāḥ ।। putrapautrasutāścaite surabhīgarbhasambhavāḥ ।। aditirditirdanuścaiva ariṣṭā surasā tathā ।।
kadrūrviśvā munis tadvat tāsāṃ putrān nibodhata ।। vaivasvate antare caite ādityā dvādaśa smṛtāḥ ।। vivasvānsavitā pūṣā aṃśumān viṣṇur eva ca ।। mārīcātkaśyapādāpa putrānaditiruttamān ।।
ete devagaṇā viprāḥ pratimanvantareṣu ca ।। ditiḥ putradvayaṃ lebhe kaśyapād iti naḥ śrutam ।। hiraṇyakaśipostadvaj jātaṃ putracatuṣṭayam ।। prahlādaputra āyuṣmān śibir bāṣkala eva ca ।।
baleḥ putraśataṃ tv āsīd bāṇajyeṣṭhaṃ tato dvijāḥ ।। nikumbhanābho gurvakṣaḥ kukṣibhīmo vibhīṣaṇaḥ ।। bāṇaḥ sahasrabāhuś ca sarvāstragaṇasaṃyutaḥ ।। mahākālatvam agamat sāmyaṃ yaśca pinākinaḥ ।।
bhūtasaṃtāpanaś caiva mahānābhastathaiva ca ।। mahābalā mahākāyā nānārūpā mahaujasaḥ ।। vipracittiḥ pradhāno abhūd yeṣāṃ madhye mahābalaḥ ।। ayomukhaḥ śambaraś ca kapiśo nāmatastathā ।।
vidrāvaṇaśca ketuśca ketuvīryaḥ śatahradaḥ ।। ekacakro mahābāhur vajrākṣas tārakas tathā ।। svarbhānurvṛṣaparvā ca evamādyā danoḥ sutāḥ ।। upadānavī mayasyāsīt tathā mandodarī kuhūḥ ।।
pulomā kālakā caiva vaiśvānarasute hi te ।। tayoḥ ṣaṣṭisahasrāṇi dānavānāmabhūtpurā ।। avadhyā ye amarāṇāṃ vai hiraṇyapuravāsinaḥ ।। vipracittiḥ saiṃhikeyān siṃhikāyām ajījanat ।।
vyaṃsaḥ kalpaśca rājendra nalo vātāpireva ca ।। narakaḥ kālanābhaśca saramāṇas tathaiva ca ।। saṃhrādasya tu daityasya nivātakavacāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। ye hatā bhargam āśritya tv arjunena raṇājire ।।
śukī śyenī ca bhāsī ca sugrīvī gṛdhrikā śuciḥ ।। śyenī śyenāṃstathā bhāsī kurarānapyajījanat ।। haṃsasārasakrauñcāṃś ca plavāñchucirajījanat ।। eṣa tāmrānvayaḥ prokto vinatāyāṃ nibodhata ।।
saudāmanī tathā kanyā yeyaṃ nabhasi viśrutā ।। sampātiputro babhruśca śīghragaścāpi viśrutaḥ ।। sāraso rajjuvālaśca bheruṇḍaścāpi tatsutāḥ ।। surasāyāḥ sahasraṃ tu sarpāṇām abhavatpurā ।।
pradhānāsteṣu vikhyātāḥ ṣaḍviṃśatir ariṃdama ।। dhanaṃjayamahānīlapadmāśvataratakṣakāḥ ।। śaṅkhapālamahāśaṅkhapuṣpadaṃṣṭraśubhānanāḥ ।। kapilo durmukhaścāpi patañjaliriti smṛtāḥ ।।
prāyaśo yatpurā dagdhaṃ janamejayamandire ।। daṃṣṭriṇāṃ niyutaṃ teṣāṃ bhīmasenādagātkṣayam ।। surabhirjanayāmāsa kaśyapātsaṃyatavratā ।। tathā kiṃnaragandharvān ariṣṭājanayad bahūn ।।
viśvā tu yakṣarakṣāṃsi janayāmāsa koṭiśaḥ ।। janayāmāsa dharmajñān sarvānamaravallabhān ।। devairjagmuśca sāpatnaiḥ kasmātte sakhyamuttamam ।। putrapautreṣu śokārtā gatvā bhūlokamuttamam ।।
bhartur ārādhanaparā tapa ugraṃ cacāra ha ।। phalāhārā tapas tepe kṛcchraṃ cāndrāyaṇādikam ।। tataḥ sā tapasā taptā vasiṣṭhādīnapṛcchata ।। vrataṃ saubhāgyaphaladam ihaloke paratra ca ।।
yasyāḥ prabhāvādabhavat sutaśokavivarjitā ।। sutānekonapañcāśad yena lebhe ditiḥ punaḥ ।। vistareṇa tadevedaṃ matsakāśānnibodhata ।। sthāpayedavraṇaṃ kumbhaṃ sitataṇḍulapūritam ।।
sitavastrayugacchannaṃ sitacandanacarcitam ।। tāmrapātraṃ guḍopetaṃ tasyopari niveśayet ।। kuryāccharkarayopetāṃ ratiṃ tasya ca vāmataḥ ।। tadabhāve kathāṃ kuryāt kāmakeśavayornaraḥ ।।
śuklapuṣpākṣatatilair arcayenmadhusūdanam ।। ūrū smarāyeti punar manmathāyeti vai kaṭim ।। mukhaṃ padmamukhāyeti bāhū pañcaśarāya vai ।। tataḥ prabhāte taṃ kumbhaṃ brāhmaṇāya nivedayet ।।
bhuktyā tu dakṣiṇāṃ dadyād imaṃ mantramudīrayet ।। hṛdaye sarvabhūtānāṃ ya ānando abhidhīyate ।। upavāsī trayodaśyām arcayedviṣṇumavyayam ।। tatastrayodaśe māsi dhṛtadhenusamanvitām ।।
kāñcanaṃ kāmadevaṃ ca śuklāṃ gāṃ ca payasvinīm ।। śayyāgandhādikaṃ dadyāt prīyatām ityudīrayet ।। gavyena haviṣā tadvat pāyasena ca dharmavit ।। ikṣudaṇḍānatho dadyāt puṣpamālāś ca śaktitaḥ ।।
sa sarvapāpanirmuktaḥ prāpnoti harisāmyatām ।। yaḥ smaraḥ saṃsmṛto viṣṇur ānandātmā maheśvaraḥ ।। etacchrutvā cakārāsau ditiḥ sarvamaśeṣataḥ ।। cakāra karkaśāṃ bhūyo rūpayauvanaśālinīm ।।
putraṃ śakravadhārthāya samarthamamitaujasam ।। uvāca kaśyapo vākyam indrahantāram ūrjitam ।। āpastambaḥ karotviṣṭiṃ putrīyāmadya suvrate ।। āpastambastataścakre putreṣṭiṃ draviṇādhikām ।।
devā mumudire daityā vimukhāḥ syuśca dānavāḥ ।। tvayā yatno vidhātavyo hy asmingarbhe varānane ।। saṃkhyāyāṃ naiva bhoktavyaṃ garbhiṇyā varavarṇini ।। nopaskareṣūpaviśen musalolūkhalādiṣu ।।
valmīkāyāṃ na tiṣṭheta na codvignamanā bhavet ।। na śayāluḥ sadā tiṣṭhed vyāyāmaṃ ca vivarjayet ।। varjayetkalahaṃ lokair gātrabhaṅgaṃ tathaiva ca ।। na śayītottaraśirā na cāparaśirāḥ kvacit ।।
nāmaṅgalyāṃ vadedvācaṃ na ca hāsyādhikā bhavet ।। sarvauṣadhībhiḥ koṣṇena vāriṇā snānamācaret ।। tiṣṭhetprasannavadanā bhartuḥ priyahite ratā ।। itivṛttā bhavennārī viśeṣeṇa tu garbhiṇī ।।
anyathā garbhapatanam avāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ ।। svastyastu te gamiṣyāmi tathetyuktastayā punaḥ ।। tataḥ sā kaśyapoktena vidhinā samatiṣṭhata ।। vihāya devasadanaṃ tacchuśrūṣuravasthitaḥ ।।
vinīto abhavad avyagraḥ praśāntavadano bahiḥ ।। tato varṣaśatānte sā nyūne tu divasais tribhiḥ ।। akṛtvā pādayoḥ śaucaṃ prasuptā muktamūrdhajā ।। tatastadantaraṃ labdhvā praviṣṭastu śacīpatiḥ ।।
tataḥ saptaiva te jātāḥ kumārāḥ sūryavarcasaḥ ।। bhūyo api rudataścaitān ekaikaṃ saptadhā hariḥ ।। evamekonapañcāśad bhūtvā te rurudurbhṛśam ।। tataḥ sa cintayāmāsa kimetaditi vṛtrahā ।।
viditvā dhyānayogena madanadvādaśīphalam ।। vajreṇāpi hatāḥ santo na vināśam avāpnuyuḥ ।। avadhyā nūnamete vai tasmāddevā bhavantviti ।। maruto nāma te nāmnā bhavantu makhabhāginaḥ ।।
arthaśāstraṃ samāsthāya mayaitad duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam ।। ditiṃ vimānamāropya sasutāmanayaddivam ।। na jagmuraikyamasurair ataste suravallabhāḥ ।। pratisargaśca ye yeṣām adhipās tānvadasva naḥ ।।
tadauṣadhīnāmadhipaṃ cakāra yajñavratānāṃ tapasāṃ ca candram ।। apāmadhīśaṃ varuṇaṃ dhanānāṃ rājñāṃ prabhuṃ vaiśravaṇaṃ ca tadvat ।। prajāpatīnāmadhipaṃ ca dakṣaṃ cakāra śakraṃ marutāmadhīśam ।। piśācarakṣaḥpaśubhūtayakṣavetālarājaṃ tv atha śūlapāṇim ।।
gandharvavidyādharakiṃnarāṇām īśaṃ punaścitrarathaṃ cakāra ।। diśāṃ gajānāmadhipaṃ cakāra gajendramairāvatanāmadheyam ।। siṃhaṃ mṛgāṇāṃ vṛṣabhaṃ gavāṃ ca plakṣaṃ punaḥ sarvavanaspatīnām ।। pūrveṇa dikpālam athābhyaṣiñcan nāmnā sudharmāṇam arātiketum ।।
sa ketumantaṃ ca digīśamīśaś cakāra paścād bhuvanāṇḍagarbhaḥ ।। adyāpi kurvanti diśām adhīśāḥ śatrūn dahantastu bhuvo abhirakṣām ।। prajāpatiḥ so asya carācarasya babhūva sūryānvayavaṃśacihnaḥ ।। pūrveṣāṃ caritaṃ brūhi manūnāṃ madhusūdana ।।
pramāṇaṃ caiva kālasya tāṃ sṛṣṭiṃ ca samāsataḥ ।। yāmā nāma purā devā āsan svāyambhuvāntare ।। āgnīdhraścāgnibāhuśca sahaḥ savana eva ca ।। svāyambhuvasyāsya manor daśaite vaṃśavardhanāḥ ।।
etat svāyambhuvaṃ proktaṃ svārociṣamataḥ param ।। nabhonabhasyaprasṛtibhānavaḥ kīrtivardhanāḥ ।। aurvo bṛhaspatiścaiva saptaite ṛṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। hastīndraḥ sukṛto mūrtir āpo jyotirayaḥ smayaḥ ।।
dvitīyametatkathitaṃ manvantaramataḥ param ।। manurnāmauttamiryatra daśa putrānajījanat ।। madhuś ca mādhavaścaiva nabhasyo atha nabhāstathā ।। bhāvanās tatra devāḥ syur ūrjāḥ saptarṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
sitaśca sasmitaścaiva saptaite yogavardhanāḥ ।। kaviḥ pṛthus tathaivāgnir akapiḥ kapireva ca ।। sādhyā devagaṇā yatra kathitāstāmase antare ।। taporatistapasyaśca tapodyutiparaṃtapau ।।
tāmasasya sutāḥ sarve daśa vaṃśavivardhanāḥ ।। devabāhuḥ subāhuśca parjanyaḥ somapo muniḥ ।। devāścābhūtarajasas tathā prakṛtayaḥ śubhāḥ ।। yukto nirutsukaḥ sattvo nirmoho atha prakāśakaḥ ।।
bhṛguḥ sudhāmā virajāḥ sahiṣṇurnāda eva ca ।। cākṣuṣasyāntare devā lekhā nāma pariśrutāḥ ।। cākṣuṣasyāntare proktā devānāṃ pañca yonayaḥ ।। proktāḥ svāyambhuve vaṃśe ye mayā pūrvameva tu ।।
saptamaṃ tatpravakṣyāmi yadvaivasvatamucyate ।। bharadvājastathā yogī viśvāmitraḥ pratāpavān ।। kṛtvā dharmavyavasthānaṃ prayānti paramaṃ padam ।। ādityāśca surāstadvat sapta devagaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
manvantareṣu sarveṣu sapta sapta maharṣayaḥ ।। sāvarṇyasya pravakṣyāmi manorbhāvi tathāntaram ।। śatānandaḥ kāśyapaśca rāmaśca ṛṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। cariṣṇur īḍyaḥ sumatir vasuḥ śukraśca vīryavān ।।
raucyādayastathānye api manavaḥ saṃprakīrtitāḥ ।। manur bhūtisutas tadvad bhautyo nāma bhaviṣyati ।। ṛtaśca ṛtadhāmā ca viṣvakseno manus tathā ।। ṣaḍūnaṃ yugasāhasram ebhir vyāptaṃ narādhipa ।।
kalpakṣaye vinirvṛtte mucyante brahmaṇā sahā ।। brahmādyā viṣṇusāyujyaṃ yātā yāsyanti vai dvijāḥ ।। Mats pārthivāḥ pṛthivīyogāt pṛthivī kasya yogataḥ ।। gaur itīyaṃ ca vikhyātā sūta kasmādbravīhi naḥ ।।
mṛtyostu duhitā tena pariṇītā sudurmukhā ।। adharmanirataścāsīd balavān vasudhādhipaḥ ।। dharmācārasya siddhyarthaṃ jagato atha maharṣibhiḥ ।। śāpena mārayitvainam arājakamayārditāḥ ।।
tatkāyānmathyamānāttu nipeturmlecchajātayaḥ ।। pituraṃśasya cāṃśena dhārmiko dharmacāriṇaḥ ।। divyatejomayavapuḥ saratnakavacāṅgadaḥ ।। sa viprairabhiṣikto api tapaḥ kṛtvā sudāruṇam ।।
niḥsvādhyāyavaṣaṭkāraṃ nirdharmaṃ vīkṣya bhūtalam ।। tato gorūpamāsthāya bhūḥ palāyitum udyatā ।। tataḥ sthitvaikadeśe tu kiṃ karomīti cābravīt ।। sarvasya jagataḥ śīghraṃ sthāvarasya carasya ca ।।
svake pāṇau pṛthurvatsaṃ kṛtvā svāyambhuvaṃ manum ।। tatastu ṛṣibhirdugdhā vatsaḥ somastadābhavat ।। devaiśca vasudhā dugdhā dogdhā mitrastadābhavat ।। devānāṃ kāñcanaṃ pātraṃ pitṝṇāṃ rājataṃ tathā ।।
alābupātraṃ nāgānāṃ takṣako vatsako abhavat ।। asurairapi dugdheyam āyase śakrapīḍinīm ।। dogdhā dvimūrdhā tatrāsīn māyā yena pravartitā ।। kṛtvā vaiśravaṇaṃ vatsam āmapātre mahīpate ।।
raupyanābho abhavaddogdhā sumālī vatsa eva tu ।। vatsaṃ caitrarathaṃ kṛtvā gandhānpadmadale tathā ।। giribhirvasudhā dugdhā ratnāni vividhāni ca ।। vatso abhūddhimavāṃs tatra pātraṃ śailamayaṃ punaḥ ।।
pālāśapātre dogdhā tu śālaḥ puṣpalatākulaḥ ।। evamanyaiśca vasudhā tadā dugdhā yathepsitam ।। na daridrastadā kaścin na rogī na ca pāpakṛt ।। nityaṃ pramuditā lokā duḥkhaśokavivarjitāḥ ।।
bhuvastalaṃ samaṃ cakre lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। kṣayātiśayaduḥkhaṃ ca nārthaśāstrasya cādaraḥ ।। kathitāni ca pātrāṇi yatkṣīraṃ ca mayā tava ।। yajñaśrāddheṣu sarveṣu mayā tubhyaṃ niveditam ।।
tadānurāgayogācca pṛthivī viśrutā budhaiḥ ।। somavaṃśaṃ ca tattvajña yathāvadvaktumarhasi ।। tasya patnītrayaṃ tadvat saṃjñā rājñī prabhā tathā ।। prabhā prabhātaṃ suṣuve tvāṣṭrī saṃjñā tathā manum ।।
tatastejomayaṃ rūpam asahantī vivasvataḥ ।। tvāṣṭrī svarūparūpeṇa nāmnā chāyeti bhāminī ।। chāye taṃ bhaja bhartāram asmadīyaṃ varānane ।। tathetyuktvā tu sā devam agamat kvāpi suvratā ।।
janayāmāsa tasyāṃ tu putraṃ ca manurūpiṇam ।। tataḥ śaniṃ ca tapatīṃ viṣṭiṃ caiva krameṇa tu ।। chāyā svaputre abhyadhikaṃ snehaṃ cakre manau tathā ।। saṃtarjayāmāsa tadā pādamudyamya dakṣiṇam ।।
pādo ayameko bhavitā pūyaśoṇitavisravaḥ ।। niṣkāraṇamahaṃ śapto mātrā deva sakopayā ।। manunā vāryamāṇāpi mama śāpam adād vibho ।। devo apyāha yamaṃ bhūyaḥ kiṃ karomi mahāmate ।।
anivāryā bhavasyāpi kā kathānyeṣu jantuṣu ।। kledaṃ ca rudhiraṃ caiva vatsāyam apaneṣyati ।। gokarṇatīrthe vairāgyāt phalapattrānilāśanaḥ ।। varaṃ prādānmahādevaḥ saṃtuṣṭaḥ śūlabhṛttadā ।।
dharmādharmātmakasyāpi jagatastu parīkṣaṇam ।। pitṝṇāṃ cādhipatyaṃ ca dharmādharmasya cānagha ।। tvaṣṭuḥ samīpamagamad ācacakṣe ca roṣavān ।। tavāsahantī bhagavan mahastīvraṃ tamonudam ।।
nivāritā mayā sā nu tvayā caiva divākara ।। tasmānmadīyaṃ bhavanaṃ praveṣṭuṃ na tvamarhasi ।। vaḍabārūpam āsthāya bhūtale sampratiṣṭhitā ।। apaneṣyāmi te tejo yantre kṛtvā divākara ।।
tathetyuktaḥ sa raviṇā bhramau kṛtvā divākaram ।। triśūlaṃ cāpi rudrasya vajramindrasya cādhikam ।। rūpaṃ cāpratimaṃ cakre tvaṣṭā padbhyāmṛte mahat ।। arcāsvapi tataḥ pādau na kaścitkārayet kvacit ।।
kuṣṭharogamavāpnoti loke asminduḥkhasaṃyutaḥ ।। na kvacitkārayetpādau devadevasya dhīmataḥ ।। kāmayāmāsa kāmārto mukha eva divākaraḥ ।। saṃjñā ca manasā kṣobham agamadbhayavihvalā ।।
tadretasas tato jātāv aśvināv iti niścitam ।। jñātvā cirācca taṃ devaṃ saṃtoṣam agamat param ।। śanistapobalādāpa grahasāmyaṃ tataḥ punaḥ ।। viṣṭirghorātmikā tadvat kālatvena vyavasthitā ।।
ilas tu prathamasteṣāṃ putreṣṭyāṃ samajāyata ।। pṛṣadhraścātha nābhāgaḥ sarve te divyamānuṣāḥ ।। jagāma tapase bhūyaḥ sa mahendravanālayam ।। bhramandvīpāni sarvāṇi kṣmābhṛtaḥ sampradharṣayan ।।
kalpadrumalatākīrṇaṃ nāmnā śaravaṇaṃ mahat ।। umayā samayastatra purā śaravaṇe kṛtaḥ ।। strītvameṣyati tatsarvaṃ daśayojanamaṇḍale ।। strītvamāpa viśann eva vaḍabātvaṃ hayastadā ।।
ileti sābhavannārī pīnonnataghanastanī ।। pūrṇenduvadanā tanvī vilāsollāsitekṣaṇā ।। tanulomā sudaśanā mṛdugambhīrabhāṣiṇī ।। kārmukabhrūyugopetā tanutāmranakhāṅkurā ।।
ko me pitāthavā bhrātā kā me mātā bhavediha ।। cintayantīti dadṛśe somaputreṇa sāṅganā ।। budhastadāptaye yatnam akarotkāmapīḍitaḥ ।। veṇudaṇḍakṛtānekapavitrakagaṇatrikaḥ ।।
baṭubhiścānvito yuktaiḥ samitpuṣpakuśodakaiḥ ।। bahir vanasyāntaritaḥ kila pādapamaṇḍale ।। tyaktvāgnihotraśuśrūṣāṃ kva gatā mandirānmama ।। ehyehi pṛthusuśroṇi saṃbhrāntā kena hetunā ।।
kṛtvopalepanaṃ puṣpair alaṃkuru gṛhaṃ mama ।। ātmānaṃ tvāṃ ca bhartāraṃ kulaṃ ca vada me anagha ।। ahaṃ ca kāmuko nāma bahuvidyo budhaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। iti sā tasya vacanāt praviṣṭā budhamandiram ।।
ilā kṛtārthamātmānaṃ mene tadbhavanasthitā ।। mama cāsya ca me bhartur aho lāvaṇyam uttamam ।। sarvabhogamaye gehe yathendrabhavane tathā ।। ikṣvākupramukhā jagmus tadā śaravaṇāntikam ।।
ratnaparyāṇakiraṇadīptakāyām anuttamām ।। ayaṃ candraprabho nāma vājī tasya mahātmanaḥ ।। tatas tu maitrāvaruṇiṃ papracchuste purodhasam ।। vasiṣṭhaścābravīt sarvaṃ dṛṣṭvā taddhyānacakṣuṣā ।।
yaḥ pumānpraviśed atra sa nārītvamavāpsyati ।। punaḥ puruṣatāmeti yathāsau dhanadopamaḥ ।। tataste mānavā jagmur yatra devo maheśvaraḥ ।। tāv ūcatur alaṅghyo ayaṃ samayaḥ kiṃtu sāmpratam ।।
dattvā kimpuruṣo vīraḥ sa bhaviṣyatyasaṃśayam ।। ikṣvākoścāśvamedhena celaḥ kimpuruṣo abhavat ।। budhasya bhavane tiṣṭhan nilo garbhadharo abhavat ।। budhaścotpādya taṃ putraṃ svarlokam agamattataḥ ।।
somārkavaṃśayor ādāv ilo abhūnmanunandanaḥ ।। ikṣvākur arkavaṃśasya tathaivoktastapodhanāḥ ।। punaḥ putratrayamabhūt sudyumnasyāparājitam ।। utkalasyotkalā nāma gayasya tu gayā matā ।।
pratiṣṭhāne abhiṣicyātha sa purūravasaṃ sutam ।। ikṣvākurjyeṣṭhadāyādo madhyadeśamavāptavān ।। nābhāgasyāmbarīṣastu dhṛṣṭasya ca sutatrayam ।। ānarto nāma śaryāteḥ sukanyā caiva dārikā ।।
ānarto nābha deśo abhūn nagarī ca kuśasthalī ।। kakudmī cāparaṃ nāma jyeṣṭhaḥ putraśatasya ca ।। karūṣasya tu kārūṣā bahavaḥ prathitā bhuvi ।। ikṣvākuvaṃśaṃ vakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvamṛṣisattamāḥ ।।
jyeṣṭhaḥ putraśatasyāsīd daśa pañca ca tatsutāḥ ।। caturdaśottaraṃ cānyac chatamasya tathābhavat ।। jyeṣṭhaḥ kakutstho nāmnābhūt tatsutastu suyodhanaḥ ।। industasya ca putro abhūd yuvanāśvastato abhavat ।।
nirmitā yena śrāvastī gauḍadeśe dvijottamāḥ ।। dhundhumāratvamagamad dhundhunāmnā hataḥ purā ।। kapilāśvaśca vikhyāto dhaundhumāriḥ pratāpavān ।। haryaśvasya nikumbho abhūt saṃhatāśvas tato abhavat ।।
yuvanāśvo raṇāśvasya māndhātā ca tato abhavat ।। mucukundaśca vikhyātaḥ śatrujicca pratāpavān ।। sambhūtistasya putro abhūt tridhanvā ca tato abhavat ।। tasmātsatyavrato nāma tasmātsatyarathaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
rohitācca vṛko jāto vṛkādbāhurajāyata ।। dve bhārye sagarasyāpi prabhā bhānumatī tathā ।। aurvastuṣṭastayoḥ prādād yatheṣṭaṃ varamuttamam ।। gṛhṇātu vaṃśakartāraṃ prabhāgṛhṇād bahūṃstadā ।।
tataḥ ṣaṣṭisahasrāṇi suṣuve yādavī prabhā ।। asamañjasastu tanayo yo aṃśumānnāma viśrutaḥ ।। yena bhāgīrathī gaṅgā tapaḥ kṛtvāvatāritā ।। nābhāgasyāmbarīṣo abhūt sindhudvīpas tato abhavat ।।
tasya kalmāṣapādastu sarvakarmā tataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। nighnaputrāv ubhau jātāv anamitraraghū nṛpau ।। raghor abhūddilīpastu dilīpādajakastathā ।। tasmāddaśaratho jātas tasya putracatuṣṭayam ।।
rāvaṇāntakarastadvad raghūṇāṃ vaṃśavardhanaḥ ।। tasya putrau kuśalavāv ikṣvākukulavardhanau ।। nalastu naiṣadhastasmān nabhāstasmādajāyata ।। tasya putro abhavadvīro devānīkaḥ pratāpavān ।।
tataścandrāvalokastu tārāpīḍastato abhavat ।। śrutāyur abhavattasmād bhārate yo nipātitaḥ ।। vīrasenasutastadvan naiṣadhaśca narādhipaḥ ।। ikṣvākuvaṃśaprabhavāḥ prādhānyena prakīrtitāḥ ।।
raveśca śrāddhadevatvaṃ somasya ca viśeṣataḥ ।। svarge pitṛgaṇāḥ sapta trayasteṣāmamūrtayaḥ ।। amūrtayaḥ pitṛgaṇā vairājasya prajāpateḥ ।। ye caite yogavibhraṣṭāḥ prāpya lokānsanātanān ।।
samprāpya tāṃ smṛtiṃ bhūyo yogaṃ sāṃkhyamanuttamam ।। yogināmeva deyāni tasmācchrāddhāni dātṛbhiḥ ।। krauñcadvīpaḥ smṛto yena caturtho ghṛtasaṃvṛtaḥ ।। umaikaparṇāparṇā ca tīvravrataparāyaṇāḥ ।।
dattā himavatā bālāḥ sarvā loke tapo adhikāḥ ।। himavadduhitā tadvat kathaṃ jātā mahītale ।। dakṣeṇa lokajananī sūta vistarato vada ।। samāhūteṣu deveṣu provāca pitaraṃ satī ।।
ayogya iti tāmāha dakṣo yajñeṣu śūlabhṛt ।। cukopātha satī dehaṃ tyakṣyāmīti tvadudbhavam ।। kṣatriyatve aśvamedhe ca rudrāttvaṃ nāśameṣyasi ।। nirdahantī tadātmānaṃ sadevāsurakiṃnaraiḥ ।।
upagamyābravīddakṣaḥ praṇipatyātha duḥkhitaḥ ।। duhitṛtvaṃ gatā devi mamānugrahakāmyayā ।। prasādaṃ kuru dharmajñe na māṃ tyaktumihārhasi ।। kiṃtvavaśyaṃ tvayā martye hatayajñena śūlinā ।।
prajāpatistvaṃ bhavitā daśānāmaṅgajo apyalam ।। matsaṃnidhau tapaḥ kurvan prāpsyase yogamuttamam ।। tīrtheṣu ca tvaṃ draṣṭavyā stotavyā kaiśca nāmabhiḥ ।। sarvalokeṣu yatkiṃcid rahitaṃ na mayā vinā ।।
smartavyā bhūtikāmair vā tāni vakṣyāmi tattvataḥ ।। mānase kumudā nāma viśvakāyā tathāmbare ।। madotkaṭā caitrarathe jayantī hastināpure ।। ekāmbhake kīrtimatī viśvāṃ viśveśvare viduḥ ।।
nandā himavataḥ pṛṣṭhe gokarṇe bhadrakarṇikā ।। śrīśaile mādhavī nāma bhadrā bhadreśvare tathā ।। rudrakoṭyāṃ ca rudrāṇī kālī kālañjare girau ।। śālagrāme mahādevī śivaliṅge jalapriyā ।।
utpalākṣī sahasrākṣe kamalākṣe mahotpalā ।। vipāśāyām amoghākṣī pāṭalā puṇḍravardhane ।। vipule vipulā nāma kalyāṇī malayācale ।। godāśrame trisaṃdhyā tu gaṅgādvāre ratipriyā ।।
rukmiṇī dvāravatyāṃ tu rādhā vṛndāvane vane ।। citrakūṭe tathā sītā vindhye vindhyādhivāsinī ।। ramaṇā rāmatīrthe tu yamunāyāṃ mṛgāvatī ।। arogā vaidyanāthe tu mahākāle maheśvarī ।।
māṇḍavye māṇḍavī nāma svāhā māheśvare pure ।। someśvare varārohā prabhāse puṣkarāvatī ।। mahālaye mahābhāgā payoṣṇyāṃ piṅgaleśvarī ।। utpalāvartake lolā subhadrā śoṇasaṃgame ।।
jālaṃdhare viśvamukhī tārā kiṣkindhaparvate ।। bhīmā devī himādrau tu puṣṭirviśveśvare tathā ।। śaṅkhoddhāre dhvanirnāma dhṛtiḥ piṇḍārake tathā ।। veṇāyāmamṛtā nāma badaryāmurvaśī tathā ।।
manmathā hemakūṭe tu mukuṭe satyavādinī ।। gāyatrī vedavadane pārvatī śivasaṃnidhau ।। sūryabimbe prabhā nāma mātṝṇāṃ vaiṣṇavī matā ।। citte brahmakalā nāma śaktiḥ sarvaśarīriṇām ।।
aṣṭottaraṃ ca tīrthānāṃ śatametadudāhṛtam ।। eṣu tīrtheṣu yaḥ kṛtvā snānaṃ paśyati māṃ naraḥ ।। yastu matparamaṃ kālaṃ karotyeteṣu mānavaḥ ।। nāmnāmaṣṭaśataṃ yastu śrāvayecchivasaṃnidhau ।।
godāne śrāddhadāne vā ahany ahani vā budhaḥ ।। evaṃ vadantī sā tatra dadāhātmānam ātmanā ।। pārvatī sābhavaddevī śivadehārdhadhāriṇī ।। arundhatī japantyetat prāpa yogamanuttamam ।।
yayātiḥ putralābhaṃ ca dhanalābhaṃ ca bhārgavaḥ ।। vaiśyāḥ śūdrāśca bahavaḥ siddhimīyuryathepsitām ।। na tatra śoko daurgatyaṃ kadācidapi jāyate ।। vartante deva pitaro devā yānbhāvayantyalam ।।
acchodā nāma teṣāṃ tu mānasī kanyakā nadī ।। acchodā tu tapaścakre divyaṃ varṣasahasrakam ।। divyarūpadharāḥ sarve divyamālyānulepanāḥ ।। tanmadhye amāvasuṃ nāma pitaraṃ vīkṣya sāṅganā ।।
yogādbhraṣṭā tu sā tena vyabhicāreṇa bhāminī ।। tithāv amāvasur yasyām icchāṃ cakre na tāṃ prati ।। pitṝṇāṃ vallabhā tasmāt tasyāmakṣayakārakam ।। sā pitṝn prārthayāmāsa pure cātmaprasiddhaye ।।
bhaviṣyamarthamālokya devakāryaṃ ca te tadā ।। divi divyaśarīreṇa yat kiṃcit kriyate budhaiḥ ।। sadyaḥ phalanti karmāṇi devatve pretya mānuṣe ।। aṣṭāviṃśe bhavitrī tvaṃ dvāpare matsyayonijā ।।
tasmādrājño vasoḥ kanyā tvam avaśyaṃ bhaviṣyasi ।। parāśarasya vīryeṇa putramekamavāpsyasi ।। sa vedamekaṃ bahudhā vibhajiṣyati te sutaḥ ।। vicitravīryastanayas tathā citrāṅgado nṛpaḥ ।।
prauṣṭhapadyaṣṭakārūpā pitṛloke bhaviṣyasi ।। āyurārogyadā nityaṃ sarvakāmaphalapradā ।। puṇyatoṣā saricchreṣṭhā loke hy acchodanāmikā ।। sāpyavāpa ca tatsarvaṃ phalaṃ yaduditaṃ purā ।।
lokā barhiṣado yatra pitaraḥ santi suvratāḥ ।। saṃkalpyā barhiṣo yatra tiṣṭhanti phaladāyinaḥ ।। yāṃś ca devāsuragaṇā gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ ।। pulastyaputrāḥ śataśas tapoyogasamanvitāḥ ।।
eteṣāṃ pīvarī kanyā mānasī divi viśrutā ।। prasanno bhagavāṃstasyā varaṃ vavre tu sā hareḥ ।। dehi deva prasannastvaṃ patiṃ me vadatāṃ varam ।। bhavitā tasya bhāryā tvaṃ yogācāryasya suvrate ।।
pāñcālādhipaterdeyā mānuṣasya tvayā tadā ।। kṛṣṇo gauraḥ prabhuḥ śambhur bhaviṣyanti ca te sutāḥ ।। tānutpādya punar yogāt savarā mokṣameṣyasi ।। nāmnā tu mānasāḥ sarve sarve te dharmamūrtayaḥ ।।
virājamānāḥ krīḍanti yatra te śrāddhadāyinaḥ ।। kiṃ punaḥ śrāddhadā viprā bhaktimantaḥ kriyānvitāḥ ।। śukrasya dayitā patnī sādhyānāṃ kīrtivardhinī ।। pitaro yatra tiṣṭhanti haviṣmanto aṅgiraḥsutāḥ ।।
rājñāṃ tu pitaraste vai svargamokṣaphalapradāḥ ।। patnī hy aṃśumataḥ śreṣṭhā snuṣā pañcajanasya ca ।। lokāḥ kāmadughā nāma kāmabhogaphalapradāḥ ।। ājyapā nāma lokeṣu kardamasya prajāpateḥ ।।
yatra śrāddhakṛtaḥ sarve paśyanti yugapadgatāḥ ।। api janmāyutairdṛṣṭān anubhūtānsahasraśaḥ ।। yā patnī nahuṣasyāsīd yayāterjananī tathā ।। traya ete gaṇāḥ proktāś caturthaṃ tu vadāmyataḥ ।।
yeṣāṃ tu mānasī kanyā narmadā nāma viśrutā ।। dharmamūrtidharāḥ sarve parato brahmaṇaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। kṛtvā sṛṣṭyādikaṃ sarvaṃ mānase sāmprataṃ sthitāḥ ।। bhūtāni yā pāvayati dakṣiṇāpathagāminī ।।
jñātvā śrāddhāni kurvanti dharmābhāve api sarvadā ।। pitṝṇāmādisarge tu śrāddhameva vinirmitam ।। dattaṃ svadhā purodhāya pitṝn prīṇāti sarvadā ।। agnyabhāve api viprasya prāṇāv api jale athavā ।।
pitṝṇām ambaraṃ sthānaṃ dakṣiṇā dikpraśasyate ।। darbhā māṃsaṃ ca pāṭhīnaṃ gokṣīraṃ madhurā rasāḥ ।। yavanīvāramudgekṣuśuklapuṣpaghṛtāni ca ।। dveṣyāṇi sampravakṣyāmi śrāddhe varjyāni yāni tu ।।
padmabilvārkadhattūrapāribhadrāṭarūṣakāḥ ।। kodravodāracaṇakāḥ kapitthaṃ madhukātasī ।। pitṝn prīṇāti yo bhaktyā te punaḥ prīṇayanti tam ।। devakāryādapi punaḥ pitṛkāryaṃ viśiṣyate ।।
śīghraprasādāstvakrodhā niḥśastrāḥ sthirasauhṛdāḥ ।। bhaktānuraktāḥ sukhadāḥ pitaraḥ pūrvadevatāḥ ।। puṇyaṃ pavitram āyuṣyaṃ kīrtanīyaṃ sadā nṛbhiḥ ।। śrāddhakālaṃ ca vividhaṃ śrāddhabhedaṃ tathaiva ca ।।
kasminvāsarabhāge vā pitṛbhyaḥ śrāddhamācaret ।। vidhinā kena kartavyaṃ kathaṃ prīṇāti tatpitṝn ।। payomūlaphalair vāpi pitṛbhyaḥ prītimāvahan ।। nityaṃ tāvatpravakṣyāmi arghyāvāhanavarjitam ।।
pārvaṇaṃ trividhaṃ proktaṃ śṛṇu tāvanmahīpate ।। pañcāgniḥ snātakaścaiva trisuparṇaḥ ṣaḍaṅgavit ।। sarvajño vedavinmantrī jñātavaṃśaḥ kulānvitaḥ ।। śivabhaktaḥ pitṛparaḥ sūryabhakto atha vaiṣṇavaḥ ।।
bhojayeccāpi dauhitraṃ yatnataḥ svasuhṛdgurūn ।। yaśca vyākurute vākyaṃ yaśca mīmāṃsate adhvaram ।। sāmago brahmacārī ca vedayukto atha brahmavit ।। ete bhojyāḥ prayatnena varjanīyānnibodha me ।।
kunakhī śyāvadantaśca kuṇḍagolāśvapālakāḥ ।। baiḍālī bakavṛttiśca dambhī devalakādayaḥ ।। triśaṅkur barbaradrāvavītadraviḍakoṅkaṇān ।। pūrvedyuraparedyurvā vinītātmā nimantrayet ।।
vāyubhūtā nu gacchanti tathāsīnānupāsate ।। evaṃ nimantrya niyamaṃ śrāvayetpitṛbāndhavān ।। bhavitavyaṃ bhavadbhiśca mayā ca śrāddhakāriṇā ।। piṇḍānvāhāryakaṃ kuryāc chrāddhamindukṣaye sadā ।।
śrāddhaṃ samācaredbhaktyā goṣṭhe vā jalasaṃnidhau ।। pitṛbhyo nirvapāmīti sarvaṃ dakṣiṇato nyaset ।। te api tasyāyatāḥ kāryāś caturaṅgulavistṛtāḥ ।। ratnimātraṃ pariślakṣṇaṃ hastākārāgramuttamam ।।
tilāḥ pātrāṇi sadvāso gandhadhūpānulepanam ।। evamāsādya tatsarvaṃ bhavanasyāgrato bhuvi ।। akṣatābhiḥ sapuṣpābhis tadabhyarcyāpasavyavat ।। āsaneṣūpakḷpteṣu darbhavatsu vidhānavat ।।
dvau daive pitṛkṛtye trīn ekaikamubhayatra ca ।। daivapūrvaṃ niyojyātha viprānarghyādinā budhaḥ ।। svagṛhyoktavidhānena kāṃsye kṛtvā caruṃ tataḥ ।। dakṣiṇāgnau pratīte vā ya ekāgnirdvijottamaḥ ।।
prācīnāvītinā kāryam ataḥ sarvaṃ vijānatā ।। dadyādudakapātrais tu satilaṃ savyapāṇinā ।। vidhāya lekhā yatnena nirvāpeṣvavanejanam ।। nidhāya piṇḍam ekaikaṃ sarvadarbheṣvanukramāt ।।
teṣu darbheṣu taṃ hastaṃ vimṛjyāllepabhāginām ।। ṣaḍapyṛtūnnamaskṛtya gandhadhūpārhaṇādibhiḥ ।। ekāgnereka eva syān nirvāpo darvikā tathā ।। tadvatpiṇḍādike kuryād āvāhanavisarjanam ।।
tāneva viprānprathamaṃ prāśayedyatnato naraḥ ।। anvāhāryakam ityuktaṃ tasmāttaccandrasaṃkṣaye ।। tatpiṇḍāgraṃ prayaccheta svadhaiṣāmastviti bruvan ।। varjayetkrodhaparatāṃ smarannārāyaṇaṃ harim ।।
sodakaṃ cānnamuddhṛtya salilaṃ prakṣipedbhuvi ।। svastivācanakaṃ sarvaṃ piṇḍopari samāharet ।। visṛjya brāhmaṇāṃstadvat teṣāṃ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇam ।। dātāro no abhivardhantāṃ vedāḥ saṃtatireva ca ।।
annaṃ ca no bahu bhaved atithīṃśca labhemahi ।। etadastviti tatproktam anvāhāryaṃ tu pārvaṇam ।। piṇḍāṃstu gojaviprebhyo dadyādagnau jale api vā ।। patnī tu madhyamaṃ piṇḍaṃ prāśayed vinayānvitā ।।
tāvaduccheṣaṇaṃ tiṣṭhed yāvadviprā visarjitāḥ ।। iṣṭaiḥ saha tataḥ śānto bhuñjīta pitṛsevitam ।। śrāddhakṛcchrāddhabhukcaiva sarvametadvivarjayet ।। anena vidhinā śrāddhaṃ nirudvāsyeha nirvapet ।।
tatrānena vidhānena deyam agnimatā sadā ।। śrāddhaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ nāma bhuktimuktiphalapradam ।। amāvāsyāṣṭakākṛṣṇapakṣe pañcadaśīṣu ca ।। gajacchāyāvyatīpāte viṣṭivaidhṛtivāsare ।।
pañcadaśī ca māghasya nabhasye ca trayodaśī ।। tathā manvantarādau ca deyaṃ śrāddhaṃ vijānatā ।। tṛtīyā caitramāsasya tathā bhādrapadasya ca ।। āṣāḍhasyāpi daśamī māghamāsasya saptamī ।।
manvantarādayaś caitā dattasyākṣayyakārikāḥ ।। māghamāsasya saptamyāṃ sā tu syādrathasaptamī ।। śrāddhaṃ kṛtaṃ tena samāḥ sahasraṃ rahasyametatpitaro vadanti ।। tīrthāyatanagoṣṭheṣu dīpodyānagṛheṣu ca ।।
viprānpūrve pare cāhni vinītātmā nimantrayet ।। dvau daive trīṃstathā pitrya ekaikamubhayatra vā ।। viśvāndevānyavaiḥ puṣpair abhyarcyāsanapūrvakam ।। śaṃ no devīty apaḥ kuryād yavo asīti yavānapi ।।
viśve devāsa ityābhyām āvāhya vikiredyavān ।। abhyarcya tābhyāmutsṛṣṭaṃ pitṛkāryaṃ samārabhet ।। khapavitrāṇi kṛtvādau śaṃ no devīty apaḥ kṣipet ।। pātraṃ vanaspatimayaṃ tathā parṇamayaṃ punaḥ ।।
sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ vāpi pitṝṇāṃ pātramucyate ।। rājatair bhājanaireṣām athavā rajatānvitaiḥ ।। tathārghyapiṇḍabhojyādau pitṝṇāṃ rājataṃ matam ।। amaṅgalaṃ tadyatnena devakāryeṣu varjayet ।।
yā divyeti piturnāma gotrairdarbhakaro nyaset ।। uśantastvā tathāyantu ṛgbhyām āvāhayetpitṝn ।। hastāttadudakaṃ pūrvaṃ dattvā saṃsravamāditaḥ ।। pitṛbhyaḥ sthānamasīti nidhāya pariṣecayet ।।
ubhābhyāmapi hastābhyām āhṛtya pariveṣayet ।। guṇāḍhyaiḥ sūpaśākaistu nānābhakṣyairviśeṣataḥ ।। māsaṃ prīṇāti vai sarvān pitṝnityāha keśavaḥ ।। aurabhreṇātha caturaḥ śākunenātha pañca vai ।।
sapta pārṣatamāṃsena tathāṣṭāv eṇajena tu ।। śaśakūrmajamāṃsena māsānekādaśaiva tu ।। rauraveṇa ca tṛpyanti māsānpañcadaśaiva tu ।। kālaśākena cānantā khaḍgamāṃsena caiva hi ।।
dattamakṣayamityāhuḥ pitaraḥ pūrvadevatāḥ ।। brahmaviṣṇvarkarudrāṇāṃ sūktāni vividhāni ca ।। bṛhadrathaṃtaraṃ tadvaj jyeṣṭhasāma sarauhiṇam ।। maṇḍalaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ tadvat prītikāri tu yatpunaḥ ।।
bhuktavatsu tatasteṣu bhojanopāntike nṛpa ।। samutsṛjedbhuktavatām agrato vikiredbhuvi ।। bhūmau dattena tṛpyantu prayāntu paramāṃ gatim ।। tattṛptaye annaṃ bhuvi dattametat prayāntu lokeṣu sukhāya tadvat ।।
ucchiṣṭabhāgadheyaḥ syād darbhe vikirayośca yaḥ ।। upalipte mahīpṛṣṭhe gośakṛnmūtravāriṇā ।। sarvavarṇena cānnena piṇḍāṃstu pitṛyajñavat ।। gandhadhūpādikaṃ dadyāt kṛtvā pratyavanejanam ।।
pitryamānīya tatkāryaṃ vidhivaddarbhapāṇinā ।। athācānteṣu cācamya vāri dadyātsakṛtsakṛt ।। satilaṃ nāmagotreṇa dadyācchaktyā ca dakṣiṇām ।। dadyādyadiṣṭaṃ viprāṇām ātmanaḥ pitureva ca ।।
tataḥ svadhāvācanakaṃ viśvadeveṣu codakam ।। aghorāḥ pitaraḥ santu santvityuktaḥ punar dvijaiḥ ।। dātāro no abhivardhantām iti caivamudīrayet ।। svastivācanakaṃ kuryāt piṇḍānuddhṛtya bhaktitaḥ ।।
tato grahabaliṃ kuryād iti dharmavyavasthitiḥ ।। dāsavargasya tatpitryaṃ bhāgadheyaṃ pracakṣate ।। aputrāṇāṃ saputrāṇāṃ strīṇāmapi narādhipa ।। vāje vāja iti japan kuśāgreṇa visarjayet ।।
bandhuvargeṇa sahitaḥ putrabhāryāsamanvitaḥ ।। vaiśvadevaṃ prakurvīta naityakaṃ balimeva ca ।। bhuñjītātithisaṃyuktaḥ sarvaṃ pitṛniṣevitam ।। śrāddhaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ nāma sarvakāmaphalapradam ।।
śūdro apyamantravatkuryād anena vidhinā budhaḥ ।। utsavānandasambhāre yajñodvāhādimaṅgale ।। tato mātāmahā rājan viśve devāstathaiva ca ।। prāṅmukho nirvapetpiṇḍān dūrvayā ca kuśairyutān ।।
yugmā dvijātayaḥ pūjyā vastrakārtasvarādibhiḥ ।। māṅgalyāni ca sarvāṇi vācayeddvijapuṃgavaiḥ ।। namaskāreṇa mantreṇa kuryādāmānnataḥ sadā ।। dānena sarvakāmāptir asya saṃjāyate yataḥ ।।
mṛte putrairyathā kāryam āśaucaṃ ca pitaryapi ।। kṣatriyeṣu daśa dve ca pakṣaṃ vaiśyeṣu caiva hi ।। naiśaṃ vākṛtacūḍasya trirātraṃ parataḥ smṛtam ।। tathāsthisaṃcayād ūrdhvam aṅgasparśo vidhīyate ।।
pātheyaṃ tasya tatproktaṃ yataḥ prītikaraṃ mahat ।। gṛhaṃ putraṃ kalatraṃ ca dvādaśāhaṃ prapaśyati ।। sarvadāhopaśāntyartham adhvaśramavināśanam ।। kṣatrādiḥ sūtakānte tu bhojayedayujo dvijān ।।
āvāhanāgnaukaraṇaṃ daivahīnaṃ vidhānataḥ ।। upatiṣṭhatāmityetad deyaṃ paścāttilodakam ।। śeṣaṃ pūrvavadatrāpi kāryaṃ vedavidā pituḥ ।। sūtakāntāddvitīye ahni śayyāṃ dadyādvilakṣaṇām ।।
saṃpūjya dvijadāmpatyaṃ nānābharaṇabhūṣaṇaiḥ ।। udakumbhaśca dātavyo bhakṣyabhojyasamanvitaḥ ।। tataḥ saṃvatsare pūrṇe sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ bhavet ।। vṛddhipūrveṣu yogyaśca gṛhasthaśca bhavettataḥ ।।
pitṝn nivāsayettatra pṛthakpretaṃ vinirdiśet ।। arghārthaṃ pitṛpātreṣu pretapātraṃ prasecayet ।। ye samānā iti dvābhyām antyaṃ tu vibhajettridhā ।। tataḥ pitṛtvamāpannaḥ sarvatastuṣṭimāgataḥ ।।
sapiṇḍīkaraṇādūrdhvaṃ tasmai tasmānna dīyate ।। tataḥ prabhṛti saṃkrāntāv uparāgādiparvasu ।। ekoddiṣṭaṃ parityajya mṛtāhe yaḥ samācaret ।। mṛtāhe pārvaṇaṃ kurvan nadho adho yāti mānavaḥ ।।
pratisaṃvatsaraṃ tasmād ekoddiṣṭaṃ samācaret ।। pretāyānnasamāyuktaṃ so aśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet ।। tenāgnaukaraṇaṃ kuryāt piṇḍāṃstenaiva nirvapet ।। yadā prāpsyati kālena tadā mucyeta bandhanāt ।।
piṇḍadaḥ saptamasteṣāṃ sāpiṇḍyaṃ sāptapauruṣam ।। gacchanti pitṛlokasthān prāpakaḥ ko atra gadyate ।। śubhāśubhātmakaiḥ pretair dattaṃ tadbhujyate katham ।। prapitāmahāṃstathādityān ityevaṃ vaidikī śrutiḥ ।।
śrāddhasya mantrāḥ śraddhā ca upayojyātibhaktitaḥ ।। nāmagotrakāladeśā bhavāntaragatānapi ।। devo yadi pitā jātaḥ śubhakarmānuyogataḥ ।। daityatve bhogarūpeṇa paśutve ca tṛṇaṃ bhavet ।।
pānaṃ bhavati yakṣatve rākṣasatve tathāmiṣam ।। manuṣyatve annapānāni nānābhogarasaṃ bhavet ।। dānaśaktiḥ savibhavā rūpamārogyameva ca ।। āyuḥ putrān dhanaṃ vidyāṃ svargaṃ mokṣaṃ sukhāni ca ।।
pañcabhirjanmasambandhair gatā viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam ।। pañcabhirjanmasambandhaiḥ kathaṃ karmakṣayo bhavet ।। nāmataḥ karmatastasya sutānsapta nibodhata ।। vāgduṣṭaḥ pitṛvartī ca gargaśiṣyāstadābhavan ।।
anāvṛṣṭiśca mahatī sarvalokabhayaṃkarī ।। khādāmaḥ kapilāmetāṃ vayaṃ kṣutpīḍitā bhṛśam ।। yadyavaśyamiyaṃ vadhyā śrāddharūpeṇa yojyatām ।। eva kurvityanujñātaḥ pitṛvartī tadānujaiḥ ।।
dvau daive bhrātarau kṛtvā pitre trīnapyanukramāt ।। cakāra mantravacchrāddhaṃ smaranpitṛparāyaṇaḥ ।। vyāghreṇa nihatā dhenur vatso ayaṃ pratigṛhyatām ।। vaidikaṃ balamāśritya krūre karmaṇi nirbhayāḥ ।।
jātismaratvaṃ prāptāste pitṛbhāvena bhāvitāḥ ।। tena te bhavane jātā vyādhānāṃ krūrakarmiṇām ।। te tu vairāgyayogena āsthāyānaśanaṃ punaḥ ।। nīlakaṇṭhasya purataḥ pitṛbhāvānubhāvitāḥ ।।
lokair avekṣyamāṇāste tīrthānte anaśanena tu ।। nāmataḥ karmataḥ sarvāñ chṛṇudhvaṃ dvijasattamāḥ ।। sunetraścāṃśumāṃścaiva saptaite yogapāragāḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā vibhrājamānaṃ tam udyāne strībhiranvitam ।।
pañcālānvayasambhūtaṃ prabhūtabalavāhanam ।। pitṛvartī ca yo vipraḥ śrāddhakṛt pitṛvatsalaḥ ।। mantritve cakratuścecchām asminmartye dvijottamāḥ ।। vibhrājaputrastveko abhūd brahmadatta iti smṛtaḥ ।।
brahmadatto abhiṣiktaḥ san purohitavipaścitā ।। yogavitsarvajantūnāṃ rutavettābhavattadā ।। saṃnatirnāma vikhyātā kapilā yābhavatpurā ।। tayā cakāra sahitaḥ sa rājyaṃ rājanandanaḥ ।।
dadarśa kīṭamithunam anaṅgakalahākulam ।। pañcabāṇābhitaptāṅgaḥ sagadgadamuvāca ha ।। madhyakṣāmātijaghanā bṛhadvakṣo abhigāminī ।। sulakṣyanetrarasanā guḍaśarkaravatsalā ।।
proṣite sati dīnā tvaṃ kruddhe api bhayacañcalā ।। sā tamāha sakopā tu kim ālapasi māṃ śaṭha ।। pradattaṃ samatikrānte dine anyasyāḥ samanmatha ।। tadekamaparādhaṃ me kṣantumarhasi bhāmini ।।
spṛśāmi pādau satyena prasīda praṇatasya me ।। ātmānam arpayāmāsa mohanāya pipīlikā ।। sarvasattvarutajñatvāt prasādāc cakrapāṇinaḥ ।। taccābhavatkasya kule cakravākacatuṣṭayam ।।
taccābhavatkasya kule cakravākacatuṣṭayam ।। vṛddhadvijasya dāyādā viprā jātismarāḥ purā ।। nāmataḥ karmataścaite sudaridrasya te sutāḥ ।। yāsyāmaḥ paramāṃ siddhim ity ūcus te dvijottamāḥ ।।
uvāca dīnayā vācā kimetaditi putrakāḥ ।। vṛddhaṃ pitaramutsṛjya daridraṃ vanavāsinaḥ ।। ūcuste kalpitā vṛttis tava tāta vadasva tat ।। dhanaṃ grāmasahasrāṇi prabhāte paṭhatastava ।।
kālañjare sapta ca cakravākā ye mānase te vayamatra siddhāḥ ।। vṛddho api rājabhavanaṃ jagāmātmārthasiddhaye ।। putrārthī devadeveśaṃ hariṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum ।। tataḥ kālena mahatā tuṣṭastasya janārdanaḥ ।।
evamuktastu devena vavre sa varamuttamam ।। pāragaṃ sarvaśāstrāṇāṃ dhārmikaṃ yogināṃ param ।। evamastviti viśvātmā tamāha parameśvaraḥ ।। tataḥ sa tasya putro abhūd brahmadattaḥ pratāpavān ।।
sarvasattvarutajñaśca sarvasattveśvareśvaraḥ ।। yatra tatkīṭamithunaṃ ramamāṇamavasthitam ।। kimapyāśaṅkya manasā tamapṛcchannareśvaram ।। hāsyahetuṃ na jānāmi yadakāle kṛtaṃ tvayā ।।
rāgavāgbhiḥ samutpannam etaddhāsyaṃ varānane ।। na sāmanyat tadā devī prāhālīkamidaṃ vacaḥ ।। kathaṃ pipīlikālāpaṃ martyo vetti vinā surān ।। tato niruttaro rājā jijñāsustatpuro hareḥ ।।
svapne prāha hṛṣīkeśaḥ prabhāte paryaṭanpuram ।। ityuktvāntardadhe viṣṇuḥ prabhāte atha nṛpaḥ purāt ।। gadantaṃ vipram āyāntaṃ taṃ vṛddhaṃ saṃdadarśa ha ।। kālañjare sapta ca cakravākā ye mānase te vayamatra siddhāḥ ।।
jātismaratvamagamat tau ca mantrivarāv ubhau ।। pāñcāla iti lokeṣu viśrutaḥ sarvaśāstravit ।। bhūtvā jātismarau śokāt patitāv agratastadā ।। evaṃ vilapya bahuśas trayaste yogapāragāḥ ।।
tatastasmai dhanaṃ dattvā prabhūtagrāmasaṃyutam ।। ātmīyaṃ nṛpatiḥ putraṃ nṛpalakṣaṇasaṃyutam ।। mānase militāḥ sarve tataste yogināṃ varāḥ ।। saṃnatiścābhavadbhraṣṭā mayaitatkila kāritam ।।
tatheti prāha rājā tu punastāmabhinandayan ।। tataste yogamāsthāya sarva eva vanaukasaḥ ।। evamāyurdhanaṃ vidyāṃ svargaṃ mokṣaṃ sukhāni ca ।। ya idaṃ pitṛmāhātmyaṃ brahmadattasya ca dvijāḥ ।।
kalpakoṭiśataṃ sāgraṃ brahmaloke mahīyate ।। tīrtheṣu keṣu ca kṛtaṃ śrāddhaṃ bahuphalaṃ bhavet ।। yatkiṃciddīyate tatra tadakṣayamudāhṛtam ।। nāmatastāni vakṣyāmi saṃkṣepeṇa dvijottamāḥ ।।
yatrāste devadeveśaḥ svayameva pitāmahaḥ ।। tatraiṣā pitṛbhirgītā gāthā bhāgamabhīpsubhiḥ ।। yajeta vāśvamedhena nīlaṃ vā vṛṣamutsṛjet ।। yatrāvimuktasāṃnidhyaṃ bhuktimuktiphalapradam ।।
pitṛtīrthaṃ prayāgaṃ tu sarvakāmaphalapradam ।। yoganidrāśayastadvat sadā vasati keśavaḥ ।। nandātha lalitā tadvat tīrthaṃ māyāpurī śubhā ।। gaṅgāsāgaramityāhuḥ sarvatīrthamayaṃ śubham ।।
tīrthaṃ tu naimiṣaṃ nāma sarvatīrthaphalapradam ।। tathā yajñavarāhastu devadevaśca śūlabhṛt ।। nemistu haricakrasya śīrṇā yatrābhavatpurā ।। devadevasya tatrāpi vārāhasya tu darśanam ।।
kṛtaśaucaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ sarvapāpaniṣūdanam ।। tīrthamikṣumatī nāma pitṝṇāṃ vallabhaṃ sadā ।। kurukṣetraṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ sarvatīrthasamanvitam ।। irāvatī nadī tadvat pitṛtīrthādhivāsinī ।।
nadī veṇumatī puṇyā parā vetravatī tathā ।। jambūmārgaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ yatra mārgo hi lakṣyate ।। nīlakuṇḍamiti khyātaṃ pitṛtīrthaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। mandākinī tathācchodā vipāśātha sarasvatī ।।
kṣiprā nadī mahākālas tathā kālañjaraṃ śubham ।। bhadreśvaraṃ viṣṇupadaṃ narmadādvārameva ca ।। etāni pitṛtīrthāni sarvapāpaharāṇi ca ।। oṃkāraṃ pitṛtīrthaṃ ca kāverī kapilodakam ।।
kurukṣetrācchataguṇaṃ tasminsnānādikaṃ bhavet ।। sarvavyādhiharaṃ puṇyaṃ śatakoṭiphalādhikam ।। kāyāvarohaṇaṃ nāma tathā carmaṇvatī nadī ।। bhairavaṃ bhṛgutuṅgaṃ ca gaurītīrthamanuttamam ।।
tathā pāpaharaṃ nāma puṇyātha tapatī nadī ।। mahābodhiḥ pāṭalā ca nāgatīrthamavantikā ।। mahārudraṃ mahāliṅgaṃ daśārṇā ca nadī śubhā ।। aṅgāravāhikā tadvan nadau tau śoṇaghargharau ।।
etāni pitṛtīrthāni śasyante snānadānayoḥ ।। droṇī vāṭanadī dhārā saritkṣīranadī tathā ।। dvārakā kṛṣṇatīrthaṃ ca tathārbudasarasvatī ।। dhūtapāpaṃ tathā tīrthaṃ samudro dakṣiṇastathā ।।
tīrthaṃ meghakaraṃ nāma svayameva janārdanaḥ ।। tathā mandodarītīrthaṃ tīrthaṃ campā nadī śubhā ।। cakravākaṃ carmakoṭaṃ tathā janmeśvaraṃ mahat ।। śrīśailaṃ śāṃkaraṃ tīrthaṃ nārasiṃhamataḥ param ।।
eteṣvapi sadā śrāddham anantaphaladaṃ smṛtam ।। tuṅgabhadrā nadī puṇyā tathā bhīmarathī sarit ।। nadī godāvarī nāma trisaṃdhyā tīrthamuttamam ।। yatrāste bhagavānīśaḥ svayameva trilocanaḥ ।।
smaraṇādapi pāpāni naśyanti śatadhā dvijāḥ ।। tathā matsyanadī puṇyā śivadhāraṃ tathaiva ca ।। puṇyaṃ rāmeśvaraṃ tadvad elāpuramalaṃ puram ।। āmrātakeśvaraṃ tadvad ekāmbhakamataḥ param ।।
sahasrākṣaṃ hiraṇyākṣaṃ tathā ca kadalī nadī ।। indrakīlaṃ mahānādaṃ tathā ca priyamelakam ।। eteṣu sarvadevānāṃ sāṃnidhyaṃ dṛśyate yataḥ ।। bāhudā ca nadīpuṇyā tathā siddhavanaṃ śubham ।।
śrāddhameteṣu sarveṣu dattaṃ koṭiśatottaram ।। yutā liṅgasahasreṇa sarvāntarajalāvahā ।। pratīkasya bhayādbhinnaṃ yatra godāvarī nadī ।। śrāddhāgnikāryadāneṣu tathā koṭiśatādhikam ।।
sendraphenā nadī puṇyā yatrendraḥ patitaḥ purā ।। tatra dattaṃ naraiḥ śrāddham anantaphaladaṃ bhavet ।। somapānaṃ ca vikhyātaṃ yatra vaiśvānarālayam ।। malaṃdarā nadī puṇyā kauśikī candrikā tathā ।।
kāverī cottarā puṇyā tathā jālaṃdharo giriḥ ।। lohadaṇḍaṃ tathā tīrthaṃ citrakūṭastathaiva ca ।। kubjābhraṃ tu tathā tīrtham urvaśīpulinaṃ tathā ।। eteṣu pitṛtīrtheṣu śrāddham ānantyamaśnute ।।
tathā vasiṣṭhatīrthaṃ nu hārītaṃ tu tataḥ param ।। piṇḍārakaṃ ca vikhyātaṃ śaṅkhoddhāraṃ tathaiva ca ।। tathā ca dharaṇītīrthaṃ rāmatīrthaṃ tathaiva ca ।। tīrthaṃ vedaśiro nāma tathaivaughavatī nadī ।।
eteṣu śrāddhadātāraḥ prayānti paramaṃ padam ।। jayantaṃ vijayaṃ caiva śakratīrthaṃ tathaiva ca ।। tathaiva śāradātīrthaṃ bhadrakāleśvaraṃ tathā ।। eteṣu śrāddhadātāraḥ prayānti paramāṃ gatim ।।
kuśeśayaṃ ca vikhyātaṃ gaurīśikharameva ca ।। diṇḍipuṇyakaraṃ tadvat puṇḍarīkapuraṃ tathā ।। tatra śrāddhaṃ pradātavyam anantaphalamīpsubhiḥ ।। vāgīśo api na śaknoti vistarāt kim u mānuṣaḥ ।।
varṇāśramāṇāṃ gehe api tīrthaṃ tu samudāhṛtam ।। yasmāttasmātprayatnena tīrthe śrāddhaṃ samācaret ।। madhyāhnastrimuhūrtaḥ syād aparāhṇastataḥ param ।। rākṣasī nāma sā velā garhitā sarvakarmasu ।।
tatrāṣṭamo muhūrto yaḥ sa kālaḥ kutapaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। tasmādanantaphaladas tadārambho viśiṣyate ।। rūpyaṃ darbhāstilā gāvo dauhitraścāṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। aṣṭāv ete yatastasmāt kutapā iti viśrutāḥ ।।
muhūrtapañcakaṃ caitat svadhābhavanamiṣyate ।। śrāddhasya rakṣaṇāyālam etatprāhurdivaukasaḥ ।। sadarbhahastenaikena śrāddhamevaṃ viśiṣyate ।। tarpaṇaṃ tūbhayenaiva vidhireṣa sadā smṛtaḥ ।।
purā malaye na kathitaṃ tīrthaśrāddhānukīrtanam ।। śṛṇoti yaḥ paṭhedvāpi śrīmānsaṃjāyate naraḥ ।। sarvapāpopaśāntyartham alakṣmīnāśanaṃ param ।। brahmārkarudrairapi pūjitaṃ ca śrāddhasya māhātmyamuśanti tajjñāḥ ।।
tadvaṃśyā ye ca rājāno babhūvuḥ kīrtivardhanāḥ ।। anuttamaṃ nāma tapaḥ sṛṣṭyarthaṃ taptavānprabhuḥ ।। brahmaviṣṇvarkarudrāṇām abhyantaramatīndriyam ।। māhātmyāttapasā viprāḥ paramānandakārakam ।।
taṃ dṛṣṭvā cāṣṭamāṃśena tasmātsomo abhavacchiśuḥ ।। dīpayanviśvamakhilaṃ jyotsnayā sacarācaram ।। garbho bhūtvodare tāsām āsthito abdaśatatrayam ।। samādāyātha taṃ garbham ekīkṛtya caturmukhaḥ ।।
syandane atha sahasrāśve vedaśaktimaye prabhuḥ ।। tatra brahmarṣibhiḥ proktam asmatsvāmī bhavatvayam ।। tuṣṭuvuḥ somadevatyair brahmādyā mantrasaṃgrahaiḥ ।। tejovitānādabhavad bhuvi divyauṣadhīgaṇaḥ ।।
tenauṣadhīśaḥ somo abhūd dvijeśaścāpi gadyate ।। kṣīyate vardhate caiva śukle kṛṣṇe ca sarvadā ।। rūpalāvaṇyasaṃyuktās tasmai kanyāḥ suvarcasaḥ ।। tapaścacāra śītāṃśur viṣṇudhyānaikatatparaḥ ।।
varaṃ vṛṇīṣva provāca paramātmā janārdanaḥ ।। pratyakṣameva bhoktāro bhavantu mama mandire ।। rakṣaḥpālaḥ śivo asmākam āstāṃ śūladharo haraḥ ।। hotātrir bhṛguradhvaryur udgātābhūccaturmukhaḥ ।।
sadasyāḥ sanakādyāstu rājasūyavidhau smṛtāḥ ।। trailokyaṃ dakṣiṇā tena ṛtvigbhyaḥ pratipāditam ।। kāmabāṇābhitaptāṅgyo nava devyaḥ siṣevire ।। dyutirvibhāvasuṃ tadvat tuṣṭirdhātāramavyayam ।।
kīrtirjayantaṃ bhartāraṃ vasurmārīcakaśyapam ।। svakīyā iva somo api kāmayāmāsa tāstadā ।। na śaśākāpacārāya śāpaiḥ śastrādibhiḥ punaḥ ।। saptalokaikanāthatvam avāpa tapasā tadā ।।
bṛhannitambastanabhārakhedāt puṣpasya bhaṅge apyatidurbalāṅgīm ।। tārāṃ sa tārādhipatiḥ smarārtaḥ keśeṣu jagrāha viviktabhūmau ।। ciraṃ vihṛtyātha jagāma tārāṃ vidhurgṛhītvā svagṛhaṃ tato api ।। bṛhaspatis tadvirahāgnidagdhas taddhyānaniṣṭhaikamanā babhūva ।।
tasyāpakartuṃ vividhairupāyair naivābhicārairapi vāgadhīśaḥ ।। sa yācyamāno api dadau na tārāṃ bṛhaspatestatsukhapāśabaddhaḥ ।। dadau yadā tāṃ na kathaṃcid indus tadā śivaḥ krodhaparo babhūva ।। tataḥ saśiṣyo giriśaḥ pinākī bṛhaspatisnehavaśānubaddhaḥ ।।
yuddhāya somena viśeṣadīptatṛtīyanetrānalabhīmavaktraḥ ।। yakṣeśvaraḥ koṭiśatair anekair yuto anvagāt syandanasaṃsthitānām ।। lakṣais tribhir dvādaśabhī rathānāṃ somo apyagāttatra vivṛddhamanyuḥ ।। jagmurbhayaṃ sapta tathaiva lokāś cacāla bhūr dvīpasamudragarbhā ।।
athābhavad bhīṣaṇabhīmasenasainyadvayasyāpi mahāhavo asau ।। śastrairathānyonyamaśeṣasainyaṃ dvayorjagāma kṣayamugratīkṣṇaiḥ ।। rudraḥ kopādbrahmaśīrṣaṃ mumoca somo api somāstramamoghavīryam ।। tadastrayugmaṃ jagatāṃ kṣayāya pravṛddhamālokya pitāmaho api ।।
akāraṇaṃ kiṃ kṣayakṛjjanānāṃ soma tvayāpīttham akāri kāryam ।। bhāryāmimāmarpaya vākpatestvaṃ na cāvamāno asti parasvahāre ।। bṛhaspatiḥ svāmapagṛhya tārāṃ hṛṣṭo jagāma svagṛhaṃ sarudraḥ ।। divyapītāmbaradharo divyābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।।
sarvārthaśāstraviddhīmān hastiśāstrapravartakaḥ ।। rājñaḥ somasya putratvād rājaputro budhaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। brahmādyāstatra cājagmur devā devarṣibhiḥ saha ।। apṛcchaṃste surāstārāṃ kena jātaḥ kumārakaḥ ।।
punaḥ punastadā pṛṣṭā lajjayantī varāṅganā ।। budha ityakaronnāmnā prādādrājyaṃ ca bhūtale ।। gṛhasāmyaṃ pradāyātha brahmā brahmarṣisaṃyutaḥ ।। ilodare ca dharmiṣṭhaṃ budhaḥ putramajījanat ।।
purūravā iti khyātaḥ sarvalokanamaskṛtaḥ ।। lokaiśvaryamagādrājā saptadvīpapatistadā ।। urvaśī yasya patnītvam agamadrūpamohitā ।। dharmeṇa pālitā tena sarvalokahitaiṣiṇā ।।
viṣṇoḥ prasādāddevendro dadāv ardhāsanaṃ tadā ।। dharmārthakāmāḥ saṃdraṣṭum ājagmuḥ kautukātpurā ।। bhaktyā cakre tatasteṣām arghyapādyādikaṃ nṛpaḥ ।। niviśyāthākarotpūjām īṣaddharme adhikāṃ punaḥ ।।
arthaḥ śāpamadāttasmai lobhāttvaṃ nāśameṣyasi ।। kumāravanamāśritya viyogādurvaśībhavāt ।। saṃtatistava rājendra yāvaccandrārkatārakam ।। ityuktvāntardadhuḥ sarve rājā rājyaṃ tadanvabhūt ।।
kadācidāruhya rathaṃ dakṣiṇāmbaracāriṇam ।। keśinā dānavendreṇa citralekhāmathorvaśīm ।। budhaputreṇa vāyavyam astraṃ muktvā yaśo arthinā ।। mitratvam agamad devair dadāv indrāya corvaśīm ।।
sarvalokātiśāyitvaṃ balamūrjo yaśaḥ śriyam ।। sā purūravasaḥ prītyā gāyantī caritaṃ mahat ।। menakāmurvaśīṃ rambhāṃ nṛtyateti tadādiśat ।। sā purūravasaṃ dṛṣṭvā nṛtyantī kāmapīḍitā ।।
śaśāpa bharataḥ krodhād viyogādasya bhūtale ।। purūravāḥ piśācatvaṃ tatraivānubhaviṣyati ।। śāpānte bharatasyātha urvaśī budhasūnutaḥ ।। āyur dṛḍhāyur aśvāyur dhanāyur dhṛtimānvasuḥ ।।
āyuṣo nahuṣaḥ putrau vṛddhaśarmā tathaiva ca ।। rajeḥ putraśataṃ jajñe rājeyamiti viśrutam ।। tapasā toṣito viṣṇur varānprādānmahīpate ।। atha devāsuraṃ yuddham abhūd varṣaśatatrayam ।।
tato devāsuraiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ prāha devaścaturmukhaḥ ।। jayāya prārthito rājā sahāyastvaṃ bhavasva naḥ ।। nāsuraiḥ pratipannaṃ tat pratipannaṃ suraistathā ।। tato vināśitāḥ sarve ye avadhyā vajrapāṇinā ।।
dattvendrāya tadā rājyaṃ jagāma tapase rajiḥ ।। yajñabhāgaṃ ca rājyaṃ ca tapobalaguṇānvitaiḥ ।। prāha vācaspatiṃ dīnaḥ pīḍito asmi rajeḥ sutaiḥ ।। rājyalābhāya me yatnaṃ vidhatsva dhiṣaṇādhipa ।।
grahaśāntividhānena pauṣṭikena ca karmaṇā ।। jinadharmaṃ samāsthāya vedabāhyaṃ sa vedavit ।। vedabāhyānparijñāya hetuvādasamanvitān ।। nahuṣasya pravakṣyāmi putrānsaptaiva dhārmikān ।।
śaryātirmeghajātiśca saptaite vaṃśavardhanāḥ ।। yayātiścākarodrājyaṃ dharmaikaśaraṇaḥ sadā ।। bhārgavasyātmajā tadvad devayānī ca suvratā ।। devayānī yaduṃ putraṃ turvasuṃ cāpyajījanat ।।
yaduḥ pūruścābhavatāṃ teṣāṃ vaṃśavivardhanau ।। pālayāmāsa sa mahīm īje ca vidhivanmakhaiḥ ।। athājayatprajāḥ sarvā yayātiraparājitaḥ ।। jarām ārchan mahāghorāṃ nāhuṣo rūpanāśinīm ।।
yaduṃ pūruṃ turvasuṃ ca druhyuṃ cānuṃ ca pārthivaḥ ।। vihartum ahamicchāmi sāhāyyaṃ kurutātmajāḥ ।। sāhāyyaṃ bhavataḥ kāryam asmābhiryauvanena kim ।। yauvanenātha bhavatāṃ careyaṃ viṣayānaham ।।
kāmārthaḥ parihīno me atṛpto ahaṃ tena putrakāḥ ।। ahaṃ tanvābhinavayā yuvā kāmānavāpnuyām ।। caturastānsa rājarṣir aśapacceti naḥ śrutam ।। jarāṃ mā dehi navayā tanvā me yauvanātsukhī ।।
evamuktaḥ sa rājarṣis tapovīryasamāśrayāt ।। pauraveṇātha vayasā rājā yauvanamāsthitaḥ ।। tato varṣasahasrānte yayātiraparājitaḥ ।। tvayā dāyādavān asmi tvaṃ me vaṃśakaraḥ sutaḥ ।।
tataḥ sa nṛpaśārdūlaḥ pūruṃ rājye abhiṣicya ca ।। yatra te bhāratā jātā bharatānvayavardhanāḥ ।। jyeṣṭhasyāpi yadorvaṃśaḥ kimarthaṃ hīyate śriyā ।। yasmāttatpuṇyamāyuṣyam abhinandyaṃ surairapi ।।
puṇyaṃ pavitramāyuṣyaṃ yayāticaritaṃ mahat ।। kathaṃ sa śukratanayāṃ lebhe paramadurlabhām ।। ānupūrvyācca me śaṃsa pūrorvaṃśadharānnṛpān ।। taṃ śukravṛṣaparvāṇau vavrāte vai yathā purā ।।
devayānyāśca saṃyogaṃ yayāternāhuṣasya ca ।। aiśvaryaṃ prati saṃgharṣas trailokye sacarācare ।। paurohitye ca yajñārthe kāvyaṃ tūśanasaṃ pare ।। tatra devā nijaghnuryān dānavān yudhi saṃgatān ।।
tataste punarutthāya yodhayāṃcakrire surān ।। na tānsaṃjīvayāmāsa bṛhaspatirudāradhīḥ ।। saṃjīvanīṃ tato devā viṣādamagamanparam ।। ūcuḥ kacamupāgamya jyeṣṭhaṃ putraṃ bṛhaspateḥ ।।
yāsau vidyā nivasati brāhmaṇe amitatejasi ।। vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ samīpe asau śakyo draṣṭuṃ tvayā dvijaḥ ।। tam ārādhayituṃ śakto nānyaḥ kaścidṛte tvayā ।। tām ārādhayituṃ śakto nānyaḥ kaścana vidyate ।।
devayānyāṃ tu tuṣṭāyāṃ vidyāṃ tāṃ prāpsyasi dhruvam ।। tathetyuktvā tu sa prāyād bṛhaspatisutaḥ kacaḥ ।। asurendrapure śukraṃ praṇamyedamuvāca ha ।। nāmnā kaceti vikhyātaṃ śiṣyaṃ gṛhṇātu māṃ bhavān ।।
anumanyasva māṃ brahman sahasraparivatsarān ।। arcayiṣye ahamarcyaṃ tvām arcito astu bṛhaspatiḥ ।। ādiṣṭaṃ kaviputreṇa śukreṇośanasā svayam ।। ārādhayannupādhyāyaṃ devayānīṃ ca bhārata ।।
gāyannṛtyanvādayaṃśca devayānīmatoṣayat ।। puṣpaiḥ phalaiḥ preṣaṇaiśca toṣayāmāsa bhārgavīm ।। anugāyantī lalanā rahaḥ paryacarattadā ।। tattattīvraṃ vrataṃ buddhvā dānavāstaṃ tataḥ kacam ।।
jaghnur bṛhaspater dveṣān nijarakṣārtham eva ca ।। tato gāvo nivṛttāstā agopāḥ svaniveśanam ।। uvāca vacanaṃ kāle devayānyatha bhārgavam ।। agopāścāgatā gāvaḥ kacastāta na dṛśyate ।।
taṃ vinā naiva jīvāmi vacaḥ satyaṃ bravīmyaham ।। tataḥ saṃjīvanīṃ vidyāṃ prayuktvā kacamāhvayat ।। hato ahamiti cācakhyau rākṣasair dhiṣaṇātmajaḥ ।। vanaṃ yayau kaco vipraḥ paṭhanbrahma ca śāśvatam ।।
prāyacchan brāhmaṇāyaiva surāyāmasurāstadā ।। puṣpāhārapreṣaṇakṛt kacastāta na dṛśyate ।। taṃ vinā naiva jīvāmi vacaḥ satyaṃ bravīmi te ।। vidyayā jīvito apyevaṃ hanyate karavāṇi kim ।।
yasyāstava brahma ca brāhmaṇāśca sendrāśca devā vasavo aśvinau ca ।। aśakyo ayaṃ jīvayituṃ dvijātiḥ saṃjīvito yo vadhyate caiva bhūyaḥ ।। ṛṣeḥ suputraṃ tamathāpi pautraṃ kathaṃ na śoce yamahaṃ na rudyām ।। kacasya mārgaṃ pratipatsye na bhokṣye priyo hi me tāta kaco abhirūpaḥ ।।
asaṃśayaṃ māmasurā dviṣanti ye me śiṣyānāgatānsūdayanti ।। tatkarmaṇāpyasya bhavedihāntaḥ kaṃ brahmahatyā na dahedapīndram ।। tamabravītkena cehopanīto mamodare tiṣṭhasi brūhi vatsa ।। na tv evaṃ syāttapasaḥ kṣayo me tata kleśaṃ ghorataraṃ smarāmi ।।
brāhmīṃ māyāṃ tv āsurī tv atra māyā tvayi sthite katham evābhibādhate ।। nānyatra kukṣermama bhedanācca dṛśyet kaco madgato devayāni ।। kacasya nāśe mama nāsti śarma tavopaghāte jīvituṃ nāsmi śaktā ।। vidyāmimāṃ prāpnuhi jīvanīṃ tvaṃ na cedindraḥ kacarūpī tvamadya ।।
brāhmaṇaṃ varjayitvaikaṃ tasmādvidyām avāpnuhi ।। avekṣethā dharmavatīmavekṣāṃ guroḥ sakāśātprāpya vidyāṃ savidyaḥ ।। prāleyādreḥ śuklamudbhidya śṛṅgaṃ rātryāgame paurṇamāsyāmivenduḥ ।। vidyāṃ siddhāṃ tāmavāpyābhivādya tataḥ kacastaṃ gurumityuvāca ।।
prāleyādriprojjvaladbhālasaṃsthaṃ pāpāṃllokāṃste vrajantyapratiṣṭhāḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā kacaṃ cāpi tathābhirūpaṃ pītaṃ tathā surayā mohitena ।। kāvyaḥ svayaṃ vākyamidaṃ jagāda surāpānaṃ pratyasau jātaśaṅkaḥ ।। apetadharmā brahmahā caiva sa syādasmiṃlloke garhitaḥ syātpare ca ।।
santo viprāḥ śuśruvāṃso gurūṇāṃ devā daityāścopaśṛṇvantu sarve ।। tāndānavāṃścaiva nigūḍhabuddhīn idaṃ samāhūya vaco abhyuvāca ।। saṃjīvanīṃ prāpya vidyāṃ mayāyaṃ tulyaprabhāvo brāhmaṇo brahmabhūtaḥ ।। anujñātaḥ kaco gantum iyeṣa tridaśālayam ।।
prasthitaṃ tridaśāvāsaṃ devayānīdamabravīt ।। bhrājase vidyayā caiva tapasā ca damena ca ।। tathā mānyaśca pūjyaśca mama bhūyo bṛhaspatiḥ ।। vratasthe niyamopete yathā vartāmyahaṃ tvayi ।।
gṛhāṇa pāṇiṃ vidhivan mama mantrapuraskṛtam ।। tathā tvamanavadyāṅgi pūjanīyatamā matā ।। tvaṃ bhadre dharmataḥ pūjyā guruputrī sadā mama ।। devayāni tathaiva tvaṃ naivaṃ māṃ vaktumarhasi ।।
tasmānmānyaśca pūjyaśca mamāpi tvaṃ dvijottama ।। tadāprabhṛti yā prītis tāṃ tvameva smarasva me ।। na māmarhasi dharmajña tyaktuṃ bhaktāmanāgasam ।। prasīda subhrūrmahyaṃ tvaṃ guror gurutarā śubhe ।।
tatrāhamuṣito bhadre kukṣau kāvyasya bhāmini ।। sukhenādhyuṣito bhadre na manyurvidyate mama ।। apramattodyatā nityam ārādhaya guruṃ mama ।। yadi māṃ dharmakāmārthaṃ pratyākhyāsyasi dharmataḥ ।।
tataḥ kaca na te vidyā siddhimeṣā gamiṣyati ।। guruṇā cābhyanujñātaḥ kāmameva śapasva mām ।। śaptuṃ nārho asmi kalyāṇi kāmato adya ca dharmataḥ ।। ṛṣiputro na te kaścij jātu pāṇiṃ grahīṣyati ।।
adhyāpayiṣyāmi ca yaṃ tasya vidyā phaliṣyati ।। tridaśeśālayaṃ śīghraṃ jagāma dvijasattamaḥ ।। bṛhaspatiṃ sabhājyedaṃ kacamāhurmudānvitāḥ ।। na te yaśaḥ praṇaśitā bhāgabhākca bhaviṣyasi ।।
kacādavetya tāṃ vidyāṃ kṛtārthā bharatarṣabha ।। kālastvadvikramasyādya jahi śatrūnpuraṃdara ।। tathetyuktvopacakrāma so apaśyadvipine striyaḥ ।। vāyurbhūtaḥ sa vastrāṇi sarvāṇyeva vyamiśrayat ।।
vastrāṇi jagṛhustāni yathāsaṃsthānyanekaśaḥ ।। vyatikramamajānantī duhitā vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ ।। devayānyāśca rājendra śarmiṣṭhāyāśca tatkṛte ।। samudācārahīnāyā na te śreyo bhaviṣyati ।।
stauti pṛcchati cābhīkṣṇaṃ nīcasthaḥ suvinītavat ।। sutāhaṃ stūyamānasya dadato na tu gṛhṇataḥ ।। lapsyase pratiyoddhāraṃ na ca tvāṃ gaṇayāmyaham ।। śarmiṣṭhā prākṣipatkūpe tataḥ svapuramāviśat ।।
anavekṣya yayau tasmāt krodhavegaparāyaṇā ।। śrāntayugyaḥ śrāntarūpo mṛgalipsuḥ pipāsitaḥ ।। dadarśa kanyāṃ tāṃ tatra dīptāmagniśikhām iva ।। sāntvayitvā nṛpaśreṣṭhaḥ sāmnā paramavalgunā ।।
dīrghaṃ dhyāyasi cātyarthaṃ kasmācchvasiṣi cāturā ।। duhitā caiva kasya tvaṃ vada sarvaṃ sumadhyame ।। tasya śukrasya kanyāhaṃ tvaṃ māṃ nūnaṃ na budhyase ।। samuddhara gṛhītvā māṃ kulīnastvaṃ hi me mataḥ ।।
tasmānmāṃ patitāṃ kūpād asmād uddhartumarhasi ।। gṛhītvā dakṣiṇe pāṇāv ujjahāra tato avaṭāt ।। āmantrayitvā suśroṇīṃ yayātiḥ svapuraṃ yayau ।। uvāca śokasaṃtaptā ghūrṇikāmāgatāṃ punaḥ ।।
nedānīṃ tu pravekṣyāmi nagaraṃ vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā kāvyamuvācedaṃ kampamānā vicetanā ।। śarmiṣṭhayā mahāprājña duhitrā vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ ।। tvarayā niryayau duḥkhān mārgamāṇaḥ sutāṃ vane ।।
bāhubhyāṃ sampariṣvajya duḥkhito vākyamabravīt ।। manye duścaritaṃ te asti tasyeyaṃ niṣkṛtiḥ kṛtā ।। śarmiṣṭhayā yaduktāsmi duhitrā vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ ।। evaṃ hi me kathayati śarmiṣṭhā vārṣaparvaṇī ।।
stuvato duhitāsi tvaṃ yācataḥ pratigṛhṇataḥ ।। krodhasaṃraktanayanā darpapūrṇānanā tataḥ ।। prasādayiṣye śarmiṣṭhām ityuktā hi sakhī mayā ।। atastvaṃ stūyamānasya duhitā devayānyasi ।।
acintyaṃ brahma nirdvaṃdvam aiśvaraṃ hi balaṃ mama ।। devayāni vijānīhi tena sarvamidaṃ jitam ।। sa yantetyucyate sadbhir na yo raśmiṣu lambate ।। devayāni vijānīhi tena sarvamidaṃ jitam ।।
yathoragastvacaṃ jīrṇāṃ sa vai puruṣa ucyate ।। yaśca tapto na tapati bhṛśaṃ so arthasya bhājanam ।। yastu kupyenna sarvasya tayorakrodhano varaḥ ।। naitatprājñastu kurvīta viduste na balābalam ।।
krodhe caivātivāde vā kāryasyāpi balābale ।। asatsaṃkīrṇavṛtteṣu vāso mama na rocate ।। na teṣu nivasetprājñaḥ śreyorthī pāpabuddhiṣu ।। teṣu sādhuṣu vastavyaṃ sa vāsaḥ śreṣṭha ucyate ।।
vāgduruktaṃ mahāghoraṃ duhiturvṛṣaparvaṇaḥ ।। yaḥ sapatnaśriyaṃ dīptāṃ hīnaśrīḥ paryupāsate ।। vṛṣaparvāṇam āsīnam ityuvācāvicārayan ।। śanairāvartyamānastu mūlānyapi nikṛntati ।।
pāpamācaritaṃ karma trivargamativartate ।। yadā ghātayase vipraṃ kacamāṅgirasaṃ tadā ।। vadhādanarhatastasya vadhācca duhiturmama ।। sthātuṃ tvadviṣaye rājan na śaknomi tvayā saha ।।
yatastvamātmanodīrṇāṃ duhitāṃ kimupekṣase ।। tvayi satyaṃ ca dharmaśca tatprasīdatu māṃ bhavān ।। samudraṃ sampravekṣyāmi nānyadasti parāyaṇam ।। duhiturnāpriyaṃ soḍhuṃ śakto ahaṃ dayitā hi me ।।
yogakṣemakaraste aham indrasyeva bṛhaspatiḥ ।। bhuvi hastirathāśvaṃ vā tasya tvaṃ mama ceśvaraḥ ।। tasyeśvaro asmi yadyetad devayānī prasādyatām ।। uvāca caināṃ subhage pratipannaṃ vacastava ।।
nābhijānāmi tatte ahaṃ rājā vadatu māṃ svayam ।। tatte ahaṃ sampradāsyāmi yadyapi syātsudurlabham ।। anuyāsyati māṃ tatra yatra dāsyati me pitā ।। yaṃ ca kāmayate kāmaṃ devayānī karotu tam ।।
uttiṣṭha bhadre śarmiṣṭhe jñātīnāṃ sukhamāvaha ।। dāsītvam abhijātāsi devayānyāḥ suśobhane ।। mā gānmanyuvaśaṃ śukro devayānī ca matkṛte ।। piturnideśāttvaritā niścakrāma purottamāt ।।
dhruvaṃ tvāṃ tatra yāsyāmi yatra dāsyati te pitā ।। stūyamānasya duhitā kathaṃ dāsī bhaviṣyasi ।। anuyāsyāmyahaṃ tatra yatra dāsyati te pitā ।। devayānī nṛpaśreṣṭha pitaraṃ vākyamabravīt ।।
amoghaṃ tava vijñānam asti vidyābalaṃ ca te ।। praviveśa puraṃ hṛṣṭaḥ pūjitaḥ sarvadānavaiḥ ।। vanaṃ tadaiva niryātā krīḍārthaṃ varavarṇinī ।। tameva deśaṃ samprāptā yathākāmaṃ cacāra sā ।।
krīḍantyo abhiratāḥ sarvāḥ pibantyo madhu mādhavam ।। punaśca nāhuṣo rājā mṛgalipsuryadṛcchayā ।। dadarśa devayānīṃ ca śarmiṣṭhāṃ tāśca yoṣitaḥ ।। upaviṣṭāṃ ca dadṛśe devayānīṃ śucismitām ।।
śarmiṣṭhayā sevyamānāṃ pādasaṃvāhanādibhiḥ ।। gotre ca nāmanī caiva dvayoḥ pṛcchāmyato hy aham ।। śuko nāmāsuraguruḥ sutāṃ jānīhi tasya mām ।। duhitā dānavendrasya śarmiṣṭhā vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ ।।
asurendrasutā subhūḥ paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me ।। vidhinā vihitaṃ jñātvā mā vicitraṃ manaḥ kṛthāḥ ।। kiṃnāmā tvaṃ kutaścāsi kasya putraśca śaṃsa me ।। rājāhaṃ rājaputraśca yayātiriti viśrutaḥ ।।
jighṛkṣurvāri yatkiṃcid athavā mṛgalipsayā ।। bahudhāpyanuyukto asmi tvam anujñātumarhasi ।। tvadadhīnāsmi bhadraṃ te sakhe bhartā ca me bhava ।। avivāhyāḥ sma rājāno devayāni pitustava ।।
ṛṣiśca ṛṣiputraśca nāhuṣādya bhajasva mām ।। pṛthagdharmāḥ pṛthakchaucās teṣāṃ vai brāhmaṇo varaḥ ।। tvaṃ pāṇimagrahīdagre vṛṇomi tvāmahaṃ tataḥ ।। gṛhītamṛṣiputreṇa svayaṃ vāpyṛṣiṇā tvayā ।।
durādharṣataro vipraḥ puruṣeṇa vijānatā ।। durādharṣataro vipra ityāttha puruṣarṣabha ।। hanti vipraḥ sarāṣṭrāṇi purāṇyapi hi kopitaḥ ।। ato adattāṃ ca pitrā tvāṃ bhadre na vivahāmyaham ।।
ayācato bhayaṃ nāsti dattāṃ ca pratigṛhṇataḥ ।। sarvaṃ nivedayāmāsa dhātrī tasmai yathātatham ।। dṛṣṭvaivam āgataṃ vipraṃ yayātiḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ ।। taṃ cāpyabhyavadatkāvyaḥ sāmnā paramavalgunā ।।
namaste dehi māmasmai loke nānyaṃ patiṃ vṛṇe ।। gṛhāṇemāṃ mayā dattāṃ mahiṣīṃ nahuṣātmaja ।। varṇasaṃkarato brahmann iti tvāṃ pravṛṇomyaham ।। asminvivāhe tvaṃ ślāghyo rahaḥ pāpaṃ nudāmi te ।।
anayā saha samprītim atulāṃ samavāpnuhi ।। saṃpūjyā satataṃ rājan na caināṃ śayane hvaya ।। jagāma svapuraṃ hṛṣṭaḥ so anujñāto mahātmanā ।। praviśyāntaḥpuraṃ tatra devayānīṃ nyaveśayat ।।
aśokavanikābhyāśe gṛhaṃ kṛtvā nyaveśayat ।। vāsobhirannapānaiśca saṃvibhajya susaṃvṛtām ।। vijahāra bahūnabdān devavanmudito bhṛśam ।। lebhe garbhaṃ prathamataḥ kumāraśca vyajāyata ।।
dadarśa yauvanaṃ prāptā ṛtuṃ sā kamalekṣaṇā ।। ṛtukālaśca samprāpto na kaścinme patirvṛtaḥ ।। devayānī prasūtāsau vṛthāhaṃ prāptayauvanā ।। apīdānīṃ sa dharmātmā raho me darśanaṃ vrajet ।।
aśokavanikābhyāśe śarmiṣṭhāṃ prāpya vismitaḥ ।। pratyudgamyāñjaliṃ kṛtvā rājānaṃ vākyamabravīt ।। tava vā nāhuṣa gṛhe kaḥ striyaṃ draṣṭumarhati ।। sā tvāṃ yāce prasādyeha rantumehi narādhipa ।।
rūpaṃ tu te na paśyāmi sūcyagramapi ninditam ।। neyam āhvayitavyā te śayane vārṣaparvaṇī ।। prāṇātyaye sarvadhanāpahāre pañcānṛtānyāhur apātakāni ।। ekārthatāyāṃ tu samāhitāyāṃ mithyā vadantaṃ hy anṛtaṃ hinasti ।।
arthakṛcchramapi prāpya na mithyā kartumutsahe ।। samaṃ vivāha ityāhuḥ sakhyā me asi patiryataḥ ।। tvaṃ ca yācasi kāmaṃ māṃ brūhi kiṃ karavāṇi tat ।। tvatto apatyavatī loke careyaṃ dharmamuttamam ।।
yatte samadhigacchanti yasya te tasya taddhanam ।। sā cāhaṃ ca tvayā rājan bharaṇīyāṃ bhajasva mām ।। pūjayāmāsa śarmiṣṭhāṃ dharmaṃ ca pratipādayan ।। anyonyaṃ cābhisaṃpūjya jagmatustau yathāgatam ।।
lebhe garbhaṃ prathamatas tasmānnṛpatisattamāt ।। kumāraṃ devagarbhābham ādityasamatejasam ।। cintayāviṣṭaduḥkhārtā śarmiṣṭhāṃ prati bhārata ।। kimarthaṃ vṛjinaṃ subhrūḥ kṛtaṃ te kāmalubdhayā ।।
sa mayā tu varaḥ kāmaṃ yācito dharmasaṃhatam ।। tasmād ṛṣer mamāpatyam iti satyaṃ bravīmi te ।। apatyaṃ yadi te labdhaṃ jyeṣṭhācchreṣṭhācca vai dvijāt ।। gotranāmābhijanataḥ śrotumicchāmi taṃ dvijam ।।
taṃ dṛṣṭvā mama saṃpraṣṭuṃ śaktir nāsīcchucismite ।। jagāma bhārgavī veśma tathyamityabhijānatī ।। yaduṃ ca turvasuṃ caiva śakraviṣṇū ivāparau ।। druhyaṃ cānuṃ ca pūruṃ ca trīnkumārānajījanat ।।
yayātisahitā rājañ jagāma haritaṃ vanam ।। krīḍamānān tu visrabdhān vismitā cedamabravīt ।। varcasā rūpataścaiva dṛśyante sadṛśāstava ।। kiṃ nāmadheyagotre vaḥ putrakā brāhmaṇaḥ pitā ।।
te adarśayanpradeśinyā tameva nṛpasattamam ।। ityuktvā sahitāstena rājānam upacakramuḥ ।। rudantaste atha śarmiṣṭhām abhyayur bālakāstadā ।। buddhvā ca tattvato devī śarmiṣṭhāmidamabravīt ।।
tamevāsuradharmaṃ tvam āsthitā na bibheṣi kim ।। nyāyato dharmataścaiva carantī na bibhemi te ।। sakhībhartā hi dharmeṇa bhartā bhavati śobhane ।। tvatto hi me pūjyataro rājarṣiḥ kiṃ na vetsi tat ।।
rājannādyeha vatsyāmi vipriyaṃ me tvayā kṛtam ।। tūrṇaṃ sakāśaṃ kāvyasya prasthitāṃ vyathitastadā ।। nyavartata na sā caiva krodhasaṃraktalocanā ।। acirādeva samprāptā kāvyasyośanaso antikam ।।
anantaraṃ yayātistu pūjayāmāsa bhārgavam ।। śarmiṣṭhā yātivṛttāsti duhitā vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ ।। durbhagāyā mama dvau tu putrau tāta bravīmi te ।। atikrāntaśca maryādāṃ kāvyaitatkathayāmi te ।।
tasmājjarā tvām acirād dharṣayiṣyati durjayā ।। bhrūṇahetyucyate brahman sa ceha brahmavādibhiḥ ।। nopaiti yo hi dharmeṇa brahmahetyucyate budhaiḥ ।। adharmabhayasaṃvignaḥ śarmiṣṭhām upajagmivān ।।
mithyācaraṇadharmeṣu cauryaṃ bhavati nāhuṣa ।। pūrvaṃ vayaḥ parityajya jarāṃ sadyo anvapadyata ।। prasādaṃ kuru me brahmañ jareyaṃ mā viśeta mām ।। jarāṃ tv etāṃ tvamanyasmin saṃkrāmaya yadīcchasi ।।
yo dadyānme vayaḥ putras tadbhavānanumanyatām ।। māmanudhyāya tattvena na ca pāpamavāpsyasi ।। āyuṣmānkīrtimāṃścaiva bahvapatyas tathaiva ca ।। putraṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ variṣṭhaṃ ca yadumityabravīddvijaḥ ।।
kāvyasyośanasaḥ śāpān na ca tṛpto asmi yauvane ।। yauvanena tvadīyena careyaṃ viṣayānaham ।। dattvā sampratipatsyāmi pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha ।। valīsaṃtatagātraśca durdarśo durbalaḥ kṛśaḥ ।।
sahopajīvibhiścaiva tajjarāṃ nābhikāmaye ।। jarāṃ grahītuṃ dharmajña putramanyaṃ vṛṇīṣva vai ।। pāpānmātulasambandhād duṣprajā te bhaviṣyati ।। yauvanena careyaṃ vai viṣayāṃstava putraka ।।
tathaiva pratipatsyāmi pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha ।। balarūpāntakaraṇīṃ buddhimānavināśinīm ।। tasmātprajā samucchedaṃ turvaso tava yāsyati ।। piśitāśiṣu lokeṣu nūnaṃ rājā bhaviṣyasi ।।
paśudharmiṣu mleccheṣu pāpeṣu prabhaviṣyasi ।। śarmiṣṭhāyāḥ sutaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ druhyuṃ vacanamabravīt ।। jarāṃ varṣasahasraṃ me yauvanaṃ svaṃ prayacchatām ।। svaṃ cādāsyāmi bhūyo ahaṃ pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha ।।
na rāgaścāsya bhavati tajjarāṃ te na kāmaye ।। taddruhyo vai priyaḥ kāmo na te sampatsyate kvacit ।। arājyabhojaśabdaṃ tvaṃ tatra prāpsyasi sānvayaḥ ।। ekaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu careyaṃ yauvanena te ।।
na juhoti ca kāle agniṃ tāṃ jarāṃ nābhikāmaye ।। jarādoṣastvayokto yas tasmāttvaṃ pratipadyase ।। agnipraskandanagatas tvaṃ cāpyevaṃ bhaviṣyasi ।। tvaṃ me priyataraḥ putras tvaṃ varīyān bhaviṣyasi ।।
kāvyasyośanasaḥ śāpān na ca tṛpto asmi yauvane ।। svaṃ caiva pratipatsye ahaṃ pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha ।। yathāttha tvaṃ mahārāja tatkariṣyāmi te vacaḥ ।। gṛhāṇa yauvanaṃ mattaś cara kāmān yathepsitān ।।
yauvanaṃ bhavate dattvā cariṣyāmi yathecchayā ।। sarvakāmasamṛddhārthā bhaviṣyati tava prajā ।। saṃkrāmayāmāsa jarāṃ tadā putre mahātmani ।। prītiyukto naraśreṣṭhaś cacāra viṣayānpriyān ।।
dharmāviruddhānrājendro yathārhati sa eva hi ।। dīnānanugrahairiṣṭaiḥ kāmaiśca dvijasattamān ।। ānṛśaṃsyena śūdrāṃśca dasyūnnigrahaṇena ca ।। yayātiḥ pālayāmāsa sākṣādindra ivāparaḥ ।।
avirodhena dharmasya cacāra sukhamuttamam ।। kālaṃ varṣasahasrāntaṃ sasmāra manujādhipaḥ ।। pūrṇam matvā tataḥ kālaṃ pūruṃ putramuvāca ha ।। haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmeva bhūya evābhivardhate ।।
nālamekasya tatsarvam iti matvā śamaṃ vrajet ।। sevitā viṣayāḥ putra yauvanena mayā tava ।। rājyaṃ caiva gṛhāṇedaṃ tvaṃ hi me priyakṛtsutaḥ ।। yauvanaṃ pratipede sa pūruḥ svaṃ punarātmanaḥ ।।
brāhmaṇapramukhā varṇā idaṃ vacanamabruvan ।। jyeṣṭhaṃ yadumatikramya rājyaṃ pūroḥ pradāsyasi ।। śarmiṣṭhāyāḥ suto druhyus tathānuḥ pūrureva ca ।। etatsaṃbodhayāmastvāṃ svadharmamanupālaya ।।
jyeṣṭhaṃ prati yato rājyaṃ na deyaṃ me kathaṃcana ।। pratikūlaḥ pituryaśca na sa putraḥ satāṃ mataḥ ।। sa putraḥ putravadyaśca vartate pitṛmātṛṣu ।। druhyuṇā cānunā caivam apyavajñā kṛtā bhṛśam ।।
kanīyānmama dāyādo jarā yena dhṛtā mama ।। śukreṇa ca varo dattaḥ kāvyenośanasā svayam ।। bhavantaḥ pratijānantu pūrū rājye abhiṣicyatām ।। sarvaṃ so arhati kalyāṇaṃ kanīyānapi sa prabhuḥ ।।
varadānena śukrasya na śakyaṃ vaktumuttaram ।। abhiṣicya tataḥ pūruṃ rājye svasutamātmajam ।। purātsa niryayau rājā brāhmaṇaistāpasaiḥ saha ।। druhyoścaiva sutā bhojā anostu mlecchajātayaḥ ।।
idaṃ varṣasahasrāttu rājyaṃ kurukulāgatam ।। rājye abhiṣicya mudito vānaprastho abhavanmuniḥ ।। phalamūlāśano dānto yathā svargamito gataḥ ।। kālasya nātimahataḥ punaḥ śakreṇa pātitaḥ ।।
sthitaścāsīd antarikṣe sa tadeti śrutaṃ mayā ।। pratardanena śibinā sametya kila saṃsadi ।। kathamindreṇa bhagavan pātito medinītale ।। kathyamānaṃ tvayā vipra devarṣigaṇasaṃnidhau ।।
vardhanaḥ kuruvaṃśasya vibhāvasusamadyutiḥ ।। śrotumicchāmi deveśa divi ceha ca sarvaśaḥ ।। divi ceha ca puṇyārthāṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśinīm ।। rājye abhiṣicya muditaḥ pravavrāja vanaṃ tadā ।।
phalamūlāśano rājā vane asau nyavasacciram ।। agnīṃśca vidhivajjuhvan vānaprasthavidhānataḥ ।। śiloñchavṛttimāsthāya śeṣānnakṛtabhojanaḥ ।। ambubhakṣaḥ sa cābdāṃstrīn āsīn niyatavāṅmanāḥ ।।
pañcāgnimadhye ca tapas tepe saṃvatsaraṃ punaḥ ।। puṇyakīrtistataḥ svargaṃ jagāmāvṛtya rodasī ।। pūjitastridaśaiḥ sādhyair marudbhirvasubhistathā ।। avasatpṛthivīpālo dīrghakālamiti śrutiḥ ।।
kathānte tatra śakreṇa pṛṣṭaḥ sa pṛthivīpatiḥ ।। tadā rājyaṃ sampradāyaiva tasmai tvayā kimuktaḥ kathayeha satyam ।। madhye pṛthivyāstvaṃ rājā bhrātaro ante adhipāstava ।। amānuṣebhyo mānuṣaśca pradhāno vidvāṃstathaivāviduṣaḥ pradhānaḥ ।।
ākroṣṭāraṃ nirdahati sukṛtaṃ cāsya vindati ।। yayāsya vācā para udvijeta na tāṃ vadedruśatīṃ pāpalaulyām ।। vidyād alakṣmīkatamaṃ janānāṃ mukhe nibaddhaṃ nirṛtiṃ vahantam ।। sadā satām ativādāṃstitikṣet satāṃ vṛttaṃ pālayansādhuvṛtaḥ ।।
parasya no marmasu te patanti tānpaṇḍito nāvasṛjetpareṣu ।। yathā maitrī ca lokeṣu dānaṃ ca madhurā ca vāk ।। pūjyānsampūjayed dadyān nābhiśāpaṃ kadācana ।। tattvāṃ pṛcchāmi nahuṣasya putra kenāpi tulyastapasā yayāte ।।
ātmanastapasā tulyaṃ kaṃcitpaśyāmi vāsava ।। tasmāllokā hy antavantastaveme kṣīṇe puṇye patito asyadya rājan ।। icchāmyahaṃ suralokādvihīnaḥ satāṃ madhye patituṃ devarāja ।। evaṃ viditvā tu punaryayāte na te avamānyāḥ sadṛśaḥ śreyase ca ।।
samprekṣya rājarṣivaro aṣṭakas tam uvāca saddharmavidhānagoptā ।। patasyudīrṇāmbudharaprakāśaḥ khe khecarāṇāṃ pravaro yathārkaḥ ।। kiṃnusvid etat patatīva sarve vitarkayantaḥ parimohitāḥ smaḥ ।। pratyudgatāstvāṃ vayamadya sarve tasmātpāte tava jijñāsamānāḥ ।।
tattvāṃ pṛcchāmi spṛhaṇīyarūpaṃ kasya tvaṃ vā kiṃnimittaṃ tvamāgāḥ ।। tvāṃ vartamānaṃ hi satāṃ sakāśe śakro na soḍhuṃ balahāpi śaktaḥ ।। te saṃgatāḥ sthāvarajaṅgameśāḥ pratiṣṭhitastvaṃ sadṛśeṣu satsu ।। prabhuḥ sūryaḥ prakāśācca satāṃ cābhyāgataḥ prabhuḥ ।।
prabhraṃśito ahaṃ surasiddhalokāt paricyutaḥ prapatāmyalpapuṇyaḥ ।। yo vidyayā tapasā janmanā vā vṛddhaḥ sa vai sambhavati dvijānām ।। yo vai vidvāṃstapasā sampravṛddhaḥ sa eva pūjyo bhavati dvijānām ।। santo asato nānvavartanta te vai yadātmanaiṣāṃ pratikūlavādī ।।
evaṃ pradhāryātmahite niviṣṭo yo vartate sa vijānāti dhīraḥ ।। tattatprāpya na vihanyeta dhīro diṣṭaṃ balīya iti matvātmabuddhyā ।। tasmāddiṣṭaṃ balavanmanyamāno na saṃjvarennāpi hṛṣyetkadācit ।। diṣṭaṃ balīya iti manyamāno na saṃjvarennāpi hṛṣyet kadācit ।।
dhātā yathā māṃ vidadhāti loke dhruvaṃ tathāhaṃ bhaviteti matvā ।। tathāśmānastṛṇakāṣṭhaṃ ca sarvaṃ diṣṭakṣaye svāṃ prakṛtiṃ bhajante ।। kiṃ kuryāṃ vai kiṃca kṛtvā na tapye tasmātsaṃtāpaṃ varjayāmyapramattaḥ ।। mātāmahaṃ sarvaguṇopapannaṃ yatra sthitaṃ svargaloke yathāvat ।।
tanme rājanbrūhi sarvaṃ yathāvat kṣetrajñavadbhāṣase tvaṃ hi dharmam ।। tatrāvasaṃ varṣasahasramātraṃ tato lokānparamānabhyupetaḥ ।। adhyāvasaṃ varṣasahasramātraṃ tato lokānparamānabhyupetaḥ ।। tatrāvasaṃ varṣasahasramātraṃ tato lokānparamānabhyupetaḥ ।।
sampūjyamānastridaśaiḥ samastais tulyaprabhāvadyutirīśvarāṇām ।। sahāpsarobhirvicaranpuṇyagandhān paśyannagān puṣpitāṃścārurūpān ।। dūto devānāmabravīdugrarūpo dhvaṃsetyuccaistriḥ plutena svareṇa ।। vāco aśrauṣaṃ cāntarikṣe surāṇām anukrośācchocatāṃ māṃ narendra ।।
tānabruvaṃ patamānastadāhaṃ satāṃ madhye nipateyaṃ kathaṃ nu ।। havirgandhair darśitāṃ yajñabhūmiṃ dhūmāpāṅgaṃ parigṛhya pratītām ।। kiṃkāraṇaṃ kārtayugapradhāna hitvā tadvai vasudhām anvapadyaḥ ।। tathā svarge kṣīṇapuṇyaṃ manuṣyaṃ tyajanti sadyaḥ khecarā devasaṃghāḥ ।।
kiṃviśiṣṭāḥ kasya dhāmopayānti tadvai brūhi kṣetravittvaṃ mato me ।। te kaṅkagomāyupalāśanārthaṃ kṣitau vivṛddhiṃ bahudhā prayānti ।। ākhyātaṃ te pārthiva sarvametad bhūyaścedānīṃ vada kiṃ te vadāmi ।। kathaṃ bhavanti kathamābhavanti tvatto bhaumaṃ narakamahaṃ śṛṇomi ।।
imaṃ bhaumaṃ narakaṃ te patanti nāvekṣante varṣapūgānanekān ।। tānvai nudante prapatantaḥ prayātān bhīmā bhaumā rākṣasās tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrāḥ ।। kathaṃ bhavanti kathamābhavanti kathaṃbhūtā garbhabhūtā bhavanti ।। tava tarayā raja āpadyate ca sa garbhabhūtaḥ samupaiti tatra ।।
catuṣpadaṃ dvipadaṃ cāpi sarva evaṃbhūtā garbhabhūtā bhavanti ।। āpadyamāno narayonimetām ācakṣva me saṃśayātpṛcchatastvam ।। etatsarvaṃ tāta ācakṣva pṛṣṭaḥ kṣetrajñaṃ tvāṃ manyamānā hi sarve ।। sa tatra tanmātrakṛtādhikāraḥ krameṇa saṃvardhayatīha garbham ।।
sa śrotrābhyāṃ vedayatīha śabdaṃ sa vai rūpaṃ paśyati cakṣuṣā ca ।। ityaṣṭakehopacitaṃ hi viddhi mahātmanaḥ prāṇabhṛtaḥ śarīre ।। abhāvabhūtaḥ sa vināśametya kenātmānaṃ cetayate purastāt ।। anyāṃ yoniṃ puṇyapāpānusārāṃ hitvā dehaṃ bhajate rājasiṃha ।।
kīṭāḥ pataṃgāśca bhavanti pāpān na me vivakṣāsti mahānubhāva ।। ākhyātametannikhilaṃ hi sarvaṃ bhūyastu kiṃ pṛcchasi rājasiṃha ।। tanme pṛṣṭaḥ śaṃsa sarvaṃ yathāvac chubhāṃllokān yena gacchetkrameṇa ।। svargasya lokasya vadanti santo dvārāṇi saptaiva mahānti puṃsām ।।
naśyanti mānena tamo abhibhūtāḥ puṃsaḥ sadaiveti vadanti santaḥ ।। tasyāntavantaḥ puruṣasya lokā na cāsya tadbrahmaphalaṃ dadāti ।। mānāgnihotramuta mānamaunaṃ mānenādhītamuta mānayajñaḥ ।। santaḥ sataḥ pūjayantīha loke nāsādhavaḥ sādhubuddhiṃ labhante ।।
ityetānyabhayānyāhus tāny avarjyāni nityaśaḥ ।। tanniḥśreyas tena saṃyogametya parāṃ śāntiṃ prāpnuyuḥ pretya ceha ।। vānaprasthaḥ satpathe saṃniviṣṭo bahūnyasmin samprati vedayanti ।। mṛdurdānto dhṛtimānapramattaḥ svādhyāyaśīlaḥ sidhyati brahmacārī ।।
anādadānaśca parairadattaṃ saiṣā gṛhasthopaniṣatpurāṇī ।। tādṛṅmuniḥ siddhimupaiti mukhyāṃ vasann araṇye niyatāhāraceṣṭaḥ ।। anokaśāyī laghu lipsamānaś caran deśānekacaraḥ sa bhikṣuḥ ।। tāmeva rātriṃ prayateta vidvān araṇyasaṃstho bhavituṃ yatātmā ।।
araṇyavāsī sukṛtaṃ dadhāti muktvā tv araṇye svaśarīradhātūn ।। bhavantīti tadācakṣva śrotum icchāmahe vayam ।। grāme vā vasato araṇyaṃ sa muniḥ syājjanādhipa ।। grāme vā vasato araṇyaṃ kathaṃ bhavati pṛṣṭhataḥ ।।
tathāsya vasato araṇye grāmo bhavati pṛṣṭhataḥ ।। kaupīnācchādanaṃ yāvat tāvadicchecca cīvaram ।। tadāsya vasato grāme araṇyaṃ bhavati pṛṣṭhataḥ ।। ātiṣṭheta munir maunaṃ sa loke siddhimāpnuyāt ।।
asitaṃ sitakarmasthaṃ kastaṃ nārcitumarhati ।। yadā bhavati nirdvaṃdvo munirmaunaṃ samāsthitaḥ ।। athāsya lokaiḥ sarvo yaḥ so amṛtatvāya kalpate ।। ubhayordhāvato rājan sūryacandramasoriva ।।
grāma eva caranbhikṣus tayoḥ pūrvataraṃ gataḥ ।। tapyeta yadi tatkṛtvā caretsograṃ tapastataḥ ।। asāvanīśaḥ sa tathaiva rājaṃs tadārjavaṃ sa samādhistadāryam ।। kuta āgataḥ katamasyāṃ diśi tvamutāhosvitpārthivasthānam asti ।।
uktvāhaṃ vaḥ prapatiṣyāmy anantaraṃ tvarantvamī brahmaṇo lokapā ye ।। śakrācca labdho hi varo mayaiṣa patiṣyatā bhūmitalaṃ narendra ।। yadyantarikṣe yadi vā divi śritāḥ kṣetrajñaṃ tvāṃ tasya dharmasya manye ।। tāvallokā divi te saṃsthitā vai tathā vijānīhi narendrasiṃha ।।
yadyantarikṣe yadi vā divi śritāstānākrama kṣipramamitrahā'thasi ।। yathā pradeyaṃ satataṃ dvijebhyas tadā dade pūrvam ahaṃ narendra ।। so ahaṃ yadevākṛtapūrvaṃ careyaṃ vivitsamānaḥ kimu tatra sādhuḥ ।। yadyantarikṣe yadi vā divi śrutāḥ kṣetrajñaṃ tvāṃ tasya dharmasya manye ।।
madhucyuto ghṛtavanto viśokās tenāntavantaḥ pratipālayanti ।। yadyantarikṣe yadi vā divi śritās tānākrama kṣipramapetamohaḥ ।। daivādeśādāpadaṃ prāpya vidvāṃś carennṛśaṃsaṃ hi na jātu rājā ।। na madvidho dharmabuddhirhi rājā hy evaṃ kuryātkṛpaṇaṃ māṃ yathāttha ।।
bruvāṇamevaṃ nṛpatiṃ yayātiṃ nṛpottamo vasumānabravīt tam ।। yadyantarikṣe prathito mahātman kṣetrajñaṃ tvāṃ tasya dharmasya manye ।। lokās tāvanto divi saṃsthitā vai te tvāṃ bhavantaṃ pratipālayanti ।। krīṇīṣvaināṃs tṛṇakenāpi rājan pratigrahaste yadi samyakpraduṣṭaḥ ।।
kuryāṃ na caivākṛtapūrvamanyair vivitsamāno vasumanna sādhu ।। nāhaṃ tānvai pratigantā narendra sarve lokāstāvakā vai bhavantu ।। yadyantarikṣe yadi vā divi śritāḥ kṣetrajñaṃ tvāṃ tasya dharmasya manye ।। tenānantā divi lokāḥ sthitā vai vidyudrūpāḥ svanavanto mahāntaḥ ।।
na cāhaṃ tānpratipadya dattvā yatra tvaṃ tāta gantāsi lokān ।। tathādya loke na rame anyadatte tasmācchibe nābhinandāmi vācam ।। sarve pradāya tāṃllokān gantāro narakaṃ vayam ।। ahaṃ tu nābhigṛhṇāmi yatkṛtaṃ na mayā purā ।।
asya pradānasya yadeva yuktaṃ tasyaiva cānantaphalaṃ bhaviṣyam ।। uccaiḥ santaḥ prakāśante jvalanto agniśikhā iva ।। āruhyaiteṣu gantavyaṃ bhavadbhiśca mayā saha ।। vayamapyanuyāsyāmo yadā kālo bhaviṣyati ।।
eṣa vo virajāḥ panthā dṛśyate devasadmagaḥ ।। ākrāmanto divaṃ bhānti dharmeṇāvṛtya rodasī ।। kasmādevaṃ śibirauśīnaro ayam eko atyayāt sarvaṃ vegena vāhān ।। uśīnarasya putro ayaṃ tasmācchreṣṭho hi vaḥ śibiḥ ।।
evaṃ vṛttaṃ hrīniṣevī bibharti tasmācchibir abhigantā rathena ।। kṛtaṃ tvayā yaddhi na tasya kartā loke tvadanyo brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vā ।। guhyaṃ mantraṃ māmakebhyo bravīmi mātāmaho bhavatāṃ suprakāśaḥ ।। medhyānaśvānnaikaśas tānsurūpāṃs tadā devāḥ puṇyabhājo bhavanti ।।
gobhiḥ suvarṇaiśca dhanaiśca mukhyair aśvāḥ sanāgāḥ śataśastvarbudāni ।। na me vṛthā vyāhṛtameva vākyaṃ satyaṃ hi santaḥ pratipūjayanti ।। sādhvaṣṭaka prabravīmīha satyaṃ pratardanaṃ vasumantaṃ śibiṃ ca । sarve devā munayaśca lokāḥ satyena pūjyā iti me manogatam ।।
anasūyur dvijāgnyebhyaḥ sa bhajennaḥ salokatām ।। tyaktvā mahīṃ paramodārakarmā svargaṃ gataḥ karmabhirvyāpya pṛthvīm ।। vaṃśo yasya prathitaṃ pauraveyo yasmiñjātastvaṃ manujendrakalpaḥ ।। vismitaḥ parayā prītyā pūrṇacandra ivābabhau ।।
