ratnairgobhiḥ suvarṇaiśca vāsobhirvividhaistathā ।। dattvā ca brāhmaṇebhyaśca śaunako antaradhīyata ।। yaduprabhṛtibhiḥ putrair yadā loke pratiṣṭhitam ।। vistareṇānupūrvyā ca gadato me nibodhata ।।
mahārathā maheṣvāsā nāmatastānnibodhata ।। sahasrajestu dāyādaḥ śatajirnāma pārthivaḥ ।। haihayaśca hayaścaiva tathā veṇuhayaśca yaḥ ।। dharmanetrasya kuntistu saṃhatastasya cātmajaḥ ।।
āsīnmahiṣmataḥ putro rudraśreṇyaḥ pratāpavān ।। rudraśreṇyasya putro abhūd durdamo nāma pārthivaḥ ।। kanakasya tu dāyādāś catvāro lokaviśrutāḥ ।। kṛtaujāśca caturtho abhūt kṛtavīryāttato arjunaḥ ।।
varṣāyutaṃ tapastepe duścaraṃ pṛthivīpatiḥ ।। tasmai dattā varāstena catvāraḥ puruṣottama ।। adharmaṃ caramāṇasya sadbhiścāpi nivāraṇam ।। saṃgrāme vartamānasya vadhaścaivādhikādbhavet ।।
saptodadhiparikṣiptā kṣāttreṇa vidhinā jitā ।। ratho dhvajaśca saṃjajña ityevamanuśuśruma ।। nirargalāni vṛttāni śrūyante tasya dhīmataḥ ।। sarve kāñcanayūpāste sarvāḥ kāñcanavedikāḥ ।।
gandharvairapsarobhiśca nityamevopaśobhitāḥ ।। kārtavīryasya rājarṣer mahimānaṃ nirīkṣya saḥ ।। yajñairdānaistapobhiśca vikrameṇa śrutena ca ।। rathī dvīpānyanucaran yogī paśyati taskarān ।।
sa sarvaratnasampūrṇaś cakravartī babhūva ha ।। sa eva vṛṣṭyā parjanyo yogitvādarjuno abhavat ।। bhāti raśmisahasreṇa śāradeneva bhāskaraḥ ।। karkoṭakasutaṃ jitvā puryāṃ tatra nyaveśayat ।।
krīḍanneva sukhodbhinnaḥ pratisroto mahīpatiḥ ।। ūrmibhrukuṭisaṃtrāsāc cakitābhyeti narmadā ।। karotyudvṛttavegāṃ tu narmadāṃ prāvṛḍuddhatām ।। bhavantyatīva niśceṣṭāḥ pātālasthā mahāsurāḥ ।।
mārutāviddhaphenaugham āvartākṣiptaduḥsaham ।। mandarakṣobhacakitā hy amṛtotpādaśaṅkitāḥ ।। sāyāhne kadalīkhaṇḍā nirvātastimitā iva ।। laṅkāyāṃ mohayitvā tu sabalaṃ rāvaṇaṃ balāt ।।
tato gatvā pulastyastu hy arjunaṃ saṃprasādayan ।। tasya bāhusahasreṇa babhūva jyātalasvanaḥ ।। aho bata vidhervīryaṃ bhārgavo ayaṃ yadāchinat ।। yatrāpavastu saṃkruddho hy arjunaṃ śaptavānprabhuḥ ।।
tasmātte duṣkaraṃ karma kṛtamanyo hariṣyati ।। tapasvī brāhmaṇaśca tvāṃ sa vadhiṣyati bhārgava ।। varaścaiva tu rājarṣeḥ svayameva vṛtaḥ purā ।। kṛtāstrā balinaḥ śūrā dharmātmāno mahābalāḥ ।।
jayadhvajaśca vaikartā avantiśca viśāṃpate ।। tasya putraśatānyeva tālajaṅghā iti śrutāḥ ।। vītihotrāśca śāryāto bhojāścāvantayastathā ।। durjeyastasya putrastu babhūva mitrakarśanaḥ ।।
kārtavīryārjuno nāma rājā bāhusahasravān ।। yastasya kīrtayennāma kalyamutthāya mānavaḥ ।। yathāvatsviṣṭapūtātmā svargaloke mahīyate ।। kārtavīryeṇa vikramya sūta prabrūhi tattvataḥ ।।
sa kathaṃ rakṣitā bhūtvā adahattattapovanam ।। tṛptimekāṃ prayacchasva ādityo ahaṃ nareśvara ।। kīdṛśaṃ bhojanaṃ dadmi hutvā tu vidadhāmyaham ।। tena tṛpto bhaveyaṃ vai sā me tṛptirhi pārthiva ।।
nirdagdhuṃ tapatāṃ śreṣṭha tena tvāṃ praṇamāmyaham ।। ye prakṣiptā jvaliṣyanti mama tejaḥsamanvitāḥ ।। śuṣkān bhasmīkariṣyanti tena tṛptirnarādhipa ।। tato dadāha samprāptān sthāvarān sarvameva ca ।।
tapovanāni ramyāṇi vanānyupavanāni ca ।। nirvṛkṣā nistṛṇā bhūmir hatā ghoreṇa tejasā ।। daśa varṣasahasrāṇi tatrāste sa mahānṛṣiḥ ।। so apaśyadāśramaṃ dagdham arjunena mahāmuniḥ ।।
kroṣṭoḥ śṛṇuta rājarṣer vaṃśamuttamapauruṣam ।। kroṣṭorevābhavatputro vṛjinīvānmahārathaḥ ।। svāhaputro abhavad rājan ruṣaṅgur vadatāṃ varaḥ ।। citraścitrarathaścāsya putraḥ karmabhiranvitaḥ ।।
śaśabinduriti khyātaś cakravartī babhūva ha ।। śaśabindostu putrāṇāṃ śatānām abhavacchatam ।। teṣāṃ śatapradhānānāṃ pṛthusāhvā mahābalāḥ ।। pṛthukīrtiḥ pṛthumanā rājānaḥ śaśabindavaḥ ।।
antarasya suyajñasya suyajñastanayo abhavat ।। ājahārāśvamedhānāṃ śatamuttamadhārmikaḥ ।। maruttastasya tanayo rājarṣīṇāmanuttamaḥ ।। putrastu rukmakavaco vidvānkambalabarhiṣaḥ ।।
dhanvino vividhairbāṇair avāpya pṛthivīmimām ।। yajñe tu rukmakavacaḥ kadācitparavīrahā ।। rukmeṣuḥ pṛthurukmaśca jyāmaghaḥ parigho hariḥ ।। rukmeṣurabhavadrājā pṛthurukmastadāśrayaḥ ।।
praśāntaścāśramasthaśca brāhmaṇenāvabodhitaḥ ।। narmadāṃ nṛpa ekākī kevalaṃ vṛttikāmataḥ ।। jyāmaghasyābhavadbhāryā caitrā pariṇatā satī ।। tasyāsīdvijayo yuddhe tatra kanyāmavāpya saḥ ।।
evamuktābravīdenaṃ kasya ceyaṃ snuṣeti ca ।। tasmātsā tapasogreṇa kanyāyāḥ samprasūyata ।। lomapādaṃ tṛtīyaṃ tu putraṃ paramadhārmikam ।। lomapādānmanuḥ putrā jñātistasya tu cātmajaḥ ।।
kratho vidarbhaputrastu kuntis tasyātmajo abhavat ।। dhṛṣṭasya putro dharmātmā nirvṛtiḥ paravīrahā ।। dāśārhāccaiva vyomāttu putro jīmūta ucyate ।। suto bhīmarathasyāsīt smṛto navarathaḥ kila ।।
tasmātkarambhaḥ kārambhir devarāto babhūva ha ।। devagarbhasamo jajñe devanakṣatranandanaḥ ।। āsīt puravasāt putraḥ purudvānpuruṣottamaḥ ।। aikṣvākī cābhavadbhāryā jantostasyāmajāyata ।।
prajāvān eti sāyujyaṃ rājñaḥ somasya dhīmataḥ ।। bhajinaṃ bhajamānaṃ tu divyaṃ devāvṛdhaṃ nṛpa ।। teṣāṃ tu sargāś catvāro vistareṇaiva tacchṛṇu ।। sṛñjayasya sute dve tu bāhyakāstu tadābhavan ।।
te bāhyakāyāṃ sṛñjayyāṃ bhajamānād vijajñire ।। putraḥ sarvaguṇopeto mama bhūyāditi spṛhan ।। tadopasparśanāttasya cakāra priyamāpagā ।। cintayātha parītātmā jagāmātha viniścayam ।।
jāyeta tasmādadyāhaṃ bhavāmyatha sahasraśaḥ ।। jñāpayāmāsa rājānaṃ tāmiyeṣa mahāvrataḥ ।। putraṃ sarvaguṇopetaṃ babhruṃ devāvṛdhānnṛpāt ।। guṇāndevāvṛdhasyāpi kīrtayanto mahātmanaḥ ।।
babhruḥ śreṣṭho manuṣyāṇāṃ devairdevāvṛdhaḥ samaḥ ।। ete amṛtatvaṃ samprāptā babhror devāvṛdhānnṛpa ।। rūpavānsumahātejāḥ śrutavīryadharastathā ।। kukuraṃ bhajamānaṃ ca śaśiṃ kambalabarhiṣam ।।
kapotaromā tasyātha taittiristasya cātmajaḥ ।। khyāyate tasya nāmnā sa nandano daradundubhiḥ ।। aśvamedhaṃ ca putrārtham ājahāra narottamaḥ ।। atastu vidvānkarmajño yajvā dātā punarvasuḥ ।।
āhukaścāhukī caiva khyātaṃ mātematāṃ vara ।। sopāsaṅgānukarṣāṇāṃ sadhvajānāṃ varūthinām ।। nāsatyavādī nātejā nāyajvā nāsahasradaḥ ।। āhukasya bhṛtiṃ prāptā ityetadvai taducyate ।।
āhukātkāśyaduhitā dvau putrau samasūyata ।। devakasya sutā vīrā jajñire tridaśopamāḥ ।। teṣāṃ svasāraḥ saptāsan vasudevāya tā dadau ।। śrīdevī satyadevī ca sutāpī ceti saptamī ।।
nyagrodhaśca sunāmā ca kaṅkaḥ śaṅkuśca bhūyasaḥ ।। teṣāṃ svasāraḥ pañcāsan kaṃsā kaṃsavatī tathā ।। ugrasenaḥ sahāpatyo vyākhyātaḥ kukurodbhavaḥ ।। rājādhidevaḥ śūraśca vidūrathasuto abhavat ।।
niyamavratapradhānau śoṇāśvaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ ।। śamī ca devaśarmā ca nikuntaḥ śakraśatrujit ।। pratikṣetraḥ suto bhojo hṛdīkastasya cātmajaḥ ।। kṛtavarmāgrajas teṣāṃ śatadhanvā ca madhyamaḥ ।।
ajāto vanajātaśca kanīyakakarambhakau ।। asāmañjāḥ sutastasya tamojātasya cātmajaḥ ।। sudaṃṣṭraśca sunābhaśca kṛṣṇa ityandhakā matāḥ ।। ātmano vipulaṃ vaṃśaṃ prajāvānāpnute naraḥ ।।
gāndhārī janayāmāsa sumitraṃ mitranandanam ।। anamitraṃ śibiṃ caiva pañcamaṃ kṛtalakṣaṇam ।। prasenaśca mahāvīryaḥ śaktisenaśca tāv ubhau ।। pṛthivyāṃ sarvaratnānāṃ rājā vai so abhavanmaṇiḥ ।।
govindo api na taṃ lebhe śakto api na jahāra saḥ ।। yathāśabdaṃ sa śuśrāva bile sattvena pūrite ।। ṛkṣaḥ prasenaṃ ca tathā ṛkṣaṃ caiva prasenajit ।। adṛṣṭastu hatastena antarbilagatastadā ।।
govindena hato vyaktaṃ praseno maṇikāraṇāt ।। hanmi cainaṃ durācāraṃ śatrubhūtaṃ hi vṛṣṇiṣu ।। yadṛcchayā ca govindo bilasyābhyāśamāgamat ।। apaśyajjāmbavantaṃ tam ṛkṣarājaṃ mahābalam ।।
jāmbavantaṃ sa jagrāha krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ ।। tatastuṣṭastu bhagavān vareṇainamarocayat ।। yo ayaṃ maṇiḥ prasenaṃ tu hatvā prāpto mayā prabho ।। kṛtakarmā mahābāhuḥ sakanyaṃ maṇimāharat ।।
tena mithyāpavādena saṃtapto ayaṃ janārdanaḥ ।। asmākaṃ tu matirhyāsīt prasenastu tvayā hataḥ ।। khyātimanto mahāvīryā bhaṅgakārastu pūrvajaḥ ।। suṣuve sukumārīstu tisraḥ kamalalocanāḥ ।।
tathā padmāvatī caiva tāśca kṛṣṇāya so adadāt ।। satyakastasya putrastu sātyakistasya cātmajaḥ ।। asaṅgo yuyudhānasya dyumnistasyātmajo abhavat ।। anamitrānvayo hy eṣa vyākhyāto vṛṣṇivaṃśajaḥ ।।
anyau tu tanayau vīrau vṛṣabhaḥ kṣatra eva ca ।। jayantastu jayantyāṃ tu putraḥ samabhavacchubhaḥ ।। akrūraḥ suṣuve tasmāt sadāyajño atidakṣiṇaḥ ।। putrānutpādayāmāsa ekādaśa mahābalān ।।
savītaraḥ sadāpakṣaḥ śatrughno vārimejayaḥ ।। sarve ca pratihotāro ratnāyāṃ jajñire ca te ।। devavānupadevaśca jajñāte devasaṃnibhau ।। aśvatthāmā subāhuśca supārśvakagaveṣaṇau ।।
abhūmir varjabhūmiśca śramiṣṭhaḥ śravaṇastathā ।। na sa mithyābhiśāpena abhiśāpyo atha kenacit ।। pauruṣājjajñire śūrād bhojāyāṃ putrakā daśa ।। devamārgastato jajñe tato devaśravāḥ punaḥ ।।
śyāmaḥ śamīkaḥ saṃyūpaḥ pañca cāsya varāṅganāḥ ।। rājādhidevī ca tathā pañcaitā vīramātaraḥ ।। kaikeyyāṃ śrutakīrtyāṃ tu jajñe so anuvrato nṛpaḥ ।। bahuśo dharmacārī sa saṃbabhūvārimardanaḥ ।।
evaṃ kuntī samākhyātā vasudevasvasā pṛthā ।। pāṇḍorarthena sā jajñe devaputrān mahārathān ।। indrāddhanaṃjayaś caiva śakratulyaparākramaḥ ।। nakulaḥ sahadevaśca rūpaśīlaguṇānvitau ।।
lebhe jyeṣṭhaṃ sutaṃ rāmaṃ sāraṇaṃ ca sutaṃ priyam ।। citrākṣyau dve kumāryau tu rohiṇyāṃ jajñire tadā ।। ṣaṣṭho bhadravidehaśca kaṃsaḥ sarvānaghātayat ।। tasyāṃ jajñe mahābāhuḥ pūrvaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।।
devakyāṃ tu mahātejā jajñe śūro mahāyaśāḥ ।। ekāṃ kanyāṃ ca subhagāṃ kaṃsastām abhyaghātayat ।। ete sarve mahātmāno hy upadevyāṃ prajajñire ।। vṛkadevyāṃ svayaṃ jajñe nandako nāma nāmataḥ ।।
gaveṣaṇaṃ mahābhāgaṃ saṃgrāmeṣvaparājitam ।। vaiśyāyāmadadhācchauriḥ putraṃ kauśikamagrajam ।। puṇḍraśca kapilaścaiva vasudevātmajau balau ।। saubhadraśca bhavaścaiva mahāsattvau babhūvatuḥ ।।
paṇḍitaṃ prathamaṃ prāhur devaśravaḥsamudbhavam ।। nidhūtasattvaṃ śatrughnaṃ śrāddhastasmādajāyata ।। sucandraṃ tu mahābhāgaṃ vīryavantaṃ mahābalam ।। cārudeṣṇaśca sāmbaśca vīryavantau mahābalau ।।
virājaśca dhanuścaiva śyāmaśca sṛñjayastathā ।। jugupsamāno bhojatvaṃ rājarṣitvamavāptavān ।। śṛṇoti mānavo nityaṃ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। vihārārthaṃ sa deveśo mānuṣeṣviha jayate ।।
caturbāhustadā jāto divyarūpo jvalañśriyā ।। uvāca vasudevastaṃ rūpaṃ saṃhara vai prabho ।। mama putrā hatāstena jyeṣṭhāste bhīmavikramāḥ ।। anujñāpya tataḥ śauriṃ nandagopagṛhe anayat ।।
ayaṃ tu garbho devakyāṃ jātaḥ kaṃsaṃ haniṣyati ।। nandagopaśca kastveṣa yaśodā ca mahāvratā ।। yā garbhaṃ janayāmāsa yā cainaṃ tv abhyavardhayat ।। brahmaṇaḥ kaśyapastvaṃśaḥ pṛthivyāstvaditistathā ।।
ye tayā kāṅkṣitā nityam ajātasya mahātmanaḥ ।। mohayansarvabhūtāni yogātmā yogamāyayā ।। kartuṃ dharmasya saṃsthānam asurāṇāṃ praṇāśanam ।। subhāmā ca tathā śaibyā gāndhārī lakṣmaṇā tathā ।।
evamādīni devīnāṃ sahasrāṇi ca ṣoḍaśa ।। cārudeṣṇaṃ raṇe śūraṃ pradyumnaṃ ca mahābalam ।। cāruhāsaṃ kaniṣṭhaṃ ca kanyāṃ cārumatīṃ tathā ।। rohito dīptimāṃścaiva tāmraś cakro jalaṃdhamaḥ ।।
jāmbavatyāḥ suto jajñe sāmbaḥ samitiśobhanaḥ ।। mitrabāhuḥ sunīthaśca nāgnajityāḥ prajā hi sā ।। śataṃ śatasahasrāṇāṃ putrāṇāṃ tasya dhīmataḥ ।। lakṣamekaṃ tathā proktaṃ putrāṇāṃ ca dvijottamāḥ ।।
bhūrīndraseno bhūriśca gaveṣaṇasutāv ubhau ।। aniruddho raṇe aruddho jajñe asya mṛgaketanaḥ ।। satyaprakṛtayo devāḥ pañca vīrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। ṣaṣṭiḥ śatasahasrāṇi vīryavanto mahābalāḥ ।।
devāsure hatā ye ca tv asurā ye mahābalāḥ ।। teṣāmutsādanārthāya utpanno yādave kule ।। sarvametatkulaṃ yāvad vartate vaiṣṇave kule ।। nideśasthāyinastasya kathyante sarvayādavāḥ ।।
śālakir nāradaścaiva siddho dhanvantaristathā ।। kimarthaṃ saṃghaśo bhūtāḥ smṛtāḥ sambhūtayaḥ kati ।। brahmakṣatreṣu śānteṣu kimarthamiha jāyate ।। punaḥ punarmanuṣyeṣu tannaḥ prabrūhi pṛcchatām ।।
yuge tv atha parāvṛtte kāle praśithile prabhuḥ ।। hiraṇyakaśipau daitye trailokyaṃ prākpraśāsati ।। sakhyamāsītparamakaṃ devānāmasuraiḥ saha ।। nideśasthāyinaścāpi tayordevāsurāḥ samam ।।
devānāmasurāṇāṃ ca ghoraḥ kṣayakaro mahān ।। bhṛgoḥ śāpanimittaṃ tu devāsurakṛte tadā ।। devāsuraṃ yathā vṛttaṃ tannaḥ prabrūhi pṛcchatām ।। varāhādyā daśa dvau ca śaṇḍāmarkāntare smṛtāḥ ।।
prathamo nārasiṃhastu dvitīyaścāpi vāmanaḥ ।। saṃgrāmaḥ pañcamaścaiva saṃjātastārakāmayaḥ ।। andhakākhyo aṣṭamasteṣāṃ navamo vṛtraghātakaḥ ।। prathito dvādaśasteṣāṃ ghoraḥ kolāhalastathā ।।
vāmanena balir baddhas trailokyākramaṇe purā ।। daṃṣṭrayā tu varāheṇa samudrastu dvidhā kṛtaḥ ।। virocanastu prāhlādir nityam indravadhodyataḥ ।। aśaknuvansa devānāṃ sarvaṃ soḍhuṃ sadaivatam ।।
asurāśca piśācāśca dānavāścāndhakāhave ।। saṃpṛkto dānavairvṛtro ghoro hālāhale hataḥ ।। dhvajalakṣaṇamāviśya vipracittiḥ sahānujaḥ ।। jayankolāhale sarvān devaiḥ parivṛto vṛṣā ।।
ete devāsure vṛttāḥ saṃgrāmā dvādaśaiva tu ।। hiraṇyakaśipū rājā varṣāṇāmarbudaṃ babhau ।। aśītiṃ ca sahasrāṇi trailokyaiśvaryatāṃ gataḥ ।। ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi niyutāni ca viṃśatiḥ ।।
tāvatkālaṃ tu prahlādo nivṛtto hy asuraiḥ saha ।। daityasaṃsthamidaṃ sarvam āsīddaśayugaṃ punaḥ ।। asapatnamidaṃ sarvam āsīddaśayugaṃ punaḥ ।। tato asurānparityajya śukro devānagacchata ।।
kiṃ tvaṃ no miṣatāṃ rājyaṃ tyaktvā yajñaṃ punargataḥ ।। evamukto abravīddaityān viṣaṇṇānsāntvayangirā ।। mantrāścauṣadhayaścaiva rasā vasu ca yatparam ।। tatsarvaṃ vaḥ pradāsyāmi yuṣmadarthe dhṛtā mayā ।।
saṃmantrayanti devā vai saṃvijñāstu jighṛkṣayā ।। sādhu gacchāmahe tūrṇaṃ yāvannādhyāpayiṣyati ।। tato devāstu saṃrabdhā dānavān upasṛtya ha ।। tataḥ kāvyastu tāndṛṣṭvā tūrṇaṃ devair abhidrutān ।।
kāvyaṃ dṛṣṭvā sthitaṃ devā niḥśaṅkamasurāñjahuḥ ।। tānuvāca tataḥ kāvyaḥ pūrvaṃ vṛttamanusmaran ।। balirbaddho hato jambho nihataśca virocanaḥ ।। taistairupāyairbhūyiṣṭhaṃ nihatā vaḥ pradhānataḥ ।।
nītiṃ yāṃ vo abhidhāsyāmi tiṣṭhadhvaṃ kālaparyayāt ।। yudhyāmahe punardevāṃs tataḥ prāpsyatha vai jayam ।। nyastaśastrā vayaṃ sarve niḥsaṃnāhā rathairvinā ।। prahlādasya vacaḥ śrutvā satyābhivyāhṛtaṃ tu tat ।।
nyastaśastreṣu daityeṣu vinivṛttāstadā surāḥ ।। nirutsiktās tapoyuktāḥ kālaṃ kāryārthasādhakam ।। tatsaṃdiśyāsurānkāvyo mahādevaṃ prapadyata ।। parābhavāya devānām asurāṇāṃ jayāya ca ।।
yadi pāsyasi bhadraṃ te tato mantrānavāpsyasi ।। vrataṃ carāmyahaṃ deva tvayādiṣṭo adya vai prabho ।। mantrārthaṃ tatra vasati brahmacaryaṃ maheśvare ।। daṃśitāḥ sāyudhāḥ sarve bṛhaspatipuraḥsarāḥ ।।
utpetuḥ sahasā te vai saṃtrastāstānvaco abruvan ।। dattvā bhavanto hy abhayaṃ samprāptā no jighāṃsayā ।। cīrakṛṣṇājinadharā niṣkriyā niṣparigrahāḥ ।। ayuddhena prapatsyāmaḥ śaraṇaṃ kāvyamātaram ।।
nivṛtte ca tathā śukre yotsyāmo daṃśitāyudhāḥ ।। prāpadyanta tato bhītās tebhyo adādabhayaṃ tu sā ।। matsaṃnidhau vartatāṃ vo na bhīr bhavitumarhati ।। abhijagmuḥ prasahyaitān avicārya balābalam ।।
devī kruddhābravīddevān anindrānvaḥ karomyaham ।। tastambha devī balavad yogayuktā tapodhanā ।। prādravanta tato bhītā indraṃ dṛṣṭvā vaśīkṛtam ।। māṃ tvaṃ praviśa bhadraṃ te nayiṣye tvāṃ surottama ।।
viṣṇunā rakṣitaṃ dṛṣṭvā devī kruddhā vaco abravīt ।। miṣatāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ dṛśyatāṃ me tapobalam ।। kathaṃ mucyeva sahitau viṣṇurindram abhāṣata ।। viśeṣaṇābhibhūto asmi tvatto ahaṃ jahi mā ciram ।।
abhidhyāya tataścakram āpaduddharaṇe tu tat ।। kruddhaḥ svamastramādāya śiraściccheda vai bhiyā ।। tato abhiśapto bhṛguṇā viṣṇur bhāryāvadhe tadā ।। tasmāttvaṃ saptakṛtveha mānuṣeṣūpapatsjase ।।
lokasya ca hitārthāya jāyate mānuyeṣviha ।। samānīya tataḥ kāyam asau gṛhyedamabravīt ।। tatastāṃ yojya śirasā abhijīveti so abravīt ।। tena satyena jīvasva yadi satyaṃ vadāmyaham ।।
tato abhivyāhṛte tasya devī saṃjīvitā tadā ।। sādhu sādhviti cakruste vacasā sarvatodiśam ।। miṣatāṃ devatānāṃ hi tadadbhutam ivābhavad ।। prajāgare tataścendro jayantīmidamabravīt ।।
tenāhaṃ vyākulaḥ putri kṛto matimatā bhṛśam ।। taistairmanonukūlaiśca hy upacārair atandritā ।। gaccha tvaṃ tasya dattā'si prayatnaṃ kuru matkṛte ।। agacchadyatra ghoraṃ sa tapa ārabhya tiṣṭhati ।।
yakṣeṇa pātyamānaṃ ca kuṇḍadhāreṇa pātitam ।। pitrā yathoktaṃ vākyaṃ sā kāvye kṛtavatī tadā ।। vratacaryānukūlābhir uvāsa bahulāḥ samāḥ ।। vareṇa cchandayāmāsa kāvyaṃ prīto bhavastadā ।।
tasmādvai tapasā buddhyā śrutena ca balena ca ।। yaccābhilaṣitaṃ brahman vidyate bhṛgunandana ।। sarvābhibhāvī tena tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi dvijottama ।। prajeśatvaṃ dhaneśatvam avadhyatvaṃ ca vai dadau ।।
tathā tiryaksthitaścaiva tuṣṭuve nīlalohitam ।। lelihānāya kāvyāya vatsarāyāndhasaḥ pate ।। saṃstutāya sutīrthāya devadevāya raṃhase ।। vasuretāya rudrāya tapase citravāsase ।।
kavaye rājavṛkṣāya takṣakakrīḍanāya ca ।। varāya bhavyarūpāya śvetāya puruṣāya ca ।। sutṛptāya suvastrāya dhanvine bhārgavāya ca ।। tāmrāya caiva bhīmāya ugrāya ca śivāya ca ।।
hiraṇyāya variṣṭhāya jyeṣṭhāya madhyamāya ca ।। mṛgavyādhāya dakṣāya sthāṇave bhīṣaṇāya ca ।। kapāline ca vīrāya mṛtyave tryambakāya ca ।। pinākine ceṣumate citrāya rohitāya ca ।।
āraṇyāya gṛhasthāya yataye brahmacāriṇe ।। anāhatāya śarvāya bhavyeśāya yamāya ca ।। catuṣpadāya medhyāya rakṣiṇe śīghragāya ca ।। bhāsvarāya pratītāya sudīptāya sumedhase ।।
saumyāya caiva mukhyāya dhārmikāya śubhāya ca ।। vyāpṛtāya viśiṣṭāya bharatāya ca sākṣiṇe ।। kartre paraśave caiva śūline divyacakṣuṣe ।। śucaye paridhānāya sadyojātāya mṛtyave ।।
vyāvṛttāya variṣṭhāya bharitāya tarakṣave ।। tigmāyudhāya vyākhyāya susiddhāya pulastaye ।। vratine yuñjamānāya śucaye cordhvaretase ।। kṛśānave pracetāya vahnaye nirmalāya ca ।।
vibhrāntāya mahāntāya arṇave durgamāya ca ।। anāśritāya vedhyāya samatvādhiṣṭhitāya ca ।। sukarmaṇe prasahyāya ceśānāya sucakṣuṣe ।। kapilāya piśaṅgāya mahādevāya dhīmate ।।
dṛḍhadhanvine kavacine rathine ca varūthine ।। amoghāya praśāntāya sumedhāya vṛṣāya ca ।। paśūnāṃ pataye tubhyaṃ bhūtānāṃ pataye namaḥ ।। vaṣaṭkārātmane caiva tubhyaṃ mantrātmane namaḥ ।।
bhūtabhavyabhaveśāya tubhyaṃ karmātmane namaḥ ।। viṣāya mārutāyaiva tubhyaṃ devātmane namaḥ ।। prajānāṃ pataye caiva tubhyaṃ brahmātmane namaḥ ।। sarvabhūtāṅgabhūtāya tubhyaṃ bhūtātmane namaḥ ।।
nirupākhyāya mitrāya tubhyaṃ sāṃkhyātmane namaḥ ।। janastapāya satyāya tubhyaṃ lokātmane namaḥ ।। ātmajñāya viśeṣāya tubhyaṃ sarvātmane namaḥ ।। buddhāya vibhave caiva tubhyaṃ mokṣātmane namaḥ ।।
satyānteṣu mahādyeṣu caturṣu ca namo astu te ।। madbhakta iti brahmaṇya tatsarvaṃ kṣantumarhasi ।। prahvo abhipraṇatastasmai prāñjalirvāgyato abhavat ।। nikāmaṃ darśanaṃ dattvā tatraivāntaradhīyata ।।
tiṣṭhantīṃ pārśvato dṛṣṭvā jayantīmidamabravīt ।। mahatā tapasā yuktā kimarthaṃ māṃ niṣevase ।। snehena caiva suśroṇi prīto asmi varavarṇini ।। tatte sampādayāmyadya yadyapi syātsuduṣkaraḥ ।।
cikīrṣitaṃ hi me brahmaṃs tvaṃ hi vettha yathātatham ।। mayā saha tvaṃ suśroṇi daśa varṣāṇi bhāmini ।। evaṃ vṛṇoṣi kāmaṃ tvaṃ matto vai valgubhāṣiṇi ।। tataḥ svagṛhamāgatya jayantyāḥ pāṇimudvahan ।।
adṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ māyayā saṃvṛtaḥ prabhuḥ ।। abhijagmurgṛhaṃ tasya muditāste didṛkṣavaḥ ।। lakṣaṇaṃ tasya tadbuddhvā pratijagmuryathāgatam ।। tuṣṭyarthaṃ daśa varṣāṇi jayantyā hitakāmyayā ।।
kāvyasya rūpamāsthāya asurān samupāhvayat ।। svāgataṃ mama yājyānāṃ prāpto ahaṃ vo hitāya ca ।। tataste hṛṣṭamanaso vidyārthamupapedire ।। buddhiṃ cakre tataḥ so atha yājyānāṃ pratyavekṣaṇe ।।
vibhrāntavīkṣite sādhvi trivarṇāyatalocane ।। eṣa dharmaḥ satāṃ brahman na dharmaṃ lopayāmi te ।। vañcitānkāvyarūpeṇa tataḥ kāvyo abravīttu tān ।। vañcitā bata yūyaṃ vai sarve śṛṇuta dānavāḥ ।।
prekṣantas tāv ubhau tatra sthitāsīnau suvismitāḥ ।। abravīt sampramūḍheṣu kāvyastānasurāṃstadā ।। anugacchata māṃ daityās tyajatainaṃ bṛhaspatim ।। yadāsurā viśeṣaṃ tu na jānantyubhayostayoḥ ।।
kāvyo vo ahaṃ gururdaityā madrūpo ayaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ ।। śrutvā tasya tataste vai sametya tu tato abruvan ।। eṣa vai gururasmākam antarepsurayaṃ dvijaḥ ।। vacanaṃ jagṛhustasya cirābhyāse na mohitāḥ ।।
ayaṃ gurur hito asmākaṃ gaccha tvaṃ nāsi no guruḥ ।। sthitā vayaṃ nideśe asya sādhu tvaṃ gaccha māciram ।। yadā na pratyapadyanta kāvyenoktaṃ mahaddhitam ।। bodhitā hi mayā yasmān na māṃ bhajatha dānavāḥ ।।
iti vyāhṛtya tānkāvyo jagāmātha yathāgatam ।। kṛtārthaḥ sa tadā hṛṣṭaḥ svarūpaṃ pratyapadyata ।। tataḥ pranaṣṭe tasmiṃstu vibhrāntā dānavābhavan ।। pṛṣṭhato abhimukhāścaiva tāḍitāṅgirasena tu ।।
prahlādamagrataḥ kṛtvā kāvyasyānupadaṃ punaḥ ।। samāgatānpunardṛṣṭvā kāvyo yājyānuvāca ha ।। tatastenāvamānena gatā yūyaṃ parābhavam ।। prahlādastaṃ tadovāca mā nastvaṃ tyaja bhārgava ।।
bhaktānarhasi vai jñātuṃ tapodīrgheṇa cakṣuṣā ।। apadhyātās tvayā hy adya praviśāmo rasātalam ।। uvācaitānna bhetavyaṃ na gantavyaṃ rasātalam ।। na śakyamanyathā kartuṃ diṣṭaṃ hi balavattaram ।।
devāñjitvā sakṛccāpi pātālaṃ pratipatsyatha ।। matprasādācca trailokyaṃ bhuktaṃ yuṣmābhirūrjitam ।। etāvantaṃ ca kālaṃ vai brahmā rājyamabhāṣata ।। lokānāmīśvaro bhāvyas tava pautraḥ punarbaliḥ ।।
vācā hṛteṣu lokeṣu tāstāstasyābhavankila ।। tasmādvṛttena prītena tubhyaṃ dattaṃ svayambhuvā ।। tasmādadṛśyo bhūtānāṃ kālāpekṣaḥ sa tiṣṭhati ।। tasmānnirutsukastvaṃ vai paryāyaṃ sahito asuraiḥ ।।
brahmaṇā pratiṣiddho ahaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ jānatā vibho ।। daivataiḥ saha saṃsṛṣṭān sarvānvo dhārayiṣyataḥ ।। hṛṣṭāstena yayuḥ sārdhaṃ prahlādena mahātmanā ।। daṃśitāḥ sāyudhāḥ sarve tato devānsamāhvayan ।।
sarve saṃbhṛtasambhārā devāstān samayodhayan ।। ajayannasurā devāṃs tato devā hy amantrayan ।। tadopāmantrayandevāḥ śaṇḍāmarkau tu tāv ubhau ।। vayaṃ yuvāṃ bhajiṣyāmaḥ saha jitvā tu dānavān ।।
tato devā jayaṃ prāpur dānavāśca parājitāḥ ।। evaṃ daityāḥ purā kāvyaśāpenābhihatāstadā ।। nirasyamānā devaiśca viviśuste rasātalam ।। tataḥ prabhṛti śāpena bhṛgornaimittikena tu ।।
kurvandharmavyavasthānam asurāṇāṃ praṇāśanam ।। manuṣyavadhyāste sarve brahmeti vyāharatprabhuḥ ।। yajñaṃ vai vartayāmāsur devā vaivasvate antare ।। yugākhyāyāṃ caturthyāṃ tu āpanneṣu sureṣu vai ।।
dvitīye narasiṃhākhye rudro hy āsītpurohitaḥ ।। tṛtīye vāmanasyārthe dharmeṇa tu purodhasā ।। mānuṣāḥ sapta yānyāstu śāpajāstā nibodhata ।। naṣṭe dharme caturthāṃśe mārkaṇḍeyapuraḥsaraḥ ।।
māndhātā cakravartī tu tadottaṅkapuraḥsare ।। jāmadagnyastathā ṣaṣṭho viśvāmitrapuraḥsaraḥ ।। saptamo rāvaṇasyārthe jajñe daśarathātmajaḥ ।। vedavyāsastathā jajñe jātūkarṇyapuraḥsaraḥ ।।
devasundararūpeṇa dvaipāyanapuraḥsaraḥ ।। kalkī tu viṣṇuyaśasaḥ pārāśaryapuraḥsaraḥ ।। sarvāṃśca bhūtāṃs timitān pāṣaṇḍāṃścaiva sarvaśaḥ ।। pragṛhītāyudhair viprair vṛtaḥ śatasahasraśaḥ ।।
brahmadviṣaḥ sapatnāṃstu saṃhṛtyaiva ca tadvapuḥ ।। śūdrān saṃśodhayitvā tu samudrāntaṃ ca vai svayam ।। utsādayitvā vṛṣalān prāyaśastānadhārmikān ।। prajāstaṃ sādhayitvā tu samṛddhāstena vai svayam ।।
kṣapayitvā tu te anyonyaṃ bhāvinārthena coditāḥ ।। nṛpeṣvatha pranaṣṭeṣu prajānāṃ saṃgrahāttadā ।। parasparaṃ ca hatvā tu nirākrandāḥ suduḥkhitāḥ ।। pranaṣṭāśramadharmāśca naṣṭavarṇāśramāstathā ।।
pramadāḥ keśaśūlāśca bhaviṣyanti yugakṣaye ।। saritparvatavāsinyo mūlapattraphalāśanāḥ ।। utpātaduḥkhāḥ svalpārthā bahubādhāśca tāḥ prajāḥ ।। tataḥ kṣayaṃ gamiṣyanti sārdhaṃ kaliyugena tu ।।
ityetatkīrtitaṃ samyag devāsuraviceṣṭitam ।। turvasostu pravakṣyāmi pūror druhyostathā hy anoḥ ।। gobhānostu suto vīras trisāriraparājitaḥ ।। duṣyantaḥ pauravasyāpi tasya putro hy akalmaṣaḥ ।।
turvasoḥ pauravaṃ vaṃśaṃ praviveśa purā kila ।। varūthāttu tathāṇḍīraḥ saṃdhānastasya cātmajaḥ ।। teṣāṃ janapadāḥ sphītāḥ pāṇḍyāścolāḥ sakeralāḥ ।। setuputraḥ śaradvāṃstu gandhārastasya cātmajaḥ ।।
āraṭṭadeśajāstasya turagā vājināṃ varāḥ ।। ghṛtācca viduṣo jajñe pracetāstasya cātmajaḥ ।। mleccharāṣṭrādhipāḥ sarve udīcīṃ diśam āśritāḥ ।। sabhānaraścākṣuṣaśca parameṣus tathaiva ca ।।
kolāhalasya dharmātmā saṃjayo nāma viśrutaḥ ।। janamejayo mahārāja puraṃjayasuto abhavat ।। āsīd indrasamo rājā pratiṣṭhitayaśābhavat ।। saptadvīpeśvaro jajñe cakravartī mahāmanāḥ ।।
uśīnaraṃ ca dharmajñaṃ titikṣuṃ caiva tāv ubhau ।। bhṛśā kṛśā navā darśā yā ca devī dṛṣadvatī ।। tapasā te tu mahatā jātā vṛddhasya dhārmikāḥ ।। dṛṣadvatyāḥ sutaścāpi śibir auśīnaro nṛpaḥ ।।
pṛthudarbhaḥ suvīraśca kekayo bhadrakastathā ।। sauvīrāścaiva paurāśca nṛgasya kekayāstathā ।। navasya navarāṣṭraṃ tu titikṣostu prajāṃ śṛṇu ।। bṛhadrathaḥ sutastasya tasya seno abhavatsutaḥ ।।
jāto mānuṣayonyāṃ tu kṣīṇe vaṃśe prajecchayā ।। putrānutpādayāmāsa kṣetrajānpañca pārthivān ।। bāleyā brāhmaṇāścaiva tasya vaṃśakarāḥ prabho ।। mahāyogitvamāyuśca kalpasya parimāṇakam ।।
traikālyadarśanaṃ caiva prādhānyaṃ prasave tathā ।। caturo niyatānvarṇān sa vai sthāpayitā prabhuḥ ।। puṇḍrāḥ kaliṅgāśca tathā aṅgasya tu nibodhata ।। kiṃnāmnī mahiṣī tasya janitā katama ṛṣiḥ ।।
māhātmyaṃ ca prabhāvaṃ ca nikhilena vadasva tat ।। patnī vai mamatā nāma babhūvāsya mahātmanaḥ ।। bṛhaspatirmahātejā mamatāmetya kāmataḥ ।। antarvatnyasmi te bhrātur jyeṣṭhasya tu viramyatām ।।
auśijo bhrātṛjanyaste sopāṅgaṃ vedamudgiran ।। asminn evaṃ gate kāle yathā vā manyase prabho ।। kāmātmā sa mahātmāpi na manaḥ so abhyavārayat ।। utsṛjantaṃ tu tadretovācaṃ garbho abhyabhāṣata ।।
amogharetāstvaṃ cāpi pūrvaṃ cāhamihāgataḥ ।। putraṃ jyeṣṭhasya vai bhrātur garbhasthaṃ bhagavānṛṣiḥ ।। māmevamuktavāṃstasmāt tamo dīrghaṃ pravekṣyasi ।। ato aṃśajo bṛhatkīrtir bṛhaspatirivaujasā ।।
sa dharmānsaurabheyāṃstu vṛṣabhācchrutavāṃstataḥ ।। tasminnivasatastasya yadṛcchātastu vai vṛṣaḥ ।। jagrāha taṃ dīrghatamāḥ śṛṅgayostu catuṣpadam ।। tato abravīdvṛṣastaṃ vai muñca māṃ balināṃ vara ।।
muñca tāteti ca punaḥ prītaste ahaṃ varaṃ vṛṇu ।। eṣa tvāṃ na vimokṣyāmi parasvādaṃ catuṣpadam ।। bhakṣyābhakṣyaṃ tathā caiva peyāpeyaṃ tathaiva ca ।। kāryākārye na vāgamyāgamanaṃ ca tathaiva ca ।।
śaktyānnapānadānāttu gopatiṃ saṃprasādayat ।। manasaiva samādadhyau tanniṣṭhastatparo hi saḥ ।। kṛtāvalepāṃ tāṃ matvā so anaḍvāniva na kṣamaḥ ।। nirbhartsya cainaṃ ruddhvā ca bāhubhyāṃ sampragṛhya ca ।।
viparyayaṃ tu tvaṃ labdhvā anaḍvāniva vartase ।। durvṛttaṃ tvāṃ tyajāmyadya gaccha tvaṃ svena karmaṇā ।। yasmāttvamandho vṛddhaśca bhartavyo duradhiṣṭhitaḥ ।। jagrāha taṃ sa dharmātmā balir vairocanistadā ।।
prītaścaiva vareṇaiva cchandayāmāsa vai balim ।। putrāndharmārthatattvajñān utpādayitumarhasi ।। andhaṃ vṛddhaṃ ca taṃ jñātvā na sā devī jagāma ha ।। tasyāṃ kakṣīvadādīṃśca śūdrayonāv ṛṣir vaśī ।।
uvāca taṃ balī rājā dṛṣṭvā kakṣīvadādikān ।। vidvān pratyakṣadharmāṇāṃ buddhimān vṛttimāñchucīn ।। natyuvāca munistaṃ vai mamaivamiti cābravīt ।। prāhiṇod avamānānme śūdrāṃ dhātreyikāṃ nṛpa ।।
baliḥ sudeṣṇāṃ tāṃ bhāryāṃ bhartsayāmāsa dānavaḥ ।। tāṃ sa dīrghatamā devīṃ tathā kṛtavatīṃ tadā ।। tatastvaṃ prāpsyase devi putrānvai manasepsitān ।। tasya sāpānam āsādya devī pariharattadā ।।
vināpānaṃ kumāraṃ tu janayiṣyasi pūrvajam ।। toṣitaśca yathāśakti prasādaṃ kuru me prabho ।। naiva dāsyati putraste pautrau vai dāsyate phalam ।। tasmād dīrghatamāṅgeṣu kukṣau spṛṣṭvedam abravīt ।।
tena tiṣṭhanti te garbhe paurṇamāsyām ivoḍurāṭ ।। tejasvinaḥ suvṛttāśca yajvāno dhārmikāśca te ।। aṅgastathā kaliṅgaśca puṇḍraḥ suhmastathaiva ca ।। ityete dīrghatamasā balerdattāḥ sutāstathā ।।
tato mānuṣayonyāṃ sa janayāmāsa vai prajāḥ ।। vicārya yasmādgodharmaṃ pramāṇaṃ te kṛtaṃ vibho ।। tasmāttubhyaṃ tamo dīrgham āghrāyāpanudāmi vai ।। jarāṃ mṛtyuṃ tamaścaiva āghrāyāpanudāmi te ।।
āyuṣmāṃśca vapuṣmāṃśca cakṣuṣmāṃśca tato abhavat ।। kākṣīvāṃstu tato gatvā saha pitrā girivrajam ।। tataḥ kālena mahatā tapasā bhāvitastu saḥ ।। tato abravītpitā taṃ vai putravānasmyahaṃ tvayā ।।
muktvātmānaṃ tato asau vai prāptavānbrahmaṇaḥ kṣayam ।। kauṣmāṇḍā gautamāścaiva smṛtāḥ kākṣīvataḥ sutāḥ ।। samāgamo vaḥ kathitaḥ saṃtatiścobhayostathā ।। kṛtārthaḥ so api dharmātmā yogamāyāvṛtaḥ svayam ।।
tatrāṅgasya tu dāyādo rājāsīddadhivāhanaḥ ।। āsīd divirathāpatyaṃ vidvāndharmaratho nṛpaḥ ।। somaḥ śukreṇa vai rājñā saha pīto mahātmanā ।। tasya satyarathaḥ putras tasmāddaśarathaḥ kila ।।
atha dāśarathir vīraś caturaṅgo mahāyaśāḥ ।। caturaṅgasya putrastu pṛthulākṣa iti smṛtaḥ ।। campasya tu purī campā pūrvaṃ yā mālinī bhavat ।। yajñe vibhāṇḍakāccāsya vāraṇaḥ śatruvāraṇaḥ ।।
haryaṅgasya tu dāyādo jāto bhadrarathaḥ kila ।। bṛhadbhānuḥ sutastasya tasmājjajñe mahātmavān ।। nāmnā jayadrathaṃ nāma tasmādbṛhadratho nṛpaḥ ।। dāyādastasya cāṅgo vai tasmātkarṇo abhavannṛpaḥ ।।
vistareṇānupūrvyācca pūrostu śṛṇuta dvijāḥ ।। etad icchāmahe śrotum atyantakuśalo hy asi ।। yaśodevī ca satyā ca tayorvaṃśaṃ ca me śṛṇu ।। sā bṛhanmanasaḥ satyā vijayaṃ nāma viśrutam ।।
bṛhadrathasya putrastu satyakarmā mahāmanāḥ ।। taccedaṃ sarvamākhyātaṃ karṇaṃ prati yathoditam ।। prācītvataḥ sutastasya yaḥ prācīmakaroddiśam ।। rājā pītāyudho nāma manasyorabhavatsutaḥ ।।
dhundhorbahuvidhaḥ putraḥ sampātistasya cātmajaḥ ।। bhadrāśvasya dhṛtāyāṃ tu daśāpsarasi sūnavaḥ ।। dhṛteyuśca vineyuśca sthaleyuścaiva sattamaḥ ।। auceyorjvalanā nāma bhāryā vai takṣakātmajā ।।
antināro manasvinyāṃ putrāñjajñe parāñchubhān ।। gaurī kanyā tṛtīyā ca māndhāturjananī śubhā ।। brahmavādaparākrāntāñ chubhadā tv ilinā hy abhūt ।। ṛṣyantamatha duṣyantaṃ pravīram anadhaṃ tathā ।।
śakuntalāyāṃ bharato yasya nāmnā ca bhāratāḥ ।। mātā bhastrā pituḥ putro yena jātaḥ sa eva saḥ ।। tvaṃ cāsya dhātā garbhasya satyamāha śakuntalā ।। putrāṇāṃ mātṛkāt kopāt sumahānsaṃkṣayaḥ kṛtaḥ ।।
saṃkrāmito bharadvājo marudbhirbharatasya tu ।। saṃkrāmito mahātejās tanno brūhi yathātatham ।। bhrāturbhāryāṃ sa dṛṣṭvā tu bṛhaspatiruvāca ha ।। evamuktābravīdenaṃ svayameva bṛhaspatim ।।
amogharetāstvaṃ cāpi dharmaṃ caivaṃ vigarhitam ।। nopadeṣṭavyo vinayas tvayā me varavarṇini ।। tato bṛhaspatiṃ garbho dharṣamāṇamuvāca ha ।। amogharetāśca bhavān nāvakāśa iha dvayoḥ ।।
abhiṣedhasi tasmāttvaṃ tamo dīrghaṃ pravekṣyasi ।। tadretastvapatadbhūmau nivṛttaṃ śiśuko abhavat ।। gamiṣyāmi gṛhaṃ svaṃ vai bharasvainaṃ bṛhaspate ।। jagṛhustaṃ bharadvājaṃ marutaḥ kṛpayā sthitāḥ ।।
putranaimittikairyajñair ayajatputralipsayā ।। tataḥ kratuṃ marutsomaṃ putrārthe samupāharat ।। upaninyurbharadvājaṃ putrārthaṃ bharatāya vai ।। saṃkrāmito bharadvājo marudbhirbharataṃ prati ।।
ādāv ātmahitāya tvaṃ kṛtārtho ahaṃ tvayā vibho ।। tatastu vitatho nāma bharadvājo nṛpo abhavat ।। dvyāmuṣyāyaṇakaulīnāḥ smṛtāste dvividhena ca ।। bharadvājo divaṃ yāto hy abhiṣicya sutamṛṣiḥ ।।
mahābhūtopamāḥ putrāś catvāro bhuvamanyavaḥ ।। narasya saṃkṛtiḥ putras tasya putro mahāyaśāḥ ।। gargasya caiva dāyādaḥ śibirvidvānajāyata ।। āhāryatanayaścaiva dhīmānāsīd urukṣavaḥ ।।
tryuṣaṇaṃ puṣkariṃ caiva kaviṃ caiva mahāyaśāḥ ।। kāvyānāṃ tu varā hy ete trayaḥ proktā maharṣayaḥ ।। saṃbhṛtāṅgiraso dakṣā bṛhatkṣatrasya ca kṣitiḥ ।। tenedaṃ nirmitaṃ pūrvaṃ puraṃ tu gajasāhvayam ।।
ajamīḍho dvimīḍhaśca purumīḍhastathaiva ca ।। nīlinī dhūminī caiva keśinī caiva viśrutā ।। tapaso ante mahātejā jātā vṛddhasya dhārmikāḥ ।। ājamīḍhasya keśinyāṃ kaṇvaḥ samabhavatkila ।।
ajamīḍhasya bhūminyāṃ jajñe bṛhadanur nṛpaḥ ।। bṛhanmanaḥsutaścāpi bṛhaddhanuriti śrutaḥ ।। aśvajittanayastasya senajit tasya cātmajaḥ ।। rucirāśvaśca kāvyaśca rājā dṛḍharathastathā ।।
rucirāśvasya dāyādaḥ pṛthuseno mahāyaśāḥ ।। nīpasyaikaśataṃ tv āsīt putrāṇām amitaujasām ।। teṣāṃ vaṃśakaraḥ śrīmān nīpānāṃ kīrtivardhanaḥ ।। samarasya pārasampārau sadaśva iti te trayaḥ ।।
pāraputraḥ pṛthurjātaḥ pṛthostu sukṛto abhavat ।। vibhrājasya tu dāyādas tv aṇuho nāma vīryavān ।। aṇuhasya tu dāyādo brahmadatto mahīpatiḥ ।। vibhrājaḥ punar ājātaḥ sukṛteneha karmaṇā ।।
ugrāyudhena tasyārthe sarve nīpāḥ praṇāśitāḥ ।। kimarthaṃ tena te nīpāḥ sarve caiva praṇāśitāḥ ।। sthāṇubhūto aṣṭasāhasraṃ taṃ bheje janamejayaḥ ।। uvāca sāntvaṃ vividhaṃ jaghnuste vai hy ubhāv api ।।
śaraṇāgatarakṣārthaṃ tasmādevaṃ śapāmi vaḥ ।। tatastān kṛpyamāṇāṃstu yamena purataḥ sa tu ।। gatānetānimānvīrāṃs tvaṃ me rakṣitumarhasi ।। tathetyuktastato rājā yamena yuyudhe ciram ।।
vijitya munaye prādāt tadadbhutamivābhavat ।। sarve yathocitaṃ kṛtvā jagmuste kṛṣṇamavyayam ।। iha loke pare caiva sukhamakṣayyamaśnute ।। atha satyadhṛteḥ putro dṛḍhanemiḥ pratāpavān ।।
āsītsudharmatanayaḥ sārvabhaumaḥ pratāpavān ।। tasyānvavāye mahati mahāpauravanandanaḥ ।। atha rukmarathasyāsīt supārśvo nāma pārthivaḥ ।। sumaterapi dharmātmā rājā saṃnatimānapi ।।
hiraṇyanābhinaḥ śiṣyaḥ kauśalyasya mahātmanaḥ ।। smṛtāste prācyasāmānaḥ kārtā nāmeha sāmagāḥ ।। babhūva yena vikramya pṛthukasya pitā hataḥ ।। ugrāyudhasya dāyādaḥ kṣemo nāma mahāyaśāḥ ।।
nṛpaṃjayācca viratha ityete pauravāḥ stutāḥ ।। nīlasya tapasogreṇa suśāntirudapadyata ।। bhadrāśvaḥ pṛthudāyādo bhadrāśvatanayāñchṛṇu ।। javīnaraśca vikrāntaḥ kapilaścaiva pañcamaḥ ।।
pañcālarakṣiṇo hy ete deśānāmiti naḥ śrutam ।। ete hy aṅgirasaḥ pakṣaṃ saṃśritāḥ kāṇvamudgalāḥ ।। indrasenaḥ sutastasya vindhyāśvastasya cātmajaḥ ।। divodāsaśca rājarṣir ahalyā ca yaśasvinī ।।
śatānandamṛṣiśreṣṭhaṃ tasyāpi sumahātapāḥ ।। āsītsatyadhṛteḥ śukram amoghaṃ dhārmikasya tu ।। mithunaṃ tatra saṃbhṛtaṃ tasminsarasi saṃbhṛtam ।। dṛṣṭvā jagrāha kṛpayā śaṃtanurmṛgayāṃ gataḥ ।।
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi divodāsasya vai prajāḥ ।। maitrāyaṇāvaraḥ so atha maitreyastu tataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। rājā caidyavaro nāma maitreyasya sutaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। ajamīḍhaḥ punarjātaḥ kṣīṇe vaṃśe tu somakaḥ ।।
putrāṇāmajamīḍhasya somakasya mahātmanaḥ ।। putrābhāve tapastepe śataṃ varṣāṇi duścaram ।। agnihotrakrameṇaiva sā suṣvāpa mahāvratā ।। ṛkṣaṃ sā janayāmāsa dhūmavarṇaṃ śatāgrajam ।।
yaḥ prayāgamatikramya kurukṣetramakalpayat ।। kṛṣyamāṇastataḥ śakro bhayāttasmai varaṃ dadau ।। tasyānvavāyaḥ sumahān yasya nāmnā tu kauravāḥ ।। parīkṣicca mahātejāḥ prajanaścārimardanaḥ ।।
cyavanastasya putrastu rājā dharmārthatattvavit ।। kṛmeḥ putro mahāvīryaḥ khyātastvindrasamo vibhuḥ ।। caidyoparicarājjajñe girikā sapta vai sutān ।। pratyaśravāḥ kuśaścaiva caturtho harivāhanaḥ ।।
bṛhadrathasya dāyādaḥ kuśāgro nāma viśrutaḥ ।। vṛṣabhasya tu dāyādaḥ puṇyavānnāma pārthivaḥ ।। dāyādastasya dhanuṣas tasmātsarvaśca jajñivān ।। dve tasya śakale jāte jarayā saṃdhitaś ca saḥ ।।
jetā sarvasya kṣatrasya jarāsaṃdho mahābalaḥ ।। sahadevātmajaḥ śrīmān somavit sa mahātapāḥ ।। jahnustvajanayatputraṃ surathaṃ nāma bhūmipam ।। vidūrathasutaścāpi sārvabhauma iti smṛtaḥ ।।
rucirāttu tato bhaumas tvaritāyustato abhavat ।। devātithestu dāyādo dakṣa eva babhūva ha ।। dilīpasya pratīpastu tasya putrās trayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। devāpistu hy apadhyātaḥ prajābhirabhavanmuniḥ ।।
ko doṣo rājaputrasya prajābhiḥ samudāhṛtaḥ ।। bhaviṣyaṃ kīrtayiṣyāmi śaṃtanostu nibodhata ।। idaṃ codāharantyatra ślokaṃ prati mahābhiṣak ।। punaryuvā ca bhavati tasmāttaṃ śaṃtanuṃ viduḥ ।।
tato avṛṇuta bhāryārthaṃ śaṃtanurjāhnavīṃ nṛpa ।। kālī vicitravīryaṃ tu dāśeyī janayatsutam ।। kṛṣṇadvaipāyano nāma kṣetre vaicitraviryake ।। dhṛtarāṣṭrastu gāndhāryāṃ putrānajanayacchatam ।।
mādrī kuntī tathā caiva pāṇḍorbhārye babhūvatuḥ ।। dharmādyudhiṣṭhiro jajñe mārutācca vṛkodaraḥ ।। nakulaṃ sahadevaṃ ca mādryaśvibhyāmajījanat ।। draupadyajanayacchreṣṭhaṃ prativindhyaṃ yudhiṣṭhirāt ।।
caturthaṃ śrutakarmāṇaṃ sahadevād ajāyata ।। tebhyo apare pāṇḍaveyāḥ ṣaḍevānye mahārathāḥ ।। kāśī baladharādbhīmāj jajñe vai sarvagaṃ sutam ।। kareṇumatyāṃ caidyāyāṃ niramitrastu nākuliḥ ।।
yaudheyaṃ devakī caiva putraṃ jajñe yudhiṣṭhirāt ।। janamejayaḥ parīkṣitaḥ putraḥ paramadhārmikaḥ ।। sa vaiśampāyanenaiva śaptaḥ kila maharṣiṇā ।। yāvatsthāsyasi tvaṃ loke tāvadeva prapatsyati ।।
abhigamya sthitāścaiva nṛpaṃ ca janamejayam ।। utsannā yājino yajñe tataḥprabhṛti sarvaśaḥ ।। sa vaiśampāyanenaiva praviśanvāritastataḥ ।। dvir aśvamedhamāhṛtya mahāvājasaneyakaḥ ।।
vivāde brāhmaṇaiḥ sārdham abhiśapto vanaṃ yayau ।। janamejayaḥ śatānīkaṃ putraṃ rājye abhiṣiktavān ।। jajñe adhisomakṛṣṇākhyaḥ sāmprataṃ yo mahāyaśāḥ ।। varṣadvayaṃ kurukṣetre dṛṣadvatyāṃ dvijottamāḥ ।।
purā kila yadetadvai vyatītaṃ kīrtitaṃ tvayā ।। teṣām āyuṣpramāṇaṃ ca nāmataścaiva tānnṛpān ।। kaliyugapramāṇaṃ ca yugadoṣaṃ yugakṣayam ।। etatsarvaṃ prasaṃkhyāya pṛcchatāṃ brūhi naḥ prabho ।।
bhāvyaṃ kaliyugaṃ caiva tathā manvantarāṇi ca ।। ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi bhaviṣyā ye nṛpāstathā ।। tānsarvānkīrtayiṣyāmi bhaviṣye kathitānnṛpān ।। kṣatrāḥ pāraśavāḥ śūdrās tathānye ye bahiścarāḥ ।।
paryāyataḥ pravakṣyāmi nāmataścaiva tānnṛpān ।। tasyānvavāye vakṣyāmi bhaviṣye kathitānnṛpān ।। gaṅgayā tu hṛte tasmin nagare nāgasāhvaye ।। bhaviṣyāṣṭau sutāstasya mahābalaparākramāḥ ।।
śucidravaścitrarathād vṛṣṇimāṃśca śucidravāt ।। tasmātsuṣeṇādbhavitā sunītho nāma pārthivaḥ ।। nṛcakṣuṣastu dāyādo bhavitā vai sukhīvalaḥ ।। pariṣṇavasutaścāpi bhavitā sutapā nṛpaḥ ।।
medhāvinaḥ sutaścāpi bhaviṣyati puraṃjayaḥ ।। tigmādbṛhadratho bhāvyo vasudāmā bṛhadrathāt ।। bhaviṣyate codayanād vīge rājā vahīnaraḥ ।। daṇḍapāṇerniramitro niramitrāttu kṣemakaḥ ।।
kṣemakaṃ prāpya rājānaṃ saṃsthāsyati kalau yuge ।। dhīmataḥ pāṇḍuputrasya cārjunasya mahātmanaḥ ।। tānidānīṃ samācakṣva tadvaṃśaṃ cānupūrvaśaḥ ।। brahmaṇo mānasaḥ putras tasmātsvāhā vyajījanat ।।
nirmathyaḥ pavamāno agnir vaidyutaḥ pāvakātmajaḥ ।। pavamānātmajo hy agnir havyavāhaḥ sa ucyate ।। devānāṃ havyavāho agniḥ prathamo brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ ।। eteṣāṃ putrapautrāśca catvāriṃśattathaiva ca ।।
pāvano laukiko hy agniḥ prathamo brahmaṇaśca yaḥ ।। vaiśvānaro havyavāho vahanhavyaṃ mamāra saḥ ।। yo atharvā laukiko hy agnir dakṣiṇāgniḥ sa ucyate ।। tasya hy alaukiko hy agnir dakṣiṇāgniḥ sa vai smṛtaḥ ।।
sa ca vai gārhapatyo agniḥ prathamo brahmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। yaḥ khalvāhavanīyo agnir abhimānī dvijaiḥ smṛtaḥ ।। godāvarīṃ vitastāṃ ca candrabhāgāmirāvatīm ।। sītāṃ manasvinīṃ caiva hrādinīṃ pāvanāṃ tathā ।।
tadā tu viharaṃstāsu dhiṣṇyecchaḥ sa babhūva ha ।। dhiṣṇyeṣu jajñire yasmāt tataste dhiṣṇavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। vibhuḥ pravāhaṇo agnīdhras tatrasthā dhiṣṇavo apare ।। anirdeśyānivāryāṇām agnīnāṃ śṛṇuta kramam ।।
samrāḍagnisuto hyaṣṭāv upatiṣṭhanti tāndvijāḥ ।। pāvakoṣṇaḥ samūhyastu vottare so agnirucyate ।। śatadhāmā sudhājyotī raudraiśvaryaḥ sa ucyate ।। ajaikapādupastheyaḥ sa vai śālāmukho yataḥ ।।
putrā hyete tu sarvasya upastheyā dvijaiḥ smṛtāḥ ।। hautriyasya suto hyagnir barhiṣo havyavāhanaḥ ।। suto hyagner viśvavedā brāhmaṇācchaṃsirucyate ।। dhiṣṇya āharaṇā hyete somenejyanta vai dvijaiḥ ।।
agniḥ so avabhṛtho jñeyo varuṇena sahejyate ।। manyumāñjaṭharaścāgnir viddhāgniḥ satataṃ smṛtaḥ ।। agnermanyumataḥ putro ghoraḥ saṃvartakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। samudravāsinaḥ putraḥ saharakṣo vibhāvyate ।।
kravyādagniḥ sutastasya puruṣānyo atti vai mṛtān ।। tataḥ sutāstu sauvīryād gandharvairasurair hṛtāḥ ।। āyur nāmnā tu bhagavān paśau yastu praṇīyate ।। pākayajñeṣv abhīmānī hutaṃ havyaṃ bhunakti yaḥ ।।
putro asya sahito hyagnir adbhutaḥ sa mahāyaśāḥ ।। adbhutasya suto vīro devāṃśastu mahānsmṛtaḥ ।। vividhāgnisutādarkād agnayo aṣṭau sutāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। surabhirvasumānnādo haryaśvaścaiva rukmavān ।।
śucyagnestu prajā hyeṣā agnayaśca caturdaśa ।। samatīte tu sarge ye yāmaiḥ saha surottamaiḥ ।। ete viharaṇīyeṣu cetanācetaneṣviha ।। kāmyanaimittikādyāste ye te karmasvavasthitāḥ ।।
ete devagaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ prathamasyāntare manoḥ ।। svārociṣādiṣu jñeyāḥ savarṇānteṣu saptasu ।। manvantareṣu sarveṣu lakṣaṇaṃ jātavedasām ।। vartante vartamānaiśca yāmairdevaiḥ sahāgnayaḥ ।।
vistareṇānupūrvyā ca kimanyacchrotumicchatha ।। tadidānīṃ samācakṣva dharmādharmasya vistaram ।। vistāramādisargasya pratisargasya cākhilam ।। karmayogaṃ ca sāṃkhyaṃ ca yathāvadvistarānvitam ।।
yasmādaviditaṃ loke na kiṃcittava suvrata ।। jñānayogasahasrāddhi karmayogaḥ praśasyate ।। karmajñānodbhavaṃ brahma na ca jñānamakarmaṇaḥ ।। vedo akhilo dharmamūlam ācāraścaiva tadvidām ।।
dayā sarveṣu bhūteṣu kṣāntī rakṣāturasya tu ।। anāyāseṣu kāryeṣu māṅgalyācārasevanam ।। tathāspṛhā paradravye parastrīṣu ca sarvadā ।। ayameva kriyāyogo jñānayogasya sādhakaḥ ।।
śrutismṛtyuditaṃ dharmam upatiṣṭhetprayatnataḥ ।। kuryādaharaharyajñair bhūtarṣigaṇatarpaṇam ।। pitṝñchrāddhair annadānair bhūtāni balikarmabhiḥ ।। kaṇḍanī peṣaṇī cullī jalakumbhī pramārjanī ।।
tatpāpanāśanāyāmī pañca yajñāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। tadyukto api na mokṣāya yastvātmaguṇavarjitaḥ ।। gobrāhmaṇānāṃ vittena sarvadā bhadramācaret ।। pūjayedbrahmaviṣṇvarkarudravasvātmakaṃ śivam ।।
vāsudevo jaganmūrtis tasya sambhūtayo hy amī ।। lokapālādhipāścaiva pitaro mātarastathā ।। brahmādyāś caturo mūlam avyaktādhipatiḥ smṛtaḥ ।। abhedātpūjitena syāt pūjitaṃ sacarācaram ।।
vedamūrtāv ataḥ pūṣā pūjanīyaḥ prayatnataḥ ।। dānairvratopavāsaiśca japahomādinā naraḥ ।। vikarmabhītasya sadā na kiṃcit prāptavyamastīha pare ca loke ।। dānadharmamaśeṣaṃ tu yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ।।
yaduktavānsa viśvātmā manave tannibodhata ।। anantaraṃ ca vaktrebhyo vedāstasya vinirgatāḥ ।। trivargasādhanaṃ puṇyaṃ śatakoṭipravistaram ।। aṅgāni caturo vedān purāṇaṃ nyāyavistaram ।।
matsyarūpeṇa ca punaḥ kalpādāvudakārṇave ।। śrutvā jagāda ca munīn prati devāṃścaturmukhaḥ ।। kālenāgrahaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā purāṇasya tato nṛpa ।। caturlakṣapramāṇena dvāpare dvāpare sadā ।।
adyāpi devaloke asmiñ chatakoṭipravistaram ।। purāṇāni daśāṣṭau ca sāmprataṃ tadihocyate ।। brahmaṇābhihitaṃ pūrvaṃ yāvanmātraṃ marīcaye ।। vaiśākhapūrṇimāyāṃ ca brahmaloke mahīyate ।।
pādmaṃ tatpañcapañcāśatsahasrāṇīha kathyate ।। jyeṣṭhe māsi tilairyuktam aśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet ।। yatprāha dharmānakhilāṃs tadyuktaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ viduḥ ।। trayoviṃśatisāhasraṃ tatpramāṇaṃ vidurbudhāḥ ।।
caturviṃśasahasrāṇi purāṇaṃ tadihocyate ।। śivaloke sa pūtātmā kalpamekaṃ vasennaraḥ ।। vṛtrāsuravadhopetaṃ tadbhāgavatamucyate ।। tadvṛttāntodbhavaṃ loke tadbhāgavatamucyate ।।
aṣṭādaśa sahasrāṇi purāṇaṃ tatpracakṣate ।। pañcaviṃśatsahasrāṇi nāradīyaṃ taducyate ।। paramāṃ siddhimāpnoti punarāvṛttidurlabhām ।। vyākhyātā vai munipraśne munibhirdharmacāribhiḥ ।।
purāṇaṃ navasāhasraṃ mārkaṇḍeyam ihocyate ।। kārttikyāṃ puṇḍarīkasya yajñasya phalabhāgbhavet ।। vasiṣṭhāyāgninā proktam āgneyaṃ tatpracakṣate ।। mārgaśīrṣyāṃ vidhānena tiladhenusamanvitam ।।
yaḥ pradadhannaraḥ so atha svargaloke mahīyate ।। manave kathayāmāsa bhūtagrāmasya lakṣaṇam ।। bhaviṣyacaritaprāyaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ tadihocyate ।। guḍakumbhasamāyuktam agniṣṭomaphalaṃ bhavet ।।
sāvarṇinā nāradāya kṛṣṇamāhātmyamuttamam ।। tadaṣṭādaśasāhasraṃ brahmavaivartamucyate ।। paurṇamāsyāṃ śubhadine brahmaloke mahīyate ।। dharmārthakāmamokṣārtham āgneyamadhikṛtya ca ।।
tiladhenusamāyuktaṃ sa yāti śivasāmyatām ।। viṣṇunābhihitaṃ kṣoṇyai tadvārāham ihocyate ।। caturviṃśatsahasrāṇi tatpurāṇamihocyate ।। varāhasya prasādena padamāpnoti vaiṣṇavam ।।
kalpe tatpuruṣaṃ vṛttaṃ caritairupabṛṃhitam ।। sahasrāṇi śataṃ caikam iti martyeṣu gadyate ।। śaivaṃ padamavāpnoti mīne copāgate ravau ।। trivargamabhyadhāttacca vāmanaṃ parikīrtitam ।।
yaḥ śaradviṣuve dadyād vaiṣṇavaṃ yātyasau padam ।। māhātmyaṃ kathayāmāsa kūrmarūpī janārdanaḥ ।। aṣṭādaśa sahasrāṇi lakṣmīkalpānuṣaṅgikam ।। gosahasrapradānasya phalaṃ samprāpnuyānnaraḥ ।।
matsyarūpeṇa manave narasiṃhopavarṇanam ।। tanmātsyamiti jānīdhvaṃ sahasrāṇi caturdaśa ।। yo dadyātpṛthivī tena dattā bhavati cākhilā ।। adhikṛtyābravītkṛṣṇo gāruḍaṃ tadihocyate ।।
sa siddhiṃ labhate mukhyāṃ śivaloke ca saṃsthitim ।। tacca dvādaśasāhasraṃ brahmāṇḍaṃ dviśatādhikam ।। tadbrahmāṇḍapurāṇaṃ ca brahmaṇā samudāhṛtam ।। hemadhenvā yutaṃ tacca brahmalokaphalapradam ।।
matpiturmama pitrā ca mayā tubhyaṃ niveditam ।। idamadyāpi deveṣu śatakoṭipravistaram ।। taccāṣṭādaśasāhasraṃ nārasiṃhamihocyate ।। nandīpurāṇaṃ tallokair ākhyātamiti kīrtyate ।।
procyate tatpunarloke sāmbametanmunivratāḥ ।। evamādityasaṃjñā ca tatraiva parigadyate ।। vijānīdhvaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhās tadetebhyo vinirgatam ।। vaṃśyānucaritaṃ caiva purāṇaṃ pañcalakṣaṇam ।।
sasaṃhārapradānāṃ ca purāṇe pañcavarṇake ।। sarveṣvapi purāṇeṣu tadviruddhaṃ ca yatphalam ।। rājaseṣu ca māhātmyam adhikaṃ brahmaṇo viduḥ ।। saṃkīrṇeṣu sarasvatyāḥ pitṝṇāṃ ca nigadyate ।।
lakṣeṇaikena yatproktaṃ vedārthaparibṛṃhitam ।। brahmaṇābhihitaṃ yacca śatakoṭipravistaram ।। evaṃ sapādāḥ pañcaite lakṣā martye prakīrtitāḥ ।। yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।।
idaṃ ca deveṣv amṛtāyitaṃ ca nityaṃ tvidaṃ pāpaharaṃ ca puṃsām ।। vratopavāsasaṃyuktān yathāmatsyoditāniha ।। yathāvṛttaṃ pravakṣyāmi dharmakāmārthasādhakam ।। vinayanamanaṅgārim anaṅgāṅgaharaṃ haram ।।
saṃyuktastava viṣṇorvā pumānbhaktaḥ kathaṃ bhavet ।। kramānmuktipradaṃ deva kiṃcidvratamihocyatām ।। śrutamapyatra yacchāntyai tadvrataṃ śṛṇu nārada ।। pādādi kuryādvidhivad viṣṇunāmānukīrtanam ।।
caitramāsaṃ samāsādya kṛtvā brāhmaṇavācanam ।। jaṅghe abhipūjye varadāya caiva dve jānunī vāśvikumāraṛkṣe ।। pūrvottarāphalguniyugmake ca meḍhraṃ namaḥ pañcaśarāya pūjyam ।। tathārcayedbhādrapadādvaye ca pārśve namaḥ keśiniṣūdanāya ।।
ṛkṣe anurādhāsu ca mādhavāya namastathoraḥsthalameva pūjyam ।। śrīśaṅkhacakrāsigadādharāya namo viśākhāsu bhujāśca pūjyāḥ ।। punarvasāvaṅgulipūrvabhāgāḥ sāmnāmadhīśāya namo abhipūjyāḥ ।। kūrmasya pādau śaraṇaṃ vrajāmi jyeṣṭhāsu kaṇṭhe harirarcanīyaḥ ।।
puṣye mukhaṃ dānavasūdanāya namo nṛsiṃhāya ca pūjanīyam ।। āsyaṃ harerbhārgavanandanāya saṃpūjanīyaṃ dvija vāruṇe tu ।। mṛgottamāṅge nayane abhipūjye namo astu te rāma vighūrṇitākṣa ।। śiro abhipūjyaṃ bharaṇīṣu viṣṇor namo astu viśveśvara kalkirūpiṇe ।।
upoṣitenarkṣadineṣu bhaktyā saṃpūjanīyā dvijapuṃgavāḥ syuḥ ।। haimīṃ viśālāyatabāhudaṇḍāṃ muktāphalendūpalavajrayuktām ।। śayyāṃ tathopaskarabhājanādiyuktāṃ pradadyāddvijapuṃgavāya ।। manorathānnaḥ saphalīkuruṣva hiraṇyagarbhācyutarudrarūpin ।।
śayyāṃ ca dadyānmantreṇa granthibhedavivarjitām ।। tathā surūpatārogyaṃ keśave bhaktimuttamām ।। śayyā mamāpyaśūnyāstu kṛṣṇa janmani janmani ।। nakṣatrapuruṣajñāya viprāyātha visarjayet ।।
bhojanaṃ ca yathāśakti vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ ।। sarvānkāmānavāpnoti viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।। ātmanā vātha pitṛbhis tatsarvaṃ kṣayamāpnuyāt ।। kalikaluṣavidāraṇaṃ murāreḥ sakalavibhūtiphalapradaṃ ca puṃsām ।।
anabhyāsena rogādvā kimiṣṭaṃ vratamuttamam ।। yasminvrate tadapyatra śrūyatāmakṣayaṃ mahat ।। yeṣu nakṣatrayogeṣu purāṇajñāḥ pracakṣate ।। sūryasya cātha saṃkrāntis tithiḥ sā sārvakāmikī ।।
sūryārcāṃ śivaliṅge ca prakurvan pūjayedyataḥ ।। yasmāttasmānmuniśreṣṭha gṛhe śambhuṃ samarcayet ।। svātīṣu jaṅghe puruṣottamāya dhātre viśākhāsu ca jānudeśam ।। jyeṣṭhāsvanaṅgāya namo astu guhyam indrāya somāya kaṭī ca mūle ।।
tīkṣṇāṃśave ca śravaṇe ca kukṣau pṛṣṭhaṃ dhaniṣṭhāsu vikartanāya ।। pūrvottarābhādrapadādvaye ca bāhū namaścaṇḍakarāya pūjyau ।। nakhāni pūjyāni tathāśvinīṣu namo astu saptāśvadhuraṃdharāya ।। grīvāgniṛkṣe adharamambujeśe sampūjayennārada rohiṇīṣu ।।
namaḥ savitre rasanāṃ śaṃkare ca nāsābhipūjyā ca punarvasau ca ।। sārpe atha mauliṃ vibudhapriyāya maghāsu karṇāviti gogaṇeśe ।। athottarāphalgunibhe bhruvau ca viśveśvarāyeti ca pūjanīye ।। gajāsurānaṅgapurāndhakādivināśamūlāya namaḥ śivāya ।।
bhoktavyamatraivamatailaśākam amāṃsamakṣāramabhuktaśeṣam ।। śāleyataṇḍulaprastham audumbaramaye ghṛtam ।। saptame vastrayugmaṃ ca pāraṇe tvadhikaṃ bhavet ।। brāhmaṇānbhojayedbhaktyā guḍakṣīraghṛtādibhiḥ ।।
śuddhamaṣṭāṅgulaṃ tacca padmarāgadalānvitam ।। sopadhānakaviśrāmasvāstaravyajanāni ca ।। bhūṣaṇairapi saṃyuktāṃ phalavastrānulepanaiḥ ।। kapilāṃ vastrasaṃyuktāṃ suśīlāṃ ca payasvinīm ।।
dadyānmantreṇa pūrvāhṇe na caināmabhilaṅghayet ।। kāntyā dhṛtyā śriyā ratyā tathā me santu siddhayaḥ ।। tathā mām uddharāśeṣaduḥkhasaṃsārasāgarāt ।। śayyāgavādi tatsarvaṃ dvijasya bhavanaṃ nayet ।।
prakāśanīyaṃ vratamindumauler yaścāpi nindāmadhikāṃ vidhatte ।। idaṃ mahāpātakabhin narāṇām apyakṣaraṃ vedavido vadanti ।। nābhyeti rogaṃ na ca śokaduḥkhaṃ yā vātha nārī kurute atibhaktyā ।। yatkīrtanenāpyakhilāni nāśam āyānti pāpāni na saṃśayo asti ।।
iti paṭhati śṛṇoti vā ya itthaṃ raviśayanaṃ puruhūtavallabhaḥ syāt । api narakagatānpitṝn aśeṣān api divamānayatīha yaḥ karoti ।। śāntirmuktiśca bhavati jayaḥ puṃsāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।। māghe maheśvaraṃ devaṃ mahādevaṃ ca phālgune ।।
jyeṣṭhe paśupatiṃ cārced āṣāḍhe ugramarcayet ।। haramāśvayuje māsi tatheśānaṃ ca kārttike ।। gobhūhiraṇyavāsobhiḥ śivabhaktānupoṣitaḥ ।। pañcagavyaṃ ca saṃprāśya śaṃkaraṃ pūjayenniśi ।।
palāśaṃ jambuvṛkṣaṃ ca viduḥ ṣaṣṭhaṃ maharṣayaḥ ।। ekaikaṃ dantapavanaṃ vṛkṣeṣveteṣu bhakṣayet ।। dadyātsamāpte dadhyannaṃ vitānadhvajacāmaram ।। aśaktastu punardadyād gāmekāmapi śaktitaḥ ।।
pumānsampūjito devaiḥ śivaloke mahīyate ।। muhurmuhurjanmani yena samyag vrataṃ samācakṣva tadindumaule ।। rahasyaṃ tava vakṣyāmi yatpurāṇavido viduḥ ।। tasminnārāyaṇasyārcām arcayad indunāmabhiḥ ।।
athavā brahmanakṣatraṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ prajāyate ।। āpyāyasveti tu japed vidvānaṣṭaśataṃ punaḥ ।। somāya varadāyātha viṣṇave ca namo namaḥ ।। pūjayetphalapuṣpaiśca somanāmāni kīrtayan ।।
ūrudvayaṃ cāpi jalodarāya sampūjayenmeḍhramanantabāhave ।। tathodaraṃ cāpyamṛtodarāya nābhiḥ śaśāṅkāya namo abhipūjyā ।। hāsyaṃ namaścandramase abhipūjyam oṣṭhau kumudvantavanapriyāya ।। netradvayaṃ padmanibhaṃ tathendor indīvaraśyāmakarāya śaureḥ ।।
lalāṭamindorudadhipriyāya keśāḥ suṣumnādhipateḥ prapūjyāḥ ।। padmapriye rohiṇi nāma lakṣmīḥ saubhāgyasaukhyāmṛtacārukāye ।। suptvātha bhūmau punarutthitena snātvā ca viprāya haviṣyayuktaḥ ।। grāsānpayaḥsarpiryutānupoṣya bhuktvetihāsaṃ śṛṇuyānmuhūrtam ।।
śubhraṃ ca viṣṇoḥ karavīrapuṣpaṃ śrīcampakaṃ candramasaḥ pradeyam ।। yasminmāse vratādiḥ syāt tatpuṣpairarcayeddharim ।। vratānte śayanaṃ dadyād darpaṇopaskarānvitam ।। candraḥ ṣaḍaṅgulaḥ kāryo rohiṇī caturaṅgulā ।।
dadyānmantreṇa pūrvāhṇe śālīkṣuphalasaṃyutam ।। savastrabhājanāṃ dhenuṃ tathā śaṅkhaṃ ca śobhanam ।। candro ayaṃ dvijarūpeṇa sabhārya iti kalpayet ।। somarūpasya te tadvan mamābhedo astu bhūtibhiḥ ।।
bhuktirmuktistathā bhaktis tvayi candrāstu me sadā ।। rūpārogyāyuṣāmetad vidhāyakamanuttamam ।। candralokamavāpnoti vidyudbhūtvā tu mucyate ।। sāpi tatphalamāpnoti punarāvṛttidurlabham ।।
matimapi ca dadāti so api śaurer bhavanagataḥ paripūjyate amaraughaiḥ ।। taḍāgārāmakūpānāṃ vāpīṣu nalinīṣu ca ।। ke tatra cartvijo nātha vedī vā kīdṛśī bhavet ।। dravyāṇi kāni śastāni sarvamācakṣva tattvataḥ ।।
purāṇeṣvitihāso ayaṃ paṭhyate vedavādibhiḥ ।। puṇye ahni viprakathite kṛtvā brāhmaṇavācanam ।। caturhastāṃ śubhāṃ vedīṃ caturasrāṃ caturmukhām ।। vedyāśca parito gartā ratnimātrāstrimekhalāḥ ।।
vitastimātrā yoniḥ syāt ṣaṭsaptāṅgulivistṛtā ।। sarvatastu savarṇāḥ syuḥ patākādhvajasaṃyutāḥ ।। maṇḍapasya pratidiśaṃ dvārāṇyetāni kārayet ।। aṣṭau tu jāpakāḥ kāryā brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ ।।
kulaśīlasamāyuktaḥ purodhāḥ syāddvijottamaḥ ।। vyajanaṃ cāmare śubhre tāmrapātre suvistṛte ।। ācāryaḥ prakṣipedbhūmāv anumantrya vicakṣaṇaḥ ।। yajamānapramāṇo vā saṃsthāpyo bhūtimicchatā ।।
kuṇḍalāni ca haimāni keyūrakaṭakāni ca ।। dadyācchayanasaṃyuktam ātmanaścāpi yatpriyam ।। evamāsādya tatsarvam ādāveva viśāṃ pate ।। sarvauṣadhyudakaistatra snāpito vedapāragaiḥ ।।
paścimaṃ dvāramāsādya praviśedyāgamaṇḍapam ।। añjasā maṇḍalaṃ kuryāt pañcavarṇena tattvavit ।। caturasraṃ ca parito vṛttaṃ madhye suśobhanam ।। vinyasenmantrataḥ sarvān pratidikṣu vicakṣaṇaḥ ।।
brahmāṇaṃ ca śivaṃ viṣṇuṃ tatraiva sthāpayedbudhaḥ ।। śāntyarthaṃ sarvalokānāṃ bhūtagrāmaṃ nyasettataḥ ।। kumbhān sajalagarbhāṃstān vāsobhiḥ pariveṣṭayet ।। paṭhadhvamiti tānbrūyād ācāryastvabhipūjayet ।।
sāmagau paścime tadvad uttareṇa tvatharvaṇau ।। yajadhvamiti tānbrūyād dhautrikānpunareva tu ।। evamādiśya tānsarvān paryukṣyāgniṃ sa mantravit ।। ṛtvigbhiścātha hotavyaṃ vāruṇaireva sarvataḥ ।।
marudbhyo lokapālebhyo vidhivadviśvakarmaṇe ।। japeyuḥ pauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ pūrvato bahvṛcaḥ pṛthak ।। saurasūktaṃ japenmantraṃ dakṣiṇena yajurvidaḥ ।। śaiśavaṃ pañcanidhanaṃ gāyatraṃ jyeṣṭhasāma ca ।।
gāyeyuḥ sāmagā rājan paścimaṃ dvāramāśritāḥ ।। japeyurmanasā devam āśritya varuṇaṃ prabhum ।। mṛdamādāya kumbheṣu prakṣipeccatvarāttathā ।। snapanaṃ tasya kartavyaṃ pañcagavyasamanvitam ।।
evaṃ kṣapātivāhyātha vidhiyuktena karmaṇā ।। pañcāśadvātha ṣaṭtriṃśat pañcaviṃśatirapyatha ।। vedaśabdaiśca gāndharvair vādyaiśca vividhaiḥ punaḥ ।। sāmagāya ca sā deyā brāhmaṇāya viśāṃ pate ।।
dhṛtāṃ caturvidhair viprair vedavedāṅgapāragaiḥ ।। uttarābhimukhīṃ dhenuṃ jalamadhye tu kārayet ।। āpo hi ṣṭheti mantreṇa kṣiptvāgatya ca maṇḍapam ।। punardināni hotavyaṃ catvāri munisattamāḥ ।।
dakṣiṇā rājaśārdūla varuṇakṣmāpaṇaṃ tataḥ ।। hemapātrīṃ ca śayyāṃ ca sthāpakāya nivedayet ।। evameṣa purāṇeṣu taḍāgavidhirucyate ।। eṣa eva vidhirdṛṣṭaḥ pratiṣṭhāsu tathaiva ca ।।
alpeṣvekāgnivatkṛtvā vittaśāṭhyādṛte nṛṇām ।। vājapeyātirātrābhyāṃ hemante śiśire sthitam ।। grīṣme api tatsthitaṃ toyaṃ rājasūyādviśiṣyate ।। sa yāti rudrālayamāśu pūtaḥ kalpānanekāndivi modate ca ।।
sahaiva viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ yat prāpnoti tadyāgaphalena bhūyaḥ ।। vidhinā kena kartavyaṃ pādapodyāpanaṃ budhaiḥ ।। yatphalaṃ labhate pretya tatsarvaṃ vaktumarhasi ।। taḍāgavidhivatsarvam āsādya jagadīśvara ।।
pūjayedbrāhmaṇāṃstadvad dhemavastrānulepanaiḥ ।। vṛkṣānmālyairalaṃkṛtya vāsobhirabhiveṣṭayet ।। añjanaṃ cāpi dātavyaṃ tadvaddhemaśalākayā ।। pratyekaṃ sarvavṛkṣāṇāṃ vedyāṃ tānyadhivāsayet ।।
saptadhānyasthitānkṛtvā vastragandhānulepanaiḥ ।। sahiraṇyānaśeṣāṃstān kṛtvā balinivedanam ।। vanaspateśca vidvadbhir homaḥ kāryo dvijātibhiḥ ।। payasvinīṃ vṛkṣamadhyād utsṛjedgāmudaṅmukhīm ।।
taireva kumbhaiḥ snapanaṃ kuryādbrāhmaṇapuṃgavaḥ ।। gobhir vibhavataḥ sarvān ṛtvijastānsamāhitaḥ ।। kṣīreṇa bhojanaṃ dadyād yāvaddinacatuṣṭayam ।। dakṣiṇā ca punastadvad deyā tatrāpi śaktitaḥ ।।
ācārye dviguṇaṃ dadyāt praṇipatya visarjayet ।। sarvānkāmānavāpnoti phalaṃ cānantyamaśnute ।। so api svarge vasedrājan yāvadindrāyutatrayam ।। paramāṃ siddhimāpnoti punarāvṛttidurlabhām ।।
so api sampūjito devair brahmaloke mahīyate ।। saubhāgyaśayanaṃ nāma yatpurāṇavido viduḥ ।। vaikuṇṭhaṃ svargamāsādya viṣṇor vakṣaḥsthalasthitam ।। ahaṃkārāvṛte loke pradhānapuruṣānvite ।।
tayābhitaptasya harer vakṣasastadviniḥsṛtam ।। rasarūpaṃ tato yāvat prāpnoti vasudhātalam ।। dakṣeṇa pītamātraṃ tad rūpalāvaṇyakārakam ।। śeṣaṃ yadapatadbhūmāv aṣṭadhā samajāyata ।।
ikṣavo rasarājāśca niṣpāvājājidhānyakam ।। lavaṇaṃ cāṣṭamaṃ tadvat saubhāgyāṣṭakamucyate ।। duhitā sābhavattasya yā satītyabhidhīyate ।। trailokyasundarīm enām upayeme pinākadhṛk ।।
tāmārādhya pumānbhaktyā nārī vā kiṃ na vindati ।। tadvidhānaṃ jagannātha tatsarvaṃ ca vadasva me ।। śuklapakṣasya pūrvāhṇe tilaiḥ snānaṃ samācaret ।। pāṇigrahaṇakair mantrair udūḍhā varavarṇinī ।।
phalairnānāvidhairdhūpair dīpanaivedyasaṃyutaiḥ ।। snāpayitvārcayed gaurīm induśekharasaṃyutām ।। śivāyeti ca saṃkīrya jayāyai gulphayor dvayoḥ ।। saṃkīrtya harikeśāya tathorū varade namaḥ ।।
kukṣidvayaṃ ca koṭavyai śūline śūlapāṇaye ।। sarvātmane namo rudram īśānyai ca kucadvayam ।। tripuraghnāya viśveśam anantāyai karadvayam ।। svāhāsvadhāyai ca mukham īśvarāyeti śūlinam ।।
sthāṇave tu haraṃ tadvad dhāsyaṃ candramukhapriye ।। nama ugrāya lokeśaṃ laliteti punarbhruvau ।। bhīmograsamarūpiṇyai śiraḥ sarvātmane namaḥ ।। sthāpayeddhṛtaniṣpāvakusumbhakṣīrajīrakam ।।
dattaṃ saubhāgyamityasmāt saubhāgyāṣṭakamityataḥ ।। rātrau śṛṅgodakaṃ prāśya tadvadbhūmāvariṃdama ।। saṃpūjya dvijadāmpatyaṃ vastramālyavibhūṣaṇaiḥ ।। prīyatāmatra lalitā brāhmaṇāya nivedayet ।।
kartavyaṃ vidhivadbhaktyā sarvasaubhāgyamīpsubhiḥ ।। śṛṅgodakaṃ caitramāse vaiśākhe gomayaṃ punaḥ ।। śrāvaṇe dadhi saṃprāśyaṃ nabhasye ca kuśodakam ।। mārge māse tu gomūtraṃ pauṣe saṃprāśayedghṛtam ।।
lalitā vijayā bhadrā bhavānī kumudā śivā ।। umā ca dānakāle tu prīyatāmiti kīrtayet ।। kubjakaṃ karavīraṃ ca bāṇamamlānakuṅkumam ।। japākusumbhakusumaṃ mālatī śatapattrikā ।।
evaṃ saṃvatsaraṃ yāvad upoṣya vidhivannaraḥ ।। vratānte śayanaṃ dadyāt sarvopaskarasaṃyutam ।। sthāpayitvātha śayane brāhmaṇāya nivedayet ।। vittaśāṭhyena rahitaḥ pūjayedgatavismayaḥ ।।
phalasyaikasya tyāgena vratametatsamācaret ।। na viyukto bhavedrājan navārbudaśatatrayam ।। pūjyamāno vasetsamyag yāvatkalpāyutatrayam ।। sāpi tatphalamāpnoti devyanugrahalālitā ।।
so api vidyādharo bhūtvā svargaloke ciraṃ vaset ।। kṛtamatha varuṇena nandinā vā kim u jananātha tato yadudbhavaḥ syāt ।। tapaḥ satyaṃ ca saptaite devalokāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। lakṣmīśca vipulā nātha kathaṃ syātpurasūdana ।।
ādiṣṭaḥ puruhūtena vināśāya suradviṣām ।। virocanaśca saṃgrāmād apalāyaṃstapodhana ।। aśakyā iti te apyagnimārutābhyāmupekṣitāḥ ।। saṃpīḍya ca munīnsarvān praviśanti punarjalam ।।
jaladurgabalādbrahman pīḍayanti jagattrayam ।। ādideśa cirādambunidhireṣa viśoṣyatām ।। tasmādbhavadbhyāmadyaiva kṣayameṣa praṇīyatām ।। adharma eṣa devendra sāgarasya vināśanam ।।
tasmānna pāpamadyāvāṃ karavāva puraṃdara ।। nivasanti suraśreṣṭha sa kathaṃ nāśamarhati ।। uvācedaṃ vaco roṣān nirdahanniva pāvakam ।। bhavatostu viśeṣeṇa māhātmyaṃ cādhitiṣṭhatoḥ ।।
dharmārthaśāstrarahitaṃ śatruṃ prati vibhāvaso ।। mārutena samaṃ loke tava janma bhaviṣyati ।। bhaviṣyatyudadhirvahne tadā devatvamāpsyasi ।। avāptāvekadehena kumbhājjanma tapodhana ।।
agastya ityugratapāḥ saṃbabhūva punarmuniḥ ।। janma kumbhādagastyasya kathaṃ syātpurasūdana ।। bhūtvā dharmasuto viṣṇuś cacāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ ।। śakreṇa mādhavānaṅgāv apsarogaṇasaṃyutau ।।
na kāmamādhavābhyāṃ ca viṣayānprati cukṣubhe ।। nārīmutpādayāmāsa trailokyajanamohinīm ।। apsarobhiḥ samakṣaṃ hi devānāmabravīddhariḥ ।। urvaśīti ca nāmneyaṃ loke khyātiṃ gamiṣyati ।।
uktā māṃ ramayasveti bāḍham ityabravīttu sā ।। varuṇena dhṛtā paścād varuṇaṃ nābhyanandata ।। uvāca varuṇaścittaṃ mayi saṃnyasya gamyatām ।। tasyai mānuṣaloke tvaṃ gaccha somasutātmajam ।।
prakṣiptamatha saṃjātau dvāveva munisattamau ।। tatrāntare abhyājagāma vasiṣṭho brahmasambhavaḥ ।। videhastvaṃ bhavasveti tatastenāpyasau muniḥ ।। jagmatuḥ śāpanāśāya brahmāṇaṃ jagataḥ patim ।।
nimeṣāḥ syuśca lokānāṃ tadviśrāmāya nārada ।। agastya iti śāntātmā babhūva ṛṣisattamaḥ ।। sabhāryaḥ saṃvṛto viprais tapaścakre suduścaram ।। jagadvīkṣya sa kopena pītavānvaruṇālayam ।।
varaṃ vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te yadabhīṣṭaṃ ca vai mune ।। vaimāniko bhaviṣyāmi dakṣiṇācalavartmani ।। sa saptalokādhipatiḥ paryāyeṇa bhaviṣyati ।। tasmādarghaḥ pradātavyo hy agastyasya sadā budhaiḥ ।।
vidhānaṃ yadagastyasya pūjane tadvadasva me ।। snānaṃ śuklatilaistadvac chuklamālyāmbaro gṛhī ।। nānābhakṣyaphalairyuktaṃ tāmrapātrasamanvitam ।। caturmukhaṃ kumbhamukhe nidhāya dhānyāni saptāmbarasaṃyutāni ।।
utkṣipya lambodaradīrghabāhum ananyacetā yamadiṅmukhaḥ san ।। dhenuṃ naraḥ kṣīravatīṃ praṇamya savatsaghaṇṭābharaṇāṃ dvijāya ।। yāvatsamāḥ sapta daśāthavā syur athordhvamapyatra vadanti kecit ।। mitrāvaruṇayoḥ putra kumbhayone namo astu te ।।
ratnavallabha deveśa laṅkāvāsinnamo astu te ।। lopāmudrāpatiḥ śrīmān yo asau tasmai namo namaḥ ।। pratyabdaṃ tu phalatyāgam evaṃ kurvanna sīdati ।। anena vidhinā yastu pumānarghyaṃ nivedayet ।।
dvitīyena bhuvarlokaṃ svargalokaṃ tataḥ param ।। yāvadāyuśca yaḥ kuryāt paraṃ brahmādhigacchati ।। matimapi ca dadāti so api viṣṇor bhavanagataḥ paripūjyate amaraughaiḥ ।। bhuktimuktipradaṃ deva tanme brūhi janārdana ।।
kailāsaśikharāsīno devyā pṛṣṭastadā kila ।। tadidānīṃ pravakṣyāmi bhuktimuktiphalapradam ।। narāṇāmatha nārīṇām ārādhanamanuttamam ।। śuklapakṣe tṛtīyāyāṃ susnāto gaurasarṣapaiḥ ।।
saubhāgyārogyadaṃ yasmāt sadā ca lalitāpriyam ।। dhārayedatha raktāni nārī cedatha saṃyatā ।। snāpayenmadhunā tadvat puṣpagandhodakena ca ।। dhānyakājājilavaṇair guḍakṣīraghṛtānvitaiḥ ।।
pādādyabhyarcanaṃ kuryāt pratipakṣaṃ varānane ।। aśokāyai namo jaṅghe pārvatyai jānunī tathā ।। padmodarāyai jaṭharam uraḥ kāmaśriyai namaḥ ।। mukhaṃ darpaṇavāsinyai smaradāyai smitaṃ namaḥ ।।
tuṣṭyai lalāṭamalakān kātyāyanyai śirastathā ।। rambhāyai lalitāyai ca vāsudevyai namo namaḥ ।। pattrairdvādaśabhiryuktaṃ kuṅkumena sakarṇikam ।। bhavānīṃ dakṣiṇe tadvad rudrāṇīṃ ca tataḥ param ।।
vāyavye pāṭalāmugrām antareṇa tato apyumām ।। kusumairakṣatairvārbhir namaskāreṇa vinyaset ।। sindūraṃ snānacūrṇaṃ ca tāsāṃ śirasi pātayet ।। na pūjyate gururyatra sarvāstatrāphalāḥ kriyāḥ ।।
bandhujīvairāśvayuje kārttike śatapattrakaiḥ ।। sinduvāreṇa jātyā vā phālgune apyarcayedumām ।। kadambairatha mālatyā śrāvaṇe pūjayetsadā ।। bilvapattrārkapuṣpaṃ ca yavāngośṛṅgavāri ca ।।
etadbhādrapadādyaṃ tu prāśanaṃ samudāhṛtam ।। pūjayitvārcayedbhaktyā vastramālyānulepanaiḥ ।। tasyai dadyātphalaṃ puṣpaṃ suvarṇotpalasaṃyutam ।। tathā mām uddharāśeṣaduḥkhasaṃsārasāgarāt ।।
lalitā kamalā gaurī satī rambhātha pārvatī ।। vratānte śayanaṃ dadyāt suvarṇakamalānvitam ।। aṣṭau ṣaḍvāpyatha punaś cānumāsaṃ samarcayet ।। uktānantatṛtīyaiṣā sadānantaphalapradā ।।
naro vā yadi vā nārī vittaśāṭhyāt patatyadhaḥ ।। yadyaśuddhā tadānyena vārayetprayatā svayam ।। kalpakoṭiśataṃ sāgraṃ śivaloke mahīyate ।। puṣpamantravidhānena so api tatphalamāpnuyāt ।।
sāpi tatphalamāpnoti gauryanugrahalālitā ।। matimapi ca dadāti so api devair amaravadhūjanakiṃnaraiśca pūjyaḥ ।। rasakalyāṇinīmetāṃ purākalpavido viduḥ ।। prātargavyena payasā tilaiḥ snānaṃ samācaret ।।
dakṣiṇāṅgāni sampūjya tato vāmāni pūjayet ।। jaṅghāṃ jānuṃ tathā śāntyai tathaivoruṃ śriyai namaḥ ।। stanau madanavāsinyai kumudāyai ca kandarām ।। bhūlalāṭaṃ ca rudrāṇyai śaṃkarāyai tathālakān ।।
madanāyai lalāṭaṃ tu mohanāyai punarbhruvau ।। utkaṇṭhinyai namaḥ kaṇṭham amṛtāyai namaḥ stanau ।। hṛdayaṃ manmathādhiṣṇyai pāṭalāyai tathodaram ।। jānujaṅghe namo gauryai gāyatryai ghuṭike namaḥ ।।
namo bhavānyai kāminyai kāmadevyai jagatpriye ।। bhojayitvānnapānena madhureṇa vimatsaraḥ ।। dattvā suvarṇakamalaṃ gandhamālyaiḥ samarcayet ।। anena vidhinā devī māsi māsi sadārcayet ।।
tailaṃ rājiṃ tathā caitre varjyaṃ ca madhu mādhave ।। śrāvaṇe varjayetkṣīraṃ dadhi bhādrapade tathā ।। dhānyakaṃ mārgaśīrṣe tu pauṣe varjyā ca śarkarā ।। dadyāddvikālavelāyāṃ pūrṇapātreṇa saṃyutam ।।
ghārikān apyapūpāṃśca piṣṭāpūpāṃśca maṇḍakān ।। māghādikramaśo dadyād etāni karakopari ।। umā ratiḥ satī tadvan maṅgalā ratilālasā ।। upavāsī bhavennityam aśakte naktamiṣyate ।।
kṛtvā tu kāñcanīṃ gaurīṃ pañcaratnasamanvitām ।। caturbhujāminduyutāṃ sitanetrapaṭāvṛtām ।। savastrabhājanaṃ dadyād bhavānī prīyatāmiti ।। kuryātsa sarvapāpebhyas tatkṣaṇādeva mucyate ।।
agniṣṭomasahasrasya yatphalaṃ tadavāpnuyāt ।। saubhāgyārogyasampannā gaurīloke mahīyate ।। matimapi ca narāṇāṃ yo dadāti priyārthaṃ vibudhapativimāne nāyakaḥ syādamoghaḥ ।। nāmnā ca loke vikhyātām ārdrānandakarīmimām ।।
darbhagandhodakaiḥ snānaṃ tadā samyaksamācaret ।। mahādevena sahitām upaviṣṭāṃ mahāsane ।। jaṅghe śokavināśinyai ānandāya namaḥ prabho ।। adityai ca kaṭiṃ devyāḥ śūlinaḥ śūlapāṇaye ।।
stanāvānandakāriṇyai śaṃkarasyendudhāriṇe ।। bāhū ca parirambhiṇyai triśūlāya harasya ca ।। smitaṃ sasmeralīlāyai viśvavaktrāya vai vibho ।। bhruvau nṛtyapriyāyai tu tāṇḍaveśāya śūlinaḥ ।।
svāhāyai mukuṭaṃ devyā vibhorgaṅgādharāya vai ।। prasannavadanau vande pārvatīparameśvarau ।। padmotpalāni rajasā nānāvarṇena kārayet ।। tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi śivaloke mahīyate ।।
pratipakṣaṃ caturmāsaṃ yāvadetannivedayet ।। catvāri saktupātrāṇi tilapātrāṇyataḥ param ।। apakvaṃ dadhi dugdhaṃ ca gośṛṅgodakameva ca ।। uśīrasalilaṃ tadvad yavacūrṇodakaṃ punaḥ ।।
māseṣu pakṣadvitayaṃ prāśanaṃ samudāhṛtam ।। dānakāle ca sarvatra mantrametamudīrayet ।। saubhāgyāyāstu lalitā bhavānī sarvasiddhaye ।। candanaṃ netrapaṭṭaṃ ca sahiraṇyāmbujena tu ।।
sapatnīkāya viprāya gaurī me prīyatāmiti ।। yāmupoṣya naro yāti śambhoryatparamaṃ padam ।। āyurārogyasampattyā na kaścicchokamāpnuyāt ।। sāpi tatphalamāpnoti devyanugrahalālitā ।।
rudrāṇīlokamabhyeti punarāvṛttidurlabham ।। śakraloke sa gandharvaiḥ pūjyate api yugatrayam ।। sā sve gṛhe sukhaśatānyanubhūya bhūyo gaurīpadaṃ sadayitā dayitā prayāti ।। yasyāṃ dattaṃ hutaṃ japtaṃ sarvaṃ bhavati cākṣayam ।।
akṣayaṃ phalamāpnoti sarvasya sukṛtasya ca ।। tatra dattaṃ hutaṃ japtaṃ sarvamakṣayamucyate ।। akṣataistu narāḥ snātā viṣṇordattvā tathākṣatān ।। yathānnabhuṅmahābhāgaḥ phalamakṣayyamaśnute ।।
etāsāmapi sarvāsāṃ tṛtīyānāṃ phalaṃ bhavet ।। rājasūyaphalaṃ prāpya gatimagryāṃ ca vindati ।। tathaiva janasaubhāgyam atividyāsu kauśalam ।। āyuśca vipulaṃ puṃsāṃ tanme kathaya mādhava ।।
yasya saṃkīrtanādeva tuṣyatīha sarasvatī ।। tadvāsarādau sampūjya viprānetānsamācaret ।। pāyasaṃ bhojayedviprān kṛtvā brāhmaṇavācanam ।। gāyatrīṃ pūjayedbhaktyā śuklamālyānulepanaiḥ ।।
tvāṃ parityajya saṃtiṣṭhet tathā bhava varapradā ।। na vihīnaṃ tvayā devi tathā me santu siddhayaḥ ।। etābhiḥ pāhi cāṣṭābhis tanubhirmāṃ sarasvati ।। maunavratena bhuñjīta sāyaṃ prātastu dharmavit ।।
kṣīraṃ dadyāddhiraṇyaṃ ca gāyatrī prīyatāmiti ।। nāntarā bhojanaṃ kuryād yāvanmāsāstrayodaśa ।। pūrvaṃ savastrayugmaṃ ca dadyādviprāya bhojanam ।। candanaṃ vastrayugmaṃ ca dadyācca śikharaṃ punaḥ ।।
vittaśāṭhyena rahito vastramālyānulepanaiḥ ।। vidyāvānarthasaṃyukto raktakaṇṭhaśca jāyate ।। nārī vā kurute yā tu sāpi tatphalagāminī ।। brahmaloke vased rājan yāvat kalpāyutatrayam ।।
vidyādharapure so api vasetkalpāyutatrayam ।। tadahaṃ śrotumicchāmi dravyamantravidhānavit ।। tasya snānaṃ pravakṣyāmi mantrauṣadhavidhānataḥ ।। sampūjya caturo viprāñ śuklamālyānulepanaiḥ ।।
sthāpayec caturaḥ kumbhān avraṇānsāgarāniti ।। rājadvārapradeśācca mṛdamānīya cākṣipet ।। rocanāṃ padmaśaṅkhau ca pañcaratnasamanvitam ।। etatsarvaṃ vinikṣipya kumbheṣvāvāhayetsurān ।।
āyāntu yajamānasya duritakṣayakārakāḥ ।। sahasranayanaścendro grahapīḍāṃ vyapohatu ।। candroparāgasambhūtām agniḥ pīḍāṃ vyapohatu ।। yamaścandroparāgotthāṃ mama pīḍāṃ vyapohatu ।।
khaḍgavyagro atibhīmaśca rakṣaḥpīḍāṃ vyapohatu ।। sa jalādhipatiś candragrahapīḍāṃ vyapohatu ।। vāyuścandroparāgotthāṃ pīḍāmatra vyapohatu ।। candroparāgakaluṣaṃ dhanado me vyapohatu ।।
candroparāgajāṃ pīḍāṃ vināśayatu śaṃkaraḥ ।। brahmaviṣṇvarkayuktāni tāni pāpaṃ dahantu vai ।। pūjayedvastragodānair brāhmaṇāniṣṭadevatāḥ ।। vastrapaṭṭe athavā padme pañcaratnasamanvitān ।।
tato ativāhayedvelām uparāgānugāminīm ।। kṛtasnānāya taṃ paṭṭaṃ brāhmaṇāya nivedayet ।। na tasya grahapīḍā syān na ca bandhujanakṣayaḥ ।। sūryagrahe sūryanāma sadā mantreṣu kīrtayet ।।
prayacchecca niśāṃ patye candrasūryoparāgayoḥ ।। sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ śakraloke mahīyate ।। mṛtavatsābhiṣekādikāryeṣu ca kimiṣyate ।। rogadaurgatyarūpeṇa tathaiveṣṭavadhena ca ।।
saptamīsnapanaṃ nāma janapīḍāvināśanam ।। tadvadvṛddhāturāṇāṃ ca yauvane cāpi vartatām ।। etad evādbhutodvegacittabhramavināśanam ।। vaivasvataśca tatrāpi yadā tu manuruttamaḥ ।।
bhavitā nṛpatirvīraḥ kṛtavīryaḥ pratāpavān ।। yāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi saptasaptati nārada ।। cyavanasya tu śāpena vināśamapayāsyati ।। kuraṅganayanaḥ śrīmān sambhūto nṛpalakṣaṇaiḥ ।।
putrasya jīvanāyālam etatsnānamavāpsyati ।। aśeṣaduṣṭaśamanaṃ sadā kalmaṣanāśanam ।। bhaviṣyati ciraṃjīvī kiṃtu kalmaṣanāśanam ।। athavā śuklasaptamyām etatsarvaṃ praśasyate ।।
tadvadvṛddhāturāṇāṃ ca kṛtyaṃ syāditareṣu ca ।। nirvapetsūryarudrābhyāṃ tanmantrābhyāṃ vidhānataḥ ।। juhuyādrudrasūktena tadvadrudrāya nārada ।। yavakṛṣṇatilairhomaḥ kartavyo aṣṭaśataṃ punaḥ ।।
hutvā snānaṃ ca kartavyaṃ maṅgalaṃ yena dhīmatā ।। sthāpayitvā tu caturaḥ kumbhānkoṇeṣu śobhanān ।। sthāpayedavraṇaṃ kumbhaṃ saptarcenābhimantritam ।। pañcaratnaphalaiḥ puṣpair vāsobhiḥ pariveṣṭayet ।।
saṃśuddhāṃ mṛdamānīya sarveṣveva vinikṣipet ।। gṛhītvā brāhmaṇastatra saurānmantrānudīrayet ।। saviprābhiśca kartavyaṃ mṛtavatsābhiṣecanam ।। ādityaścandramāḥ sārdhaṃ grahanakṣatramaṇḍalaiḥ ।।
te te cānye ca devaughāḥ sadā pāntu kumārakam ।। pīḍāṃ kurvantu bālasya mā māturjanakasya vai ।। saptakaṃ pūjayedbhaktyā strīṇāmatha guruṃ punaḥ ।। pratimāṃ dharmarājasya gurave vinivedayet ।।
pūjayedbrāhmaṇāṃstadvad vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ ।। dīrghāyurastu bālo ayaṃ yāvadvarṣaśataṃ sukhī ।। brahmā rudro vasuḥ skando viṣṇuḥ śakro hutāśanaḥ ।। evamādīni vākyāni vadantaṃ pūjayedgurum ।।
caruṃ ca putrasahitā praṇamya raviśaṃkarau ।। idamevādbhutodvegaduḥsvapneṣu praśasyate ।। śāntyarthaṃ śuklasaptamyām etatkurvanna sīdati ।। saṃvatsarāṇāmayutaṃ śaśāsa pṛthivīmimām ।।
kathayitvā dvijaśreṣṭha tatraivāntaradhīyata ।। sarvaduṣṭopaśamanaṃ bālānāṃ paramaṃ hitam ।। īśvarājjñānam anvicchen mokṣam icchejjanārdanāt ।। śṛṇoti yaścainamananyacetās tasyāpi siddhiṃ munayo vadanti ।।
mandarastho mahādevaḥ pinākī brahmaṇā svayam ।। svalpena tapasā deva bhavenmokṣo athavā nṛṇām ।। svalpakenātha tapasā mahatphalamihocyatām ।। umāpatiruvācedaṃ manasaḥ prītikārakam ।।
vārāho bhavitā kalpas tasya manvantare śubhe ।। dvāparākhyaṃ yugaṃ tadvad aṣṭāviṃśatimaṃ jaguḥ ।। bhārāvataraṇārthāya tridhā viṣṇurbhaviṣyati ।। kaṃsādidarpamathanaḥ keśavaḥ kleśanāśanaḥ ।।
tvaṣṭā mamājñayā tadvat kariṣyati jagatpateḥ ।। bhāryābhirvṛṣṇibhiścaiva bhūbhṛdbhir bhūridakṣiṇaiḥ ।। pravṛttāsu purāṇīṣu dharmasambandhinīṣu ca ।। tvayā pṛṣṭasya dharmasya rahasyasyāsya bhedakṛt ।।
pravartako asya dharmasya pāṇḍuputro mahābalaḥ ।। mayā dattaḥ sa dharmātmā tena cāsau vṛkodaraḥ ।। bhaviṣyatyajaraḥ śrīmān kandarpa iva rūpavān ।। idaṃ vratamaśeṣāṇāṃ vratānāmadhikaṃ yataḥ ।।
aśeṣayajñaphaladam aśeṣāghavināśanam ।। bhaviṣyaṃ ca bhaviṣyāṇāṃ purāṇānāṃ purātanam ।। anyeṣvapi dinarkṣeṣu na śaktastvam upoṣitum ।। upoṣya vidhinānena gaccha viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam ।।
ghṛtenābhyañjanaṃ kṛtvā tilaiḥ snānaṃ samācaret ।। kṛṣṇāya pādau sampūjya śiraḥ sarvātmane namaḥ ।। sarve nārāyaṇasyaivaṃ saṃpūjyā bāhavaḥ kramāt ।। ūrū saubhāgyanāthāya jānunī bhūtadhāriṇe ।।
namo devyai namaḥ śāntyai namo lakṣmyai namaḥ śriyai ।। viṣapramāthine nityaṃ garuḍaṃ cābhipūjayet ।। gandhairmālyaistathā dhūpair bhakṣyairnānāvidhairapi ।। sarpiṣā saha bhuktvā ca gatvā śatapadaṃ budhaḥ ।।
gṛhītvā dhāvayeddantān ācāntaḥ prāgudaṅmukhaḥ ।। namo nārāyaṇāyeti tvāmahaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।। rātriṃ ca sakalāṃ sthitvā snānaṃ ca payasā tathā ।। sahaiva puṇḍarīkākṣa dvādaśyāṃ kṣīrabhojanam ।।
evamuktvā svapedbhūmāv itihāsakathāṃ punaḥ ।। snānaṃ kṛtvā mṛdā tadvat pāṣaṇḍān abhivarjayet ।। praṇamya ca hṛṣīkeśaṃ saptalokaikamīśvaram ।। daśahastamathāṣṭau vā karānkuryādviśāṃ pate ।।
caturhastapramāṇaṃ ca vinyasettatra toraṇam ।। tasya dhārāṃ ca śirasā dhārayetsakalāṃ niśām ।। aratnimātraṃ kuṇḍaṃ ca kuryāttatra trimekhalam ।। tilāṃśca viṣṇudevatyair mantrairekāgnivattadā ।।
niṣpāvārdhapramāṇāṃ vai dhārāmājyasya pātayet ।। bhakṣyairnānāvidhairyuktān sitavastrairalaṃkṛtān ।। caturbhirbahvṛcairhomas tatra kārya udaṅmukhaiḥ ।। ariṣṭavargasahitāny abhitaḥ paripāṭhayet ।।
pūjayedaṅgulīyaiśca kaṭakairhemasūtrakaiḥ ।। evaṃ kṣapātivāhyā ca gītamaṅgalaniḥsvanaiḥ ।। tataḥ prabhāte vimale samutthāya trayodaśa ।। payasvinīḥ śīlavatīḥ kāṃsyadohasamanvitāḥ ।।
tāstu teṣāṃ tato bhaktyā bhakṣyabhojyānnatarpitān ।। bhuktvā cākṣāralavaṇam ātmanā ca visarjayet ।। prīyatāmatra deveśaḥ keśavaḥ kleśanāśanaḥ ।। yathāntaraṃ na paśyāmi tathā me svasti cāyuṣaḥ ।।
vāsāṃsi caiva sarveṣāṃ gṛhāṇi prāpayedbudhaḥ ।। śayyāṃ dadyāddvijāteśca sarvopaskarasaṃyutām ।। taddinaṃ naraśārdūla ya icchedvipulāṃ śriyam ।। kuru vratamidaṃ samyak snehāttava mayeritam ।।
yā tu kalyāṇinī nāma purā kalpeṣu paṭhyate ।। yasyāḥ smarankīrtanamapyaśeṣaṃ vinaṣṭapāpastridaśādhipaḥ syāt ।। ābhīrakanyātikutūhalena saivorvaśī samprati nākapṛṣṭhe ।। tatrāpi tasyāḥ paricārikeyaṃ mama priyā samprati satyabhāmā ।।
asyāṃ ca kalyāṇatithau vivasvān sahasradhāreṇa sahasraraśmiḥ ।। phalamasya na śakyate abhivaktuṃ yadi jihvāyutakoṭayo mukhe syuḥ ।। api narakagatānpitṝn aśeṣān alamuddhartumihaiva yaḥ karoti ।। tithimiha sakalārthabhāṅnarendras tava caturānana sāmyatāmupaiti ।।
sā pāṇḍuputreṇa kṛtā bhaviṣyaty anantapuṇyānagha bhīmapūrvā ।। paṇyastrīṇāṃ sadācāraṃ śrotumicchāmi tattvataḥ ।। vāsudevasya nārīṇāṃ bhaviṣyantyambujodbhava ।। puṣpite pavanotphullakahlārasarasastaṭe ।।
kuraṅganayanaḥ śrīmān mālatīkṛtaśekharaḥ ।। sākṣātkandarpo rūpeṇa sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।। pravṛddho manmathastāsāṃ bhaviṣyati yadātmani ।। matparokṣaṃ yataḥ kāmalaulyādīdṛgvidhaṃ kṛtam ।।
tābhiḥ śāpābhitaptābhir bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ ।। upadekṣyatyanantātmā bhāvikalyāṇakārakam ।। ityuktvā tāḥ pariṣvajya gato dvāravatīśvaraḥ ।। nivṛtte mausale tadvat keśave divamāgate ।।
hṛtāsu kṛṣṇapatnīṣu dāsabhogyāsu cāmbudhau ।। āgamiṣyati yogātmā dālbhyo nāma mahātapāḥ ।। lālapyamānā bahuśo bāṣpaparyākulekṣaṇāḥ ।। bhartāraṃ jagatāmīśam anantamaparājitam ।।
praśnamevaṃ kariṣyanti munerabhimukhaṃ sthitāḥ ।। svadharmāccyavane asmākam asminnaḥ śaraṇaṃ bhava ।। kasmādīśena saṃyogaṃ prāpya veśyātvamāgatāḥ ।। kathayiṣyatyatastāsāṃ sa dālbhyaścaikitāyanaḥ ।।
bhavatīnāṃ ca sarvāsāṃ nārado abhyāśamāgataḥ ।। kathaṃ nārāyaṇo asmākaṃ bhartā syād ityupādiśa ।। śayyādvayapradānena madhumādhavamāsayoḥ ।। bhartā nārāyaṇo nūnaṃ bhaviṣyatyanyajanmani ।।
caurairapahṛtāḥ sarvā veśyātvaṃ samavāpsyatha ।। idānīmapi yadvakṣye tacchṛṇudhvaṃ varāṅganāḥ ।। dānavāsuradaityeṣu rākṣaseṣu tatastataḥ ।। tāni sarvāṇi deveśaḥ provāca vadatāṃ varaḥ ।।
bhaktimatyo varārohās tathā devakuleṣu ca ।। bhaviṣyati ca saubhāgyaṃ sarvāsāmapi śaktitaḥ ।। nidhanenopacāryo vaḥ sa tadānyatra dāmbhikāt ।। brāhmaṇānāṃ varārohāḥ kāryāṇi vacanāni ca ।।
avicāreṇa sarvābhir anuṣṭheyaṃ ca tatpunaḥ ।। yadā sūryadine hastaḥ puṣyo yātha punarvasuḥ ।। arcayetpuṇḍarīkākṣam anaṅgasyānukīrtanaiḥ ।। meḍhraṃ kandarpanidhaye kīṭaṃ prītimate namaḥ ।।
hṛdayaṃ hṛdayeśāya stanāvāhlādakāriṇe ।। vāmāṅgaṃ puṣpacāpāya puṣpabāṇāya dakṣiṇam ।। sarvātmane ca sarvāṅgaṃ devadevasya pūjayet ।। gadine pītavastrāya śaṅkhacakradharāya ca ।।
sarvaśāntyai namaḥ prītyai namo ratyai nama śriyai ।। gandhairmaulyaistathā dhūpair naivedyena ca kāminī ।। avyaṅgāvayavaṃ pūjya gandhapuṣpārcanādibhiḥ ।। tasmai viprāya sā dadyān mādhavaḥ prīyatāmiti ।।
ratyarthaṃ kāmadevo ayam iti citte avadhārya tam ।। sarvabhāvena cātmānam arpayetsmitabhāṣiṇī ।। taṇḍulaprasthadānaṃ ca yāvanmāsāstrayodaśa ।। viprasyopaskarairyuktāṃ śayyāṃ dadyādvilakṣaṇām ।।
pradīpopānahacchattrapādukāsanasaṃyutām ।। sūkṣmavastraiḥ sakaṭakair dhūpamālyānulepanaiḥ ।। tāmrapātrāsanagataṃ haimanetrapaṭāvṛtam ।। dadyādetena mantreṇa tathaikāṃ gāṃ payasvinīm ।।
tathaiva sarvakāmāptir astu viṣṇo sadā mama ।। tathā mamāpi deveśa śarīre sve kuru prabho ।। ka idaṃ kasmā adāditi vaidikaṃ mantramīrayet ।। śayyāsanādikaṃ sarvaṃ brāhmaṇasya gṛhaṃ nayet ।।
sa mānyaḥ sūryavāre ca sa mantavyo bhavettadā ।। tarpayeta yathākāmaṃ proṣite anyaṃ samācaret ।। ātmano api yathāvighnaṃ garbhabhūtikaraṃ priyam ।। sācārānaṣṭapañcāśad yathāśaktyā samācaret ।।
adharmo ayaṃ tato na syād veśyānāmiha sarvadā ।। tadidaṃ sāmprataṃ sarvaṃ bhavatīṣvapi yujyate ।। kalyāṇīnāṃ ca kathitaṃ tatkurudhvaṃ varānanāḥ ।। sā pūjitā devagaṇair aśeṣair ānandakṛtsthānam upaiti viṣṇoḥ ।।
svasthānameṣyatyanu tāḥ samastaṃ vrataṃ kariṣyanti ca devayānaiḥ ।। tasyāpi niṣkṛtiṃ deva vada sarvakṛpākara ।। śokavyādhibhayaṃ duḥkhaṃ na bhavedyena tadvada ।। kṣīrārṇave sapatnīkaḥ sadā vasati keśavaḥ ।।
gobhūhiraṇyadānādi saptakalpaśatānugam ।। tasyāṃ sampūjayedviṣṇum ebhirmantrairvidhānataḥ ।। gārhasthyaṃ mā praṇāśaṃ me yātu dharmārthakāmadam ।। pitaro mā praṇaśyantu māstu dāmpatyabhedanam ।।
tathā kalatrasambandho deva mā me viyujyatām ।। śayyā mamāpyaśūnyāstu tathaiva madhusūdana ।। ghaṇṭā bhavedaśaktasya sarvavādyamayī yataḥ ।। naktamakṣāralavaṇaṃ yāvattatsyāccatuṣṭayam ।।
dīpānnabhājanairyuktāṃ śayyāṃ dadyādvilakṣaṇām ।। abhīṣṭopaskarairyuktāṃ śuklapuṣpāmbarāvṛtām ।। tathābharaṇadhānyaiśca yathāśaktyā samanvitām ।। dātavyā vedaviduṣe bhāvenāpatitāya ca ।।
patnyāstu bhājanaṃ dadyād bhakṣyabhojyasamanvitam ।। pratimāṃ devadevasya sodakumbhāṃ nivedayet ।। vittaśāṭhyena rahito nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ ।। na virūpau na śokārtau dampatī bhavataḥ kvacit ।।
kurvannaśūnyaśayanaṃ viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।। pippalādasya saṃvādo yudhiṣṭhirapuraḥsaraiḥ ।। yudhiṣṭhiro dharmaputro dharmayuktastapodhanam ।। avyaṅgatā śive bhaktir vaiṣṇavo vā bhavetkatham ।।
śṛṇuṣva yadvakṣyati vai dharmaputrāya dhārmikaḥ ।। aṅgāravratam ityetat sa vakṣyati mahīpateḥ ।। virocanasya saṃvādaṃ bhārgavasya ca dhīmataḥ ।। rūpeṇāpratimaṃ kāntyā so ahasadbhṛgunandanaḥ ।।
tattathā hasitaṃ tasya papraccha surasūdanaḥ ।। sādhusādhviti māmevam uktavāṃstvaṃ vadasva me ।। vismayādvratamāhātmyād dhāsyametatkṛtaṃ mayā ।। atha tadbhīmavaktrasya svedabindurlalāṭajaḥ ।।
anekavaktranayano jvalajjvalanabhīṣaṇaḥ ।। trijagannirdahanbhūyaḥ śivena vinivāritaḥ ।। idānīmalametena lokadāhena karmaṇā ।। prekṣiṣyante janāḥ pūjāṃ kariṣyanti varānmama ।।
devaloke advitīyaṃ ca tava rūpaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। rūpamārogyamaiśvaryaṃ teṣvanantaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। saṃjātastatkṣaṇādrājan grahatvam agamatpunaḥ ।। dṛṣṭavānkriyamāṇaṃ ca śūdreṇa ca vyavasthitaḥ ।।
vividhā ca rucirjātā yasmāttava vidūragā ।। īdṛśīṃ rūpasampattiṃ dṛṣṭvā vismitavānaham ।। paśyato api bhavedrūpam aiśvaryaṃ kimu kurvataḥ ।। ālokitaṃ tena surārigarbhe sambhūtireṣā tava daitya jātā ।।
prahrādanandano vīraḥ punaḥ papraccha vismitaḥ ।। dīyamānaṃ tu yaddānaṃ mayā dṛṣṭaṃ bhavāntare ।। iti tadvacanaṃ śrutvā punaḥ provāca vistarāt ।। mṛdā snānaṃ tadā kuryāt padmarāgavibhūṣitaḥ ।।
śūdrastūṣṇīṃ smaranbhaumam āste bhogavivarjitaḥ ।। prāṅgaṇaṃ puṣpamālābhir akṣatābhiḥ samantataḥ ।। kuṅkumasyāpyabhāve tu raktacandanamiṣyate ।। taṇḍulai raktaśālīyaiḥ padmarāgaiśca saṃyutāḥ ।।
gandhamālyādikaṃ sarvaṃ tathaiva vinivedayet ।। dhuraṃdharaṃ raktamatīva saumyaṃ dhānyāni saptāmbarasaṃyutāni ।। caturbhujaṃ hemamaye niviṣṭaṃ pātre guḍasyopari sarpiyukte ।। samarpayedvipravarāya bhaktyā kṛtāñjaliḥ pūrvamudīrya mantram ।।
rūpārthī tvāṃ prapanno ahaṃ gṛhāṇārghyaṃ namo astu te ।। tato arcayedvipravaraṃ raktamālyāmbarādibhiḥ ।। śayyāṃ ca śaktito dadyāt sarvopaskarasaṃyutām ।। tattadguṇavate deyaṃ tadevākṣayyamicchatā ।।
naktamakṣāralavaṇam aśnīyādghṛtasaṃyutam ।। caturo vātha vā tasya yatpuṇyaṃ tadvadāmi te ।। viṣṇau vātha śive bhaktaḥ saptadvīpādhipo bhavet ।। tasmāttvamapi daityendra vratametatsamācara ।।
tvaṃ cāpi rājankuru sarvametad yato akṣayaṃ vedavido vadanti ।। śṛṇoti yaścainamananyacetās tasyāpi siddhiṃ bhagavānvidhatte ।। yātrārambhe avasāne ca tathā śukrodaye tviha ।। śuklapuṣpāmbarayute sitataṇḍulapūrite ।।
mantreṇānena tatsarvaṃ sāmagāya nivedayet ।। kave sarvārthasiddhyarthaṃ gṛhāṇārghyaṃ namo astu te ।। sarvānkāmānavāpnoti viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।। tāvadannaṃ na cāśnīyāt tribhiḥ kāmārthasiddhaye ।।
suvarṇapātre sauvarṇam amareśapurohitam ।। palāśāśvatthayogena pañcagavyajalena ca ।। praṇamya ca gavā sārdhaṃ brāhmaṇāya nivedayet ।। krūragrahaiḥ pīḍitānām amṛtāya namo namaḥ ।।
kurvanbṛhaspateḥ pūjāṃ sarvānkāmānsamaśnute ।। kiṃcidvrataṃ samācakṣva svargārogyasukhapradam ।। viśokasaptamīṃ tadvat phalāḍhyāṃ pāpanāśinīm ।। mandārasaptamīṃ tadvac chubhadāṃ śubhasaptamīm ।।
vidhānamāsāṃ vakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ।। sā tu kalyāṇinī nāma vijayā ca nigadyate ।। tataḥ śuklāmbaraḥ padmam akṣatābhiḥ prakalpayet ।। puṣpākṣatābhirdeveśaṃ vinyasetsarvataḥ kramāt ।।
yāmye divākarāyeti vidhātra iti nairṛte ।। saumye vikartanāyeti ravaye cāṣṭame dale ।। mantrairebhiḥ samabhyarcya namaskārāntadīpitaiḥ ।। sthaṇḍile pūjayedbhaktyā guḍena lavaṇena ca ।।
tilapātraṃ hiraṇyaṃ ca brāhmaṇāya nivedayet ।। kṛtasnānajapo vipraiḥ sahaiva ghṛtapāyasam ।। ghṛtapātraṃ sakanakaṃ sodakumbhaṃ nivedayet ।। anena vidhinā sarvaṃ māsi māsi vrataṃ caret ।।
vastrālaṃkārasaṃyuktāḥ suvarṇāsyāḥ payasvinīḥ ।। na vittaśāṭhyaṃ kurvīta yato mohātpatatyadhaḥ ।। āyurārogyamaiśvaryam anantamiha jāyate ।। sarvaduṣṭopaśamanī sadā kalyāṇasaptamī ।।
śṛṇoti paṭhate ceha sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। yāmupoṣya naraḥ śokaṃ na kadācidihāśnute ।। upavāsavrataṃ kṛtvā brahmacārī bhavenniśi ।। karavīreṇa raktena raktavastrayugena ca ।।
tathā viśokatā me astu tvadbhaktiḥ pratijanma ca ।। suptvā saṃprāśya gomūtram utthāya kṛtanaityakaḥ ।। tadvastrayugmaṃ padmaṃ ca brāhmaṇāya nivedayet ।। tataḥ purāṇaśravaṇaṃ kartavyaṃ bhūtimicchatā ।।
kṛtvā yāvatpunarmāghaśuklapakṣasya saptamī ।। śayyāṃ sopaskarāṃ dadyāt kapilāṃ ca payasvinīm ।। viśokasaptamīṃ kuryāt sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। tāvanna śokamabhyeti rogadaurgatyavarjitaḥ ।।
niṣkāmaḥ kurute yastu sa paraṃ brahma gacchati ।। so apīndralokamāpnoti na duḥkhī jāyate kvacit ।। yāmupoṣya naraḥ pāpād vimuktaḥ svargabhāgbhavet ।। tāmupoṣyātha kamalaṃ kārayitvā tu kāñcanam ।।
dadyāddvikālavelāyāṃ bhānurme prīyatāmiti ।। dattvā kuryātphalayutaṃ yāvatsyātkṛṣṇesaptamī ।। tadvaddhaimaphalaṃ dattvā suvarṇakamalānvitam ।। saṃvatsaraṃ ca tenaiva vidhinobhayasaptamīm ।।
śrīmānvibhāvasustvaṣṭā varuṇaḥ prīyatāmiti ।। pratipakṣaṃ phalatyāgam etatkurvansamācaret ।। śarkarākalaśaṃ dadyād dhemapadmadalānvitam ।। tathānantaphalāvāptir astu me saptajanmasu ।।
sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā sūryaloke mahīyate ।। tatsarvaṃ nāśamāyāti yaḥ kuryātphalasaptamīm ।। yaḥ śṛṇoti paṭhedvāpi so api kalyāṇabhāgbhavet ।। āyurārogyamaiśvaryaṃ yayānantaṃ prajāyate ।।
prātaḥ snātvā tilaiḥ śuklaiḥ śuklamālyānulepanaḥ ।। tasminnamaḥ savitre tu gandhadhūpau nivedayet ।। suvarṇena samāyuktaṃ mantreṇānena pūjayet ।। sarvasyāmṛtameva tvam ataḥ śāntiṃ prayaccha me ।।
saurasūktaṃ smarannāste purāṇaśravaṇena ca ।। tatsarvaṃ viduṣe tadvad brāhmaṇāya nivedayet ।। bhuñjītātailalavaṇaṃ svayamapyatha vāgyataḥ ।। saṃvatsarānte śayanaṃ śarkarākalaśānvitam ।।
gṛhaṃ ca śaktimāndadyāt samastopaskarānvitam ।। daśabhirvātha niṣkeṇa tadardhenāpi śaktitaḥ ।। na vittaśāṭhyaṃ kurvīta kurvandoṣaṃ samaśnute ।। nipeturye dharaṇyāṃ tu śālimudgekṣavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
iṣṭā raverataḥ puṇyā śarkarā havyakavyayoḥ ।। sarvaduṣṭapraśamanī putrapautrapravardhinī ।। kalpamekaṃ vasetsvarge tato yāti paraṃ padam ।। matimapi ca dadāti so api devair amaravadhūjanamālayābhipūjyaḥ ।।
yasyāḥ saṃkīrtanādeva tuṣyatīha divākaraḥ ।। tilapātre ca sauvarṇe vidhāya kamalaṃ śubham ।। namaḥ kamalahastāya namaste viśvadhāriṇe ।। tato dvikālavelāyām udakumbhasamanvitām ।।
śaktyā ca kapilāṃ dadyād alaṃkṛtya vidhānataḥ ।। yathāśaktyatha bhuñjīta māṃsatailavivarjitam ।। sarvaṃ samācaredbhaktyā vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ ।। gāṃ ca dadyātsvaśaktyā tu suvarṇāḍhyāṃ payasvinīm ।।
lakṣmīmanantāmabhyeti sūryaloke mahīyate ।। apsarobhiḥ parivṛtas tato yāti parāṃ gatim ।। so apyatra lakṣmīmacalāmavāpya gandharvavidyādharalokabhāksyāt ।। sarvakāmapradāṃ ramyāṃ nāmnā mandārasaptamīm ।।
dantakāṣṭhaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā ṣaṣṭhīmupavasedbudhaḥ ।। tataḥ prabhāta utthāya kṛtvā snānaṃ punardvijān ।। sauvarṇaṃ puruṣaṃ tadvat padmahastaṃ suśobhanam ।। haimamandārakusumair bhāskarāyeti pūrvataḥ ।।
dakṣiṇe tadvadarkāya tathāryamṇe ca nairṛte ।। pūṣṇetyuttarataḥ pūjyam ānandāyetyataḥ param ।। śuklavastraiḥ samāveṣṭya bhakṣyairmālyaphalādibhiḥ ।। bhuñjītātailalavaṇaṃ vāgyataḥ prāṅmukho gṛhī ।।
kuryātsaṃvatsaraṃ yāvad vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ ।। gobhirvibhavataḥ sārdhaṃ dātavyaṃ bhūtimicchatā ।। tvaṃ rave tārayasvāsmān saṃsārabhayasāgarāt ।। vipāpmā sa sukhī martyaḥ kalpaṃ ca divi modate ।।
