gacchanpragṛhya saṃsāre sarvārthāṃśca labhennaraḥ ।। yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। yāmupoṣya naro rogaśokaduḥkhaiḥ pramucyate ।। vācayitvā tato viprān ārabhecchubhasaptamīm ।।
tvāmahaṃ śubhakalyāṇaśarīrāṃ sarvasiddhaye ।। kāñcanaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ tadvad gandhamālyaguḍānvitaiḥ ।। dadyāddvikālavelāyām aryamā prīyatāmiti ।। tataḥ prabhāte saṃjāte bhaktyā sampūjayeddvijān ।।
vāsasā vṛṣabhaṃ haimaṃ tadvadgāṃ kāñcanodbhavām ।। sopadhānakaviśrāmaṃ bhājanāsanasaṃyutam ।। dadyādvedavide sarvaṃ viśvātmā prīyatāmiti ।। tasya śrīrvipulā kīrtir bhavejjanmani janmani ।।
kalpādāvavatīrṇastu saptadvīpādhipo bhavet ।। nāśāyālamiyaṃ puṇyā paṭhyate śubhasaptamī ।। so apyatra sarvāghavimuktadehaḥ prāpnoti vidyādharanāyakatvam ।। sa saptalokādhipatiḥ krameṇa bhūtvā padaṃ yāti paraṃ murāreḥ ।।
vibhavodbhavakāri bhūtale asmin bhavabhīterapi sūdanaṃ ca puṃsaḥ ।। tava bhaktimatastathāpi vakṣye vratamindrāsuramānaveṣu guhyam ।। daśamyāṃ laghubhugvidvān ārabhenniyamena tu ।। śriyaṃ vābhyarcya vidhivad bhokṣyāmi tvapare ahani ।।
śuklamālyāmbaradharaḥ pūjayecchrīśamutpalaiḥ ।। śrīśāya jānunī tadvad ūrū ca jalaśāyine ।। dāmodarāyetyudaraṃ pārśve ca vipulāya vai ।। śrīdharāya vibhorvakṣaḥ karau madhujite namaḥ ।।
vaikuṇṭhāya namaḥ kaṇṭham āsyaṃ yajñamukhāya vai ।। lalāṭaṃ vāmanāyeti haraye ca punarbhruvau ।। namaḥ sarvātmane tadvac chira ityabhipūjayet ।। tatastu maṇḍalaṃ kṛtvā sthaṇḍilaṃ kārayenmudā ।।
ślakṣṇaṃ hṛdyaṃ ca parito vapratrayasamāvṛtam ।। sthaṇḍilasyopariṣṭācca bhittiraṣṭāṅgulā bhavet ।। sthaṇḍile śūrpamāropya lakṣmīmityarcayedbudhaḥ ।। namaḥ puṣṭyai namastuṣṭyai vṛṣṭyai hṛṣṭyai namo namaḥ ।।
viśokā cāstu sampattyai viśokā sarvasiddhaye ।। vastrairnānāvidhaistadvat suvarṇakamalena ca ।। tatastu gītanṛtyādi kārayetsakalāṃ niśām ।। abhigamya ca viprāṇāṃ mithunāni tadārcayet ।।
śayanasthāni pūjyāni namo astu jalaśāyine ।। prabhāte ca tataḥ snānaṃ kṛtvā dāmpatyamarcayet ।। bhuktvā śrutvā purāṇāni taddinaṃ cātivāhayet ।। sopadhānakaviśrāmaṃ sāstarāvaraṇaṃ śubham ।।
tathā surūpatārogyam aśokaścāstu me sadā ।। tathā viśokatā me astu bhaktiragryā ca keśave ।। śūrpaṃ ca lakṣmyā sahitaṃ dātavyaṃ bhūtimicchatā ।। kadambaṃ kubjakaṃ jātiḥ śastānyetāni sarvadā ।।
kiṃrūpaṃ kena mantreṇa dātavyaṃ tadihocyatām ।। tadidānīṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvapāpavināśanam ।। gomayenānuliptāyāṃ darbhānāstīrya sarvataḥ ।। prāṅmukhīṃ kalpayeddhenum udakpādāṃ savatsakām ।।
vatsaṃ bhāreṇa kurvīta dvābhyāṃ vai madhyamā smṛtā ।। caturthāṃśena vatsaḥ syād gṛhavittānusārataḥ ।। śuktikarṇāvikṣupādau śucimuktāphalekṣaṇau ।। tāmragaṇḍakapṛṣṭhau tau sitacāmararomakau ।।
kṣaumapucchau kāṃsyadohāv indranīlakatārakau ।। ityevaṃ racayitvā tau dhūpadīpairathārcayet ।। dhenurūpeṇa sā devī mama śāntiṃ prayacchatu ।। dhenurūpeṇa sā devī mama pāpaṃ vyapohatu ।।
candrārkaśakraśaktiryā dhenurūpāstu sā śriye ।। lakṣmīryā lokapālānāṃ sā dhenurvaradāstu me ।। sarvapāpaharā dhenus tasmācchāntiṃ prayaccha me ।। vidhānametaddhenūnāṃ sarvāsām abhipaṭhyate ।।
tāsāṃ svarūpaṃ vakṣyāmi nāmāni ca narādhipa ।। tiladhenustṛtīyā tu caturthī jalasaṃjñitā ।। rasadhenuśca navamī daśamī syāt svarūpataḥ ।। suvarṇadhenumapyatra kecidicchanti bhānavaḥ ।।
etadevaṃvidhānaṃ syāt ta evopaskarāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। yathāśraddhaṃ pradātavyā bhuktimuktiphalapradāḥ ।। aśeṣayajñaphaladāḥ sarvāḥ pāpaharāḥ śubhāḥ ।। tadaṅgatvena caivātra guḍadhenuḥ praśasyate ।।
guḍadhenvādayo deyās tūparāgādiparvasu ।। yāmupoṣya naro yāti tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ।। vaiṣṇavaṃ puramāpnoti maraṇe ca smaranharim ।। na śokaduḥkhadaurgatyaṃ tasya saṃjāyate nṛpa ।।
nṛtyagītaparā nityaṃ sāpi tatphalamāpnuyāt ।। kartavyaṃ bhūtikāmena bhaktyā tu parayā nṛpa ।। matimāpa ca janānāṃ yo dadātīndraloke vasati sa vibudhaughaiḥ pūjyate kalpamekam ।। yadakṣayaṃ pare loke devarṣigaṇapūjitam ।।
yatpradānānnaro lokān āpnoti surapūjitān ।। na tatphalamadhīteṣu kṛteṣviha yadaśnute ।। prathamo dhānyaśailaḥ syād dvitīyo lavaṇācalaḥ ।। pañcamastilaśailaḥ syāt ṣaṣṭhaḥ kārpāsaparvataḥ ।।
rājato navamastadvad daśamaḥ śarkarācalaḥ ।। ayane viṣuve puṇye vyatīpāte dinakṣaye ।। vivāhotsavayajñeṣu dvādaśyāmatha vā punaḥ ।। dhānyaśailādayo deyā yathāśāstraṃ vijānatā ।।
prāgudakpravaṇaṃ tadvat prāṅmukhaṃ ca vidhānataḥ ।। tanmadhye parvataṃ kuryād viṣkambhaparvatānvitam ।। madhyamaḥ pañcaśatikaḥ kaniṣṭhaḥ syāt tribhiḥ śataiḥ ।। pūrveṇa muktāphalavajrayukto yāgyena gomedakapuṣparāgaiḥ ।।
śrīkhaṇḍakhaṇḍairabhitaḥ pravālair latānvitaḥ śuktiśilātalaḥ syāt ।। mūrdhanyavasthānamamatsareṇa kāryaṃ tvanekaiśca punardvijaughaiḥ ।। tathekṣuvaṃśāvṛtakandarastu ghṛtodakaprasravaṇaiśca dikṣu ।। vāsāṃsi paścādatha karburāṇi raktāni caivottarato ghanālī ।।
nānāphalālī ca samantataḥ syān manoramaṃ mālyavilepanaṃ ca ।। itthaṃ niveśyāmaraśailamagryaṃ merostu viṣkambhagirīn krameṇa ।। pūrveṇa mandaramanekaphalāvalībhir yuktaṃ yavaiḥ kanakabhadrakadambacihnaiḥ ।। kṣīrāruṇodasarasātha vanena caivaṃ raupyeṇa śaktighaṭitena virājamānam ।।
haimena yajñapatinā ghṛtamānasena vastraiśca rājatavanena ca saṃyutaḥ syāt ।। ākārayedrajatapuṣpavanena tadvad vastrānvitaṃ dadhisitodasaras tathāgre ।। puṣpaiśca hemavaṭapādapaśekharaṃ tam ākārayet kanakadhenuvirājamānam ।। homaścaturbhiratha vedapurāṇavidbhir dāntair anindyacaritākṛtibhirdvijendraiḥ ।।
rātrau ca jāgaramanuddhatagītatūryair āvāhanaṃ ca kathayāmi śiloccayānām ।। kṣemaṃ vidhatsva kuru śāntimanuttamāṃ naḥ sampūjitaḥ paramabhaktimatā mayā hi ।। mūrtāmūrtātparaṃ bījam ataḥ pāhi sanātana ।। rudrādityavasūnāṃ ca tasmācchāntiṃ prayaccha me ।।
tasmānmām uddharāśeṣaduḥkhasaṃsārasāgarāt ।। yasmāccaitrarathena tvaṃ bhadrāśvena ca varṣataḥ ।। yasmāccūḍāmaṇirjambūdvīpe tvaṃ gandhamādana ।। yasmāttvaṃ ketumālena vaibhrājena vanena ca ।।
uttaraiḥ kurubhiryasmāt sāvitreṇa vanena ca ।। evamāmantrya tānsarvān prabhāte vimale punaḥ ।। viṣkambhaparvatāndadyād ṛtvigbhyaḥ kramaśo mune ।। nava sapta tathāṣṭau vā pañca dadyād aśaktimān ।।
parvatānāmaśeṣāṇām eṣa eva vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।। grahāṇāṃ lokapālānāṃ brahmādīnāṃ ca sarvadā ।। upavāsī bhavennityam aśakte naktamiṣyate ।। dānakāle ca ye mantrāḥ parvateṣu ca yatphalam ।।
annādbhavanti bhūtāni jagadannena vartate ।। dhānyaparvatarūpeṇa pāhi tasmānnagottama ।। manvantaraśataṃ sāgraṃ devaloke mahīyate ।। dharmakṣaye rājarājyam āpnotīha na saṃśayaḥ ।।
yatpradānānnaro lokān āpnoti śivasaṃyutān ।। madhyamaḥ syāttadardhena caturbhiradhamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। caturthāṃśena viṣkambhaparvatānkārayetpṛthak ।। tadvaddhemamayānsarvāṃl lokapālānniveśayet ।।
kuryājjāgaraṇaṃ cāpi dānamantrānnibodhata ।। taddānakartṛkatvena tvaṃ māṃ pāhi nagottama ।। priyaṃ ca śivayornityaṃ tasmācchāntiṃ prayaccha me ।। tasmātparvatarūpeṇa pāhi saṃsārasāgarāt ।।
umāloke vasetkalpaṃ tato yāti parāṃ gatim ।। yatpradānānnaraḥ svargam āpnoti surapūjitam ।। tribhirbhāraiḥ kaniṣṭhaḥ syāt tadardhenālpavittavān ।। viṣkambhaparvatāṃstadvat sarāṃsi vanadevatāḥ ।।
dhānyaparvatavat kuryād imaṃ mantramudīrayet ।। sāmavedastu vedānāṃ mahādevastu yoginām ।। tathā rasānāṃ pravaraḥ sadaivekṣuraso mataḥ ।। nivāsaścāpi pārvatyās tasmācchāntiṃ prayaccha me ।।
pūjyamānaḥ sa gandharvair gaurīloke mahīyate ।। āyurārogyasampannaḥ śatrubhiścāparājitaḥ ।। yasya pradānādbhavanaṃ vairiñcaṃ yāti mānavaḥ ।। dadyādekapalādūrdhvaṃ yathāśaktyā vimatsaraḥ ।।
viṣkambhaśailāstadvacca ṛtvigbhyaḥ pratipādayet ।। yasmādanantaphaladas tasmātpāhi śiloccaya ।। hemaparvatarūpeṇa tasmātpāhi nagottama ।। tatra kalpaśataṃ tiṣṭhet tato yāti parāṃ gatim ।।
yatpradānānnaro yāti viṣṇulokaṃ sanātanam ।। tribhiḥ kaniṣṭho viprendra tilaśailaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। dānamantrān pravakṣyāmi yathāvanmunipuṃgava ।। tilāḥ kuśāśca māṣāśca tasmācchāntyai bhavatviha ।।
bhavāduddhara śailendra tilācala namo astu te ।। sa vaiṣṇavaṃ padaṃ yāti punarāvṛttidurlabham ।। pitṛbhirdevagandharvaiḥ pūjyamāno divaṃ vrajet ।। yatpradānānnaro nityam āpnoti paramaṃ padam ।।
bhāreṇālpadhano dadyād vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ ।। prabhātāyāṃ tu śarvaryāṃ dadyādidamudīrayet ।। kārpāsādre namastubhyam aghaughadhvaṃsano bhava ।। rudraloke vasetkalpaṃ tato rājā bhavediha ।।
tejo amṛtamayaṃ divyaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam ।। daśabhirmadhyamaḥ proktaḥ pañcabhistvadhamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। viṣkambhaparvatāṃstadvac caturbhāgeṇa kalpayet ।। kārayetsaṃhatānuccān yathāśobhaṃ vidhānataḥ ।।
dhānyaparvatavaccheṣaṃ vidhānamiha paṭhyate ।। viṣkambhaparvatāṃstadvad ṛtvigbhyaḥ śāntamānasaḥ ।। tasmāddhṛtārcirviśvātmā prīyatāmatra śaṃkaraḥ ।। ghṛtaparvatarūpeṇa tasmāttvaṃ pāhi no aniśam ।।
mahāpātakayukto api lokamāpnoti śāṃkaram ।। viharetpitṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam ।। muktāphalasahasreṇa parvataḥ syādanuttamaḥ ।। caturthāṃśena viṣkambhaparvatāḥ syuḥ samantataḥ ।।
padmarāgayutaḥ kāryo vidvadbhirgandhamādanaḥ ।। padmarāgaiḥ sasauvarṇair uttareṇa ca vinyaset ।। tadvadāvāhanaṃ kuryād vṛkṣāndevāṃśca kāñcanān ।। pūrvavadguruṛtvigbhya imānmantrānudīrayet ।।
tvaṃ ca ratnamayo nityaṃ namaste astu sadācala ।। sadā ratnapradānena tasmānnaḥ pāhi parvata ।। sa yāti viṣṇusālokyam amareśvarapūjitaḥ ।। rūpārogyaguṇopetaḥ saptadvīpādhipo bhavet ।।
tatsarvaṃ nāśamāyāti girirvajrahato yathā ।। yatpradānānnaro yāti somalokamanuttamam ।। pañcabhirmadhyamaḥ proktas tadardhenādhamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। viṣkambhaparvatāṃstadvat turīyāṃśena kalpayet ।।
kaladhautamayāṃstadval lokeśānarcayedbudhaḥ ।। rājataṃ syādyadanyeṣāṃ sarvaṃ tadiha kāñcanam ।। dadyāttataḥ prabhāte tu gurave raupyaparvatam ।। imaṃ mantraṃ paṭhandadyād darbhapāṇirvimatsaraḥ ।।
pāhi rājata tasmāttvaṃ śokasaṃsārasāgarāt ।। gavāmayutadānasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ ।। pūjyamāno vasedvidvān yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam ।। yasya pradānādviṣṇvarkarudrāstuṣyanti sarvadā ।।
caturbhirmadhyamaḥ prokto bhārābhyāmadhamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। viṣkambhaparvatānkuryāt turīyāṃśena mānavaḥ ।। merorupari tadvacca sthāpyaṃ hematarutrayam ।। etadvṛkṣatrayaṃ mūrdhni sarveṣvapi niyojayet ।।
niveśyau sarvaśaileṣu viśeṣāccharkarācale ।। gandhamādanaśṛṅge tu dhanadaḥ syādudaṅmukhaḥ ।। haimī supārśve surabhir dakṣiṇābhimukhī bhavet ।। ṛtvigbhyaś caturaḥ śailān imānmantrānudīrayan ।।
tasmādānandakārī tvaṃ bhava śailendra sarvadā ।। devānāṃ tatsamutthastvaṃ pāhi naḥ śarkarācala ।। tanmayo asi mahāśaila pāhi saṃsārasāgarāt ।। sarvapāpair vinirmuktaḥ sa yāti paramaṃ padam ।।
sahaiva yānamātiṣṭhet tatra viṣṇupracoditaḥ ।। āyurārogyasampanno yāvajjanmārbudatrayam ।। parvatopaskarānsarvān prāpayedbrāhmaṇālayam ।। suhṛcchakrasya nihatā yena daityāḥ sahasraśaḥ ।।
yathecchārūpadhārī ca manuṣyo apyaparājitaḥ ।। lakṣmīvad divyarūpeṇa nirjitāmarasundarī ।। daśanārīsahasrāṇāṃ madhye śrīriva rājate ।। vismayenāvṛto rājā vasiṣṭhamṛṣisattamam ।।
kasmācca vipulaṃ tejo maccharīre sadottamam ।। hemavṛkṣādibhiḥ sārdhaṃ yathāvadvidhipūrvakam ।। bhṛtyo līlāvatīgehe tena hemnā vinirmitāḥ ।। dharmakāryamiti jñātvā na gṛhṇāti kathaṃcana ।।
līlāvatī gireḥ pārśve paricaryāṃ ca pārthiva ।। sā ca līlāvatī veśyākālena mahatāpi ca ।। sarvapāpavinirmuktā jagāma śivamandiram ।। na maulyamādādveśyātaḥ sa bhavāniha sāmpratam ।।
samyagujjvālitāḥ patnyā seyaṃ bhānumatī tava ।। yasmātkṛtaṃ tatparikarma rātrāv anuddhatābhyāṃ lavaṇācalasya ।। tasmāttvamapyatra vidhānapūrvaṃ dhānyācalādīndaśadhā kuruṣva ।। dhānyācaladīñchataśo murārer lokaṃ jagāmāmarapūjyamānaḥ ।।
śṛṇoti bhaktyātha matiṃ dadāti vikalmaṣaḥ so api divaṃ prayāti ।। yaḥ kuryātkimu munipuṃgaveha samyak śāntātmā sakalagirīndrasampradānam ।। sarvakāmāptaye nityaṃ kathaṃ śāntikapauṣṭikam ।। yena brahmanvidhānena tanme nigadataḥ śṛṇu ।।
grahaśāntiṃ pravakṣyāmi purāṇaśruticoditām ।। grahāngrahādhidevāṃśca sthāpya homaṃ samārabhet ।। prathamo ayutahomaḥ syāl lakṣahomastataḥ param ।। ayutenāhutīnāṃ ca navagrahamakhaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
gartasyottarapūrveṇa vitastidvayavistṛtām ।। saṃsthāpanāya devānāṃ caturasrāmudaṅmukhām ।। devatānāṃ tataḥ sthāpyā viṃśatirdvādaśādhikā ।। rāhuḥ keturiti proktā grahā lokahitāvahāḥ ।।
uttareṇa guruṃ vidyād budhaṃ pūrvottareṇa tu ।। paścimottarataḥ ketuṃ sthāpayecchuklataṇḍulaiḥ ।। skandamaṅgārakasyāpi budhasya ca tathā harim ।। śanaiścarasya tu yamaṃ rāhoḥ kālaṃ tathaiva ca ।।
agnirāpaḥ kṣitirviṣṇur indra aindrī ca devatāḥ ।। āvāhayedvyāhṛtibhis tathaivāśvikumārakau ।। mandarāhū tathā kṛṣṇau dhūmraṃ ketugaṇaṃ viduḥ ।। śobhanaṃ sthāpayetprājñaḥ phalapuṣpasamanvitam ।।
aṅgārakāya saṃyāvaṃ budhāya kṣīraṣaṣṭike ।। citraudanaṃ ca ketubhyaḥ sarvabhakṣyairathārcayet ।। cūtapallavasaṃchannaṃ phalavastrayugānvitam ।। sthāpayedavraṇaṃ kumbhaṃ varuṇaṃ tatra vinyaset ।।
gajāśvarathyāvalmīkasaṃgamāddhradagokulāt ।। snānārthaṃ vinyasettatra yajamānasya dharmavit ।। āyāntu yajamānasya duritakṣayakārakāḥ ।। homaṃ samārabhetsarpir yavavrīhitilādinā ।।
audumbaraḥ śamī dūrvā kuśāśca samidhaḥ kramāt ।। hotavyā madhusarpirbhyāṃ dadhnā caiva samanvitāḥ ।। samidhaḥ kalpayetprājñaḥ sarvakarmasu sarvadā ।। svena svenaiva mantreṇa hotavyāḥ samidhaḥ pṛthak ।।
mantrairdaśāhutīrhutvā homaṃ vyāhṛtibhistataḥ ।। mantravantaśca kartavyāś caravaḥ pratidaivatam ।। ākṛṣṇeti ca sūryāya homaḥ kāryo dvijanmanā ।। agnirmūrdhā divo mantra iti bhaumāya kīrtayet ।।
bṛhaspate paridīyā ratheneti gurormataḥ ।। śanaiścarāyeti punaḥ śaṃ no devīti homayet ।। ketuṃ kṛṇvann api brūyāt ketūnāmapi śāntaye ।। āpo hi ṣṭhetyumāyāstu syoneti svāminastathā ।।
indram iddevatāteti indrāya juhuyāttataḥ ।। kālasya brahma jajñānam iti mantraḥ praśasyate ।। agniṃ dūtaṃ vṛṇīmaha iti vahnerudāhṛtaḥ ।। bhūmeḥ pṛthivyantarikṣam iti vedeṣu paṭhyate ।।
indrāyendo marutvata iti śakrasya śasyate ।। prajāpateḥ punarhomaḥ prajāpatiriti smṛtaḥ ।। eṣa brahmā ya ṛtvigbhya iti brahmaṇyudāhṛtaḥ ।। jātavedase sunavāma durgāmantro ayamucyate ।।
krāṇā śiśurmahīnāṃ ca vāyormantraḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। pūrṇāhutistu mūrdhānaṃ diva ityabhipātayet ।। pūrṇakumbhena tenaiva homānte prāgudaṅmukham ।। yajamānasya kartavyaṃ caturbhiḥ snapanaṃ dvijaiḥ ।।
pradyumnaścāniruddhaśca bhavantu vijayāya te ।। brahmaṇā sahitaḥ śeṣo dikpālāstvāmavantu te ।। etāstvāmabhiṣiñcantu dharmapatnyaḥ samāgatāḥ ।। grahāstvāmabhiṣiñcantu rāhuḥ ketuśca tarpitāḥ ।।
ṛṣayo munayo gāvo devamātara eva ca ।। astrāṇi sarvaśastrāṇi rājāno vāhanāni ca ।। ete tvāmabhiṣiñcantu sarvakāmārthasiddhaye ।। sarvauṣadhaiḥ sarvagandhaiḥ snāpito dvijapuṃgavaiḥ ।।
dakṣiṇābhiḥ prayatnena pūjayedgatavismayaḥ ।। raktaṃ dhuraṃdharaṃ dadyād bhaumāya ca kakudminam ।। śvetāśvaṃ daityagurave kṛṣṇāṃ gāmarkasūnave ।। suvarṇena samā kāryā yajamānena dakṣiṇā ।।
samantreṇaiva dātavyāḥ sarvāḥ sarvatra dakṣiṇāḥ ।। tīrthadevamayī yasmād ataḥ śāntiṃ prayaccha me ।। viṣṇunā vidhṛtaścāsi tataḥ śāntiṃ prayaccha me ।। aṣṭamūrteradhiṣṭhānam ataḥ śāntiṃ prayaccha me ।।
anantapuṇyaphaladam ataḥ śāntiṃ prayaccha me ।। pradānāttasya me viṣṇo hy ataḥ śāntiṃ prayaccha me ।। candrārkavāhano nityam ataḥ śāntiṃ prayaccha me ।। sarvapāpaharā nityam ataḥ śāntiṃ prayaccha me ।।
lāṅgalādyāyudhādīni tasmācchāntiṃ prayaccha me ।। yānaṃ vibhāvasornityam ataḥ śāntiṃ prayaccha me ।। yasmāttasmācchriye me syād iha loke paratra ca ।। śayyā mamāpyaśūnyāstu dattā janmani janmani ।।
tathā ratnāni yacchantu ratnadānena me surāḥ ।। dānānyanyāni me śāntir bhūmidānādbhavatviha ।। ratnakāñcanavastraughair dhūpamālyānulepanaiḥ ।। sarvānkāmānavāpnoti pretya svarge mahīyate ।।
taṃ ca yatnena sampūjya śeṣānapyarcayedbudhaḥ ।। pūjitāḥ pūjayantyete nirdahantyavamānitāḥ ।। tadvaddaivopaghātānāṃ śāntirbhavati vāraṇam ।। sampūrṇayā dakṣiṇayā yasmādeko api tuṣyati ।।
vivāhotsavayajñeṣu pratiṣṭhādiṣu karmasu ।। kathito ayutahomo ayaṃ lakṣahomamataḥ śṛṇu ।। pitṝṇāṃ vallabhaṃ sākṣād bhuktimuktiphalapradam ।। gṛhasyottarapūrveṇa maṇḍapaṃ kārayedbudhaḥ ।।
daśahastamathāṣṭau vā hastānkuryādvidhānataḥ ।। prāguttaraṃ samāsādya pradeśaṃ maṇḍapasya tu ।। caturasraṃ samantāttu yonivaktraṃ samekhalam ।। prāgudakplavanā kāryā sarvataḥ samavasthitā ।।
yasmāttasmāt susampūrṇaṃ śāntikuṇḍaṃ vidhīyate ।। āhutībhiḥ prayatnena dakṣiṇābhistathaiva ca ।। lakṣahome bhavetkuṇḍaṃ yonivaktraṃ trimekhalam ।। prāgudakplavanaṃ tacca caturasraṃ samantataḥ ।।
saṃsthāpanāya devānāṃ vapratrayasamāvṛtam ।। aṅgulocchrayasaṃyuktaṃ vapradvayamathopari ।। tasminnāvāhayeddevān pūrvavatpuṣpataṇḍulaiḥ ।। sthāpanīyā muniśreṣṭha nottareṇa parāṅmukhāḥ ।।
viṣapāpaharo nityam ataḥ śāntiṃ prayaccha me ।। ghṛtakumbhavasordhārāṃ pātayedanalopari ।। ghṛtadhārāṃ tayā samyag agnerupari pātayet ।। mahāvaiśvānaraṃ sāma jyeṣṭhasāma ca vācayet ।।
dātavyā yajamānena pūrvavaddakṣiṇāḥ pṛthak ।। navagrahamakhe viprāś catvāro vedavedinaḥ ।। kāryāvayutahome tu na prasajyeta vistare ।। kartavyāḥ śaktitastadvac catvāro vā vimatsaraḥ ।।
bhakṣyāndadyānmuniśreṣṭha bhūṣaṇānyapi śaktitaḥ ।। karṇāṅgulipavitrāṇi kaṇṭhasūtrāṇi śaktimān ।। adadallobhato mohāt kulakṣayam avāpnute ।। annahīnaḥ kṛto yasmād durbhikṣaphalado bhavet ।।
yaṣṭāraṃ dakṣiṇāhīnaṃ nāsti yajñasamo ripuḥ ।। yasmātpīḍākaro nityaṃ yajñe bhavati vigrahaḥ ।। dakṣiṇābhiḥ prayatnena na bahūnalpavittavān ।। yataḥ sarvānavāpnoti kurvankāmānvidhānataḥ ।।
yāvatkalpaśatānyaṣṭāv atha mokṣamavāpnuyāt ।। sa taṃ kāmamavāpnoti padamānantyam aśnute ।। bhāryārthī śobhanāṃ bhāryāṃ kumārī ca śubhaṃ patim ।। niṣkāmaḥ kurute yastu sa paraṃ brahma gacchati ।।
āhutībhiḥ prayatnena dakṣiṇābhiḥ phalena ca ।। kuṇḍamaṇḍapavedīnāṃ viśeṣo ayaṃ nibodha me ।। yonivaktradvayopetaṃ tadapyāhus trimekhalam ।। tryaṅgulābhyucchritā tadvad dvitīyā parikīrtitā ।।
dvyaṅgulaśceti vistāraḥ pūrvayoreva śasyate ।। kūrmapṛṣṭhonnatā madhye pārśvayoścāṅgulocchritā ।। etatsarveṣu kuṇḍeṣu yonilakṣaṇamucyate ।। vedī ca koṭihome syād vitastīnāṃ catuṣṭayam ।।
vaprapramāṇaṃ pūrvoktaṃ vedīnāṃ ca tathocchrayaḥ ।। pūrvadvāre ca saṃsthāpya bahvṛcaṃ vedapāragam ।। atharvavedinaṃ tadvad uttare sthāpayedbudhaḥ ।। pūrvavatpūjayedbhaktyā vastrābharaṇabhūṣaṇaiḥ ।।
pūrvato bahvṛcaḥ śāntiṃ paṭhannāste hyudaṅmukhaḥ ।। pāṭhayeddakṣiṇadvāri yajurvedinamuttamam ।। jyeṣṭhamāsa tathā śāntiṃ chandogaḥ paścime japet ।। pauṣṭikaṃ ca mahārājyam uttareṇāpyatharvavit ।।
snāne dāne ca mantrāḥ syus ta eva munisattama ।। sarvānkāmānavāpnoti tato viṣṇupadaṃ vrajet ।। sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā padamindrasya gacchati ।। kṛtvā yatphalamāpnoti kauṭihomāt tadaśnute ।।
koṭihomena naśyanti yathāvacchivabhāṣitam ।। navagrahamakhaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ kāmyaṃ samācaret ।। tasmādayutahomasya vidhānaṃ pūrvamācaret ।। trimekhalaṃ caikavaktram aratnirvistareṇa tu ।।
candanāguruṇā tadvat kuṅkumenābhiṣiñcitāḥ ।। sahasrāṇi daśaivoktaṃ sarvadaiva svayambhuvā ।। sumitriyā na āpa oṣadhaya iti homayet ।। snānaṃ sarvauṣadhaiḥ kṛtvā śuklapuṣpāmbaro gṛhī ।।
sūkṣmavastrāṇi deyāni śuklā gāvaḥ sakāñcanāḥ ।। amitrāṇyapi mitrāṇi homo ayaṃ pāpanāśanaḥ ।। dvimekhalaṃ koṇamukhaṃ hastamātraṃ ca sarvaśaḥ ।। nivītalohitoṣṇīṣā lohitāmbaradhāriṇaḥ ।।
hotavyā muktakeśaistu dhyāyadbhiraśivaṃ ripau ।। śyenābhicāramantreṇa kṣuraṃ samabhimantrya ca ।। ripurūpasya śakalān yathaivāgnau viniṣkṣipet ।। vidveṣaṇaṃ tathā kurvan netadeva samācaret ।।
tasmācchāntikamevātra kartavyaṃ bhūtimicchatā ।। sa viṣṇoḥ padamāpnoti punarāvṛttidurlabham ।। na tasya grahapīḍā syān na ca bandhujanakṣayaḥ ।। na pīḍā tatra bālānāṃ na rogo na ca bandhanam ।।
koṭihomaṃ viduḥ prājñā bhuktimuktiphalapradam ।। dvādaśāhamakhas tadvan navagrahamakhaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। paripaṭhati ya itthaṃ yaḥ śṛṇoti prasaṅgād abhibhavati sa śatrūnāyurārogyayuktaḥ ।। saptāśvaḥ saptarajjuśca dvibhujaḥ syātsadā raviḥ ।।
gadāpāṇirdvibāhuśca kartavyo varadaḥ śaśī ।। caturbhujaḥ śvetaromā varadaḥ syād dharāsutaḥ ।। khaḍgacarmagadāpāṇiḥ siṃhastho varado budhaḥ ।। daṇḍinau varadau kāryau sākṣasūtrakamaṇḍalū ।।
bāṇabāṇāsanadharaḥ kartavyo arkasutas tathā ।। nīlasiṃhāsanasthaśca rāhuratra praśasyate ।। gṛdhrāsanagatā nityaṃ ketavaḥ syurvarapradāḥ ।। svāṅgulenocchritāḥ sarve śatamaṣṭottaraṃ sadā ।।
bhuktimuktiphalāyālaṃ tatpunar vaktumarhasi ।। matsamastapasā brahman purāṇaśrutivistaraiḥ ।। dharmānmāheśvarān vakṣyat yataḥprabhṛti nārada ।। ādiṣṭastvaṃ śiveneha vada māheśvaraṃ vratam ।।
triṣu lokeṣu vikhyātā nāmnā śivacaturdaśī ।। prārthayeddevadeveśaṃ tvāmahaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।। suvarṇavṛṣabhaṃ dattvā bhokṣyāmi ca pare ahani ।। pūjayetkamalaiḥ śubhrair gandhamālyānulepanaiḥ ।।
trinetrāyeti netrāṇi lalāṭaṃ haraye namaḥ ।। sadyojātāya karṇau tu vāmadevāya vai bhujau ।। stanau tatpuruṣāyeti tatheśānāya codaram ।। ūrū cānantavairāgyasiṃhāyetyabhipūjayet ।।
pradhānāya namo jaṅghe gulphau vyomātmane namaḥ ।। namaḥ puṣṭyai namastuṣṭyai pārvatīṃ cāpi pūjayet ।। bhakṣyairnānāvidhairyuktaṃ brāhmaṇāya nivedayet ।। pṛṣadājyaṃ ca saṃprāśya svapedbhūmāvudaṅmukhaḥ ।।
tadvatkṛṣṇacaturdaśyām etatsarvaṃ samācaret ।। ye tu māse viśeṣāḥ syus tānnibodha kramādiha ।। śaṃkarāya namaste astu namaste karavīraka ।। namaste astu mahādeva sthāṇave ca tataḥ param ।।
namaste paramānanda namaḥ somārdhadhāriṇe ।। gomūtraṃ gomūyaṃ kṣīraṃ dadhi sarpiḥ kuśodakam ।। pratimāsaṃ caturdaśyor ekaikaṃ prāśanaṃ smṛtam ।। sinduvārairaśokaiśca mallikābhiśca pāṭalaiḥ ।।
ekaikena caturdaśyor arcayetpārvatīpatim ।। annair nānāvidhair bhakṣyair vastramālyavibhūṣaṇaiḥ ।। umāmaheśvaraṃ haimaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ ca gavā saha ।। sarvopaskarasaṃyuktāṃ śayyāṃ dadyāt sakumbhakām ।।
sthāpya viprāya śāntāya vedavrataparāya ca ।। guṇajñe śrotriye dadyād ācārye tattvavedini ।। sapatnīkāya sampūjya vastramālyavibhūṣaṇaiḥ ।। na vittaśāṭhyaṃ kurvīta kurvandoṣātpatatyadhaḥ ।।
so aśvamedhasahasrasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ ।। pitṛbhirbhrātṛbhirvāpi tatsarvaṃ nāśamāpnuyāt ।। gaṇādhipatyaṃ divi kalpakoṭiśatānyuṣitvā padameti śambhoḥ ।। na ca siddhagaṇo apyalaṃ na cāhaṃ yadi jihvāyutakoṭayo api vaktre ।।
imāṃ śivacaturdaśīmamarakāminīkoṭayaḥ stuvanti tamaninditaṃ kimu samācaredyaḥ sadā ।। sāpi prasādātparameśvarasya paraṃ padaṃ yāti pinākapāṇeḥ ।। yadakṣayaṃ paraṃ loke sarvakāmaphalapradam ।। ārabhecchuklapakṣasya kṛtvā brāhmaṇavācanam ।।
sadakṣiṇaṃ pāyasena bhojayecchaktito dvijān ।। savṛṣaṃ kāñcanaṃ rudraṃ dharmarājaṃ ca kārayet ।। āmrātakaṃ kapitthāni kaliṅgamatha vālukam ।। kāśmaraṃ dāḍimaṃ śaktyā kāladhautāni ṣoḍaśa ।।
kaṅkolailākatuṇḍīrakarīrakuṭajaṃ śamī ।। raupyāṇi kārayecchaktyā phalānīmāni ṣoḍaśa ।। piṇḍārakāśmaryaphalaṃ tathā sūraṇakandakam ।। citravallīphalaṃ tadvat kūṭaśālmalijaṃ phalam ।।
tāmrāṇi ṣoḍaśaitāni kārayecchaktito naraḥ ।। tataśca kārayecchayyāṃ yathopari suvāsasī ।। sapatnīkāya sampūjya puṇye ahni vinivedayet ।। tathā sarvaphalatyāgavratādbhaktiḥ śive astu me ।।
tadyuktaphaladānena tau syātāṃ me varapradau ।। tathānantaphalāvāptir astu janmani janmani ।। tathā mamāstu viśvātmā śaṃkaraḥ śaṃkaraḥ sadā ।। śaktiścecchayanaṃ dadyāt sarvopaskarasaṃyutam ।।
tathodakumbhasaṃyuktau śivadharmau ca kāñcanau ।। anyānyapi yathāśaktyā bhojayecchaktito dvijān ।। śubhaṃ sarvaphalatyāgavrataṃ vedavido viduḥ ।। vratamasti muniśreṣṭha yadanantaphalapradam ।।
tāvadyugasahasrāṇi rudraloke mahīyate ।। janmāntareṣvapi na putraviyogaduḥkham āpnoti dhāma ca puraṃdaralokajuṣṭam ।। pāpairviyuktavapuratra puraṃ murārer ānandakṛtpadamupaiti munīndra so api ।। yacchāntaye ca martyānāṃ vada nandīśa tadvratam ।।
sūryāgnicandrarūpeṇa tattridhā jagati sthitam ।। tasmādādityavāreṇa sadā naktāśano bhavet ।। tadā śanidine kuryād ekabhaktaṃ vimatsaraḥ ।। pattrairdvādaśasaṃyuktaṃ raktacandanapaṅkajam ।।
divākaraṃ tathāgneye vivasvantamataḥ param ।। mahendramanile tadvad ādityaṃ ca tathottare ।। karṇikāpūrvapattre tu sūryasya turagānnyaset ।। uttare tu raviṃ devaṃ karṇikāyāṃ ca bhāskaram ।।
tasminpadme tato dadyād imaṃ mantramudīrayet ।। yasmādagnīndrarūpastvam ataḥ pāhi divākara ।। agna āyāhi varada namaste jyotiṣāṃ pate ।। puruṣaṃ ca yathāśaktyā kārayeddvibhujaṃ tathā ।।
pūrṇe guḍasyopari tāmrapātre nidhāya padmaṃ puruṣaṃ ca dadyāt ।। avyaṅgarūpāya jitendriyāya kuṭumbine deyamanuddhatāya ।। sāmargyajurdhāmanidhe vidhātre bhavābdhipotāya jagatsavitre ।। so adhirohati vinaṣṭakalmaṣaḥ sūryadhāma dhutacāmarāvaliḥ ।।
dvīpasaptakapatiḥ punaḥ punar varmamūrtir amitaujasā yutaḥ ।। sāpi lokamamareśavanditā yāti nārada raverna saṃśayaḥ ।। so api śakrabhuvanasthito amaraiḥ pūjyate vasati cākṣayaṃ divi ।। yadakṣayaṃ pare loke sarvakāmaphalapradam ।।
saṃkrāntivāsare prātas tilaiḥ snānaṃ vidhīyate ।। padmaṃ sakarṇikaṃ kuryāt tasminnāvāhayedravim ।। nama uṣṇārciṣe yāmye namo ṛṅmaṇḍalāya ca ।। vāyavye tu bhagaṃ nyasya punaḥ punarathārcayet ।।
gandhamālyaphalairbhakṣyaiḥ sthaṇḍile pūjayettataḥ ।। kamalaṃ ca yathāśaktyā kārayitvā nivedayet ।। namo ananta namo dhātre ṛksāmayajuṣāṃ pate ।। vatsarānte athavā kuryāt sarvaṃ dvādaśadhā naraḥ ।।
kumbhānpunardvādaśa dhenuyuktān saratnahairaṇmayapadmayuktān ।। daurgatyayuktaḥ kapilāmathaikāṃ nivedayedbrāhmaṇapuṃgavāya ।। na vittaśāṭhyaṃ puruṣo atra kuryāt kurvannadho yāti na saṃśayo atra ।। tāvatsa gandharvagaṇair aśeṣaiḥ sampūjyate nārada nākapṛṣṭhe ।।
sṛṣṭermukhe avyaṅgavapuḥ sabhāryaḥ prabhūtaputrānvayavanditāṅghriḥ ।। matimapi ca dadāti so api devair amarapaterbhavane prapūjyate ca ।। vibhūtidvādaśī nāma sarvadevanamaskṛtam ।। kṛtvā sāyantanīṃ saṃdhyāṃ gṛhṇīyānniyamaṃ budhaḥ ।।
dvādaśyāṃ dvijasaṃyuktaḥ kariṣye bhojanaṃ vibho ।। namo nārāyaṇāyeti vācyaṃ ca svapatā niśi ।। pūjayetpuṇḍarīkākṣaṃ śuklamālyānulepanaiḥ ।। namaḥ śivāyetyūrū ca viśvamūrte namaḥ kaṭim ।।
dāmodarāyetyudaraṃ vāsudevāya ca stanau ।। śrīdharāya mukhaṃ keśān keśavāyeti nārada ।। śiraḥ sarvātmane brahman nama ityabhipūjayet ।। udakumbhasamāyuktam agrataḥ sthāpayedbudhaḥ ।।
rātrau jāgaraṇaṃ kuryād itihāsakathādinā ।। sakāñcanotpalaṃ devaṃ sodakumbhaṃ nivedayet ।। tathā māmuddharāśeṣaduḥkhasaṃsārakardamāt ।। dadyādevaṃ samā yāvat pāṣaṇḍānabhivarjayet ।।
śayyāṃ dadyānmuniśreṣṭha gurave dhenusaṃyutām ।। guruṃ sampūjya vidhivad vastrālaṃkārabhūṣaṇaiḥ ।। alpavitto yathāśaktyā stokaṃ stokaṃ samācaret ।। puṣpārcanavidhānena sa kuryādvatsaradvayam ।।
kuryātpāpavinirmuktaḥ pitṝṇāṃ tārayecchatam ।। vaiṣṇavo vātha śaivo vā bhavejjanmani janmani ।। tāvatsvarge vasedbrahman bhūpatiśca punarbhavet ।। nāmnā lokeṣu vikhyātas tejasā sūryasaṃnibhaḥ ।।
kamalaṃ kāñcanaṃ dattaṃ yathākāmagamaṃ mune ।। dvīpāni suralokaṃ ca yatheṣṭaṃ vyacarattadā ।। loke ca pūjitaṃ yasmāt puṣkaradvīpamucyate ।। puṣpavāhanamityāhus tasmāttaṃ devadānavāḥ ।।
nāmnā ca lāvaṇyavatī babhūva sā pārvatīveṣṭatamā bhavasya ।। so abhyāgataṃ vīkṣya munipravīraṃ prācetasaṃ vākyamidaṃ babhāṣe ।। bhāryā mamālpatapasā paritoṣitena dattaṃ mamāmbujagṛhaṃ ca munīndra dhātrā ।। no lakṣyate kva gatamambaramadhya indus tārāgaṇairiva gataḥ paritaḥ sphuradbhiḥ ।।
bhagavanmayātha tanayair athavānayāpi bhadraṃ yadetadakhilaṃ kathaya pracetaḥ ।। janmābhavattava tu lubdhakule atighore jātastvamapyanudinaṃ kila pāpakārī ।। na ca te suhṛn na sutabandhujano na tātas tv ādṛksvasā na jananī ca tadābhiśastā ।। kṣutpīḍitenātha tadā na kiṃcid āsāditaṃ dhānyaphalāmiṣādyam ।।
padmānyathādāya tato bahūni gataḥ puraṃ vaidiśanāmadheyam ।। kretā na kaścitkamaleṣu jātaḥ śrānto bhṛśaṃ kṣutparipīḍitaśca ।। atha maṅgalaśabdaśca tvayā rātrau mahāñśrutaḥ ।। tatra maṇḍapamadhyasthā viṣṇorarcāvalokitā ।।
samāptau māghamāsasya lavaṇācalamuttamam ।। alaṃkṛtya hṛṣīkeśaṃ sauvarṇāmarapādapam ।। kimebhiḥ kamalaiḥ kāryaṃ varaṃ viṣṇuralaṃkṛtaḥ ।। śayyā ca puṣpaprakaraiḥ pūjitā bhūśca sarvataḥ ।।
dīyatāmādideśātha kaladhautaśatatrayam ।। ānīya vyāhṛtaṃ cātra bhujyatāmiti bhūpate ।। prasaṅgādupavāsena tavādya sukhamāvayoḥ ।। tatprasaṅgāttayormadhye dharmaleśastu te anagha ।।
prabhāte ca tadā dattā śayyā salavaṇācalā ।। vastrālaṃkārasaṃyuktā gāvaśca karakānvitāḥ ।। tacca lubdhakadāmpatyaṃ pūjayitvā visarjitam ।। puṣkaraprakarāttasmāt keśavasya na pūjanāt ।।
tasya sattvasya māhātmyād alpena tapasā nṛpa ।। saṃtuṣṭastava rājendra brahmarūpī janārdanaḥ ।। lokeṣvānandajananī sakalāmarapūjitā ।। kuru rājendra nirvāṇam avaśyaṃ samavāpsyasi ।।
rājā yathoktaṃ ca punar akarotpuṣpavāhanaḥ ।। yathākathaṃcit kamalair dvādaśa dvādaśīr mune ।। na vittaśāṭhyaṃ kurvīta bhaktyā tuṣyati keśavaḥ ।। iti kaluṣatridāraṇaṃ janānāmapi paṭhatīha śṛṇoti cātha bhaktyā ।
matimapi ca dadāti devaloke vasati sa koṭiśatāni vatsarāṇām ।। rudreṇābhihitāṃ divyāṃ mahāpātakanāśanam ।। haimaṃ cakraṃ triśūlaṃ ca dadyādviprāya vāsasī ।। etaddevavrataṃ nāma mahāpātakanāśanam ।।
etadrudravrataṃ nāma pāpaśokavināśanam ।। sa vaiṣṇavaṃ padaṃ yāti līlāvratamidaṃ smṛtam ।। jane prītikaraṃ nṝṇāṃ prītivratamihocyate ।। dadyādvastrāṇi sūkṣmāṇi rasapātraiśca saṃyutam ।।
etadgaurīvrataṃ nāma bhavānīlokadāyakam ।। aśokaṃ kāñcanaṃ dadyād ikṣuyuktaṃ daśāṅgulam ।। etat kāmavrataṃ nāma sadā śokavināśanam ।। vārtākaṃ ca caturmāsaṃ madhusarpirghaṭānvitam ।।
sa rudralokamāpnoti śivavratamidaṃ smṛtam ।। puṣpatrayaṃ ca phālgunyāṃ kṛtvā śaktyā ca kāñcanam ।। dattvā paraṃ padaṃ yāti saumyavratamidaṃ smṛtam ।। samāpte śayanaṃ dadyād gṛhaṃ copaskarānvitam ।।
gaurīloke vasetkalpaṃ saubhāgyavratamucyate ।। vastrayugmaṃ tilānghaṇṭāṃ brāhmaṇāya nivedayet ।। etatsārasvataṃ nāma rūpavidyāpradāyakam ।। samānte hemakamalaṃ dadyāddhenusamanvitam ।।
etat sampadvrataṃ nāma sadā pāpavināśanam ।। yāvadabdaṃ punardadyād dhenuṃ jalaghaṭānvitām ।। etad āyurvrataṃ nāma sarvakāmapradāyakam ।। ekabhaktaṃ naraḥ kuryād abdamekaṃ vimatsaraḥ ।।
etat kīrtivrataṃ nāma bhūtikīrtiphalapradam ।। akṣatābhiḥ supuṣpābhiḥ kṛtvā gomayamaṇḍalam ।। sāmagāya tataścaitat sāmavratamihocyate ।। bhojayitvāsanaṃ dadyād dhaimakañcukavāsasī ।।
etadvīravrataṃ nāma nārīṇāṃ ca sukhapradam ।। samānte śrāddhakṛddadyāt pañca gāstu payasvinīḥ ।। kalpānte rājarājaḥ syāt pitṛvratam idaṃ smṛtam ।। vratānte maṇikaṃ dadyād annavastrasamanvitam ।।
kalpānte bhūpatirnūnam ānandavratamucyate ।। vatsarānte punardadyād dhenuṃ pañcāmṛtena hi ।। rājā bhavati kalpānte dhṛtivratamidaṃ smṛtam ।। ahiṃsāvratamityuktaṃ kalpānte bhūpatirbhavet ।।
sūryaloke vasetkalpaṃ sūryavratamidaṃ smṛtam ।। sa vaiṣṇavaṃ padaṃ yāti viṣṇuvratamidaṃ śubham ।। tadante puṣpadāmāni ghṛtadhenvā sahaiva tu ।। etacchīlavrataṃ nāma śīlārogyaphalapradam ।।
samānte dīpikāṃ dadyāc cakraśūle ca kāñcane ।। rudralokamavāpnoti dīptivratamidaṃ smṛtam ।। naktaṃ caredabdamekam abdānte goprado bhavet ।। etadrudravrataṃ nāma sadā kalyāṇakārakam ।।
vāruṇaṃ padamāpnoti dṛḍhavratamidaṃ smṛtam ।। etatkāntivrataṃ nāma kāntikīrtiphalapradam ।। tryahaṃ tilaprado bhūtvā vahniṃ saṃtarpya sadvijam ।। śaktitastripalādūrdhvaṃ viśvātmā prīyatāmiti ।।
etadbrahmavrataṃ nāma nirvāṇapadadāyakam ।। etaddhenuvrataṃ nāma punarāvṛttidurlabham ।। dattvā brahmapadaṃ yāti kalpavratamidaṃ smṛtam ।। sa vaiṣṇavaṃ padaṃ yati bhīmavratamidaṃ smṛtam ।।
dharāvratamidaṃ proktaṃ saptakalpaśatānugam ।। mahāvratamidaṃ nāma paramānandakārakam ।। kalpānte rājarājaḥ syāt prabhāvratamidaṃ smṛtam ।। śivaloke vasetkalpaṃ prāptivratamidaṃ smṛtam ।।
pauraṃdaraṃ puraṃ yāti sugativratamucyate ।। vaiśvānaravrataṃ nāma sarvapāpavināśanam ।। etat kṛṣṇavrataṃ nāma kalpānte rājyabhāgbhavet ।। lakṣmīlokamavāpnoti hy etad devīvrataṃ smṛtam ।।
sūryalokamavāpnoti bhānuvratamidaṃ smṛtam ।। vrataṃ vaināyakaṃ nāma śivalokaphalapradam ।। etat phalavrataṃ nāma viṣṇulokaphalapradam ।। etat sauravrataṃ nāma sūryalokaphalapradam ।।
paramaṃ padaṃ prāpnoti viṣṇuvratamidaṃ smṛtam ।। śaivaṃ padamavāpnoti vārṣavratamidaṃ smṛtam ।। viprāṇāṃ śāṃkaraṃ yāti prājāpatyamidaṃ vratam ।। śaivaṃ padamavāpnoti traiyambakamidaṃ vratam ।।
ghṛtavratamidaṃ prāhur brahmalokaphalapradam ।। śakraloke vasennityam indravratamidaṃ smṛtam ।। iha cānandakṛtpuṃsāṃ śreyovratamidaṃ smṛtam ।। kalpānte rājarājaḥ syād aśvavratamidaṃ smṛtam ।।
bhavedupoṣito bhūtvā karivratamidaṃ smṛtam ।। yakṣādhipatyamāpnoti sukhavratamidaṃ smṛtam ।। vāruṇaṃ lokamāpnoti varuṇavratamucyate ।। candravratamidaṃ proktaṃ candralokaphalapradam ।।
yātyaṣṭamīcaturdaśyo rudravratamidaṃ smṛtam ।। samānte dhenudo yāti bhavānīvratamucyate ।। divi kalpamuṣitveha rājā syātpavanaṃ vratam ।। ādityalokamāpnoti dhāmavratamidaṃ smṛtam ।।
annaṃ gāśca samāpnoti mokṣamindravratādiha ।। kalpānte rājarājaḥ syāt somavratamidaṃ smṛtam ।। vaiśvānarapadaṃ yāti śivavratamidaṃ smṛtam ।। etad viśvavrataṃ nāma mahāpātakanāśanam ।।
manvantaraśataṃ so api gandharvādhipatirbhavet ।। śrotuṃ tavecchā tadudīrayāmi priyeṣu kiṃ vākathanīyam asti ।। tasmānmanoviśuddhyarthaṃ snānamādau vidhīyate ।। namo nārāyaṇāyeti mūlamantra udāhṛtaḥ ।।
prakalpyāvāhayed gaṅgām ebhirmantrairvicakṣaṇaḥ ।। pāhi nas tvenasas tasmād ājanmamaraṇāntikāt ।। divi bhuvyantarikṣe ca tāni te santi jāhnavi ।। dakṣā pṛthvī ca vihagā viśvakāyāmṛtā śivā ।।
kṣemā ca jāhnavī caiva śāntā śāntipradāyinī ।। bhavetsaṃnihitā tatra gaṅgā tripathagāminī ।। snānaṃ kuryānmṛdā tadvad āmantrya tu vidhānataḥ ।। mṛttike hara me pāpaṃ yanmayā duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam ।।
āruhya mama gātrāṇi sarvaṃ pāpaṃ pracodaya ।। namaste sarvalokānāṃ prabhavāraṇi suvrate ।। tatastu tarpaṇaṃ kuryāt trailokyāpyāyanāya vai ।। krūrāḥ sarpāḥ suparṇāśca taravo jambukāḥ khagāḥ ।।
nirādhārāśca ye jīvā ye tu dharmaratāstathā ।। kṛtopavītī devebhyo nivītī ca bhavettataḥ ।। sanakaśca sanandaśca tṛtīyaśca sanātanaḥ ।। sarve te tṛptimāyāntu maddattenāmbunā sadā ।।
devabrahmaṛṣīn sarvāṃs tarpayed akṣataudakaiḥ ।। agniṣvāttāstathā saumyā haviṣmantastathoṣmapāḥ ।। saṃtarpyāḥ pitaro bhaktyā satilodakacandanaiḥ ।। vaivasvatāya kālāya sarvabhṛtakṣayāya ca ।।
darbhapāṇistu vidhinā pitṝnsaṃtarpayedbudhaḥ ।। saṃtarpya vidhinā bhaktyā imaṃ mantramudīrayet ।। te tṛptimakhilāṃ yāntu yaś cāsmatto abhivāñchati ।। arghyaṃ dadyātprayatnena sūryanāmāni kīrtayet ।।
sahasraraśmaye nityaṃ namaste sarvatejase ।। jagatsvāminnamaste astu divyacandanabhūṣita ।। namaste sarvalokeśa jagatsarvaṃ vibodhase ।। satyadeva namaste astu prasīda mama bhāskara ।।
dvijaṃ gāṃ kāñcanaṃ spṛṣṭvā tato viṣṇugṛhaṃ vrajet ।। mārkaṇḍeyena kathitaṃ yatpurā pāṇḍusūnave ।। etasminnantare rājā kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।। āsītsuyodhano rājā ekādaśacamūpatiḥ ।।
vāsudevaṃ samāśritya pañca śeṣāstu pāṇḍavāḥ ।। duryodhanaṃ ca rājānaṃ putrabhrātṛsamanvitam ।। kiṃ no rājyena govinda kiṃ bhogairjīvitena vā ।। nirviceṣṭo nirutsāhaḥ kiṃcit tiṣṭhatyadhomukhaḥ ।।
kataro viniyogo vā niyamaṃ tīrthameva ca ।। yatra sthitvā naro yāti viṣṇulokamanuttamam ।। dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ kathaṃ pṛcche yasya putraśataṃ hatam ।। rudanti pāṇḍavāḥ sarve bhrātṛśokapariplutāḥ ।।
bhūmau nipatitāḥ sarve rudantastu samantataḥ ।। yathā vaiklavyamāpanno rudamānastu duḥkhitaḥ ।। samprāpto hāstinapuraṃ rājadvāre hyatiṣṭhata ।। tvarito dharmaputrastu dvāramāgādataḥ param ।।
adya me saphalaṃ janma adya me tāritaṃ kulam ।। adyāhaṃ pūtadeho asmi yattvayā saha darśanam ।। yudhiṣṭhiro mahātmā vai pūjayāmāsa taṃ munim ।। kena vā viklavībhūtaḥ kā bādhā te kimapriyam ।।
etatsarvaṃ viditvā tu cintāvaśamupāgataḥ ।। naiva dṛṣṭaṃ raṇe pāpaṃ yudhyamānasya dhīmataḥ ।। tadevaṃ hṛdayaṃ kṛtvā tasmātpāpaṃ na cintayet ।। papraccha vinayopetaḥ sarvapātakanāśanam ।।
kathaya tvaṃ samāsena yena mucyeta kilbiṣāt ।। prayāgagamanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ narāṇāṃ puṇyakarmaṇām ।। brahmaṇā devamukhyena yathāvatkathitaṃ mune ।। mṛtānāṃ kā gatistatra snātānāṃ tatra kiṃ phalam ।।
etanme sarvamākhyāhi paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me ।। purā hi sarvaviprāṇāṃ kathyamānaṃ mayā śrutam ।। etatprajāpateḥ kṣetraṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam ।। tato brahmādayo devā rakṣāṃ kurvanti saṃgatāḥ ।।
saṃkṣepeṇa pravakṣyāmi prayāgasya tu kīrtanam ।। yamunāṃ rakṣati sadā savitā saptavāhanaḥ ।। maṇḍalaṃ rakṣati harir daivataiḥ saha saṃgataḥ ।। sthānaṃ rakṣanti vai devāḥ sarvapāpaharaṃ śubham ।।
prayāgaṃ smaramāṇasya sarvamāyāti saṃkṣayam ।। mṛttikālambhanādvāpi naraḥ pāpātpramucyate ।। prayāgasya praveśe tu pāpaṃ naśyati tatkṣaṇāt ।। api duṣkṛtakarmā tu labhate paramāṃ gatim ।।
avagāhya ca pītvā tu punātyāsaptamaṃ kulam ।। dharmānusārī tattvajño gobrāhmaṇahite rataḥ ।। manasā cintayankāmān avāpnoti supuṣkalān ।। īpsitāṃllabhate kāmān yatra yatrābhijāyate ।।
tatra saṃnihito nityaṃ sākṣāddevo maheśvaraḥ ।। tadupaspṛśya rājendra svargalokamupāsate ।। yacchrutvā sarvapāpebhyo mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। sthānamuktaṃ prayāgaṃ tu nākhyeyaṃ tu kadācana ।।
gaṅgāyamunayormadhye yastu prāṇānparityajet ।। gandharvāpsarasāṃ madhye svarge krīḍati mānavaḥ ।। varāṅganāsamākīrṇair modate śubhalakṣaṇaiḥ ।। yāvanna smarate janma tāvatsvarge mahīyate ।।
tadeva smarate tīrthaṃ smaraṇāttatra gacchati ।। brahmalokamavāpnoti vadanti ṛṣipuṃgavāḥ ।। ṛṣayo munayaḥ siddhās tatra loke sa gacchati ।। modate ṛṣibhiḥ sārdhaṃ sukṛteneha karmaṇā ।।
tataḥ svargātparibhraṣṭo jambūdvīpapatirbhavet ।। guṇavānvittasampanno bhavatīha na saṃśayaḥ ।। gaṅgāyamunayormadhye yastu gāṃ samprayacchati ।। saphalaṃ tasya tattīrthaṃ yathāvatpuṇyamāpnuyāt ।।
nimitteṣu ca sarveṣu hy apramatto bhaveddvijaḥ ।। svarṇaśṛṅgīṃ raupyakhurāṃ kāṃsyadohāṃ payasvinīm ।। śuklāmbaradharaṃ śāntaṃ dharmajñaṃ vedapāragam ।। vāsāṃsi ca mahārhāṇi ratnāni vividhāni ca ।।
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate ।। uttarānsa kurūnprāpya modate kālamakṣayam ।। putrāndārāṃstathā bhṛtyān gaurekā prati tārayet ।। gaureva rakṣāṃ kurute tasmāddeyā dvijottame ।।
tathā tathā pramucye ahaṃ sarvapāpairna saṃśayaḥ ।। prayāge yo vidhiḥ proktas tanme brūhi mahāmune ।। ārṣeṇa vidhinānena yathādṛṣṭaṃ yathāśrutam ।। balīvardasamārūḍhaḥ śṛṇu tasyāpi yatphalam ।।
salilaṃ na ca gṛhṇanti pitarastasya dehinaḥ ।। yathātmanā tathā sarvaṃ dānaṃ vipreṣu dāpayet ।। niṣphalaṃ tasya tatsarvaṃ tasmādyānaṃ vivarjayet ।। ārṣeṇaiva vivāhena yathāvibhavasambhavam ।।
putrāndārāṃśca labhate dhārmikānrūpasaṃyutān ।। svarge tiṣṭhati rājendra yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam ।। sarvalokānatikramya rudralokaṃ sa gacchati ।। nirdahanti jagatsarvaṃ vaṭamūlaṃ na dahyate ।।
sthīyate tatra vai viṣṇur yajamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।। sadā sevanti tattīrthaṃ gaṅgāyamunasaṃgamam ।। yatra brahmādayo devā ṛṣayaḥ siddhacāraṇāḥ ।। sanatkumārapramukhās tathaiva paramarṣayaḥ ।।
tathā nāgāḥ suparṇāśca siddhāśca khecarāśca ye ।। hariśca bhagavanāste prajāpatipuraḥsaraḥ ।। tataḥ puṇyatamaṃ nāsti triṣu lokeṣu bhārata ।। mṛttikālambhanādvāpi naraḥ pāpātpramucyate ।।
tulyaṃ phalamavāpnoti rājasūyāśvamedhayoḥ ।। matir utkramaṇīyā te prayāgagamanaṃ prati ।। teṣāṃ sāṃnidhyamatraiva tatastu kurunandana ।। sā gatistyajataḥ prāṇān gaṅgāyamunasaṃgame ।।
ye prayāgaṃ na samprāptās triṣu lokeṣu vañcitāḥ ।। mucyate sarvapāpebhyaḥ śaśāṅka iva rāhuṇā ।। tatra snātvā ca pītvā ca sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। narastārayate sarvān daśa pūrvāndaśāparān ।।
svargalokamavāpnoti yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam ।। kūpaṃ caiva tu sāmudraṃ pratiṣṭhānaṃ ca viśrutam ।। sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā so aśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet ।। haṃsaprapatanaṃ nāma tīrthaṃ trailokyaviśrutam ।।
yāvaccandraśca sūryaśca tāvatsvarge mahīyate ।। parityajati yaḥ prāṇāñ śṛṇu tasyāpi yatphalam ।। sevyate pitṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ svargaloke narādhipa ।। pūjyate satataṃ putra ṛṣigandharvakiṃnaraiḥ ।।
urvaśīsadṛśīnāṃ tu kanyānāṃ labhate śatam ।। daśagrāmasahasrāṇāṃ bhoktā bhavati bhūmipaḥ ।। bhuktvā tu vipulān bhogāṃs tattīrthaṃ bhajate punaḥ ।। ekaṃ kālaṃ tu bhuñjāno māsaṃ bhūmipatirbhavet ।।
pṛthivyām āsamudrāyāṃ mahābhūmipatirbhavet ।। bhuktvā tu vipulānbhogāṃs tattīrthaṃ labhate punaḥ ।। upavāsī śuciḥ saṃdhyāṃ brahmalokamavāpnuyāt ।। koṭivarṣasahasrāṇāṃ svargaloke mahīyate ।।
suvarṇamaṇimuktāḍhyakule jāyeta rūpavān ।। daśāśvamedhakaṃ nāma tīrthaṃ tatrāparaṃ bhavet ।। dhanāḍhyo rūpavāndakṣo dātā bhavati dhārmikaḥ ।। ahiṃsāyāṃ tu yo dharmo gamanādeva tatphalam ।।
kurukṣetrāddaśaguṇā yatra vindhyena saṃgatā ।। siddhakṣetraṃ hi tajjñeyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। divi tārayate devāṃs tena tripathagā smṛtā ।। tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate ।।
mokṣadā sarvabhūtānāṃ mahāpātakināmapi ।। tatra snātvā divaṃ yānti ye mṛtāste apunarbhavāḥ ।। gatim anviṣyamāṇānāṃ nāsti gaṅgāsamā gatiḥ ।। maheśvaraśirobhraṣṭā sarvapāpaharā śubhā ।।
dvāpare tu kurukṣetraṃ kalau gaṅgā viśiṣyate ।। nānyatkaliyuge ghore bheṣajaṃ nṛpa vidyate ।। yacchrutvā sarvapāpebhyo mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। trirātropoṣito bhūtvā sarvakāmānavāpnuyāt ।।
sa tatphalamavāpnoti tattīrthaṃ smarate punaḥ ।। mṛtastu labhate svargaṃ narakaṃ ca na paśyati ।। bahuvarṣasahasrāṇi svargaṃ rājendra bhuñjati ।। suvarṇamaṇimuktāḍhye jāyate vipule kule ।।
māghamāse gamiṣyanti gaṅgāyamunasaṃgamam ।। prayāge māghamāse tu tryahasnānāttu tatphalam ।। ahīnāṅgo hyarogaśca pañcendriyasamanvitaḥ ।। tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate ।।
sa bhuktvā vipulānbhogāṃs tattīrthaṃ smarate punaḥ ।। rāhugraste tathā some vimuktaḥ sarvakilbiṣaiḥ ।। ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate ।। paribhraṣṭastu rājendra samṛddhe jāyate kule ।।
śatavarṣasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate ।। bhuktvā tu vipulānbhogāṃs tattīrthaṃ bhajate punaḥ ।। vihagairupabhuktasya śṛṇu tasyāpi yatphalam ।। tasmādapi paribhraṣṭo rājā bhavati dhārmikaḥ ।।
bhuktvā tu vipulānbhogāṃs tattīrthaṃ bhajate punaḥ ।। ṛṇapramocanaṃ nāma tattīrthaṃ paramaṃ smṛtam ।। svargalokamavāpnoti anṛṇaśca sadā bhavet ।। viśuddhaṃ me adya hṛdayaṃ prayāgasya tu kīrtanāt ।।
yaṃ ca lokamavāpnoti viśuddhaḥ sarvakilbiṣaiḥ ।। prāpnoti puruṣo dhīmāñ śraddadhāno jitendriyaḥ ।। aśvamedhaphalaṃ tasya gacchatastu pade pade ।। mucyate sarvapāpebhyo gacchettu paramaṃ padam ।।
alpenaiva prayatnena bahūndharmānavāpnute ।। imaṃ me saṃśayaṃ chinddhi paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ saṃnidhau pūrvaṃ kathyamānaṃ mayā śrutam ।। praviṣṭamātre tadbhūmāv aśvamedhaḥ pade pade ।।
narastārayate sarvān yastu prāṇānparityajet ।। na prāpnuvanti tatsthānaṃ prayāgaṃ devarakṣitam ।। kathaṃ tīrthaphalaṃ teṣāṃ kathaṃ puṇyaphalaṃ bhavet ।। prayāge kā gatistasya tanme brūhi pitāmaha ।।
mucyate sarvapāpebhyaḥ sa gacchetparamaṃ padam ।। tribhirmāsaiḥ sa mucyeta prayāge tu na saṃśayaḥ ।। sthānaṃ ca labhate nityaṃ dhanadhānyasamākulam ।। tāritāḥ pitarastena narakātprapitāmahāḥ ।।
tvatpriyārthaṃ samākhyātaṃ guhyametatsanātanam ।। prīto asmyanugṛhīto asmi darśanādeva te mune ।। idānīṃ vedmi cātmānaṃ bhagavangatakalmaṣam ।। kīrtanādvardhate puṇyaṃ śrutātpāpapraṇāśanam ।।
etanme sarvamākhyāhi yathādṛṣṭaṃ yathāśrutam ।। samākhyātā mahābhāgā yamunā tatra nimnagā ।। yojanānāṃ sahasreṣu kīrtanātpāpanāśinī ।। kīrtanāllabhate puṇyaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhadrāṇi paśyati ।।
prāṇāṃstyajati yastatra sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।। paścime dharmarājasya tīrthaṃ tu narakaṃ smṛtam ।। evaṃ tīrthasahasrāṇi yamunādakṣiṇe taṭe ।। tīrthaṃ nirañjanaṃ nāma yatra devāḥ savāsavāḥ ।।
devāḥ sevanti tattīrthaṃ ye cānye vibudhā janāḥ ।। teṣu snātvā divaṃ yānti ye mṛtāste apunarbhavāḥ ।। kevalaṃ jyeṣṭhabhāvena gaṅgā sarvatra pūjyate ।। yāvajjīvakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇādeva naśyati ।।
mucyate sarvapāpebhyaḥ svargalokaṃ sa gacchati ।। sarve puṇyāḥ pavitrāśca gatiśca paramā smṛtā ।। tasmātsarvaprayatnena tatra snānaṃ samācaret ।। trayāṇāmapi lokānāṃ kurukṣetraṃ viśiṣyate ।।
apramāṇaṃ tu tatroktam aśraddheyamanuttamam ।। etanme saṃśayaṃ brūhi yathādṛṣṭaṃ yathāśrutam ।। narasyāśraddadhānasya pāpopahatacetasaḥ ।। ete pātakinaḥ sarve tenedaṃ bhāṣitaṃ tvayā ।।
pratyakṣaṃ ca parokṣaṃ ca yathānyastaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। śāstraṃ pramāṇaṃ kṛtvā ca yujyate yogamātmanaḥ ।। janmāntarasahasrebhyo yogo labhyeta mānavaiḥ ।। yastu sarvāṇi ratnāni brāhmaṇebhyaḥ prayacchati ।।
prayāge tu mṛtasyedaṃ sarvaṃ bhavati nānyathā ।। yathā sarveṣu bhūteṣu brahma sarvatra dṛśyate ।। evaṃ sarveṣu bhūteṣu brahma sarvatra pūjyate ।। pūjyate tīrtharājastu satyameva yudhiṣṭhira ।।
tīrtharājam anuprāpya na cānyatkiṃcidarhati ।। yathā puṇyatamaṃ cāsti tathaiva kathitaṃ mayā ।। kathaṃ yogena tatprāptiḥ svargavāsastu karmaṇā ।। tāni karmāṇi pṛcchāmi punastaiḥ prāpyate mahī ।।
gāmagniṃ brāhmaṇaṃ śāstraṃ kāñcanaṃ salilaṃ striyaḥ ।। na teṣāmūrdhvagamanam idamāha prajāpatiḥ ।। gacchanti narakaṃ ghoraṃ ye narāḥ pāpakarmiṇaḥ ।। parokṣaṃ harate yastu paścāddānaṃ prayacchati ।।
anenakarmaṇā yuktāḥ pacyante narake punaḥ ।। niruktaṃ tu pravakṣyāmi yathāha svayamaṃśumān ।। naimiṣaṃ puṣkaraṃ caiva gotīrthaṃ sindhusāgaram ।। ete cānye ca bahavo ye ca puṇyāḥ śiloccayāḥ ।।
prayāge saṃsthitā nityam evamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ ।। prayāgādabhiniṣkrāntā sarvatīrthanamaskṛtā ।। yamunā gaṅgayā sārdhaṃ saṃgatā lokabhāvinī ।। prayāgaṃ rājaśārdūla kalāṃ nārhati ṣoḍaśīm ।।
divi bhuvyantarikṣe ca tatsarvaṃ jāhnavī smṛtā ।। bhogavatyatha yā caiṣā vedireṣā prajāpateḥ ।। prajāpatim upāsante ṛṣayaśca tapodhanāḥ ।। tataḥ puṇyatamaṃ nāsti triṣu lokeṣu bhārata ।।
daśa tīrthasahasrāṇi tisraḥ koṭyastathā parāḥ ।। siddhakṣetraṃ ca vijñeyaṃ gaṅgātīrasamanvitam ।। suhṛdaśca japetkarṇe śiṣyasyānugatasya ca ।। idaṃ puṇyamidaṃ dharmyaṃ pāvanaṃ dharmamuttamam ।।
adhītya ca dvijo apyetan nirmalaḥ svargamāpnuyāt ।। jātismaratvaṃ labhate nākapṛṣṭhe ca modate ।। snāhi tīrtheṣu kauravya na ca vakramatirbhava ।। pitarastāritāḥ sarve tathaiva ca pitāmahāḥ ।।
prayāgasya tu sarve te kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ।। trikālaṃ jāyate jñānaṃ svargalokaṃ gamiṣyati ।। etannaḥ sarvamākhyāhi yathā hi mama tārayet ।। brahmā viṣṇustatheśāno devatāḥ prabhuravyayaḥ ।।
tānyetāni paraṃ loke viṣṇuḥ saṃvardhate prajāḥ ।। tadā prayāgatīrthaṃ ca na kadācidvinaśyati ।। yatnenānena tiṣṭhanti te yānti paramāṃ gatim ।। kena vā kāraṇenaiva tiṣṭhante lokasattamāḥ ।।
kāraṇaṃ tatpravakṣyāmi śṛṇu tattvaṃ yudhiṣṭhira ।। tiṣṭhanti rakṣaṇāyātra pāpakarmanivāraṇāt ।। veṇīmādhavarūpī tu bhagavāṃstatra tiṣṭhati ।। rakṣanti maṇḍalaṃ nityaṃ pāpakarmanivāraṇāt ।।
evaṃ brahmā ca viṣṇuśca prayāge sa maheśvaraḥ ।। rakṣamāṇāśca tiṣṭhanti yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam ।। yat pṛthivī tatsamāśritya nirmitā daivatais tribhiḥ ।। svarājyaṃ kuru rājendra bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito anagha ।।
brāhmaṇebhyo namaskṛtya gurūndevānatarpayat ।। pāṇḍavaiḥ sahitaiḥ sarvaiḥ pūjyamānastu mādhavaḥ ।। abhiṣiktaḥ svarājye ca dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।। tataḥ svastīti coktvā tu kṣaṇādāśramamāgamat ।।
mahādānaṃ tato dattvā dharmaputro mahāmanāḥ ।। mucyate sarvapāpebhyo rudralokaṃ sa gacchati ।। nityaṃ japasva juhvasva prayāge vigatajvaraḥ ।। svayaṃ prāpsyasi rājendra svargalokaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।।
sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā rudralokaṃ sa gacchati ।। ahaṃkāranivṛttaśca sa tīrthaphalamaśnute ।। ātmopamaśca bhūteṣu sa tīrthaphalamaśnute ।। na hi śakyā daridreṇa yajñāḥ prāptuṃ mahīpate ।।
prāpyante pārthivairetaiḥ samṛddhairvai naraiḥ kvacit ।। tulyo yajñaphalaiḥ puṇyais tannibodha yudhiṣṭhira ।। tīrthānugamanaṃ puṇyaṃ yajñebhyo api viśiṣyate ।। māghamāse gamiṣyanti gaṅgāyāṃ bharatarṣabha ।।
punardrakṣyasi rājendra yajamāno viśeṣataḥ ।। yudhiṣṭhirasya nṛpates tatraivāntaradhīyata ।। yathoktenātha vidhinā parāṃ nirvṛtimāgamat ।। abhiṣekaṃ tu kṛtvādya kṛtakṛtyo bhaviṣyasi ।।
nārado api jagāmāśu prayāgābhimukhastathā ।। dānaṃ dattvā dvijāgryebhyo gataḥ svabhavanaṃ tadā ।। kiyanti caiva varṣāṇi teṣu nadyaśca kāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। paryāptiṃ parimāṇaṃ ca gatiścandrārkayostathā ।।
tvaduktametatsakalaṃ śrotumicchāmahe vayam ।। na śakyante krameṇeha vaktuṃ vai sakalaṃ jagat ।। teṣāṃ manuṣyatarkeṇa pramāṇāni pracakṣate ।। prakṛtibhyaḥ paraṃ yacca tadacintyasya lakṣaṇam ।।
vistaraṃ maṇḍalaṃ yacca yojanaistānnibodhata ।। nānājanapadākīrṇaṃ puraiśca vividhaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। sarvadhātupinaddhaistaiḥ śilājālasamudgataiḥ ।। prāgāyatā mahāpārśvāḥ ṣaḍime varṣaparvatāḥ ।।
himaprāyaśca himavān hemakūṭaśca hemavān ।। caturviṃśatsahasrāṇi vistīrṇaḥ sa caturdiśam ।। nānāvarṇaiḥ samaḥ pārśvaiḥ prajāpatiguṇānvitaḥ ।। pūrvataḥ śvetavarṇastu brāhmaṇyaṃ tasya tena vai ।।
tenāsya śūdratā siddhā meror nāmārthakarmataḥ ।। tenāsya kṣatrabhāvaḥ syād iti varṇāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। mayūrabarhavarṇaśca śātakaumbhaḥ sa śṛṅgavān ।। teṣāmantaraviṣkambho navasāhasramucyate ।।
caturviṃśatsahasrāṇi vistīrṇo yojanaiḥ samaḥ ।। vedyardhaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ meror uttarārdhaṃ tathottaram ।। dve dve sahasre vistīrṇā yojanairdakṣiṇottaram ।। nīlaśca niṣadhaścaiva teṣāṃ hīnāśca ye pare ।।
jambūdvīpapramāṇeṇa ṛṣabhaḥ parikīrtyate ।। aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi hemakūṭo mahāgiriḥ ।। dvīpasya maṇḍalībhāvād dhrāsavṛddhī prakīrtite ।। teṣāṃ madhye janapadās tāni varṣāṇi sapta vai ।।
sapta tāni nadībhedair agamyāni parasparam ।। imaṃ haimavataṃ varṣaṃ bhārataṃ nāma viśrutam ।। hemakūṭācca niṣadhaṃ harivarṣaṃ taducyate ।। ilāvṛtātparaṃ nīlaṃ ramyakaṃ nāma viśrutam ।।
hiraṇyakātparaṃ caiva śṛṅgaśākaṃkuraṃ smṛtam ।। dīrghāṇi tasya catvāri madhyamaṃ tadilāvṛtam ।। paraṃ tvilāvṛtaṃ paścād vedyardhaṃ tu taduttaram ।। dakṣiṇena tu nīlasya niṣadhasyottareṇa tu ।।
dvātriṃśatā sahasreṇa pratīcyāṃ sāgarānugaḥ ।। dvātriṃśattvevamapyuktaḥ parvato gandhamādanaḥ ।। cāturvarṇyasamo varṇaiś caturasraḥ samucchritaḥ ।। uttaraṃ tasya raktaṃ vai iti varṇasamanvitaḥ ।।
ādityataruṇābhāso vidhūma iva pāvakaḥ ।। praviṣṭaḥ ṣoḍaśādhastād aṣṭāviṃśativistṛtaḥ ।। sa parvato mahādivyo divyauṣadhisamanvitaḥ ।। śailarāje pramodante sarvato apsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ ।।
yasyeme caturo deśā nānāpārśveṣu saṃsthitāḥ ।। uttarāścaiva kuravaḥ kṛtapuṇyapratiśrayāḥ ।। vipulaśca supārśvaśca sarvaratnavibhūṣitāḥ ।। teṣāmupari catvāri sarāṃsi ca vanāni ca ।।
jambūvṛkṣastathāśvattho vipule atha vaṭaḥ param ।। dvātriṃśacca sahasrāṇi yojanaiḥ sarvataḥ samaḥ ।। tatra kālānalāḥ sarve mahāsattvā mahābalāḥ ।। tatra divyo mahāvṛkṣaḥ panasaḥ pattrabhāsuraḥ ।।
dvātriṃśacca sahasrāṇi tatrāpi śatamucyate ।। bhadramālavanaṃ tatra kālāmraśca mahādrumaḥ ।। striyaḥ kumudavarṇābhāḥ sundaryaḥ priyadarśanāḥ ।। candraśītalagātrāśca striyo hyutpalagandhikāḥ ।।
kālāmrasya rasaṃ pītvā te sarve sthirayauvanāḥ ।। pūrvaṃ mamānugrahakṛd bhūyaḥ kiṃ varṇayāmi vaḥ ।। jātakautūhalāḥ sarve pratyūcuste mudānvitāḥ ।। uttarāṇāṃ ca varṣāṇāṃ parvatānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ ।।
evamuktastu ṛṣibhis tebhyastvākhyātavānpunaḥ ।। dakṣiṇena tu nīlasya niṣadhasyottareṇa tu ।। śuklābhijanasampannāḥ sarve te priyadarśanāḥ ।। tasyāpi te phalarasaṃ pibanto vartayanti hi ।।
jīvanti te mahābhāgāḥ sadā hṛṣṭā narottamāḥ ।। varṣaṃ hiraṇvataṃ nāma yatra hairaṇvatī nadī ।। śuklābhijanasampannāḥ sarve ca priyadarśanāḥ ।। āyuṣpramāṇaṃ jīvanti śatāni daśa pañca ca ।।
tasya pītvā phalarasaṃ tatra jīvanti mānavāḥ ।। sarvaratnamayaṃ caikaṃ bhuvanairupaśobhitam ।। kuravastatra tadvaryaṃ puṇyaṃ siddhaniṣevitam ।। vastrāṇi te prasūyante phalaiścābharaṇāni ca ।।
ye rakṣanti sadā kṣīraṃ ṣaḍrasaṃ cāmṛtopamam ।। sarvatra sukhasaṃsparśā niḥśabdāḥ pavanāḥ śubhāḥ ।। śuklābhijanasampannāḥ sarve te sthirayauvanāḥ ।। teṣāṃ te kṣīriṇāṃ kṣīraṃ pibanti hyamṛtopamam ।।
samaṃ rūpaṃ ca śīlaṃ ca samaṃ caiva mriyanti vai ।। anāmayā hyaśokāśca nityaṃ muditamānasāḥ ।। jīvanti ca mahāsattvā na cānyā strī pravartate ।। dṛṣṭaḥ paramadharmajñāḥ kiṃ bhūyaḥ kathayāmi vaḥ ।।
uttaraśravaṇe bhūyaḥ papracchuḥ sūtanandanam ।। caturdaśaiva manavaḥ prajāsargaṃ sasarjire ।। uttaraśravaṇaṃ bhūyaḥ prabrūhi vadatāṃ vara ।। paurāṇikastadā sūta ṛṣīṇāṃ bhāvitātmanām ।।
tebhyastu kathayāmāsa uttaraśravaṇaṃ tadā ।। bharaṇātprajanāccaiva manurbharata ucyate ।। yataḥ svargaśca mokṣaśca madhyamaścāpi hi smṛtaḥ ।। bhāratasyāsya varṣasya nava bhedānnibodhata ।।
nāgadvīpastathā saumyo gandharvastvatha vāruṇaḥ ।। yojanānāṃ sahasraṃ tu dvīpo ayaṃ dakṣiṇottaraḥ ।। tiryagūrdhvaṃ tu vistīrṇaḥ sahasrāṇi daśaiva tu ।। yavanāśca kirātāśca tasyānte pūrvapaścime ।।
ijyāyutavaṇijyādi vartayanto vyavasthitāḥ ।। dharmārthakāmasaṃyukto varṇānāṃ tu svakarmasu ।। iha svargāpavargārthaṃ pravṛttiriha mānuṣe ।। ya enaṃ jayate kṛtsnaṃ sa samrāḍiti kīrtitaḥ ।।
svarāḍasau smṛto lokaḥ punarvakṣyāmi vistarāt ।। mahendro malayaḥ sahyaḥ śuktimānṛkṣavānapi ।। teṣāṃ sahasraśaścānye parvatāstu samīpataḥ ।। anye tebhyaḥ parijñātā hrasvā hrasvopajīvinaḥ ।।
pibanti bahulā nadyo gaṅgā sindhuḥ sarasvatī ।। airāvatī vitastā ca viśālā devikā kuhūḥ ।। kauśikī tu tṛtīyā ca niścalā gaṇḍakī tathā ।। parṇāśā narmadā caiva kāverī mahatī tathā ।।
śiprā hyavantī kuntī ca pāriyātrāśritāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। tamasā pippalī śyenī tathā citrotpalāpi ca ।। ṛṣyavantaprasūtās tā nadyo amalajalāḥ śubhāḥ ।। veṇā vaitaraṇī caiva viśvamālā kumudvatī ।।
vindhyapādaprasūtās tāḥ sarvāḥ śītajalāḥ śubhāḥ ।। dakṣiṇāpathanadyastāḥ sahyapādādviniḥsṛtāḥ ।। malayaprasūtā nadyas tāḥ sarvāḥ śītajalāḥ śubhāḥ ।। mahendratanayāḥ sarvāḥ prakhyātāḥ śubhagāminīḥ ।।
kṛpā ca pāśinī caiva śuktimantātmajās tu tāḥ ।। viśvasya mātaraḥ sarvāḥ sarvapāpaharāḥ śubhāḥ ।। tāsvime kurupāñcālāḥ śālvāścaiva sajāṅgalāḥ ।। matsyāḥ kirātāḥ kulyāśca kuntalāḥ kāśikośalāḥ ।।
madhyadeśā janapadāḥ prāyaśaḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। pṛthivyāmapi kṛtsnāyāṃ sa pradeśo manoramaḥ ।। rāmapriyārthaṃ svargīyā vṛkṣā divyāstathauṣadhīḥ ।। tataḥ puṣpavaro deśas tena jajñe manoramaḥ ।।
puraṃdhrāścaiva śūdrāśca pallavāś cāttakhaṇḍikāḥ ।। śakā druhyāḥ pulindāśca pāradāhāramūrtikāḥ ।। kṣatriyopaniveśyāśca vaiśyāḥ śūdrakulāni ca ।। ete deśā udīcyāstu prācyāndeśānnibodhata ।।
suhmottarāḥ pravijayā mārgavā geyamālavāḥ ।। śālvamāgadhagonardāḥ prācyā janapadāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। pāṇḍyāśca keralāścaiva colāḥ kulyāstathaiva ca ।। navarāṣṭrā māhiṣikāḥ kaliṅgāścaiva sarvaśaḥ ।।
pulindā vindhyapuṣikā vaidarbhā daṇḍakaiḥ saha ।। tathā taittirikāścaiva sarve kāraskarāstathā ।। bhārukacchāḥ samāheyāḥ saha sārasvataistathā ।। ityete aparāntāstu śṛṇu ye vindhyavāsinaḥ ।।
auṇḍrā māṣā daśārṇāśca bhojāḥ kiṣkindhakaiḥ saha ।। tumurās tumbarāścaiva padgamā naiṣadhaiḥ saha ।। ete janapadāḥ khyātā vindhyapṛṣṭhanivāsinaḥ ।। nirāhārāḥ sarvagāśca kupathā apathāstathā ।।
trigartā maṇḍalāścaiva kirātāścāmaraiḥ saha ।। teṣāṃ nisargaṃ vakṣyāmi upariṣṭācca kṛtsnaśaḥ ।। śuśrūṣavastamūcuste prakāmaṃ laumaharṣaṇim ।। ācakṣva no yathātattvaṃ kīrtitaṃ bhārataṃ tvayā ।।
dvīpānāṃ vāsināṃ teṣāṃ vṛkṣāṇāṃ prabravīhi naḥ ।। uvāca ṛṣibhirdṛṣṭaṃ purāṇābhimataṃ tathā ।। jambūvarṣaḥ kimpuruṣaḥ sumahānandanopamaḥ ।। jāyante mānavāstatra sutaptakanakaprabhāḥ ।।
tasya kimpuruṣāḥ sarve pibanto rasamuttamam ।। suvarṇavarṇāśca narāḥ striyaścāpsarasaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। mahārajatasaṃkāśā jāyante yatra mānavāḥ ।। harivarṣe narāḥ sarve pibantīkṣurasaṃ śubham ।।
ekādaśa sahasrāṇi teṣāmāyuḥ prakīrtitam ।। na tatra sūryastapati na ca jānanti mānavāḥ ।। padmaprabhāḥ padmavarṇāḥ padmapattranibhekṣaṇāḥ ।। jambūphalarasāhārā aniṣpandāḥ sugandhinaḥ ।।
trayodaśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ te narottamāḥ ।। merostu dakṣiṇe pārśve niṣadhasyottareṇa vā ।। nityapuṣpaphalopetaḥ siddhacāraṇasevitaḥ ।। yojanānāṃ sahasraṃ ca śatadhā ca mahānpunaḥ ।।
tasya jambūphalaraso nadī bhūtvā prasarpati ।। taṃ pibanti sadā hṛṣṭā jambūrasamilāvṛte ।। na kṣudhā na klamo vāpi na duḥkhaṃ ca tathāvidham ।। indragopakasaṃkāśaṃ jāyate bhāsuraṃ ca yat ।।
skannaṃ tu kāñcanaṃ śubhraṃ jāyate devabhūṣaṇam ।। īśvarānugrahādbhūmir mṛtāṃśca grasate tu tān ।। hemakūṭe tu vijñeyā gandharvāḥ sāpsarogaṇāḥ ।। mahāmerau trayastriṃśat krīḍante yajñiyāḥ śubhāḥ ।।
daityānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca śvetaḥ parvata ucyate ।। ityetāni mayoktāni navavarṣāṇi bhārate ।। aśakyā parisaṃkhyātuṃ śraddheyā ca bubhūṣatā ।। śrutaḥ śrāddhavidhiḥ puṇyaḥ sarvapāpapraṇāśanaḥ ।।
kṛṣṇājinapradānaṃ ca vṛṣotsargastathaiva ca ।। kautūhalaṃ samutpannaṃ tanmamācakṣva pṛcchataḥ ।। avāpa tādṛśaṃ rūpaṃ saubhāgyamapi cottamam ।। urvaśī saṃmatā tyaktvā sarvabhāvena taṃ nṛpam ।।
avāpa tādṛśaṃ rūpaṃ saubhāgyamapi cottamam ।। purūravā iti khyāto madradeśādhipo hi saḥ ।। sa vai nṛpaguṇairyuktaḥ kevalaṃ rūpavarjitaḥ ।। babhūva karmaṇā kena rūpavāṃścaiva sūtaja ।।
nadyāḥ kūle mahārājaḥ pūrvajanmani pārthivaḥ ।। tasmiñjanmanyasau vipro dvādaśyāṃ tu sadānagha ।। cakāra sopavāsaśca snānam abhyaṅgapūrvakam ।। upoṣitas tathābhyaṅgād rūpahīno vyajāyata ।।
varjanīyaṃ prayatnena rūpaghnaṃ tatparaṃ nṛpa ।। madreśvaratvacaritaṃ śṛṇu tasya mahīpateḥ ।। janānurāgo naivāsīd rūpahīnasya tasya vai ।। rājyaṃ mantrigataṃ kṛtvā jagāma himaparvatam ।।
draṣṭuṃ sa tīrthasadanaṃ viṣayānte svake nadīm ।। airāvatīti vikhyātāṃ dadarśātimanoramām ।। tuhinagiribhavāṃ mahaughavegāṃ tuhinagabhastisamānaśītalodām ।। tuhinasadṛśahaimavarṇapuñjāṃ tuhinayaśāḥ saritaṃ dadarśa rājā ।।
gandharvaiśca samākīrṇāṃ nityaṃ śakreṇa sevitām ।। madhyena śakracāpābhāṃ tasminnahani sarvadā ।। dadarśa tapanīyābhāṃ mahārājaḥ purūravāḥ ।। sābhiṣiktāmiva satāṃ paśyanprītiṃ parāṃ yayau ।।
kṣayavṛddhiyutāṃ ramyāṃ somamūrtimivāparām ।। sutāṃ himavataḥ śreṣṭhāṃ cañcadvīcivirājitām ।। svargārohaṇaniḥśreṇīṃ sarvakalmaṣanāśinīm ।। sarvalokasya cautsukyakāriṇīṃ sumanoharām ।।
gokulākulatīrāntāṃ ramyāṃ śaivālavarjitām ।। āvartanābhigambhīrāṃ dvīporujaghanasthalīm ।। balākāpaṅktidaśanāṃ calanmatsyāvalibhruvam ।। haṃsanūpurasaṃghuṣṭāṃ mṛṇālavalayāvalīm ।।
madhyāhnasamaye rājan krīḍantyapsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ ।। svatīradrumasambhūtanānāvarṇasugandhinīm ।। surebhajanitāghātavikūladvayabhūṣitām ।। saṃyutaṃ salilaṃ tasyāḥ ṣaṭpadair upasevyate ।।
tathāpakṛṣṭasaṃbhrāntabhramarastanitākulāḥ ।। tapovanāśca ṛṣayas tathā devāḥ sahāpsarāḥ ।। striyaśca nākabahulāḥ padmendupratimānanāḥ ।। pulindairnṛpasaṃghaiśca vyāghravṛndairapīḍitam ।।
sa tāṃ paśyanyayau rājā satāmīpsitakāmadām ।। yā sadā vividhairviprair devaiścāpi niṣevyate ।। yānugatā saritāṃ hi kadambair yānugatā satataṃ hi munīndraiḥ ।। yā ca yutā satataṃ suravṛndair yā ca janaiḥ svahitāya śritā vai ।।
sūryāṃśutāpaparivṛddhivivṛddhaśītā śītāṃśutulyayaśasā dadṛśe nṛpeṇa ।। sa gacchanneva dadṛśe himavantaṃ mahāgirim ।। pakṣiṇāmapi saṃcārair vinā siddhagatiṃ śubhām ।। asaṃśrutānyaśabdaṃ taṃ śītatoyaṃ manoramam ।।
meghottarīyakaṃ śailaṃ dadṛśe sa narādhipaḥ ।। himānuliptasarvāṅgaṃ kvaciddhātuvimiśritam ।। sālaktakairapsarasāṃ mudritaṃ caraṇaiḥ kvacit ।। darīmukhaiḥ kvacidbhīmaiḥ pibantaṃ salilaṃ mahat ।।
upagītaṃ tathā mukhyaiḥ kiṃnarāṇāṃ gaṇaiḥ kvacit ।। puṣpaiḥ saṃtānakādīnāṃ divyaistam upaśobhitam ।। mṛditābhiḥ samākīrṇaṃ gandharvāṇāṃ manoramam ।। kvacic ca kusumairyuktam atyantaruciraṃ śubham ।।
mṛgairyathānucaritaṃ dantibhinnamahādrumam ।। dṛśyate na ca saṃśrāntaṃ gajānāmākulaṃ kulam ।। ratnairyasya samutpannais trailokyaṃ samalaṃkṛtam ।। ahīnaḥ paśyati girim ahīnaṃ ratnasampadā ।।
yasya darśanamātreṇa sarvakalmaṣanāśanam ।। vāyunītaiḥ sadā tṛptikṛtadeśaṃ kvacitkvacit ।। nityārkatāpaviṣamair agamyairmanasā yutam ।। vaṃśastambavanākāraiḥ pradeśairupaśobhitam ।।
śabdalabhyāmbuviṣamaṃ himasaṃruddhakandaram ।। babhrāma tatraiva mudā sametaḥ sthānaṃ tadā kiṃcidathāsasāda ।। agamyaṃ mānuṣair anyair daivayogād upāgataḥ ।। meghaśyāmaṃ ca taṃ deśaṃ drumakhaṇḍairanekaśaḥ ।।
nyagrodhaiśca tathāśvatthaiḥ śirīṣaiḥ śiṃśapadrumaiḥ ।। bhūrjaiḥ samuñjakair bāṇair vṛkṣaiḥ saptacchadadrumaiḥ ।। devadārumahāvṛkṣais tathā kāleyakadrumaiḥ ।। mātāmrariṣṭakākṣoṭair abdakaiśca tathārjunaiḥ ।।
prācīnāmalakaiścāpi dhanakaiḥ samarāṭakaiḥ ।। tantumālair dhavairbhavyaiḥ kāśmīrīparṇibhistathā ।। mandāraiḥ kovidāraiśca kiṃśukaiḥ kusumāṃśukaiḥ ।। raktātiraṅganāraṅgair hiṅgubhiḥ sapriyaṅgubhiḥ ।।
mucukundaistathā kundair āṭarūṣaparūṣakaiḥ ।। śobhāñjanair añjanaiśca sukaliṅganikoṭakaiḥ ।। manmathasya śarākāraiḥ sahakārairmanoramaiḥ ।। jātyā campakajātyā ca tumbaraiścāpyatumbaraiḥ ।।
tathā supuṣpāvaraṇaiś cavyakaiḥ kāmivallabhaiḥ ।। dhārākadambaiḥ kuṭajaiḥ kadambair girikuṭajaiḥ ।। kaṭphalairbadarairnīpair dīpairiva mahojjvalaiḥ ।। bandhūkaiśca subandhūkaiḥ kuñjakānāṃ tu jātibhiḥ ।।
kurabakair himavarair jambūbhir nṛpajambubhiḥ ।। bimbaiśca pratibimbaiśca saṃtānakavitānakaiḥ ।। tṛṇaśūnyaiḥ karavīrair aśokaiś cakramardanaiḥ ।। tintiḍīkaistathā lodhrair viḍaṅgaiḥ kṣīrikādrumaiḥ ।।
bhallātakairindrayavair valgujaiḥ siddhisādhakaiḥ ।। rudrākṣairdrākṣasambhūtaiḥ saptāhvaiḥ putrajīvakaiḥ ।। pratānaiḥ pippalīnāṃ ca nāgavalyaśca bhāgaśaḥ ।। mṛdvīkāmaṇḍapairmukhyair atimuktakamaṇḍapaiḥ ।।
kūṣmāṇḍānāṃ pratānaiśca alābūnāṃ tathā kvacit ।। karkoṭakīvitānaiśca vārtākair bṛhatīphalaiḥ ।। kahlāraiśca vidāryā ca rurūṭaiḥ svādukaṇṭakaiḥ ।। suvarcalābhiḥ sarvābhiḥ sarṣapābhistathaiva ca ।।
kāsamardīsahāsadbhiḥ sakandalasakāṇḍakaiḥ ।। śimbīdhānyaistathā dhānyaiḥ sarvairniravaśeṣataḥ ।। āyuṣyābhiryaśasyābhir balyābhiśca narādhipa ।। saubhāgyajananībhiśca kutsnābhiścāpyanekaśaḥ ।।
kāśaiḥ śaśāṅkakāśaiśca śaragulmaistathaiva ca ।। kārpāsajātivargeṇa durlabhena śubhena ca ।। tathā marakataprakhyaiḥ pradeśaiḥ śādvalānvitaiḥ ।। tagarātiviṣāmāṃsīgranthikaistu surāgadaiḥ ।।
jambīrakairbhūstṛṇakaiḥ sarasaiḥ saśukaistathā ।। jalajaiśca tathā vaṇair nānāvarṇaiḥ sugandhibhiḥ ।। tapanīyasavarṇaiśca atasīpuṣpasaṃnibhaiḥ ।। pañcavarṇaiḥ samākīrṇair bahuvarṇaistathaiva ca ।।
tathā vahniśikhākārair gajavaktrotpalaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।। śṛṅgāṭakamṛṇālaiśca karaṭai rājatotpalaiḥ ।। vividhaiścaiva nīvārair munibhojyairnarādhipa ।। na tanmūlaṃ na tatkandaṃ na tatpuṣpaṃ narādhipa ।।
anūpotthaṃ vanotthaṃ ca tatra yannāsti pārthivaḥ ।। madreśvaraḥ sa dadṛśe tapasā hyatiyogataḥ ।। mayūrān śatapattrāṃśca kalaviṅkāṃśca kokilān ।। kurarānkālakūṭāṃśca khaṭvāṅgān lubdhakāṃs tathā ।।
ghātukāṃścakravākāṃśca kaṭukānṭiṭṭibhān bhaṭān ।। pārāvatāṃśca kamalān sārikā jīvajīvakān ।। tāmracūḍānsvarṇacūḍān kukkuṭān kāṣṭhakukkuṭān ।। bhṛṅgarājān sīrapādān bhūliṅgān ḍiṇḍimān navān ।।
etāṃścānyāṃśca subahūn pakṣisaṃghānmanoharān ।। vyāghrānkesariṇaḥ siṃhān dvīpinaḥ śarabhānvṛkān ।। śaśalomān sakādambān mārjārān vāyuveginaḥ ।। camarān sṛmarāṃścaiva tathā gaurakharānapi ।।
nīlāṃścaiva mahānālān karālānmṛgamātṛkān ।। karālānkṛtamālāṃśca kālapucchāṃśca toraṇān ।। etān adviṣṭānmadreśo viruddhāṃśca parasparam ।। taccāśramapadaṃ puṇyaṃ babhūvātreḥ purā nṛpam ।।
hiṃsanti hi na cānyonyaṃ hiṃsakāstu parasparam ।। nirmitāstatra cātyartham atriṇā sumahātmanā ।। payaḥ kṣaranti te divyam amṛtasvādukaṇṭakam ।। śilāḥ kṣīreṇa sampūrṇā dadhnā cānyatra vā bahiḥ ।।
sarāṃsi tatra divyāni nadyaśca vimalodakāḥ ।। kandarāṇi ca śailasya susevyāni pade pade ।। upatyakā suśailasya śikharasya na vidyate ।। himapātaṃ ghanā yatra kurvanti sahitāḥ sadā ।।
nityamevābhivarṣanti śilābhiḥ śikharaṃ varam ।। suramukhyopayogitvāc chākhināṃ saphalāḥ phalāḥ ।। sarvapāpakṣayakaraṃ śailasyeva prahārakam ।। himapuñjāḥ kṛtāstatra candrabimbasamaprabhāḥ ।।
śailavāṭaiḥ parivṛtam agamyaṃ manujaiḥ sadā ।। tadāśramapadaṃ prāpto devadevaprasādataḥ ।। kṛtaṃ svayaṃ ruciramathātriṇā śubhaṃ śubhāvahaṃ ca hi dadṛśe sa madrarāṭ ।। tṛtīyaṃ tu tayormadhye śṛṅgamatyantamucchritam ।।
tasyādhastādvṛkṣagaṇe diśāṃ bhāge ca paścime ।। dṛṣṭvaiva kautukāviṣṭas taṃ viveśa mahīpatiḥ ।। nalvamātramatikramya svaprabhābharaṇojjvalam ।। na tatra sūryastapati na virājati candramāḥ ।।
krośādhikaparīmāṇaṃ sarasā ca virājitam ।। sauvarṇai rājatairvṛkṣair vidrumairupaśobhitam ।। tasminsarasi padmāni padmarāgacchadāni tu ।। pattrair marakatair nīlair vaiḍūryasya mahīpate ।।
tasminsarasi yā bhūmir na sā vajrasamākulā ।। kapardikānāṃ śuktīnāṃ śaṅkhānāṃ ca mahīpate ।। tatra marakatakhaṇḍāni vajrāṇāṃ ca sahasraśaḥ ।। puṣparāgāṇi sarvāṇi tathā karkoṭakāni ca ।।
rājāvartasya mukhyasya rucirākṣasya cāpyatha ।। jyotīrasasya ramyasya syamantasya ca bhāgaśaḥ ।। gomedapittakānāṃ ca dhūlīmarakatasya ca ।। vajrasyaiva ca mukhyasya tathā brahmamaṇerapi ।।
muktāphalāni muktānāṃ tārāvigrahadhāriṇām ।। vaiḍūryasya śilā madhye sarasastasya śobhanā ।। caturasrā tathā ramyā tapasā nirmitātriṇā ।। pradeśaḥ sa tu rājendra dvīpe tasminmanohare ।।
suśītāmalapānīyā jalajaiśca virājitā ।। tasyāstadudakaṃ svādu laghu śītaṃ sugandhikam ।। tṛptiṃ vidhatte paramāṃ śarīre ca mahatsukham ।। rukmasetupraveśāntaṃ sarvaratnamayaṃ śubham ।।
ramyavaiḍūryasopānaṃ vidrumāmalasārakam ।। vajrāṃśujālaiḥ sphuritaṃ ramyaṃ dṛṣṭimanoramam ।। bhogibhogāvalīsuptaḥ sarvālaṃkārabhūṣitaḥ ।। phaṇīndrasaṃniviṣṭo aṅghrir dvitīyaśca tathānagha ।।
phaṇīndrabhogasaṃnyastabāhuḥ keyūrabhūṣaṇaḥ ।। ekaṃ vai devadevasya dvitīyaṃ tu prasāritam ।। kiṃcidākuñcitaṃ caiva nābhideśakarasthitam ।। āttasaṃtānakusumaṃ ghrāṇadeśānusarpiṇam ।।
saṃtānamālāmukuṭaṃ hārakeyūrabhūṣitam ।। phaṇīndraphaṇavinyastacāruratnaśirojjvalam ।। siddhānupūjyaṃ satataṃ saṃtānakusumārcitam ।। surasaiḥ suphalairhṛdyaiḥ siddhairupahṛtaiḥ sadā ।।
tataḥ sammukham udvīkṣya vavande sa narādhipaḥ ।। nāmnāṃ sahasreṇa tadā tuṣṭāva madhusūdanam ।। ramyamāyatanaṃ dṛṣṭvā tatrovāsāśrame punaḥ ।। tapaścakāra tatraiva pūjayanmadhusūdanam ।।
nityaṃ triṣavaṇasnāyī vahnipūjāparāyaṇaḥ ।। sarvāhāraparityāgaṃ kṛtvā tu manujeśvaraḥ ।। na tasya glānimāyāti śarīraṃ ca tadadbhutam ।। tatrāśrame kālamuvāsa kaṃcit svargopame duḥkham avindamānaḥ ।।
krīḍāvihāraṃ gandharvaiḥ paśyannapsarasāṃ saha ।। agraṃ nivedya devāya gandharvebhyastadā dadau ।। ceṣṭā nānāvidhākārāḥ paśyannapi na paśyati ।। sakhījanena saṃtyaktā kāntenābhisamujjhitā ।।
madhupairākulamukhī kāntena parimocitā ।। kāntaniḥśvāsavātena nīrajaskakṛtekṣaṇā ।। kāntasaṃgrathitaiḥ puṣpai rarāja kṛtaśekharā ।। kṛtakṛtyamivātmānaṃ mene manmathavardhinī ।।
kācidevaṃ raho nītā ramaṇena riraṃsunā ।। sarvābhyaḥ kācidātmānaṃ mene sarvaguṇādhikam ।। krīḍamānāstu gandharvair devarāmā manoramāḥ ।। tāḍyamānātha kāntena prītiṃ kācidupāyayau ।।
adṛśyata varārohā śvāsanṛtyatpayodharā ।। keśākulamukhī bhāti madhupairiva padminī ।। channā kācic cirātprāptā kāntenānviṣya yatnataḥ ।। ramaṇāliṅganaṃ cakre mano abhilaṣitaṃ ciram ।।
dhārayantī janaṃ cakre kācit tatra samanmatham ।। truṭyatsragdāmapatitaṃ ramaṇaṃ prāhasacciram ।। saṃbhrāntā kāntaśaraṇaṃ magnā kācidgatā ciram ।। śilātalagatā bhartrā dṛṣṭā kāmārtacakṣuṣā ।।
ratikrīḍitakānteva rarāja tatsarodakam ।। pūjyamānaṃ ca dadṛśe devadevaṃ janārdanam ।। maṇḍayantīḥ svagātrāṇi kāntasaṃnyastamānasāḥ ।। śṛṇvatī kāntavacanam adhikā tu tathā babhau ।।
kurvāṇā naiva bubudhe manmathāviṣṭacetanā ।। kācitpibantī dadṛśe maireyaṃ nīlaśādvale ।। kācitpapau varārohā kāntapāṇisamarpitam ।। pītvā papraccha ramaṇaṃ kva gate te mamotpale ।।
tathā viditvā mugdhatvād babhūva vrīḍitā bhṛśam ।। saviśeṣarasaṃ pānaṃ papau manmathavardhanam ।। śuśrāva vividhaṃ gītaṃ tantrīsvaravimiśritam ।। rājansadopanṛtyanti nānāvādyapuraḥsarāḥ ।।
āvasansaṃyutāḥ kāntaiḥ pararddhiracitāṃ guhām ।। nānāvicitraśayanāṃ kusumotkaramaṇḍitām ।। tapastepe mahārājan keśavārpitamānasaḥ ।। rājansvargopamaṃ deśam imaṃ prāpto asyariṃdama ।।
tānādāya gṛhaṃ gaccha tiṣṭheha yadi vā punaḥ ।। varaṃ vitaratādyaiva prasādaṃ madhusūdanāt ।। tatrovāsa sukhī māsaṃ pūjayāno janārdanam ।। tutoṣa sa jano rājñas tasyālaulyena karmaṇā ।।
māsasya madhye sa nṛpaḥ praviṣṭastadāśramaṃ ratnasahasracitram । toyāśanastatra hyuvāsa māsaṃ yāvatsitānto nṛpa phālgunasya ।। tasyaiva devadevasya śrutavāngaditaṃ śubham ।। tena rājansamāgamya kṛtakṛtyo bhaviṣyasi ।।
pratyūṣakāle vidhivat snātaḥ sa prayatendriyaḥ ।। dadarśātriṃ muniṃ rājā pratyakṣaṃ tapasāṃ nidhim ।। tataḥ śuśrāva vacanaṃ devatānāṃ samīritam ।। evaṃ prasādaṃ samprāpya devadevājjanārdanāt ।।
sarvānkāmānavāpto asau varadānena keśavāt ।। nānāratnamayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ kalpadrumasamanvitaiḥ ।। tasminnivasati śrīmān kuberaḥ saha guhyakaiḥ ।। kailāsapādasambhūtaṃ puṇyaṃ śītajalaṃ śubham ।।
tasmāt pravahate divyā nadī mandākinī śubhā ।। prāguttareṇa kailāsād divyaṃ saugandhikaṃ girim ।। candraprabho nāma giriḥ yaḥ śubhro ratnasaṃnibhaḥ ।। tasmātprabhavate divyā nadī hyacchodakā śubhā ।।
tasmingirau nivasati maṇibhadraḥ sahānugaḥ ।। puṇyā mandākinī nāma nadī hyacchodakā śubhā ।। kailāsadakṣiṇe prācyāṃ śivaṃ sarvauṣadhiṃ girim ।। lohito hemaśṛṅgastu giriḥ sūryaprabho mahān ।।
tasmātprabhavate puṇyo lauhityaśca nado mahān ।। tasmingirau nivasati yakṣo maṇidharo vaśī ।। kailāsātpaścimodīcyāṃ kakudmānauṣadhīgiriḥ ।। tadañjanaṃ traikakudaṃ śailaṃ trikakudaṃ prati ।।
tasya pāde mahaddivyaṃ mānasaṃ siddhasevitam ।। yasyāstīre vanaṃ divyaṃ vaibhrājaṃ nāma viśrutam ।। brahmadhātā nivasati rākṣaso anantavikramaḥ ।। varuṇaḥ parvataśreṣṭho rukmadhātuvibhūṣitaḥ ।।
śātakaumbhamayairdivyaiḥ śilājālaiḥ samācitaḥ ।। śṛṅgavānsumahādivyo durgaḥ śailo mahācitaḥ ।। tasya pādātprabhavati śailodaṃ nāma tatsaraḥ ।। sā cakṣusī tayormadhye praviṣṭā paścimodadhim ।।
gauraṃ tu parvataśreṣṭhaṃ haritālamayaṃ prati ।। tasya pāde mahaddivyaṃ saraḥ kāñcanavālukam ।। gaṅgārthe sa tu rājarṣir uvāsa bahulāḥ samāḥ ।। tatra tripathagā devī prathamaṃ tu pratiṣṭhitā ।।
yūpā maṇimayāstatra vimānāśca hiraṇmayāḥ ।। divyaśchāyāpathas tatra nakṣatrāṇāṃ tu maṇḍalam ।। antarikṣaṃ divaṃ caiva bhāvayitvā bhuvaṃ gatā ।। tasyā ye bindavaḥ kecit kruddhāyāḥ patitā bhuvi ।।
tatastasyā niruddhāyā bhavena sahasā ruṣā ।। bhittvā viśāmi pātālaṃ srotasā gṛhya śaṃkaram ।। tirobhāvayituṃ buddhir āsīdaṅgeṣu tāṃ nadīm ।। dhamanīsaṃtataṃ kṣīṇaṃ kṣudhāvyākulitendriyam ।।
buddhvā'sya varadānaṃ tu tataḥ kopaṃ nyayacchata ।। tato visarjayāmāsa saṃruddhāṃ svena tejasā ।। tato visarjayāmāsa sapta srotāṃsi gaṅgayā ।। srotāṃsi tripathāyāstu pratyapadyanta saptadhā ।।
sītā cakṣuśca sindhuśca tisrastā vai pratīcyagāḥ ।। tasmādbhāgīrathī sā vai praviṣṭā dakṣiṇodadhim ।। prasūtāḥ sapta nadyastu śubhā bindusarodbhavāḥ ।। saśailānkukurānraudhrān barbarānyavanānkhasān ।।
kṛtvā dvidhā himavantaṃ praviṣṭā dakṣiṇodadhim ।। tukarānbarbarākārān pahlavānpāradāñchakān ।। daradorjaguḍāṃścaiva gāndhārānaurasānkuhūn ।। saindhavānurvasānbarbān kupathānbhīmaromakān ।।
gandharvānkinnarānyakṣān rakṣovidyādharoragān ।। kirātāṃśca pulindāṃśca kurūnvai bhāratānapi ।। brahmottarāṃśca vaṅgāṃśca tāmraliptāṃstathaiva ca ।। tataḥ pratihatā vindhye praviṣṭā dakṣiṇodadhim ।।
plāvayantyupakāṃścaiva niṣādānapi sarvaśaḥ ।। kekarānekakarṇāṃśca kirātānapi caiva hi ।। sā maṇḍale samudrasya tīre bhūtvā tu sarvaśaḥ ।। kupathānplāvayantī sā indradyumnasarāṃsyapi ।।
madhyenojjānakamarūn kuthaprāvaraṇānyayau ।। tatastu pāvanī prāyāt prācīmāśāṃ javena tu ।। karṇaprāvaraṇānprāpya gatā sāśvamukhānapi ।। śaimimaṇḍalakoṣṭhaṃ tu sā praviṣṭā mahatsaraḥ ।।
upagacchanti tā nadyo yato varṣati vāsavaḥ ।। hiraṇyaśṛṅgo vasati vidvānkauberako vaśī ।। tatrāgastyaiḥ parivṛtā vidvabhirdbrahmarākṣasaiḥ ।। evameva tu vijñeyā siddhiḥ parvatavāsinām ।।
hemakūṭasya pṛṣṭhe tu sarpāṇāṃ tatsaraḥ smṛtam ।। avagāḍhe hyubhayataḥ samudrau pūrvapaścimau ।। yasmādagre prabhavati gandharvānukule ca te ।। jambūścaiva nadī puṇyā yasyāṃ jāmbūnadaṃ smṛtam ।।
puṇḍarīkātpayodācca tasmād dve samprasūyatām ।। mṛgyā ca mṛgakāntā ca tasmād dve samprasūyatām ।। nāmnā te vai jayā nāma dvādaśodadhisaṃnibhāḥ ।। kimpuruṣādyāni yānyaṣṭau teṣu devo na varṣati ।।
balāhakaśca ṛṣabho cakro maināka eva ca ।। candrakāntastathā droṇaḥ sumahāṃśca śiloccayaḥ ।। cakro badhirakaścaiva tathā nāradaparvataḥ ।। jīmūto drāvaṇaścaiva mainākaścandraparvataḥ ।।
cakramainākayormadhye divi san dakṣiṇāpathe ।। agniḥ samudravāsastu aurvo asau vaḍavāmukhaḥ ।। chidyamāneṣu pakṣeṣu purā indrasya vai bhayāt ।। te bhāratasya varṣasya bhedā yena prakīrtitāḥ ।।
uttarottarameteṣāṃ varṣam udricyate guṇaiḥ ।। samanvitāni bhūtāni teṣu varṣeṣu bhāgaśaḥ ।। ityetaddhārayadviśvaṃ pṛthvī jagadidaṃ sthitā ।। kathyamānaṃ nibodha tvaṃ śākaṃ dvīpaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।।
vistārāttriguṇaścāpi pariṇāhaḥ samantataḥ ।। tatra puṇyā janapadāś cirācca mriyate janaḥ ।। tatrāpi parvatāḥ śubhrāḥ saptaiva maṇibhūṣitāḥ ।। ṛjvāyatāḥ pratidiśaṃ niviṣṭā varṣaparvatāḥ ।।
samoditāḥ pratidiśaṃ dvīpavistāramānataḥ ।। śākadvīpe tu vakṣyāmi sapta divyānmahācalān ।। prāgāyataḥ sa sauvarṇa udayo nāma parvataḥ ।। tasyāpareṇa sumahāñ jaladhāro mahāgiriḥ ।।
tasmānnityamupādatte vāsavaḥ paramaṃ jalam ।। tatrācalau samutpannau pūrvaṃ nāradaparvatau ।। yatra śyāmatvamāpannāḥ prajāḥ pūrvamimāḥ kila ।। śabdamṛtyuḥ purā tasmin dundubhistāḍitaḥ suraiḥ ।।
tasyāpareṇa rajato mahānasto giriḥ smṛtaḥ ।। saṃbhṛtaṃ ca hṛtaṃ caiva māturarthe garutmatā ।। hiraṇyākṣo varāheṇa tasmiñchaile niṣūditaḥ ।। vibhrājastu samākhyātaḥ sphāṭikastu mahāngiriḥ ।।
saiveha keśavetyukto yato vāyuḥ pravāti ca ।। śṛṇudhvaṃ nāmatastāni yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ।। udayasyodayaṃ varṣaṃ jaladhāreti viśrutam ।। dvitīyaṃ jaladhārasya sukumāramiti smṛtam ।।
nāradasya ca kaumāraṃ tadeva ca sukhodayam ।। ānandakamiti proktaṃ tadeva munibhiḥ śubham ।। tadevāsitam ityuktaṃ varṣaṃ somakasaṃjñitam ।। tadeva dhavamityuktaṃ varṣaṃ vibhrājasaṃjñitam ।।
jambūdvīpena saṃkhyātaṃ tasya madhye vanaspatiḥ ।। eteṣu devagandharvāḥ siddhāśca saha cāraṇaiḥ ।। tatra puṇyā janapadāś cāturvarṇyasamanvitāḥ ।। dvināmnā caiva tāḥ sarvā gaṅgāḥ saptavidhāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
munitaptā ca nāmnaiṣā nadī samparikīrtitā ।। nandā ca pāvanī caiva tṛtīyā parikīrtitā ।। ikṣuśca pañcamī jñeyā tathaiva ca punaḥ kuhūḥ ।। sukṛtā ca gabhastī ca saptamī parikīrtitā ।।
bhāvayanti janaṃ sarvaṃ śākadvīpanivāsinam ।। bahūdakaparisrāvā yato varṣati vāsavaḥ ।। na śakyaṃ parisaṃkhyātuṃ puṇyāstāḥ sariduttamāḥ ।। ete śāntabhayāḥ proktāḥ pramodā ye ca vai śivāḥ ।।
varṇāśramācārayutā deśāste sapta viśrutāḥ ।। avasarpiṇī na teṣvasti tathaivotsarpiṇī punaḥ ।। tretāyugasamaḥ kālas tathā tatra pravartate ।। deśasya tu vicāreṇa kālaḥ svābhāvikaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
dharmasya cāvyabhīcārād ekāntasukhinaḥ prajāḥ ।। viparyayo na teṣvasti tadvai svābhāvikaṃ smṛtam ।। svadharmeṇa ca dharmajñās te rakṣanti parasparam ।। nadījalaiḥ parivṛtaḥ parvataścābhrasaṃnibhaiḥ ।।
anyaiśca vividhākārai ramyairjanapadaistathā ।। nityaṃ puṣpaphalopetaḥ sarvaratnasamāvṛtaḥ ।। ānupūrvyātsamāsena kuśadvīpaṃ nibodhata ।। kuśadvīpena kṣīrodaḥ sarvataḥ parivāritaḥ ।।
tatrāpi parvatāḥ sapta vijñeyā ratnayonayaḥ ।। dvināmānaśca te sarve śākadvīpe yathā tathā ।। vidrumoccaya ityuktaḥ sa eva ca mahīdharaḥ ।। dvitīyaḥ parvatastatra unnato nāma viśrutaḥ ।।
haritālamayaiḥ śṛṅgair dvīpamāvṛtya sarvaśaḥ ।। dyutimānnāmataḥ proktaḥ sa eva ca mahīdharaḥ ।। viśalyakaraṇī caiva mṛtasaṃjīvanī tathā ।। kaṅkastu pañcamasteṣāṃ parvato nāma sāravān ।।
divyapuṣpaphalopeto divyavirutsamanvitaḥ ।। sa eva tu punaḥ prokto harirityabhiviśrutaḥ ।। saptamaḥ parvatastatra kakudmānsa hi bhāṣate ।। manda ityeṣa yo dhātur apāmarthe prakāśakaḥ ।।
tatra ratnānyanekāni svayaṃ rakṣati vāsavaḥ ।। teṣāmantaraviṣkambho dviguṇaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ ।। teṣāṃ varṣāṇi vakṣyāmi saptaiva tu vibhāgaśaḥ ।। unnatasya tu vijñeyaṃ varṣaṃ lohitasaṃjñakam ।।
balāhakasya jīmūtaḥ svairathākāramityapi ।। kaṅkasyāpi kakun nāma dhṛtimaccaiva tatsmṛtam ।। kakudminastu tadvarṣaṃ kapilaṃ nāma viśrutam ।। varṣāṇi parvatāścaiva nadīsteṣu nibodhata ।।
dvināmavatyastāḥ sarvāḥ sarvāḥ puṇyajalāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। sītā dvitīyā vijñeyā sā caiva hi niśā smṛtā ।। caturthī hlādinītyuktā candrabhā iti ca smṛtā ।। puṇḍrā ṣaṣṭhī tu vijñeyā punaścaiva vibhāvarī ।।
anyāstābhyo api saṃjātāḥ śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।। ityeṣa saṃniveśo vaḥ kuśadvīpasya varṇitaḥ ।। kuśadvīpaḥ samudreṇa ghṛtamaṇḍodakena ca ।। vistārānmaṇḍalāccaiva kṣīrodāddviguṇo mataḥ ।।
kuśadvīpasya vistārād dviguṇastasya vistaraḥ ।। cakranemipramāṇena vṛto vṛttena sarvaśaḥ ।। devanātparataścāpi govindo nāma parvataḥ ।। krauñcātpare pāvanakaḥ pāvanādandhakārakaḥ ।।
devāvṛtaḥ pareṇāpi puṇḍarīko mahāngiriḥ ।। parasparasya dviguṇo viṣkambho varṣaparvataḥ ।। krauñcasya kuśalo deśo vāmanasya manonugaḥ ।। uṣṇātpare pāvanakaḥ pāvanādandhakārakaḥ ।।
munideśātpare cāpi procyate dundubhisvanaḥ ।। śrutāstatraiva nadyastu prativarṣaṃ gatāḥ śubhāḥ ।। khyātī ca puṇḍarīkā ca gaṅgā saptavidhā smṛtā ।। abhigacchanti tā nadyo bahulāśca bahūdakāḥ ।।
na śakyo vistarādvaktum api varṣaśatairapi ।। ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi śālmalasya nibodhata ।। parivārya samudraṃ tu dadhimaṇḍodakaṃ sthitaḥ ।। kuta eva tu durbhikṣaṃ kṣamātejoyutā hi te ।।
pītastu madhyamaścāsīt tataḥ kumbhamayo giriḥ ।। tṛtīyaścaiva sauvarṇo bhṛṅgapattranibho giriḥ ।। sumanāḥ kuśalo deśaḥ sukhodarkaḥ sukhodayaḥ ।। tatra ratnānyanekāni svayaṃ rakṣati vāsavaḥ ।।
na tatra meghā varṣanti śītoṣṇaṃ ca na tadvidham ।। na graho na ca candro asti īrṣyāsūyā bhayaṃ tathā ।। bhojanaṃ ṣaḍrasaṃ tatra teṣāṃ svayamupasthitam ।। ārogyabalavantaśca ekāntasukhino narāḥ ।।
sukhamāyuśca rūpaṃ ca dharmaiśvaryaṃ tathaiva ca ।। vyākhyātaḥ śālmalāntānāṃ dvīpānāṃ tu vidhiḥ śubhaḥ ।। surodena samudreṇa dviguṇena samanvitaḥ ।। surodakasamudrastu gomedena samāvṛtaḥ ।।
tasmindvīpe tu vijñeyau parvatau dvau samāhitau ।। dvitīyaḥ kumudo nāma sarvauṣadhisamanvitaḥ ।। samudrekṣurasodena vṛto gomedakaśca saḥ ।। dhātakīkumudaścaiva havyaputrau suvistṛtau ।।
dhātakinaḥ smṛtaṃ tadvai prathamaṃ prathamasya tu ।। kumudasya dvitīyasya dvitīyaṃ kumudaṃ tataḥ ।। pūrveṇa tasya dvīpasya sumanāḥ parvataḥ sthitaḥ ।। paścārdhe kumudastasya evameva sthitastu vai ।।
dakṣiṇārdhaṃ tu dvīpasya dhātakīkhaṇḍamucyate ।। etau janapadau dvau tu gomedasya tu vistṛtau ।। samudrekṣurasaṃ caiva gomedāddviguṇaṃ hi saḥ ।। puṣkareṇa vṛtaḥ śrīmāṃś citrasānumahāgiriḥ ।।
dvīpasyaiva tu pūrvārdhe citrasānuḥ sthito mahān ।। ūrdhvaṃ sa vai caturviṃśadyojanānāṃ mahābalaḥ ।। sthito velāsamīpe tu pūrvacandra ivoditaḥ ।। tasya putro mahāvītaḥ paścimārdhasya rakṣitā ।।
svādūdakenodadhinā puṣkaraḥ parivāritaḥ ।। triṃśadvarṣasahasrāṇi teṣu jīvanti mānavāḥ ।। ārogyaṃ sukhabāhulyaṃ mānasīṃ siddhimāsthitāḥ ।। adhamottamau na teṣvāstāṃ tulyāste vīryarūpataḥ ।।
na lobho na ca dambho vā na ca dveṣaḥ parigrahaḥ ।। varṇāśramāṇāṃ vārttā ca pāśupālyaṃ vaṇikkṛṣiḥ ।। na tatra varṣaṃ nadyo vā śītoṣṇaṃ ca na vidyate ।। tulyottarakurūṇāṃ tu kālastatra tu sarvadā ।।
sargastu dhātakīkhaṇḍe mahāvīte tathaiva ca ।। dvīpasyānantaro yastu samudrastatsamastu vai ।। apāṃ caiva samudrekāt samudra iti saṃjñitaḥ ।। ṛṣiratyeva ramaṇe varṣantvetena teṣu vai ।।
prakṣīyamāne bahule kṣīyate astamite ca vai ।। tato vai kṣīyamāṇe tu svātmanyeva hy apāṃ kṣayaḥ ।। tathā sa tu samudro api vardhate śaśinodaye ।। udaye astamaye cendoḥ pakṣayoḥ śuklakṛṣṇayoḥ ।।
daśottarāṇi pañcāhur aṅgulānāṃ śatāni ca ।। dvirāpatvāt smṛto dvīpo dadhanāccodadhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।। śākadvīpe tu vai śākaḥ parvatastena cocyate ।। krauñcadvīpe giriḥ krauñcas tasya nāmnā nigadyate ।।
gomedake tu gomedaḥ parvatastena cocyate ।। pūjyate sa mahādevair brahmāṃśo avyaktasambhavaḥ ।। tatra devā upāsante trayastriṃśanmaharṣibhiḥ ।। jambūdvīpātpravartante ratnāni vividhāni ca ।।
ārjavādbrahmacaryeṇa satyena ca damena ca ।। dvīpeṣu teṣu sarveṣu yathoktaṃ varṣakeṣu ca ।। bhojanaṃ cāprayatnena sadā svayamupasthitam ।। pareṇa puṣkarasyātha āvṛtyāvasthito mahān ।।
svādūdakasya paritaḥ śailastu parimaṇḍalaḥ ।। ālokastatra cārvākca nirālokastataḥ param ।। praticchinnaṃ samantāttu udakenāvṛtaṃ mahat ।। adbhyo daśaguṇaścāgniḥ sarvato dhārayaty apaḥ ।।
tiryakca maṇḍalo vāyur bhūtānyāveṣṭya dhārayan ।। bhūtādirdhārayanvyoma tasmāddaśaguṇastu vai ।। mahattattvaṃ hyanantena avyaktena tu dhāryate ।। pṛthvyādayo vikārāste paricchinnāḥ parasparam ।।
evaṃ parasparotpannā dhāryante ca parasparam ।। āsaṃste hyaviśeṣāśca viśeṣā anyaveśanāt ।। bhūtebhyaḥ paratas tebhyo hy alokaḥ sarvataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। pātre mahati pātrāṇi yathā hyantargatāni ca ।।
tathā hyāloka ākāśe bhedāstvantargatāgatāḥ ।। yāvadetāni tattvāni tāvadutpattirucyate ।। pratyākhyāyeha bhūtāni kāryotpattir na vidyate ।। te kāraṇātmakāścaiva syurbhedā mahadādayaḥ ।।
saptadvīpasamudrāṇāṃ yāthātathyena vai mayā ।। viśvarūpaṃ pradhānasya parimāṇaikadeśinaḥ ।। etāvadeva śrotavyaṃ saṃniveśasya pārthiva ।। sūryācandramasāvetau bhrājantau yāvadeva tu ।।
vistarārdhaṃ pṛthivyāstu bhavedanyatra bāhyataḥ ।। paryāsapārimāṇyāttu budhaistulyaṃ divaḥ smṛtam ।। acirāttu prakāśena avanāttu raviḥ smṛtaḥ ।। mahitatvānmahacchabdo hy asminnarthe nigadyate ।।
maṇḍalaṃ bhāskarasyātha yojanaistannibodhata ।। vistārāttriguṇaścāpi pariṇāho atra maṇḍale ।। ataḥ pṛthivyā vakṣyāmi pramāṇaṃ yojanaiḥ punaḥ ।। ityetadiha saṃkhyātaṃ purāṇe parimāṇataḥ ।।
abhimānino hyatītā ye tulyāste sāmprataistviha ।। tasmādvai sāmpratairdevair vakṣyāmi vasudhātalam ।। śatārdhakoṭivistārā pṛthivī kṛtsnaśaḥ smṛtā ।। merormadhye pratidiśaṃ koṭirekā tu sā smṛtā ।।
pañcāśacca sahasrāṇi pṛthivyardhasya vistaraḥ ।। tisraḥ koṭyastu vistārāt saṃkhyātāstu caturdiśam ।। saptadvīpasamudrāyāḥ pṛthivyāḥ sa tu vistaraḥ ।। gaṇitaṃ yojanānāṃ tu koṭyastvekādaśa smṛtāḥ ।।
ityetadvai prasaṃkhyātaṃ pṛthivyantaramaṇḍalam ।। paryāptasaṃniveśasya bhūmestāvattu maṇḍalam ।। meroḥ prācyāṃ diśāyāṃ tu mānasottaramūrdhani ।। dakṣiṇena punarmeror mānasasya tu pṛṣṭhataḥ ।।
pratīcyāṃ tu punarmeror mānasasya tu mūrdhani ।। diśyuttarasyāṃ merostu mānasasyaiva mūrdhani ।। mānasottarapṛṣṭhe tu lokapālāścaturdiśam ।। lokapālopariṣṭāttu sarvato dakṣiṇāyane ।।
dakṣiṇopakrame sūryaḥ kṣipteṣuriva sarpati ।। madhyagaścāmarāvatyāṃ yadā bhavati bhāskaraḥ ।। suṣāyāmardharātrastu vibhāvaryāstam eti ca ।। suṣāyāmatha vāruṇyām uttiṣṭhansa tu dṛśyate ।।
suṣāyāmatha vāruṇyāṃ madhyāhne tu raviryadā ।। mahendrasyāmarāvatyām udgacchati divākaraḥ ।। sa śīghrameva paryeti bhānurālātacakravat ।। evaṃ caturṣu pārśveṣu dakṣiṇānteṣu sarpati ।।
pūrvāhṇe cāparāhṇe ca dvau dvau devālayau tu saḥ ।। udito vardhamānābhir madhyāhne tapate raviḥ ।। udayāstamayābhyāṃ ca smṛte pūrvāpare tu vai ।। yatrodayastu dṛśyeta teṣāṃ sa udayaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
sarveṣāmuttare merur lokālokasya dakṣiṇe ।। śrayante raśmayo yasmāt tena rātrau na dṛśyate ।। evaṃ puṣkaramadhye tu yadā bhavati bhāskaraḥ ।। yojanānāṃ sahasrasya imāṃ saṃkhyāṃ nibodhata ।।
pañcāśacca sahasrāṇi tathānyānyadhikāni ca ।। etena kramayogeṇa yadā kāṣṭhāṃ tu dakṣiṇām ।। madhyena puṣkarasyātha bhramate dakṣiṇāyane ।। sarvato dakṣiṇasyāṃ tu kāṣṭhāyāṃ tannibodhata ।।
tathā śatasahasrāṇi catvāriṃśacca pañca ca ।। dakṣiṇādiṅnivṛtto asau viṣuvastho yadā raviḥ ।। maṇḍalaṃ viṣuvaccāpi yojanaistannibodhata ।। tathā śatasahasrāṇi viṃśatyekādhikāni tu ।।
gomedasya paradvīpe uttarāṃ ca diśaṃ caran ।। dakṣiṇottaramadhyāni tāni vindyād yathākramam ।। vaiśvānaraṃ dakṣiṇato nirdiṣṭamiha tattvataḥ ।। ubhe āṣāḍhamūlaṃ tu ajavīthyādayas trayaḥ ।।
aśvinī kṛttikā yāmyā nāgavīthyas trayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। puṣyāśleṣā punarvasvor vīthī cairāvatī smṛtā ।। pūrvottarā ca phalgunyau maghā caivārṣabhī bhavet ।। śravaṇaṃ ca dhaniṣṭhā ca vāruṇaṃ ca jaradgavam ।।
hastaścitrā tathā svātī hy ajavīthiriti smṛtā ।। mūlaṃ pūrvottarāṣāḍhe vīthī vaiśvānarī bhavet ।। kāṣṭhayorantaraṃ caitad vakṣyate yojanaiḥ punaḥ ।। śatāni trīṇi cānyāni trayastriṃśattathaiva ca ।।
kāṣṭhayorlekhayoścaiva ayane dakṣiṇottare ।। ekaikamantaraṃ tadvad yuktānyetāni saptabhiḥ ।। lekhayoḥ kāṣṭhayoścaiva bāhyābhyantarayoścaran ।। bāhyato dakṣiṇenaiva satataṃ sūryamaṇḍalam ।।
abhyantaraṃ sa paryeti kramate maṇḍalāni tu ।। yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi daśa cāṣṭau tathā smṛtam ।। viṣkambho maṇḍalasyaiva tiryaksa tu vidhīyate ।। kulālacakraparyanto yathā candro ravistathā ।।
tasmātprakṛṣṭāṃ bhūmiṃ tu kālenālpena gacchati ।। trayodaśārdhamṛkṣāṇāṃ madhye carati maṇḍalam ।। kulālacakramadhyastho yathā mandaṃ prasarpati ।। tasmāddīrgheṇa kālena bhūmiṃ so alpāṃ prasarpati ।।
