muhūrtaistāni ṛkṣāṇi rātrau dvādaśabhiścaran ।। mṛtpiṇḍa iva madhyastho bhramate asau dhruvastathā ।। ubhayoḥ kāṣṭhayormadhye bhramate maṇḍalāni tu ।। tasyaiva tu punarnaktaṃ śīghrā sūryasya vai gatiḥ ।।
gatiḥ sūryasya vai naktaṃ mandā cāpi vidhīyate ।। ajavīthyāṃ dakṣiṇāyāṃ lokālokasya cottaram ।। vyuṣṭiryāvatprabhā saurī puṣkarātsampravartate ।। yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi daśordhvaṃ cocchrito giriḥ ।।
nakṣatracandrasūryāśca grahāstārāgaṇaiḥ saha ।। etāvāneva lokastu nirālokastataḥ param ।। lokālokau tu saṃdhatte yasmātsūryaḥ paribhraman ।। uṣā rātriḥ smṛtā viprair vyuṣṭiścāpi ahaḥ smṛtam ।।
hrāso vṛddhiraharbhāgair divasānāṃ yathā tu vai ।। lekhāprabhṛtyathāditye trimuhūrtāgate tu vai ।। tasmātprātargatātkālān muhūrtāḥ saṃgavas trayaḥ ।। tasmānmadhyaṃdinātkālād aparāhṇa iti smṛtaḥ ।।
aparāhṇavyatītācca kālaḥ sāyaṃ sa ucyate ।। daśapañcamuhūrtaṃ vai ahastu viṣuve smṛtam ।। ahastu grasate rātriṃ rātristu grasate ahaḥ ।। ālokāntaḥ smṛto loko lokāccāloka ucyate ।।
catvāraste mahātmānas tiṣṭhantyābhūtasaṃplavam ।। hiraṇyaromā parjanyaḥ ketumānrājasaśca saḥ ।। lokapālāḥ sthitāstvete lokāloke caturdiśam ।। pitṛyānaḥ smṛtaḥ panthā vaiśvānarapathādbahiḥ ।।
lokasya saṃtānakarāḥ pitṛyāne pathi sthitāḥ ।। prārabhante lokakāmās teṣāṃ panthāḥ sa dakṣiṇaḥ ।। saṃtaptatapasā caiva maryādābhiḥ śrutena ca ।। paścimāścaiva pūrveṣāṃ jāyante nidhaneṣviha ।।
aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi ṛṣīṇāṃ gṛhamedhinām ।। kriyāvatāṃ prasaṃkhyaiṣā ye śmaśānāni bhejire ।। icchādveṣaratāccaiva maithunopagamācca vai ।। ityetaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ siddhāḥ śmaśānānīha bhejire ।।
saṃtatiṃ te jugupsante tasmānmṛtyurjitastu taiḥ ।। udakpanthā na paryantam āśrityābhūtasaṃplavam ।। īrṣyādveṣanivṛttyā ca bhūtārambhavivarjanāt ।। ityetaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ śuddhais te amṛtatvaṃ hi bhejire ।।
trailokyasthitikālo hi na punarmāragāmiṇām ।। ābhūtasamplavānte tu kṣīyante cordhvaretasaḥ ।। etadviṣṇupadaṃ divyaṃ tṛtīyaṃ vyomni bhāsvaram ।। dharme dhruvasya tiṣṭhanti ye tu lokasya kāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।।
sūryācandramasoś cāraṃ grahāṇāṃ caiva sarvaśaḥ ।। avyūhenaiva sarvāṇi tathā cāsaṃkareṇa vā ।। etadveditum icchāmas tato nigada sattama ।। pratyakṣamapi dṛśyaṃ tat saṃmohayati vai prajāḥ ।।
uttānapādaputro asau meḍhībhūto dhruvo divi ।। bhramantamanusarpanti nakṣatrāṇi ca cakravat ।। vātānīkamayair bandhair dhruve baddhaḥ prasarpati ।। astodayāstathotpātā ayane dakṣiṇottare ।।
jīmūtā nāma te meghā yadebhyo jīvasambhavaḥ ।। ito yojanamātrācca adhyardhavikṛtā api ।। puṣkarāvartakā nāma ye meghāḥ pakṣasambhavāḥ ।। kāmagānāṃ samṛddhānāṃ bhūtānāṃ nāśamicchatām ।।
puṣkarāvartakā nāma kāraṇeneha śabditāḥ ।। kalpāntavṛṣṭikartāraḥ kalpāntāgner niyāmakāḥ ।। yānyasyāṇḍasya bhinnasya prākṛtānyabhavaṃstadā ।। tānyevāṇḍakapālāni sarve meghāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।।
teṣāṃ śreṣṭhaśca parjanyaś catvāraścaiva diggajāḥ ।। kulamekaṃ dvidhā bhūtaṃ yonirekā jalaṃ smṛtam ।। tuṣāravarṣaṃ varṣanti vṛddhā hyannavivṛddhaye ।। yau asau bibharti bhagavān gaṅgāmākāśagocarām ।।
tasyā vispanditaṃ toyaṃ diggajāḥ pṛthubhiḥ karaiḥ ।। dakṣiṇena giriryo asau hemakūṭa iti smṛtaḥ ।। puṇḍraṃ nāma samākhyātaṃ samyagvṛṣṭivivṛddhaye ।। tato himavato vāyur himaṃ tatra samudbhavam ।।
himavantamatikramya vṛṣṭiśeṣaṃ tataḥ param ।। varṣadvayaṃ samākhyātaṃ samyagvṛṣṭivivṛddhaye ।। sūrya eva tu vṛṣṭīnāṃ sraṣṭā samupadiśyate ।। śubhāśubhaphalānīha dhruvātsarvaṃ pravartate ।।
sarvabhūtaśarīreṣu tv āpo hyanuśritāśca yāḥ ।। dhūmabhūtāstu tā hyāpo niṣkrāmantīha sarvaśaḥ ।। tejobhiḥ sarvalokebhya ādatte raśmibhirjalam ।। tatastvṛtuvaśātkāle parivartandivākaraḥ ।।
abhrasthāḥ prapatantyāpo vāyunā samudīritāḥ ।। vāyubhiḥ stanitaṃ caiva vidyutastvagnijāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। sraṣṭāsau vṛṣṭisargasya dhruveṇādhiṣṭhito raviḥ ।। grahannivṛttyā sūryāttu carate ṛkṣamaṇḍalam ।।
ataḥ sūryarathasyāpi saṃniveśaṃ pracakṣate ।। cakreṇa bhāsvatā sūryaḥ syandanena prasarpiṇā ।। dviguṇā ca rathopasthād īṣādaṇḍaḥ pramāṇataḥ ।। asaṅgaḥ kāñcano divyo yuktaḥ pavanagairhayaiḥ ।।
vāruṇasya rathasyeha lakṣaṇaiḥ sadṛśaśca saḥ ।। saṃvatsarasyāvayavaiḥ kalpitāni yathākramam ।। arāḥ saṃvatsarāstasya nemyaḥ ṣaḍṛtavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। akṣakoṭyoryugānyasya ārtavāhāḥ kalāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
nimeṣaścānukarṣo asya īṣā cāsya kalā smṛtā ।। saptāśvarūpāśchandāṃsi vahante vāyuraṃhasā ।। paṅktiśca bṛhatī caiva uṣṇigeva tu saptamam ।। sahacakro bhramatyakṣaḥ sahākṣo bhramati dhruvaḥ ।।
evamarthavaśāttasya saṃniveśo rathasya tu ।। tenāsau taraṇirdevo nabhasaḥ sarpate divam ।। bhramato bhramato raśmī tau cakrayugayostu vai ।। kulālacakrabhramavan maṇḍalaṃ sarvatodiśam ।।
saṃkramete dhruvamaho maṇḍale sarvatodiśam ।। vardhete dakṣiṇeṣvatra bhramato maṇḍalāni tu ।। dhruveṇa pragṛhītau tau rathau yau vanato ravim ।। tadā so abhyantare sūryo bhramate maṇḍalāni tu ।।
dhruveṇa mucyamānena punā raśmiyugena ca ।। udveṣṭayanvai vegena maṇḍalāni tu gacchati ।। tato vahatyathādityaṃ bahubhir ṛṣibhiḥ saha ।। ete vasanti vai sūrye māsau dvau dvau krameṇa ca ।।
uragau vāsukiścaiva saṃkīrṇaścaiva tāvubhau ।। kṛtasthalāpsarāścaiva yā ca sā puñjikasthalā ।। rakṣo hetiḥ prahetiśca yātudhānāvubhau ṛtau ।। vasangrīṣme tu dvau māsau mitraśca varuṇaśca vai ।।
menakā sahajanyā ca hāhā hūhūśca gāyakau ।। puruṣādo vadhaścaiva yātudhānau tu tau smṛtau ।। tataḥ sūrye punaścānyā nivasanti sma devatāḥ ।। elāpattrastathā sarpaḥ śaṅkhapālaśca pannagaḥ ।।
pramlocetyapsarāścaiva nimrocantī ca te ubhe ।। nabhasyanabhasoretair vasantaśca divākare ।। parjanyaścaiva pūṣā ca bharadvājaḥ sagautamaḥ ।। viśvācī ca ghṛtācī ca ubhe te puṇyalakṣaṇe ।।
senajicca suṣeṇaśca senānīr grāmaṇīs tathā ।। vasantyete ca vai sūrye māsayośca tviṣorjayoḥ ।। aṃśo bhagaśca dvāvetau kaśyapaśca kratuśca tau ।। citrasenaśca gandharvaḥ pūrṇāyuścaiva gāyanau ।।
tārkṣyaścāriṣṭanemiśca senānīr grāmaṇīś ca tau ।। sahe caiva sahasye ca vasantyete divākare ।। tvaṣṭā viṣṇurjamadagnir viśvāmitrastathaiva ca ।। gandharvau dhṛtarāṣṭraśca sūryavarcāśca tāvubhau ।।
grāmaṇīr ṛtajiccaiva satyajicca mahābalaḥ ।। ityete nivasanti sma dvau dvau māsau divākare ।। sūryamāpādayantyete tejasā teja uttamam ।। gandharvāpsarasaścaiva gītanṛtyairupāsate ।।
sarpāḥ sarpanti vai sūrye yātudhānānuyānti ca ।। eteṣāmeva devānāṃ yathāvīryaṃ yathātapaḥ ।। tathā tapatyasau sūryas teṣāmiddhastu tejasā ।। mānavānāṃ śubhairhyetair hriyate duritaṃ tu vai ।।
ete sahaiva sūryeṇa bhramanti sānugā divi ।। gopāyanti sma bhūtāni īhante hyanukampayā ।। atītānāgatānāṃ ca vartante sāmprataṃ ca ye ।। caturdaśeṣu vartante gaṇā manvantareṣu vai ।।
dharmaṃ himaṃ ca varṣaṃ ca yathākramamaharniśam ।। śukle ca kṛṣṇe tadahaḥkrameṇa kālakṣaye caiva surāḥ pibanti ।। sarve amṛtaṃ tatpitaraḥ pibanti devāśca saumyāśca tathaiva kāvyāḥ ।। vṛṣṭyābhivṛṣṭābhir athauṣadhībhir martyā athānnena kṣudhaṃ jayanti ।।
annena jīvantyaniśaṃ manuṣyāḥ sūryaḥ śritaṃ taddhi bibharti gobhiḥ ।। tatra tairakramairaśvaiḥ sarpate asau dinakṣaye ।। punaḥ pramuñcatyatha tāśca yo hariḥ sa muhyamāno haribhisturaṃgamaiḥ ।। saptadvīpasamudrāṃśca saptabhiḥ saptabhirdrutam ।।
kāmarūpaiḥ sakṛdyuktaiḥ kāmagaistairmanojavaiḥ ।। bāhyato anantaraṃ caiva maṇḍalaṃ divasakramāt ।। āvṛto vālakhilyaiśca bhramate rātryahāni tu ।। sevyate gītanṛtyaiśca gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ ।।
vīthyāśrayāṇi carati nakṣatrāṇi tathā śaśī ।। tricakrobhayato aśvaśca vijñeyaḥ śaśino rathaḥ ।। sahāraistaistribhiścakrair yuktaḥ śuklairhayottamaiḥ ।। sakṛdyukte rathe tasmin vahantastvāyugakṣayam ।।
aśvāstamekavarṇāste vahante śaṅkhavarcasaḥ ।। aṃśumān saptadhātuśca haṃso vyomamṛgastathā ।। evaṃ candramasaṃ devaṃ vahanti smāyugakṣayam ।। somasya śuklapakṣādau bhāskare parataḥ sthite ।।
tataḥ pītakṣayaṃ somaṃ yupagadvyāpayan raviḥ ।। āpūrayandadau tena bhāgaṃ bhāgamahaḥkramāt ।। tasmāddhrasanti vai kṛṣṇe śukle hyāpyāyayanti ca ।। paurṇamāsyāṃ pradṛśyeta śuklaḥ sampūrṇamaṇḍalaḥ ।।
tato dvitīyāprabhṛti bahulasya caturdaśī ।। pibantyambumayaṃ devā madhu saumyaṃ tathāmṛtam ।। bhakṣārthamāgataṃ somaṃ paurṇamāsyāmupāsate ।। somasya kṛṣṇapakṣādau bhāskarābhimukhasya vai ।।
trayaśca triṃśatā sārdhaṃ trayastriṃśacchatāni tu ।। ityevaṃ pīyamānasya kṛṣṇe vardhanti tāḥ kalāḥ ।। evaṃ dinakramātpīte devaiścāpi niśākare ।। pitaraścopatiṣṭhanti amāvāsyāṃ niśākaram ।।
tato aparāhṇe pitaro jaghanyadivase punaḥ ।। viniḥsṛṣṭaṃ tvamāvāsyāṃ gabhastibhyastadāmṛtam ।। saumyā barhiṣadaścaiva agniṣvāttāśca ye smṛtāḥ ।। saṃvatsarāśca ye kāvyāḥ pañcābdā vai dvijāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
agniṣvāttās trayaścaiva pitṛsargasthitā dvijāḥ ।। yāvacca kṣīyate tasmād bhāgaḥ pañcadaśastu saḥ ।। evaṃ sūryanimitte te kṣayavṛddhī niśākare ।। atha tejomayaḥ śubhraḥ somaputrasya vai rathaḥ ।।
śvetaḥ piśaṅgaḥ sāraṅgo nīlaḥ śyāmo vilohitaḥ ।। daśabhistu mahābhāgair uttamairvātasambhavaiḥ ।। sarpate asau kumāro vai ṛjuvakrānuvakragaḥ ।। gaurāśvena tu raukmeṇa syandanena visarpati ।।
abdaṃ vasati yo rāśau svadiśaṃ tena gacchati ।। rathena kṣipravegeṇa bhārgavastena gacchati ।। kārṣṇāyasaṃ samāruhya syandanaṃ yātyasau śaniḥ ।। rathaṃ tamomayaṃ tasya vahanti sma sudaṃśitāḥ ।।
ādityameti somācca tamaso anteṣu parvasu ।। palāladhūmavarṇābhāḥ kṣāmadehāḥ sudāruṇāḥ ।। sarve dhruve nibaddhāste nibaddhā vātaraśmibhiḥ ।। vāya yābhiradṛśyābhiḥ prabaddhā vātaraśmibhiḥ ।।
yāvattamanuparyeti dhruvaṃ ca jyotiṣāṃ gaṇaḥ ।। tasmādyāni pragṛhyante vyomni devagṛhā iti ।। sarvā dhruvanibaddhāstā bhramantyo bhrāmayanti ca ।। tathā bhramanti jyotīṃṣi vātabaddhāni sarvaśaḥ ।।
yasmātpravahate tāni pravahastena sa smṛtaḥ ।। eṣa tārāmayaḥ proktaḥ śiśumāre dhruvo divi ।। śiśumāraśarīrasthā yāvatyastārakāstu tāḥ ।। śiśumārākṛtiṃ jñātvā pravibhāgena sarvaśaḥ ।।
yajño adharastu vijñeyo dharmo mūrdhānamāśritaḥ ।। varuṇaścāryamā caiva paścime tasya sakthinī ।। pucche agniśca mahendraśca marīciḥ kaśyapo dhruvaḥ ।। nakṣatracandrasūryāśca grahāstārāgaṇaiḥ saha ।।
dhruveṇādhiṣṭhitāścaiva dhruvameva pradakṣiṇam ।। āgnīdhrakāśyapānāṃ tu teṣāṃ sa paramo dhruvaḥ ।। merumālokayanneva pratiyāti pradakṣiṇam ।। kathaṃ devagṛhāṇi syuḥ punarjyotīṃṣi varṇaya ।।
yathā devagṛhāṇi syuḥ sūryācandramasostathā ।। avyākṛtamidaṃ tvāsīn naiśena tamasā vṛtam ।। svayambhūr bhagavāṃstatra lokatattvārthasādhakaḥ ।। jñātvāgniṃ kalpakālādāv apaḥ pṛthvīṃ ca saṃśritā ।।
pācako yastu loke asmin pārthivaḥ so agnirucyate ।। vaidyuto jāṭharaḥ saumyo vaidyutaścāpyabindhanaḥ ।। kāṣṭhendhanastu nirmathyaḥ so adbhiḥ śāmyati pāvakaḥ ।। yaścāsau maṇḍale śukle nirūṣmā na prakāśate ।।
agnimāviśate rātrau tasmādagniḥ prakāśate ।। pādena tejasaścāgnes tasmāt saṃtapate divā ।। parasparānupraveśād āpyāyete divāniśam ।। uttiṣṭhati punaḥ sūrye rātrirāviśate hy apaḥ ।।
astaṃ gate punaḥ sūrye aharvai praviśaty apaḥ ।। etena kramayogeṇa bhūmyardhe dakṣiṇottare ।। yaścāsau tapate sūryaḥ so apaḥ pibati raśmibhiḥ ।। ādatte sa tu nāḍīnāṃ sahasreṇa samantataḥ ।।
tasya raśmisahasreṇa śītavarṣoṣṇaniḥsravaḥ ।। candanāścaiva medhyāśca ketanāś cetanāstathā ।। candratārāgrahaiḥ sarvaiḥ pītā bhānorgabhastayaḥ ।। śuklāśca kakubhaścaiva gāvo viśvasṛtaśca yāḥ ।।
saṃbibhrati hi tāḥ sarvā manuṣyāndevatāḥ pitṝn ।। amṛtena surānsarvān saṃtataṃ paritarpayan ।। varṣāsu ca śaradyevaṃ caturbhiḥ saṃpravarṣati ।। oṣadhīṣu balaṃ dhatte sudhāṃ ca svadhayā punaḥ ।।
evaṃ raśmisahasraṃ tu sauraṃ lokārthasādhakam ।। ityevaṃ maṇḍalaṃ śuklaṃ bhāsvaraṃ lokasaṃjñitam ।। candra ṛkṣagrahāḥ sarve vijñeyāḥ sūryasambhavāḥ ।। harikeśaḥ purastāttu yo vai nakṣatrayonikṛt ।।
viśvāvasuśca yaḥ paścāc chukrayoniśca sa smṛtaḥ ।। ṣaṣṭhastu hyaśvabhū raśmir yoniḥ sa hi bṛhaspateḥ ।। na kṣīyate yatastāni tasmānnakṣatratā smṛtā ।। kṣetrāṇi teṣāmādatte sūryo nakṣatratā tataḥ ।।
tāraṇāttārakā hyetāḥ śuklatvāccaiva śuklikāḥ ।। tapanastejaso yogād āditya iti gadyate ।। sravaṇāttejasaścaiva tenāsau savitā smṛtaḥ ।। śuklatve hyamṛtatve ca śītatve hlādane api ca ।।
jalatejomaye śukle vṛttakumbhanibhe śubhe ।। manvantareṣu sarveṣu ṛṣisūryagrahādayaḥ ।। sauraṃ sūryo aviśatsthānaṃ saumyaṃ somastathaiva ca ।। bṛhaspatirbṛhattvaṃ ca lohitaṃ cāpi lohitaḥ ।।
budho api vai budhasthānaṃ bhānuṃ svarbhānureva ca ।। jyotīṃṣi sukṛtām ete jñeyā devagṛhāstu vai ।। manvantareṣu sarveṣu devasthānāni tāni vai ।। atītāstu sahātītair bhāvyā bhāvyaiḥ suraiḥ saha ।।
sūryo devo vivasvāṃśca aṣṭamastvaditeḥ sutaḥ ।। śukro daityastu vijñeyo bhārgavo asurayājakaḥ ।। budho manoharaścaiva śaśiputrastu sa smṛtaḥ ।। agnirvikeśyāṃ jajñe tu yuvāsau lohitādhipaḥ ।।
svarbhānuḥ siṃhikāputro bhūtasaṃsādhano asuraḥ ।। sthānānyetāni coktāni sthāninyaścaiva devatāḥ ।। sahasrāṃśutviṣaḥ sthānam ammayaṃ taijasaṃ tathā ।। śukraḥ ṣoḍaśaraśmistu yastu devo hyapomayaḥ ।।
bṛhaddvādaśaraśmīkaṃ haridrābhaṃ tu vedhasaḥ ।। svarbhānostvāyasaṃ sthānaṃ bhūtasaṃtāpanālayam ।। tāraṇāttārakā hyetāḥ śuklatvāccaiva tārakāḥ ।। maṇḍalaṃ triguṇaṃ cāsya vistāro bhāskarasya tu ।।
triguṇaṃ maṇḍalaṃ cāsya vaipulyācchaśinaḥ smṛtam ।। yojanārdhapramāṇāni tābhyo anyāni gaṇāni tu ।। uddhūtya pārthivīṃ chāyāṃ nirmitāṃ maṇḍalākṛtim ।। ādityātsa tu niṣkramya somaṃ gacchati parvasu ।।
svabhāsā tudate yasmāt svarbhānuriti sa smṛtaḥ ।। viṣkambhānmaṇḍalāccaiva yojanānāṃ tu sa smṛtaḥ ।। bṛhaspateḥ pādahīnau ketuvakrāvubhau smṛtau ।। tārānakṣatrarūpāṇi vapuṣmantīha yāni vai ।।
tārānakṣatrarūpāṇi hīnāni tu parasparam ।। sarvopari nisṛṣṭāni maṇḍalāni tu tārakāḥ ।। upariṣṭāttu ye teṣāṃ grahā ye krūrasāttvikāḥ ।। tebhyo adhastāttu catvāraḥ punaścānye mahāgrahāḥ ।।
yāvanti caiva ṛkṣāṇi koṭyastāvanti tārakāḥ ।। vistīrṇaṃ maṇḍalaṃ kṛtvā tasyordhvaṃ carate śaśī ।। nakṣatrebhyo budhaścordhvaṃ budhāccordhvaṃ tu bhārgavaḥ ।। tasmācchanaiścaraścordhvaṃ devācāryopari sthitaḥ ।।
saptarṣibhyo dhruvaścordhvaṃ samastaṃ tridivaṃ dhruve ।। grahāntaram athaikaikam ūrdhvaṃ nakṣatramaṇḍalāt ।। grahāśca candrasūryau ca divi divyena tejasā ।। candrārkagrahanakṣatrā nīcoccagṛhamāśritāḥ ।।
parasparaṃ sthitā hyevaṃ yujyante ca parasparam ।। ityevaṃ saṃniveśo vai pṛthivyā jyotiṣāṃ ca yaḥ ।। varṣāṇāṃ ca nadīnāṃ ca ye ca teṣu vasanti vai ।। āvartaḥ sāntaro madhye saṃkṣiptaśca dhruvāttu sa ।।
lokasaṃvyavahārārtham īśvareṇa vinirmitaḥ ।। ityeṣa saṃniveśo vai sarvasya jyotirātmakaḥ ।। gatāgataṃ manuṣyeṇa jyotiṣāṃ māṃsacakṣuṣā ।। dadāha ca kathaṃ devas tanno vistarato vada ।।
devenaikeṣuṇā dagdhaṃ tathā no vada mānada ।। mayo nāma mahāmāyo māyānāṃ janako asuraḥ ।। tapasyantaṃ tu taṃ viprā daityāvanyāvanugrahāt ।। vidyunmālī ca balavāṃs tārakākhyaśca vīryavān ।।
lokā iva yathā mūrtās trayas traya ivāgnayaḥ ।। hemante jalaśayyāsu grīṣme pañcatape tathā ।। sevānāḥ phalamūlāni puṣpāṇi ca jalāni ca ।। magnāḥ śaivālapaṅkeṣu vimalāvimaleṣu ca ।।
teṣāṃ tapaḥprabhāvena prabhāvavidhutaṃ yathā ।। dahyamāneṣu lokeṣu taistribhirdānavāgnibhiḥ ।। tataḥ sāhasakartāraḥ prāhuste sahasāgatam ।। atha tāndānavānbrahmā tapasā tapanaprabhān ।।
varado ahaṃ hi vo vatsās tapastoṣita āgataḥ ।। ityevamucyamānāstu pratipannaṃ pitāmaham ।। deva daityāḥ purā devaiḥ saṃgrāme tārakāmaye ।। devairvairānubandhācca dhāvanto bhayavepitāḥ ।।
so ahaṃ tapaḥprabhāvena tava bhaktyā tathaiva ca ।। tasmiṃśca tripure durge matkṛte kṛtināṃ vara ।। devapraharaṇānāṃ ca devānāṃ ca prajāpateḥ ।। viśvakarmā itīvoktaḥ sa tadā viśvakarmaṇā ।।
sarvāmaratvaṃ naivāsti asadvṛttasya dānava ।। pitāmahavacaḥ śrutvā tadaivaṃ dānavo mayaḥ ।। yastadekeṣuṇā durgaṃ sakṛnmuktena nirdahet ।। evamastviti cāpyuktvā mayaṃ devaḥ pitāmahaḥ ।।
gate pitāmahe daityā gatā mayaraviprabhāḥ ।। sa mayastu mahābuddhir dānavo vṛṣasattamaḥ ।। kathaṃ nāma bhaveddurgaṃ tanmayā tripuraṃ kṛtam ।। yathācaikeṣuṇā tena tatpuraṃ na hi hanyate ।।
vistāro yojanaśatam ekaikasya purasya tu ।। puṣyayogeṇa nirmāṇaṃ purāṇaṃ ca bhaviṣyati ।। puṣyayogeṇa yuktāni yastānyāsādayiṣyati ।। āyasaṃ tu kṣititale rājataṃ tu nabhastale ।।
śatayojanaviṣkambhair antaraistaddurāsadam ।। dvārairmahāmandaramerukalpaiḥ prākāraśṛṅgaiḥ suvirājamānam ।। ko nāma hantuṃ tripuraṃ samartho muktvā trinetraṃ bhagavantamekam ।। cakāra tripuraṃ durgaṃ manaḥsaṃcāracāritam ।।
iha cāṭṭālakadvāram iha cāṭṭālagopuram ।। rathyoparathyāḥ sattrikā iha catvara eva ca ।। savaṭāni taḍāgāni hy atra vāpyaḥ sarāṃsi ca ।। upanirgamo dānavānāṃ bhavatyatra manoharaḥ ।।
mayena tatpuraṃ sṛṣṭaṃ tripuraṃ tviti naḥ śrutam ।। tārakākhyo adhipastatra kṛtasthānādhipo avasat ।। vidyunmālī prabhustatra vidyunmālī tvivāmbudaḥ ।। svayameva mayastatra gatastadadhipaḥ prabhuḥ ।।
vidyunmālipuraṃ cāpi śatayojanake antare ।। puṣyasaṃyogamātreṇa kālena sa mayaḥ purā ।। yena yena mayo yāti prakurvāṇaḥ puraṃ purāt ।। rukmarūpyāyasānāṃ ca śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।।
prāsādaśatajuṣṭāni kūṭāgārotkaṭāni ca ।। sodyānavāpīkūpāni sapadmasaravanti ca ।। citraśālāviśālāni catuḥśālottamāni ca ।। bahudhvajapatākāni sragdāmālaṃkṛtāni ca ।।
susaṃyuktopaliptāni puṣpanaivedyavanti ca ।। gaganāvaraṇābhāni haṃsapaṅktinibhāni ca ।। muktākalāpairlambadbhir hasantīva śaśiśriyam ।। pañcendriyasukhairnityaṃ samaiḥ satpuruṣairiva ।।
prākārāstripure tasmin giriprākārasaṃnibhāḥ ।। sapatākādhvajavatāṃ dṛśyante giriśṛṅgavat ।। svargātiriktaśrīkāṇi tatra kanyāpurāṇi ca ।। sarobhiśca saridbhiśca vanaiścopavanairapi ।।
parikhāśatagambhīrāḥ kṛtā māyānivāraṇaiḥ ।। diteḥ sutā daivatarājavairiṇaḥ sahasraśaḥ prāpuranantavikramāḥ ।। babhūva pūrṇaṃ tripuraṃ tathā purā yathāmbaraṃ bhūrijalair jalapradaiḥ ।। taddurgaṃ durgatāṃ prāpa baddhavairaiḥ surāsuraiḥ ।।
mayādiṣṭāni viviśur gṛhāṇi hṛṣitāśca te ।। roṣaiścaivātipāruṣyaiḥ śarīramiva saṃhataiḥ ।। tripuraṃ saṃkulaṃ jātaṃ daityakoṭiśatākulam ।। upatasthuḥ payodābhā ye ca giryupajīvinaḥ ।।
tasya tasya mayastatra māyayā vidadhāti saḥ ।। ārāmeṣu sacūteṣu tapodhanavaneṣu ca ।। mṛṣṭābharaṇavastrāśca mṛṣṭasraganulepanāḥ ।। nārībhiḥ satataṃ remur muditāścaiva dānavāḥ ।।
arthe dharme ca kāme ca nidadhuste matīḥ svayam ।। vrajati sma sukhaṃ kālaḥ svargasthānāṃ yathā tathā ।। vimuktakalahāścāpi prītayaḥ pracurābhavan ।। arcayanto diteḥ putrās tripurāyatane haram ।।
svanūpuraravonmiśrān veṇuvīṇāravānapi ।। tripure dānavendrāṇāṃ ramatāṃ śrūyate sadā ।। dharmārthakāmamantrāṇāṃ mahānkālo abhyavartata ।। kaliśca kalahaścaiva tripuraṃ viviśuḥ saha ।।
samadhyāsuḥ samaṃ ghorāḥ śarīrāṇi yathāmayāḥ ।। svapne bhayāvahā dṛṣṭā āviśantastu dānavān ।। mayaḥ sabhāmāviveśa bhāskarābhyāmivāmbudaḥ ।। āsīnāḥ kāñcanagireḥ śṛṅge toyamuco yathā ।।
upaviṣṭau mayasyānte hastinaḥ kalabhāviva ।। upaviṣṭā dṛḍhaṃ viddhā dānavā devaśatravaḥ ।। mayo māyāvijanaka ityuvāca sa dānavān ।। niśāmayadhvaṃ svapno ayaṃ mayā dṛṣṭo bhayāvahaḥ ।।
kopānalādīptamukhāḥ praviṣṭās tripurārdinaḥ ।। praviṣṭāḥ sma śarīrāṇi bhūtvā bahuśarīriṇaḥ ।। sagṛhaṃ saha yuṣmābhiḥ sāgarāmbhasi majjitam ।। puruṣaḥ sindutilakaś caturaṅghris trilocanaḥ ।।
īdṛśī pramadā dṛṣṭā mayā cātibhayāvahā ।। dṛṣṭaḥ kathaṃ hi kaṣṭāya asurāṇāṃ bhaviṣyati ।। nibodhadhvaṃ sumanaso na cāsūyitum arhatha ।। satye dame ca dharme ca munivāde ca tiṣṭhata ।।
yadi nāmāsya svapnasya hy evaṃ coparamo bhavet ।। bhaviṣyāṇi ca dṛśyante yato nastripure asurāḥ ।। svapnodayaṃ pratīkṣadhvaṃ kālodayamathāpi ca ।। krodherṣyāvasthayā yuktā dṛśyante ca vināśagāḥ ।।
tatraiva dṛṣṭvā te anyonyaṃ sakrodhāpūritekṣaṇāḥ ।। hitvā satyaṃ ca dharmaṃ ca akāryāṇyupacakramuḥ ।। guruṃ caiva na manyante hy anyonyaṃ cāpi cukrudhuḥ ।। parasparaṃ ca nindanti ahamityeva vādinaḥ ।।
akasmātsāśrunayanā jāyante ca samutsukāḥ ।। bhakṣayanti ca śeranta ucchiṣṭāḥ saṃvṛtāstathā ।। saṃviśanti ca śayyāsu śaucācāravivarjitāḥ ।। bhāryāṃ gatvā na śudhyanti rahovṛttiṣu nistrapāḥ ।।
devāṃstapodhanāṃścaiva bādhante tripurālayāḥ ।। vipriyāṇyeva viprāṇāṃ kurvāṇāḥ kalahaiṣiṇaḥ ।। aśokaṃ ca varāśokaṃ sarvartukamathāpi ca ।। vidhvaṃsayanti saṃkruddhās tapodhanavanāni ca ।।
jagadbabhūvāmararājaduṣṭair abhidrutaṃ sasyamivālivṛndaiḥ ।। lokeṣūtsādyamāneṣu tapodhanavaneṣu ca ।। trailokye bhayasaṃmūḍhe tamondhanvam upāgate ।। bhītāḥ śaraṇamājagmur brahmāṇāṃ prapitāmaham ।।
nemurūcuśca sahitāḥ pañcāsyaṃ caturānanam ।। bādhante asmānyathā preṣyān anuśādhi tato anagha ।। dānavānāṃ bhayāttadvad bhramāmo hi pitāmaha ।। dānavairbhrāmyamāṇānāṃ vismṛtāni tato anagha ।।
dānavairlomamohāndhaiḥ kriyante ca bhramanti ca ।। dharṣaṇānena nirdevaṃ nirmanuṣyāśramaṃ jagat ।। pratyāha tridaśān sendrān indutulyānanaḥ prabhuḥ ।। tasyānta eṣa samprāpto yaḥ purokto mayā surāḥ ।।
ekeṣupātamokṣeṇa hantavyaṃ neṣuvṛṣṭibhiḥ ।। yastu caikaprahāreṇa puraṃ hanyāt sadānavam ।। ekaṃ muktvā mahādevaṃ maheśānaṃ prajāpatim ।। yācāmaḥ sahitā devaṃ tripuraṃ sa haniṣyati ।।
puṣyayogeṇa yuktāni tāni caikakṣaṇena tu ।। pitāmahaśca taiḥ sārdhaṃ bhavasaṃsadamāgataḥ ।। paśyanti comayā sārdhaṃ nandinā ca mahātmanā ।। agnyādityasahasrābham agnivarṇavibhūṣitam ।।
astuvangopatiṃ śambhuṃ varadaṃ pārvatīpatim ।। paśūnāṃ pataye nityam ugrāya ca kapardine ।। īśānāya bhayaghnāya namastvandhakaghātine ।। kumāraśatrunighnāya kumārajanakāya ca ।।
nityaṃ nīlaśikhaṇḍāya śūline divyaśāyine ।। acintyāyāmbikābhartre sarvadevastutāya ca ।। tapyamānāya salile brahmaṇyāyājitāya ca ।। namo astu divyarūpāya prabhave divyaśambhave ।।
bhaktānukampine nityaṃ diśate yanmanogatam ।। prajāpatimuvācedaṃ devānāṃ kva bhayaṃ mahat ।। tāvadeva prayacchāmi nāstyadeyaṃ mayā hi vaḥ ।। carāmi mahadatyugraṃ yaccāpi paramaṃ tapaḥ ।।
teṣāmabhāvaḥ saṃpādyo yuṣmākaṃ bhava eva ca ।। rudramāhurmahābhāgaṃ bhāgārhāḥ sarva eva te ।। asurairvadhyamānāḥ sma vayaṃ tvāṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।। tripuraṃ yena taddurgaṃ kṛtaṃ pāṇḍuragopuram ।।
bādhante asmānmahādeva preṣyamasvāminaṃ yathā ।। varāścāpsarasaḥ sarvā rambhādyā danujairhṛtāḥ ।। airāvatādyā apahṛtā devatānāṃ maheśvara ।। jātāśca dānavānāṃ te rathayogyāsturaṃgamāḥ ।।
tanno vyapahṛtaṃ daityaiḥ saṃśayo jīvite punaḥ ।। uvāca devāndeveśo varado vṛṣavāhanaḥ ।। tadahaṃ tripuraṃ dhakṣye kriyatāṃ yadbravīmi tat ।। rathamaupayikaṃ mahyaṃ sajjayadhvaṃ kimāsyate ।।
tathetyuktvā mahādevaṃ cakruste rathamuttamam ।। adhiṣṭhānaṃ śiro meror akṣo mandara eva ca ।। kṛṣṇapakṣaṃ śuklapakṣaṃ pakṣadvayamapīśvarāḥ ।। ādidvayaṃ pakṣayantraṃ yantrametāśca devatāḥ ।।
bhārgavaścāṅgirāścaiva budho aṅgāraka eva ca ।। varūthaṃ gaganaṃ cakruś cārurūpaṃ rathasya te ।। maṇimuktendranīlaiśca vṛtaṃ hyaṣṭamukhaiḥ suraiḥ ।। vitastā ca vipāśā ca yamunā gaṇḍakī tathā ।।
etāḥ saridvarāḥ sarvā veṇusaṃjñā kṛtā rathe ।। vāsukeḥ kulajā ye ca ye ca raivatavaṃśajāḥ ।। avatasthuḥ śarā bhūtvā nānājātiśubhānanāḥ ।। tṛṣā bubhukṣā sarvogrā mṛtyuḥ sarvaśamastathā ।।
gadā bhūtvā śaktayaśca tadā devarathe abhyayuḥ ।। caturvarṇāḥ salīlāśca babhūvuḥ svarṇakuṇḍalāḥ ।। dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa nāgena baddhaṃ balavatā mahat ।। vedāś catvāra evaite catvārasturagābhavan ।।
tānyāsanvājināṃ teṣāṃ bhūṣaṇāni sahasraśaḥ ।। nāgā babhūvurevaite hayānāṃ vālabandhanāḥ ।। upadravāḥ pratīkārāḥ paśubandheṣṭayastathā ।। maṇimuktāpravālaistu bhūṣitāni sahasraśaḥ ।।
yoktrāṇyāsaṃsturaṃgāṇām apasarpaṇavigrahāḥ ।। avadātāḥ patākāstu babhūvuḥ pavaneritāḥ ।। ajarā jyābhavaccāpi sāmbikā dhanuṣo dṛḍhā ।। tasmādumā kālarātrir dhanuṣo jyājarābhavat ।।
sa iṣurviṣṇusomāgnitridaivatamayo abhavat ।। tejasaḥ samavāyo atha ceṣostejo rathāṅgadhṛk ।। tejaḥsaṃvasanārthaṃ vai mumocātiviṣo viṣam ।। lokādhipatimabhyetya idaṃ vacanamabruvan ।।
idamāpatparitrāṇaṃ devānsendrapurogamān ।। praśasya devānsādhviti rathaṃ paśyati śaṃkaraḥ ।। uvāca sendrānamarān amarādhipatiḥ svayam ।। īdṛśo rathasampattyā yantā śīghraṃ vidhīyatām ।।
avāpurmahatīṃ cintāṃ kathaṃ kāryamiti bruvan ।। muktvā cakrāyudhaṃ devaṃ so apyasyeṣuṃ samāśritaḥ ।। niśvasantaḥ surāḥ sarve kathametaditi bruvan ।। ahaṃ sārathirityuktvā jagrāhāśvāṃstato agrajaḥ ।।
pratodahastaṃ samprekṣya brahmāṇaṃ sūtatāṃ gatam ।। sadṛśaḥ sūta ityuktvā cāruroha rathaṃ haraḥ ।। jānubhiḥ patitā bhūmau rajogrāsaśca grāsitaḥ ।। ujjahāra pitṝnārtān suputra iva duḥkhitān ।।
jayaśabdaśca devānāṃ saṃbabhūvārṇavopamaḥ ।। svayambhūḥ prayayau vāhān anumantrya yathājavam ।। mukhebhyaḥ sasṛjuḥ śvāsān ucchvasanta ivoragāḥ ।। vrajanti te aśvā javanāḥ kṣayakāla ivānilāḥ ।।
ākramya nandī vṛṣabhas tasthau tasmiñchivecchayā ।। rathacakre tu rakṣete rudrasya priyakāṅkṣiṇau ।। śarahasto rathaṃ pāti śayanaṃ brahmaṇastadā ।। draviṇādhipatirvyālaṃ surāṇāmadhipo dvipam ।।
guha āsthāya varado yugopamarathaṃ pituḥ ।। pṛṣṭhataścāpi pārśvābhyāṃ lokasya kṣayakṛdyathā ।। anujagmū rathaṃ śārvaṃ nakrā iva mahārṇavam ।। marīciratrirbhagavānathāṅgirāḥ parāśarāgastyamukhā maharṣayaḥ ।।
rathastripure sakāñcanācalo vrajati sapakṣa ivādrirambare ।। karigiriravimeghasaṃnibhāḥ sajalapayodaninādanādinaḥ । pramathagaṇāḥ parivārya devaguptaṃ rathamabhitaḥ prayayuḥ svadarpayuktāḥ ।। vrajati rathavaro atibhāsvaro hy aśaninipātapayodaniḥsvanaḥ ।।
pramatheṣu nadatsūgraṃ pravadatsu ca sādhviti ।। jayatsu vipreṣu tathā garjatsu turageṣu ca ।। kāntyā candropamastūrṇaṃ tripuraṃ puramāgataḥ ।। nāradaścātra bhagavān prādurbhūtastapodhanaḥ ।।
uttasthurnāradaṃ dṛṣṭvā abhivādanavādinaḥ ।। nāradaṃ pūjayāmāsur brahmāṇamiva vāsavaḥ ।। nāradaḥ sukhamāsīnaḥ kāñcane paramāsane ।। yathārhaṃ dānavaiḥ sārdham āsīno dānavādhipaḥ ।।
abravīdvacanaṃ tuṣṭo hṛṣṭaromānanekṣaṇaḥ ।। vartate vartamānajña vada tvaṃ hi ca nārada ।। vinā ca vāyunā ketuḥ patate ca tathā bhuvi ।। hiṃsa hiṃseti śrūyante giraśca bhayadāḥ pure ।।
muktvaikaṃ varadaṃ sthāṇuṃ bhaktābhayakaraṃ haram ।। anāgatamatītaṃ ca bhavāñjānāti tattvataḥ ।। kathayasva muniśreṣṭha prapannasya tu nārada ।। ityukto nāradastena mayenāmayavarjitaḥ ।।
dhāraṇācca mahattvena dharma eṣa nirucyate ।। itaraścāniṣṭaphala ācāryairnopadiśyate ।। vināśastasya nirdeśya iti vedavido viduḥ ।। apakāriṣu devānāṃ kuruṣe tvaṃ sahāyatām ।।
vaināśikāni dṛśyante dānavānāṃ tathaiva ca ।। āyāti tripuraṃ hantuṃ maya tvāmasurānapi ।। yāsyase saha putreṇa dānavaiḥ saha mānada ।। dānavānāṃ punardevo deveśapadamāgataḥ ।।
śūrasaṃmatamityevaṃ dānavānāha dānavaḥ ।। yudhyadhvaṃ daivataiḥ sārdhaṃ kartavyaṃ cāpi no bhayam ।। devāṃśca sendrakānhatvā lokānbhokṣyāmahe asurāḥ ।। daṃśitā yuddhasajjāśca tiṣṭhadhvaṃ prodyatāyudhāḥ ।।
tiṣṭhadhvaṃ laṅghanīyāni bhaviṣyanti purāṇi ca ।। tāḥ prayatnena vāryāśca vidāryāścaiva sāyakaiḥ ।। yuvatijanaviṣaṇṇamānasaṃ tat tripurapuraṃ sahasā viveśa rājā ।। śaraṇamupajagāma devadevaṃ madanāryandhakayajñadehaghātam ।।
tadabhimatamadāttataḥ śaśāṅkī sa ca kila nirbhaya eva dānavo abhūt ।। āgatya caiva tripurāt sabhāyāmāsthitaḥ svayam ।। yatra yajño balervṛtto baliryatra ca saṃyataḥ ।। vivāhāḥ kratavaścaiva jātakarmādikāḥ kriyāḥ ।।
reme nityaṃ bhavo yatra sahāyaiḥ pārṣadairgaṇaiḥ ।। devānāmadhipaṃ prāha gaṇapāṃśca maheśvaraḥ ।। vimānaiśca patākābhir dhvajaiśca samalaṃkṛtam ।। ete janā giriprakhyāḥ sakuṇḍalakirīṭinaḥ ।।
ime ca toyadābhāsā danujā vikṛtānanāḥ ।। nirgacchanti puro daityāḥ sāyudhā vijayaiṣiṇaḥ ।। sahadbhirmāmakairbhṛtyair vyāpādaya mahāsurān ।। puraḥ purasya randhrārthī sthāsyāmi vijayāya vaḥ ।।
tadetannirdahiṣyāmi śareṇaikena vāsava ।। yayau tattripuraṃ jetuṃ tena sainyena saṃvṛtaḥ ।। kṛtasiṃharavopetair udgacchadbhirivāmbudaiḥ ।। utpatya dudruvuśceluḥ sāyudhāḥ khe gaṇeśvarān ।।
sasiṃhanādaṃ vāditraṃ vādayāmāsuruddhatāḥ ।। grasto abhūddaityanādaiśca candrastoyadharairiva ।। tripuraṃ prabhavattadvad bhīmarūpamahāsuraiḥ ।। aṭṭālakānsamāruhya kecic calitavādinaḥ ।।
kecin nadanti danujās toyamattā ivāmbudāḥ ।। kimetaditi papracchur anyonyaṃ gṛhamāśritāḥ ।। jñāsyase anantareṇeti kālo vistārato mahān ।। tiṣṭhate tripuraṃ pīḍya dehaṃ vyādhirivocchritaḥ ।।
ehi āyudham ādāya kva me pṛcchā bhaviṣyati ।। āsādya pṛcchanti tadā dānavāstripurālayāḥ ।। nirgatāḥ kupitāstūrṇaṃ bilādiva mahoragāḥ ।। niruddhā gajarājāno yathā kesariyūthapaiḥ ।।
rūpāṇi jajvalusteṣām agnīnāmiva dhamyatām ।। nikṛṣya jaghnuranyonyam iṣubhiḥ prāṇabhojanaiḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvāhasannuccair dānavā rūpasampadā ।। bhaṭavarmeṣu viviśus taḍāgānīva pakṣiṇaḥ ।।
ityevaṃ paruṣāṇyuktvā dānavāḥ pārṣadarṣabhān ।। khaṇḍaśailaśilāvṛkṣair bibhidur daityadānavān ।। dānavākulamatyarthaṃ tatpuraṃ sakalaṃ babhau ।। indracāpāṅkitoraskā jaladā iva durdinam ।।
cakruste dehaniryāsaṃ svarṇadhātumivācalāḥ ।। cūrṇyante abhihatā daityāḥ kācāṣṭaṅkahatā iva ।। tripuraṃ prabhavat tadvad bhīmarūpamahāsuraiḥ ।। jayatīndraśca rudraśca ityeva ca gaṇeśvarāḥ ।।
niḥsvananto ambusamaye jalagarbhā ivāmbudāḥ ।। yuddhabhūmirbhayavatī māṃsaśoṇitapūritā ।। dṛḍhāhatāḥ patan pūrvaṃ dānavāḥ pramathāstathā ।। dṛḍhaprahārahṛṣitāḥ sādhu sādhviti cukruśuḥ ।।
nadanto meghaśabdena śarabhā iva roṣitāḥ ।। viśanti kruddhavadanā valmīkamiva pannagāḥ ।। saśastrā nipatanti sma sapakṣā iva bhūdharāḥ ।। vidyunmālī mayaścaiva magnau ca drumavadraṇe ।।
ādāya parighaṃ ghoraṃ tāḍayāmāsa nandinam ।। bhramate madhunā vyaktaḥ purā nārāyaṇo yathā ।। dudruvurjātasaṃrambhā vidyunmālinamāsuram ।। tataśca sāyakaiḥ sarvān gaṇapāngaṇapākṛtīn ।।
bhittvā bhittvā rurāvoccair nabhasyambudharo yathā ।। saṃjñāṃ prāpya tataḥ so api vidyunmālinamādravat ।। vajraṃ vajranibhāṅgasya dānavasya sasarja ha ।। papāta vakṣasi tadā vajraṃ daityasya bhīṣaṇam ।।
papāta vajrābhihataḥ śakreṇādririvāhataḥ ।। cukruśurdānavāḥ prekṣya dudruvuśca gaṇādhipāḥ ।। drumaśailamahāvṛṣṭiṃ payodāḥ sasṛjuryathā ।। kartavyaṃ na viduḥ kiṃcid vandyamādhārmikā iva ।।
satarūṇāṃ girīṇāṃ vai tulyarūpadharo babhau ।। virejurbhujagā mantrair vāryamāṇā yathā tathā ।। bhramanti bahuśabdālāḥ pañjare śakunā iva ।। dadāha ca balaṃ sarvaṃ śuṣkendhanamivānalaḥ ।।
gaṇeśā vidhurā jātā jīrṇamūlā yathā drumāḥ ।। girīndrāṃśca harīnvyāghrān vṛkṣān sṛmaravarṇakān ।। mayo māyābalenaiva pātayatyeva śatruṣu ।। nāśaknuvaṃste manasāpi ceṣṭituṃ yathendriyārthā muninābhisaṃyatāḥ ।।
vibādhyamānāstamasā vimohitāḥ samudramadhyeṣviva gādhakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।। tataḥ surāṇāṃ pravarābhirakṣituṃ riporbalaṃ saṃviviśuḥ sahāyudhāḥ ।। svayaṃ ca śakraḥ sitanāgavāhanaḥ kulīśapāṇiḥ suralokapuṃgavaḥ ।। ete ripūṇāṃ prabalābhirakṣitaṃ tadā balaṃ saṃviviśurmadoddhatāḥ ।।
yathā ca siṃhairvijaneṣu gokulaṃ tathā balaṃ tattridaśair abhidrutam ।। svarjyotiṣāṃ jyotir ivoṣmavān harir yathā tamo ghorataraṃ narāṇām ।। tato apakṛṣṭe ca tamaḥprabhāve astraprabhāve ca vivardhamāne ।। saṃkhye vibhagnā vikarā vipādāś chinnottamāṅgāḥ śarapūritāṅgāḥ ।।
vajreṇa bhīmena ca vajrapāṇiḥ śaktyā ca śaktyā ca mayūraketuḥ ।। śūlena kālena ca yakṣarājo vīryeṇa tejasvitayā sukeśaḥ ।। utsādayante danuputravṛndān yathaiva indrāśanayaḥ patantyaḥ ।। śareṇa bhittvā sa hi tārakāsutaṃ sa tārakākhyāsuram ābabhāṣe ।।
viśrāmamūrjaskaramapyavāpya punaḥ kariṣyāmi raṇaṃ prapannaiḥ ।। jayaiṣiṇaste jayakāśinaśca gaṇeśvarā lokavarādhipāśca ।। viveśa tūrṇaṃ tripuraṃ diteḥ sutaiḥ sutairadityā yudhi vṛddhaharṣaiḥ ।। tataḥ saśaṅkhānakabheribhīmaṃ sasiṃhanādaṃ harasainyamābabhau ।
mayānugaṃ ghoragabhīragahvaraṃ yathā siṃhanāditam ।। viveśa tūrṇaṃ tripuram abhraṃ nīlamivāmbaram ।। dadhyau lokakṣaye prāpte kālaṃ kāla ivāparaḥ ।। sa cāpi nidhanaṃ prāpto vidyunmālī mahāyaśāḥ ।।
tasyāpyeṣo anayaḥ prāpto na durgaṃ kāraṇaṃ kvacit ।। kāle kruddhe kathaṃ kālāt trāṇaṃ no adya bhaviṣyati ।। kālasya tadvaśaṃ sarvam iti paitāmaho vidhiḥ ।। laṅghane kaḥ samarthaḥ syād ṛte devaṃ maheśvaram ।।
svāmī caiṣāṃ tu devānāṃ durjayaḥ sa maheśvaraḥ ।। tadadya darśayiṣyāmi yāvadvīrāḥ samantataḥ ।। jīviṣyanti tadā daityāḥ saṃjīvanavarauṣadhaiḥ ।। māyayā sasṛje vāpīṃ rambhāmiva pitāmahaḥ ।।
ārohasaṃkramavatīṃ citrarūpāṃ kathāmiva ।। pūrṇāṃ paramatoyena guṇapūrṇāmivāṅganām ।। candrabhāskaravarṇābhair bhīmair āvaraṇairvṛtām ।। kāmaiṣibhir ivākīrṇāṃ jīvānāmaraṇīm iva ।।
tasyāṃ prakṣālayāmāsa vidyunmālinamāditaḥ ।। uttasthāvindhanairiddhaḥ sadyo huta ivānalaḥ ।। vidyunmālīti vacanaṃ mayamutthāya cābravīt ।। yudhyāmo arīn viniṣpīḍya dayā deheṣu kā hi naḥ ।।
tairvā vinihatā yuddhe bhaviṣyāmo yamāśanāḥ ।। taṃ pariṣvajya sārdrākṣa idamāha mahāsuraḥ ।। tvayā vinā mahābāho kimanyena mahāsura ।। sṛṣṭā dānavadaityānāṃ hatānāṃ jīvavardhinī ।।
durgatāvanayagrastaṃ bhokṣyāmo adya mahānidhim ।। hṛṣṭānanākṣā daityendrā idaṃ vacanamabruvan ।। mayena nirmitā vāpī hatānsaṃjīvayiṣyati ।। vādyamānā nanādoccai rauravī sā punaḥ punaḥ ।।
nyapatannasurāstūrṇaṃ tripurādyuddhalālasāḥ ।। āmuktaiḥ kuṇḍalairhārair mukuṭairapi cotkaṭaiḥ ।। āyudhāni samādāya kāśino dṛḍhavikramāḥ ।। karocchrayā iva gajāḥ siṃhā iva ca nirbhayāḥ ।।
drumā iva ca daityendrās trāsayanto balaṃ mahat ।। yuyutsavo abhidhāvanti dānavāndānavārayaḥ ।। cakruḥ saṃhatya saṃgrāmaṃ codyamānā balena ca ।। bāṇaiśca dṛḍhanirmuktair abhijaghnuḥ parasparam ।।
rūpāṇyāsanmaholkānāṃ patantīnāmivāmbarāt ।। nirayeṣviva nirmagnāḥ kūjante pramathāsurāḥ ।। śirāṃsyurvyāṃ patanti sma girikūṭā ivātyaye ।। chinnāḥ karivarākārā nipetuste dharātale ।।
sādhayantyapare siddhā yuddhagāndharvamadbhutam ।। iti coccārayanvācaṃ vāraṇā raṇadhūrgatāḥ ।। vamante rudhiraṃ vaktraiḥ svarṇadhātumivācalāḥ ।। drumaiśca giriśṛṅgaiśca gāḍhamevāhave hatāḥ ।।
utkṣipya cikṣipur vāpyāṃ mayadānavacoditāḥ ।। uttasthurvāpīmāsādya sadrūpābharaṇāmbarāḥ ।। āsphoṭya siṃhanādaṃ ca kṛtvādhāvaṃstathāsurāḥ ।। hatānapi hi vo vāpī punarujjīvayiṣyati ।।
drutamevaitya deveśam idaṃ vacanamabravīt ।। uttiṣṭhanti punarbhīmāḥ sasyā iva jalokṣitāḥ ।। nihatā nihatā yatra kṣiptā jīvanti dānavāḥ ।। abhavandānavabala utpātā vai sudāruṇāḥ ।।
abhyadhāvatsusaṃkruddho mahādevarathaṃ prati ।। dānavā niḥsṛtā dṛṣṭvā devadevarathe suram ।। dṛṣṭvā kṣobhamagādrudraḥ svayambhūśca pitāmahaḥ ।। anāyatanam āsādya sīdate guṇavāniva ।।
śaithilyaṃ yāti sa rathaḥ sneho viprakṛto yathā ।। ujjahāra mahāprāṇo rathaṃ trailokyarūpiṇam ।। vṛṣarūpaṃ mahatkṛtvā rathaṃ jagrāha durdharam ।। pragṛhyodvahate sajjaṃ kulaṃ kulavaho yathā ।।
abhyadravattadā devaṃ brahmāṇaṃ hatavāṃśca saḥ ।। vijajvāla muhurbrahmā śvāsaṃ vaktrāt samudgiran ।। tārakākhyasya pūjārthaṃ kṛto jaladharopamaḥ ।। dititanayabalaṃ vimardya sarvaṃ tripurapuraṃ praviveśa keśavaḥ ।।
suragururapibatpayo amṛtaṃ tad raviriva saṃcitaśārvaraṃ tamo andham ।। nardamāno mahābāhuḥ praviveśa śaraṃ tataḥ ।। parāṅmukhā bhīmamukhaiḥ kṛtā raṇe yathā nayābhyudyatatatparairnaraiḥ ।। puraṃ parāvṛtya nu te śarārditā yathā śarīraṃ pavanodaye gatāḥ ।।
vineduruccairjahasuśca durmadā jayema candrādidigīśvaraiḥ saha ।। puraṃ praviviśurbhītāḥ pramathairbhagnagopuram ।। yathā vipakṣāḥ śakunā nadyaḥ kṣīṇodakā yathā ।। babhūvuste vimanasaḥ kathaṃ kāryamiti bruvan ।।
uvāca daityo daityānāṃ paramādhipatirmayaḥ ।। toṣayitvā tathā yuddhe pramathānamaraiḥ saha ।। praviṣṭā nagaraṃ trāsāt pramathairbhṛśamarditāḥ ।। yatra nāma mahābhāgāḥ praviśanti girervanam ।।
yatredṛśasya durgasya uparodho avamāgataḥ ।। babhūvurniṣprabhā daityā grahā indūdaye yathā ।। mayamāhuryamaprakhyaṃ sāñjalipragrahāḥ sthitāḥ ।। samākulotpalavanā samīnākulapaṅkajā ।।
vāpī sā sāmprataṃ dṛṣṭā mṛtasaṃjñā ivāṅganā ।। kaṣṭamityasakṛtprocya ditijānidamabravīt ।। vinaṣṭāḥ sma na saṃdehas tripuraṃ dānavā gatam ।। pītā vā yadi vā vāpī pītā vai pītavāsasā ।।
pāsyate viṣṇumajitaṃ varjayitvā gadādharam ।। yatra madvarakauśalyaṃ vijñātaṃ na vṛtaṃ budhaiḥ ।। navāmbhaḥpūritaṃ kṛtvā bādhante asmānmarudgaṇāḥ ।। pramathānāṃ mahāvegaṃ sahāmaḥ śvasanopamam ।।
nirutsāhā bhaviṣyanti etadrathapathāvṛtāḥ ।। sāgaro ambarasaṃkāśaḥ śaraṇaṃ no bhaviṣyati ।। tripureṇa yayau tūrṇaṃ sāgaraṃ sindhubāndhavam ।। avatasthuḥ purāṇyeva gopurābharaṇāni ca ।।
pitāmahamuvācedaṃ vedavādaviśāradam ।। vipulaṃ sāgaraṃ te tu dānavāḥ samupāśritāḥ ।। tata eva rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ prāpayasva pitāmaha ।। parivārya yayurhṛṣṭāḥ sāyudhāḥ paścimodadhim ।।
nardayanto yayustūrṇaṃ sāgaraṃ dānavālayam ।। atha cārupatākabhūṣitaṃ paṭahāḍambaraśaṅkhanāditam । tripuramabhisamīkṣya devatā vividhabalā nanaduryathā ghanāḥ ।। danutanayaninādamiśritaḥ pratinidhisaṃkṣubhitāṇavopamaḥ ।।
tridaśagaṇapatirhyuvāca śakraṃ tripuragataṃ sahasā nirīkṣya śatrum ।। yamavaruṇakuberaṣaṇmukhaistat saha gaṇapairapi hanmi tāvadeva ।। sa rathavaragato bhavaḥ samartho hy udadhimagāttripuraṃ punarnihantum ।। abhibhavatripuraṃ sadānavendraṃ śaravarṣairmusalaiśca vajramiśraiḥ ।।
asuravaravadhārthamudyatānāṃ pratividadhāmi sukhāya te anagha ।। tripurapurajighāṃsayā hariḥ pravikasitāmbujalocano yayau ।। lokapālā yayuḥ sarve gaṇapālāśca sarvaśaḥ ।। khagatāstu virejuste pakṣavanta ivācalāḥ ।।
nādayantaḥ puro devā dṛṣṭāstripuravāsibhiḥ ।। ājagmuḥ paramaṃ kṣobham atyayeṣviva sāgarāḥ ।। ninedurvādayantaśca nānāvādyānyanekaśaḥ ।। pūrvadevāśca devāśca sūdayantaḥ parasparam ।।
pravṛttaṃ yuddhamatulaṃ prahārakṛtaniḥsvanam ।। girīndrā iva kampanto garjanta iva toyadāḥ ।। pravṛddhormitaraṃgaughāḥ kṣubhyanta iva sāgarāḥ ।। yuyudhurniścalā bhūtvā vajrā iva mahācalaiḥ ।।
kālānugānāṃ meghānāṃ yathā viyati vāyunā ।। praharāśu sthito asmyatra ehi darśaya pauruṣam ।। ityanyonyam anūccārya prayayuryamasādanam ।। kecinmudgaracūrṇāśca kecidbāhubhirāhatāḥ ।।
nipatantyarṇavajale bhīmanakratimiṅgile ।। saṃbabhūvārṇave śabdaḥ sajalāmbudanisvanaḥ ।। mattā lohitagandhena kṣobhayanto mahārṇavam ।। bhramante bhakṣayantaśca dānavānāṃ ca lohitam ।।
jagrasustimayo daityān drāvayanto jalecarān ।। ambare ambhasi ca tathā yuddhaṃ cakrurjalecarāḥ ।। yathaiva chindanti parasparaṃ tu tathaiva krandanti vibhinnadehāḥ ।। kṛto muhūrtena samudradeśaḥ saraktatoyaḥ samudīrṇatoyaḥ ।।
nipīḍya tasthau mahatā balena yukto amarāṇāṃ mahatā balena ।। skandaḥ puradvāramathāruroha vṛddho astaśṛṅgaṃ prapatannivārkaḥ ।। devāriṇastasya purasya dvāraṃ tābhyāṃ tu tatpaścimato niruddham ।। taddakṣiṇadvāramareḥ purasya ruddhvāvatasthau bhagavāṃstrinetraḥ ।।
prahlādarūpāḥ pramathāvaruddhā jyotīṃṣi meghā iva cāśmavarṣāḥ ।। prakṣipya prakṣipya samudramadhye kālāmbudābhāḥ pramathā vineduḥ ।। utpāṭyamāneṣu gṛheṣu nāryas tv anāryaśabdānvividhānpracakruḥ ।। mahāsurāḥ sāgaratulyavegā gaṇeśvarāḥ kopavṛtāḥ pratīyuḥ ।।
śarīrasadmakṣapaṇaṃ sughoraṃ yuddhaṃ pravṛttaṃ dṛḍhavairabaddham ।। śabdo babhūvāmaradānavānāṃ yugāntakāleṣviva sāgarāṇām ।। gaṇeśvarāste asurapuṃgavāśca yudhyanti śabdaṃ ca mahadudgirantaḥ ।। kṛtā muhūrtena sukhena gantuṃ chinnottamāṅgāṅghrikarāḥ karālāḥ ।।
tasminkṣaṇe dvāravaraṃ rirakṣo ruddhaṃ bhavenādbhutavikrameṇa ।। cacāra cāptendriyagarvadṛptaḥ purādviniṣkramya rarāsa ghoram ।। nivārito rudrarathaṃ jighṛkṣur yathārṇavaḥ sarpati cātivelaḥ ।। te tārakākhyābhigatā gatājau kṣobhaṃ yathā vāyuvaśātsamudrāḥ ।।
bibheda saṃdhīṣu balābhipannaḥ kūjanninādāṃśca karoti ghorān ।। tasthau bhavaḥ sodyatabāṇacāpaḥ purasya tatsaṅgasamīkṣamāṇaḥ ।। petuḥ stanāśca dantāśca pīḍitābhyāṃ triśūlinā ।। mūḍhāḥ samabhavaṃstena cādṛśyatvamupāgatāḥ ।।
rudrāntike susaṃruddho nandinā kulanandinā ।। takṣayāmāsa vai takṣā candanaṃ gandhado yathā ।। dudrāva khaḍgaṃ niṣkṛṣya tārakākhyo gaṇeśvaram ।। gaṇeśvaraiḥ kṛtastatra tārakākhye niṣūdite ।।
pārśvasthaḥ sumahāpārśvaṃ vidyunmāliṃ mayo abravīt ।। vada vacanaṃ taḍinmālin kiṃ kim etadgaṇapālā yuyudhuryayurgajendrāḥ ।। raṇaśirasi samāgataḥ surāṇāṃ nijagādedam ariṃdamo atiharṣāt ।। sakalasamaraśīrṣaparvatendro yuddhvā yastapati hi tārako gaṇendraiḥ ।।
hṛṣitasakalanetralomasattvāḥ pramathāstoyamuco yathā nadanti ।। raṇaśirasy asitāñjanācalābho jagade vākyamidaṃ navendumālim ।। karomi vikrameṇaitat puraṃ vyasanavarjitam ।। gaṇāñjaghnustu drāghiṣṭhāḥ sahitāstairmahāsuraiḥ ।।
tena tena puraṃ śūnyaṃ pramathaiḥ prahṛtaiḥ kṛtam ।। sakaratalapuṭaiśca siṃhanādair bhavamabhipūjya tadā surā avatasthuḥ ।। abhiṣṭutaḥ satyaratais tapodhanair yathāstaśṛṅgābhigato divākaraḥ ।। uvāca dānavānbhūyo bhūyaḥ sa tu bhayāvṛtān ।।
yatkartavyaṃ mayā caiva yuṣmābhiśca mahābalaiḥ ।। yadaikaṃ tripuraṃ sarvaṃ kṣaṇamekaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। sa kālaḥ puṣyayogasya purasya ca mayā kṛtaḥ ।। sa enaṃ kārayeccūrṇaṃ balinaikaiṣuṇā suraḥ ।।
tatkṛtvā hṛdaye caiva pālayadhvamidaṃ puram ।। vimukhīkurutātyarthaṃ yathā notsṛjate śaram ।। pratīkṣiṣyanti vivaśāḥ puṣyayogaṃ divaukasaḥ ।। muhuḥ siṃharutaṃ kṛtvā mayamūcuryamopamāḥ ।।
tathā kurmo yathā rudro na mokṣyati pure śaram ।। kathayanti diteḥ putrā hṛṣṭā bhinnatanūruhāḥ ।। adānavaṃ vā bhavitā nārāyaṇapadatrayam ।। adaivatam adaityaṃ vā lokaṃ drakṣyanti mānavāḥ ।।
pradoṣe muditā bhūtvā cerurmanmathacāratām ।। tamāṃsyutsārya bhagavāṃś candro jṛmbhati so ambaram ।। siṃho yathā copaviṣṭo vaiḍūryaśikhare mahān ।। bhrājate bhrājayaṃl lokān sṛjañjyotsnārasaṃ balāt ।।
pradoṣe lalitaṃ cakrur gṛhamātmānameva ca ।। dīpāścampakapuṣpābhā nālpasnehapradīpitāḥ ।। jvalato adīpayandīpāṃś candrodaya iva grahāḥ ।। upadravaiḥ kulamiva pīyate tripure tamaḥ ।।
ratyarthino vai danujā gṛheṣu sahāṅganābhiḥ suciraṃ viremuḥ ।। tatrāsureṣvāsurapuṃgaveṣu svāṅgāṅganāḥ svedayutā babhūvuḥ ।। mattapralāpeṣu ca kokilānāṃ sacāpabāṇo madano mamantha ।। khe rohiṇīṃ tāṃ ca priyāṃ sametya candraḥ prabhābhiḥ kurute adhirājyam ।।
viśeṣakaṃ cārutaraṃ karoti tenānanaṃ svaṃ samalaṃkaroti ।। smṛtvā varāṅgī ramaṇeritāni tenaiva bhāvena ratīmavāpa ।। svayaṃ drutaṃ yānti madābhibhūtāḥ kṣapā yathā cārkadināvasāne ।। kācitpriyasyāticirātprasannā āsītpralāpeṣu ca samprasannā ।।
manojñarūpā rucirā babhūvuḥ pūrṇāmṛtasyeva suvarṇakumbhāḥ ।। tantrīpralāpāstripureṣu raktāḥ strīṇāṃ pralāpeṣu punarviraktāḥ ।। āpānabhūmīṣu sukhaprameyaṃ geyaṃ pravṛttaṃ tvatha sādhayanti ।। kecitpriyāṃ samprati bodhayanti saṃbudhya saṃbudhya ca rāmayanti ।।
samarmaro nūpuramekhalānāṃ śabdaśca saṃbādhati kokilānām ।। sucārubāṣpāṅkurapallavānāṃ navāmbusiktā iva bhūmirāsīt ।। mādhuryabhūtābharaṇā mahāntaḥ svanā babhūvurmadaneṣu tulyāḥ ।। āroha me śroṇimimāṃ viśālāṃ pīnonnatāṃ kāñcanamekhalāḍhyām ।।
daityāṅganā yūthagatā vibhānti tārā yathā candramaso divānte ।। saṃdolayante kalasamprahāsāḥ provāca kāñcī guṇasūkṣmanādā ।। śrūyanti vācaḥ kaladhautakalpā vāpīṣu cānye kalahaṃsaśabdāḥ ।। chindanti tāsāmasurāṅganānāṃ priyālayān manmathamārgaṇānām ।।
sucāruveśābharaṇairupetas tārāgaṇair jyotirivāsa candraḥ ।। dolābhūmistairvicitrā vibhāti candrasya pārśvopagatair vicitrā ।। śaravyayaṃ prāpya pure asurāṇāṃ prakṣīṇabāṇo madanaścacāra ।। iti tatra pure amaradviṣāṇāṃ sapadi hi paścimakaumudī tadāsīt ।
raṇaśirasi parābhaviṣyatāṃ vai bhavaturagaiḥ kṛtasaṃkṣayā arīṇām ।। vichāyatāṃ hi samupetya na bhāti tadvad bhāgyakṣaye dhanapatiśca naro vivarṇaḥ ।। sthitvodayāgramukuṭe bahureva sūryo bhātyambare timiratoyavahāṃ tariṣyan ।। nadaddevabalaṃ kṛtsnaṃ yugānta iva sāgaraḥ ।।
savittadaḥ savaruṇas tripuraṃ prayayau haraḥ ।। yayuḥ siṃharavair ghorair vāditraninadairapi ।। babhūva tadbalaṃ divyaṃ vanaṃ pracalitaṃ yathā ।। saṃkṣobho dānavendrāṇāṃ samudrapratimo babhau ।।
śarāsanāni vajrāṇi gurūṇi musalāni ca ।। nijaghnuḥ parvataghnāya ghanā iva tapātyaye ।। modamānāḥ samāsedur devadevaiḥ surārayaḥ ।। abalānāṃ camūrhyāsīd abalāvayavā iva ।।
prayudhya yuddhakuśalāḥ parasparakṛtāgasaḥ ।। kopādvā yuddhalubdhāśca kuṭṭayante parasparam ।। anye vidāritāścakraiḥ patanti hyudadherjale ।। timinakragaṇe caiva patanti pramathāḥ surāḥ ।।
vajraśūlarṣṭipātānāṃ paṭṭiśānāṃ ca sarvataḥ ।। āyudhānāṃ mahānoghaḥ sāgaraughe patatyapi ।। āyudhaistrastanakṣatraḥ kriyate saṃkṣayo mahān ।। devāsuragaṇais tadvat timinakrakṣayo abhavat ।।
vidyurmālaghanonnādo nandīśvaramabhidrutaḥ ।। uvāca yudhi śailādiṃ dānavo ambudhiniḥsvanaḥ ।। na vidyunmālihananaṃ vacobhiryudhi dānava ।। uvāca praharaṃstatra vākyālaṃkārakovidaḥ ।।
śakto hantuṃ kimātmānaṃ jātidoṣād vibṛṃhasi ।। idānīṃ vā kathaṃ nāma na hiṃsye kratudūṣaṇam ।। so api māṃ śaknuyānnaiva cakṣurbhyāṃ samavekṣitum ।। bibhedaikeṣuṇā daityaḥ kareṇārka ivāmbudam ।।
sūryastvātmaprabhāveṇa nadyarṇavajalaṃ yathā ।। hastena vṛkṣamutpāṭya cikṣepa gajarāḍiva ।। vidyunmāliśaraiśchinnaḥ papāta patageśavat ।। roṣamāhārayattīvraṃ nandīśvaraḥ suvigrahaḥ ।।
dudrāva hantuṃ sa krūraṃ mahiṣaṃ gajarāḍiva ।। vidyunmālī śaraśataiḥ pūrayāmāsa nandinam ।। arergṛhya rathaṃ tasya mahataḥ prayayau javāt ।। papāta muniśāpena sādityo arkaratho yathā ।।
ājaghāna tadā śaktyā śailādiṃ samavasthitam ।। vidyunmālinamuddiśya cikṣepa pramathāgraṇīr ।। vidyunmālyapatadbhūmau vajrāhata ivācalaḥ ।। sādhu sādhviti coktvā te pūjayanta umāpatim ।।
dadāha pramathānīkaṃ vanamagnirivoddhataḥ ।। iṣubhirgāḍhaviddhāśca patanti pramathārṇave ।। atha vajradharo yamo arthadaḥ sa ca nandī sa ca ṣaṇmukho guhaḥ । mayam asuravīrasampravṛttaṃ vividhuḥ śastravarairhatārayaḥ ।।
yamaṃ ca vittādhipatiṃ ca viddhvā rarāsa mattāmbudavattadānīm ।। bhṛśānuviddhāstripuraṃ praveśitā yathā śivaścakradhareṇa saṃyuge ।। kapardisainye prababhuḥ samantato nipātyamānā yudhi vajrasaṃnibhāḥ ।। babhūva cāpi saṃyuktaṃ tadyogena puratrayam ।।
mumoca tripure tūrṇaṃ trinetrastripathādhipaḥ ।। ākāśaṃ svarṇasaṃkāśaṃ kṛtaṃ sūryeṇa rañjitam ।। dhigdhiṅ māmiti cakranda kaṣṭaṃ kaṣṭamiti bruvan ।। kimidaṃ tviti papraccha śūlapāṇiṃ maheśvaram ।।
uvāca nandinaṃ bhaktaḥ sa mayo adya vinaṅkṣyati ।। śare tripuramāyāti tripuraṃ praviveśa saḥ ।। anenaiva gṛheṇa tvam apakrāma bravīmyaham ।। tenaiva gṛhamukhyeṇa tripurād apasarpitaḥ ।।
tridhā iva hutāśaśca somo nārāyaṇastathā ।। duṣputradoṣāddahyante kulānyūrdhvaṃ yathā tathā ।। sakapāṭagavākṣāṇi balibhiḥ śobhitāni ca ।। sajalāni samākhyāni sāvalokanakāni ca ।।
dahyante dahanābhāni dahanena sahasraśaḥ ।। vātāyanagatāścānyāś cākāśasya taleṣu ca ।। dahyante dānavendrāṇām agninā hyapi tāḥ striyaḥ ।। puraḥ priyasya pañcatvaṃ gatāgnivadane kṣayam ।।
dharmasākṣī trilokasya na māṃ spraṣṭumihārhasi ।। pareṇa praihi muktvedaṃ gṛhaṃ ca dayitaṃ hi me ।। hutāśanasamīpasthā ityuvāca hutāśanam ।। nārhasyenamupādātuṃ dayitaṃ ṣaṇmukhapriya ।।
nipatantyarṇavajale siñjamānavibhūṣaṇāḥ ।। cakrandustripure nāryaḥ pāvakajvālavepitāḥ ।। tathā strīvaktrapadmāni cādahattripure analaḥ ।। tathaiva so agnistripurāṅganānāṃ dadāha vaktrekṣaṇapaṅkajāni ।।
babhūva kāñcīguṇanūpurāṇām ākranditānāṃ ca ravo atimiśraḥ ।। dagdhāni dagdhāni gṛhāṇi tatra patanti rakṣārthamivārṇavaughe ।। kuputradoṣaiḥ prahatānuviddhaṃ yathā kulaṃ yāti dhanānvitasya ।। vitrāsayāmāsa timīnsanakrāṃs timiṅgilāṃstatkvathitāṃstathānyān ।।
taireva sārdhaṃ bhavanaiḥ papāta śabdaṃ mahāntaṃ janayansamudre ।। nāmāvaśeṣaṃ tripuraṃ prajajñe hutāśanāhārabaliprayuktam ।। duḥkhaṃ mahatprāpya jalāvamagnaṃ yasminmahānsaudhavaro mayasya ।। śaśāpa tadgṛhaṃ cāpi mayasyāditinandanaḥ ।।
bhaviṣyati mayagṛhaṃ nityameva yathānalaḥ ।। tadetadadyāpi gṛhaṃ mayasyāmayavarjitam ।। tasya no gatimākhyāhi mayasya camasodbhava ।। tataścyuto anyaloke asmiṃs trāṇārthaṃ vai cakāra saḥ ।।
tatrāśaktaṃ tato gantuṃ taṃ caikaṃ puramuttamam ।। pūjyamānaṃ ca bhūteśaṃ sarve tuṣṭuvurīśvaram ।। harṣād vavalgur jahasuśca devā jagmurnanardustu viṣaktahastāḥ ।। rathācca saṃpatya hareṣudagdhaṃ kṣiptaṃ puraṃ tanmakarālaye ca ।।
vijayaṃ tasya kṛtyeṣu dadāti vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ ।। anantaṃ tasya puṇyaṃ syāt sarvayajñaphalapradam ।। idaṃ śrutvā paṭhitvā ca yānti rudrasalokatām ।। etadicchāmahe śrotuṃ prabhāvaṃ tasya dhīmataḥ ।।
sūryaputrāya covāca yathā tanme nibodhata ।। ailasya divi saṃyogaṃ somena saha dhīmatā ।। saumyā barhiṣadaḥ kāvyā agniṣvāttāstathaiva ca ।। amāvāsyāṃ nivasata ekasminnatha maṇḍale ।।
amāvāsyāmamāvāsyāṃ mātāmahapitāmahau ।। pracaskanda tataḥ somam arcayitvā pariśramāt ।। tataḥ sa divi somaṃ vai hy upatasthe pitṝnapi ।। sinīvālīpramāṇālpakuhūmātravratodaye ।।
tamupāsya tataḥ somaṃ kalāpekṣī pratīkṣate ।। kṛṣṇapakṣabhujāṃ prītir druhyate paramāṃśubhiḥ ।। nivāpeṣvatha datteṣu pitryeṇa vidhinā tu vai ।। saumyā barhiṣadaḥ kāvyā agniṣvāttāstathaiva ca ।।
jajñire ṛtavastasmād ṛtubhyo hyārtavā abhavan ।। prapitāmahāḥ smṛtā devāḥ pañcābdā brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ ।। smṛtā barhiṣadaste vai purāṇe niścayaṃ gatāḥ ।। aṣṭakāpatayaḥ kāvyāḥ pañcābdāṃstu nibodhata ।।
somas tviḍvatsaraś caiva vāyuścaivānuvatsaraḥ ।। kālenādhiṣṭhitasteṣu candramāḥ sravate sudhām ।। tāṃstena tarpayāmāsa yāvadāsītpurūravāḥ ।। etattadamṛtaṃ somam avāpa madhu caiva hi ।।
āpyāyate suṣumnena somaṃ tu somapāyinam ।। suṣumnāpyāyamānasya bhāgaṃ bhāgamahaḥkramāt ।। evaṃ sā sūryavīryeṇa candrasyāpyāyitā tanuḥ ।। devaiḥ pītasudhaṃ somaṃ purā paścātpibedraviḥ ।।
āpyāyayatsuṣumnena bhāgaṃ bhāgamahaḥkramāt ।। tasmāddhrasanti vai kṛṣṇāḥ śuklā hyāpyāyayanti ca ।। samṛddhirevaṃ somasya pakṣayoḥ śuklakṛṣṇayoḥ ।। kāntaḥ pañcadaśaiḥ sārdhaṃ sudhābhṛtaparisravaiḥ ।।
yathā grathnanti parvāṇi āvṛttādikṣuveṇuvat ।। paurṇamāsyāstu yo bhedo granthayaḥ saṃdhayastathā ।। agnyādhānakriyā yasmān nīyante parvasaṃdhiṣu ।। lavau dvāveva rākāyāḥ kālo jñeyo aparāhṇikaḥ ।।
sāyāhne pratipadyeṣa sa kālaḥ paurṇamāsikaḥ ।। yugāntarodite caiva candre lekhopari sthite ।। tau tu vai pratipadyāvat tasminkāle vyavasthitau ।। sa caiva satkriyākālaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ kālo abhidhīyate ।।
tasmādāpyāyate naktaṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ niśākaraḥ ।। candrādityo aparāhṇe tu pūrṇatvātpūrṇimā smṛtā ।। tasmādanumatirnāma pūrṇatvātpūrṇimā smṛtā ।। rañjanāccaiva candrasya rāketi kavayo viduḥ ।।
ekā pañcadaśī rātrir amāvāsyā tataḥ smṛtā ।। anyonyaṃ candrasūryau tu darśanāddarśa ucyate ।। dvyakṣaraḥ kuhūmātraśca parvakālastu sa smṛtaḥ ।। sūryeṇa sahasodgacchet tataḥ prātastanāttu vai ।।
pratipacchuklapakṣasya candramāḥ sūryamaṇḍalāt ।। etadṛtumukhaṃ jñeyam amāvāsyāṃ tu pārvaṇam ।। tasmāddivā tvamāvāsyāṃ gṛhyate yo divākaraḥ ।। tatkālasaṃjñitā hyeṣā amāvāsyā kuhūḥ smṛtā ।।
amāvāsyā viśatyarkaṃ sinīvālī tadā smṛtā ।। etāsāṃ dvilavaḥ kālaḥ kuhūmātrā kuhūḥ smṛtā ।। parvaṇāṃ tulyakālastu tulyāhutivaṣaṭkriyāḥ ।। pratipatpratipannastu parvakālo dvimātrakaḥ ।।
arkanirmaṇḍale some parvakālaḥ kalāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। daśabhiḥ pañcabhiścaiva kalābhirdivasakramāt ।। tasmātsomasya viproktaḥ pañcadaśyāṃ mayā kṣayaḥ ।। ārtavā ṛtavo athābdā devāstānbhāvayanti hi ।।
teṣāṃ gatiṃ ca sattatvaṃ prāptiṃ śrāddhasya caiva hi ।। tapasā hi prasiddhena kiṃ punarmāṃsacakṣuṣā ।। teṣāṃ te dharmasāmarthyāt smṛtāḥ sāyujyagā dvijaiḥ ।। anye cātra prasīdanti śraddhāyukteṣu karmasu ।।
śrāddhena vidyayā caiva cānnadānena saptadhā ।। svargatā divi modante pitṛmanta upāsate ।। teṣāṃ nivāpe dattaṃ hi tatkulīnaistu bāndhavaiḥ ।। ete manuṣyāḥ pitaro māsaśrāddhabhujastu vai ।।
bhraṣṭāścāśramadharmeṣu svadhāsvāhāvivarjitāḥ ।। svakarmāṇyanuśocanto yātanāsthānamāgatāḥ ।। kṣutpipāsābhibhūtāste vidravanti tvitastataḥ ।। parānnānyabhikāṅkṣantaḥ kālyamānā itastataḥ ।।
śālmalyāṃ vaitaraṇyāṃ ca kumbhīpākeddhavāluke ।। tatrasthānāṃ tu teṣāṃ vai duḥkhitānām aśāyinām ।। prāptāṃstu tarpayantyeva pretasthāneṣvadhiṣṭhitān ।। paścādye sthāvarānte vai bhūtānīke svakarmabhiḥ ।।
yadāhārā bhavantyete tāsu tāsviha yoniṣu ।। prāpnuvantyannamādattaṃ yatra yatrāvatiṣṭhate ।। tathā śrāddheṣu dṛṣṭānto mantraḥ prāpayate tu tam ।। sanatkumāraḥ provāca paśyandivyena cakṣuṣā ।।
kṛṣṇapakṣastvahasteṣāṃ śuklaḥ svapnāya śarvarī ।। anyonyapitaro hyete devāśca pitaro divi ।। pitā pitāmahaścaiva tathaiva prapitāmahaḥ ।। etatpitṛmahattvaṃ hi purāṇe niścayaṃ gatam ।।
avāptiṃ śraddhayā caiva pitṝṇāṃ caiva tarpaṇam ।। samāsātkīrtitastubhyaṃ sarga eṣa sanātanaḥ ।। aśakyaṃ parisaṃkhyātuṃ śraddheyaṃ bhūtimicchatā ।। vistareṇānupūrvyācca bhūyaḥ kiṃ kathayāmi vaḥ ।।
eṣāṃ nisargasaṃkhyāṃ ca śrotumicchāma vistarāt ।। tatpramāṇaṃ prasaṃkhyāya vistarāccaiva kṛtsnaśaḥ ।। nimeṣatulyakālāni mātrālabdhekṣarāṇi ca ।। triṃśatkalāścaiva bhavenmuhūrtas taistriṃśatā rātryahanī samete ।।
rātriḥ svapnāya bhūtānāṃ ceṣṭāyai karmaṇāmahaḥ ।। kṛṣṇapakṣas tvahasteṣāṃ śuklaḥ svapnāya śarvarī ।। pitryaḥ saṃvatsaro hyeṣa mānuṣeṇa vibhāvyate ।। daśa ca dvyadhikā māsāḥ pitṛsaṃkhyeha kīrtitā ।।
etaddivyamahorātram ityeṣā vaidikī śrutiḥ ।। ete rātryahanī divye prasaṃkhyāte tayoḥ punaḥ ।। tathaiva saha saṃkhyāto divya eṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।। divyaḥ saṃvatsaro hyeṣa mānuṣeṇa prakīrtitaḥ ।।
triṃśadanyāni varṣāṇi smṛtaḥ saptarṣivatsaraḥ ।। varṣāṇi navatiścaiva dhruvasaṃvatsaraḥ smṛtaḥ ।। divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu prāhuḥ saṃkhyāvido janāḥ ।। divyenaiva pramāṇena yugasaṃkhyā prakalpitā ।।
kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparaṃ ca kaliścaivaṃ caturyugam ।। dvāparaṃ ca kaliścaiva yugāni parikalpayet ।। tasya tāv acchatī saṃdhyā saṃdhyāṃśaśca tathāvidhaḥ ।। ekapāde nivartante sahasrāṇi śatāni ca ।।
tasyāpi triśatī saṃdhyā saṃdhyāṃśaḥ saṃdhyayā samaḥ ।। dve śate ca tathānye ca saṃdhyāsaṃdhyāṃśayoḥ smṛte ।। kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparaṃ ca kaliśceti catuṣṭayam ।। aṣṭāviṃśatsahasrāṇi kṛtaṃ yugamathocyate ।।
tretāyugasya saṃkhyaiṣā mānuṣeṇa tu saṃjñitā ।। catuḥṣaṣṭisahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ dvāparaṃ yugam ।। etatkaliyugaṃ proktaṃ mānuṣeṇa pramāṇataḥ ।। caturyugasya saṃkhyātā saṃdhyā saṃdhyāṃśakaiḥ saha ।।
kṛtatretādiyuktā sā manorantaramucyate ।। ekatriṃśattathā koṭyaḥ saṃkhyātāḥ saṃkhyayā dvijaiḥ ।। sahasrāṇi tu dvātriṃśac chatānyaṣṭādhikāni ca ।। manvantarasya saṃkhyaiṣā mānuṣeṇa prakīrtitā ।।
sahasrāṇāṃ śatānyāhuḥ sa ca vai parisaṃkhyayā ।। manvantarasya kālastu yugaiḥ saha prakīrtitaḥ ।। krameṇa parivṛttā sā manorantaramucyate ।। tatastu pralayaḥ kṛtsnaḥ sa tu saṃpralayo mahān ।।
caturyugākhyā vyākhyātā kṛtaṃ tretāyugaṃ ca vai ।। yugapatsamavetau dvau dvidhā vaktuṃ na śakyate ।। ṛṣivaṃśaprasaṅgena vyākulatvāttathā kramāt ।। śrautasmārtaṃ bruvandharmaṃ brahmaṇā tu pracoditāḥ ।।
ityādibahulaṃ śrautaṃ dharmaṃ saptarṣayo abruvan ।। varṇāśramācārayutaṃ manuḥ svāyambhuvo abravīt ।। teṣāṃ sutaptatapasām ārṣeṇānukrameṇa ha ।। abuddhipūrvakaṃ tena sakṛtpūrvakameva ca ।।
ādikalpe tu devānāṃ prādurbhūtāstu te svayam ।। te mantrā vai punasteṣāṃ pratimāyāmupasthitāḥ ।। saptarṣibhiśca ye proktāḥ smārtaṃ tu manurabravīt ।। ṛṣayastapasā vedān ahorātramadhīyate ।।
vikriyante svadharmaṃ tu vedavādādyathāyugam ।। paricārayajñāḥ śūdrāśca japayajñāśca brāhmaṇāḥ ।। kriyāvantaḥ prajāvantaḥ samṛddhāḥ sukhinaśca vai ।। vaiśyāñchūdrā anuvartante parasparamanugrahāt ।।
tretāyuge hyavikale karmārambhaḥ prasidhyati ।। sarvasādhāraṇaṃ hyetad āsīttretāyuge tu vai ।। saṃhitāśca tathā mantrā ārogyaṃ dharmaśīlatā ।। yajñaḥ pravartitaścaiva tadā hyeva tu daivataiḥ ।।
svāyambhuve antare devais te yajñāḥ prākpravartitāḥ ।। yadā dharmasya hrasate śākhādharmasya vardhate ।। nyastadaṇḍā mahāyogā yajvāno brahmavādinaḥ ।। siṃhoraskā mahāsattvā mattamātaṃgagāminaḥ ।।
sarvalakṣaṇapūrṇāste nyagrodhaparimaṇḍalāḥ ।। samucchrayaḥ parīṇāho nyagrodhaparimaṇḍalaḥ ।। proktāni sapta ratnāni pūrvaṃ svāyambhuve antare ।। manvantareṣu sarveṣu hy atītānāgateṣu vai ।।
tretāyugāni teṣvatra jāyante cakravartinaḥ ।। atyadbhutāni catvāri balaṃ dharmaṃ sukhaṃ dhanam ।। artho dharmaśca kāmaśca yaśo vijaya eva ca ।। śrutena tapasā caiva ṛṣīṃste abhibhavanti hi ।।
lakṣaṇaiścaiva jāyante śarīrasthairamānuṣaiḥ ।। śyāmaprabhāścaturdaṃṣṭrāḥ suvaṃśāścordhvaretasaḥ ।। pariṇāhapramāṇābhyāṃ siṃhaskandhāśca medhinaḥ ।। pañcāśītisahasrāṇi jīvanti hyajarāmayāḥ ।।
antarikṣe samudreṣu pātāle parvateṣu ca ।। maryādāsthāpanārthaṃ ca daṇḍanītiḥ pravartate ।। trīṇi varṣasahasrāṇi jīvante tatra tāḥ prajāḥ ।। eṣa tretāyuge bhāvas tretāsaṃkhyāṃ nibodhata ।।
saṃdhyāpādaḥ svabhāvācca yo aṃśaḥ pādena tiṣṭhati ।। pūrve svāyambhuve sarge yathāvatprabravīhi naḥ ।। kālākhyāyāṃ pravṛttāyāṃ prāpte tretāyuge tadā ।। pratiṣṭhitāyāṃ vārttāyāṃ grāmeṣu ca pureṣu ca ।।
etacchrutvābravītsūtaḥ śrūyatāṃ tatpracoditam ।। tathā viśvabhugindrastu yajñaṃ prāvartayatprabhuḥ ।। tasyāśvamedhe vitate samājagmurmaharṣayaḥ ।। hūyamāne devahotre agnau bahuvidhaṃ haviḥ ।।
parikrānteṣu laghuṣu adhvaryupuruṣeṣu ca ।। āhūteṣu ca deveṣu yajñabhukṣu tatastadā ।। tānyajanti tadā devāḥ kalyādiṣu bhavanti ye ।। viśvabhujaṃ te tvapṛcchan kathaṃ yajñavidhistava ।।
navaḥ paśuvidhistviṣṭas tava yajñe surottama ।। āgamena bhavāndharmaṃ prakarotu yadīcchati ।। yajñabījaiḥ suraśreṣṭha trivargaparimoṣitaiḥ ।। ukto na pratijagrāha mānamohasamanvitaḥ ।।
jaṅgamaiḥ sthāvaraiḥ kena yaṣṭavyamiti cocyate ।। saṃdhāya samamindreṇa papracchuḥ khacaraṃ vasum ।। auttānapāde prabrūhi saṃśayaṃ nastuda prabho ।। vedaśāstramanusmṛtya yajñatattvamuvāca ha ।।
yaṣṭavyaṃ paśubhirmedhyair atha mūlaphalairapi ।। tathaite bhāvitā mantrā hiṃsāliṅgā maharṣibhiḥ ।। tatpramāṇaṃ mayā coktaṃ tasmācchamitum arhatha ।। tathā pravartatāṃ yajño hy anyathā mānṛtaṃ vacaḥ ।।
avaśyambhāvinaṃ dṛṣṭvā tamadho hyaśapaṃstadā ।। ūrdhvacārī nṛpo bhūtvā rasātalacaro abhavat ।। dharmāṇāṃ saṃśayachettā rājā vasuradhogataḥ ।। bahudhārasya dharmasya sūkṣmā duranugā gatiḥ ।।
devānṛṣīnupādāya svāyambhuvamṛte manum ।। ṛṣikoṭisahasrāṇi svaistapobhirdivaṃ gatāḥ ।। uñchaṃ mūlaṃ phalaṃ śākam udapātraṃ tapodhanāḥ ।। adrohaścāpyalobhaśca damo bhūtadayā śamaḥ ।।
sanātanasya dharmasya mūlameva durāsadam ।। yajñaiśca devānāpnoti vairājaṃ tapasā punaḥ ।। jñānātprāpnoti kaivalyaṃ pañcaitā gatayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ devatānāṃ ca pūrve svāyambhuve antare ।।
vasorvākyamanādṛtya jagmuste vai yathāgatam ।। śrūyante hi tapaḥsiddhā brahmakṣatrādayo nṛpāḥ ।। sudhāmā virajāścaiva śaṅkhapādrājasastathā ।। ete cānye ca bahavas te tapobhirdivaṃ gatāḥ ।।
tasmādviśiṣyate yajñāt tapaḥ sarvaistu kāraṇaiḥ ।। tasmānnāpnoti tadyajñāt tapomūlamidaṃ smṛtam ।। tadāprabhṛti yajño ayaṃ yugaiḥ sārdhaṃ pravartitaḥ ।। tatra tretāyuge kṣīṇe dvāparaṃ pratipadyate ।।
parivṛtte yuge tasmiṃs tataḥ sā vai praṇaśyati ।। lobho dhṛtirvaṇigyuddhaṃ tattvānām aviniścayaḥ ।। yātrā vadhaḥ paro daṇḍo māno darpo akṣamā balam ।। ādye kṛte nādharmo asti sa tretāyāṃ pravartitaḥ ।।
varṇānāṃ dvāpare dharmāḥ saṃkīryante tathāśramāḥ ।। dvidhā śrutiḥ smṛtiścaiva niścayo nādhigamyate ।। dharmatattve hyavijñāte matibhedastu jāyate ।। ato dṛṣṭivibhinnaistaiḥ kṛtamatyākulaṃ tvidam ।।
saṃkṣepādāyuṣaścaiva vyasyate dvāpareṣviha ।। ṛṣiputraiḥ punarvedā bhidyante dṛṣṭivibhramaiḥ ।। saṃhṛtā ṛgyajuḥsāmnāṃ saṃhitāstairmaharṣibhiḥ ।। brāhmaṇaṃ kalpasūtrāṇi bhāṣyavidyāstathaiva ca ।।
dvāpareṣu pravartante bhinnārthaistaiḥ svadarśanaiḥ ।। sāmānyaviparītārthaiḥ kṛtaṃ śāstrākulaṃ tvidam ।। tathaivātharvaṇāṃ sāmnāṃ vikalpaiḥ svasya saṃkṣayaiḥ ।। dvāpare saṃnivṛtte te vedā naśyanti vai kalau ।।
adṛṣṭirmaraṇaṃ caiva tathaiva vyādhyupadravāḥ ।। nirvedājjāyate teṣāṃ duḥkhamokṣavicāraṇā ।। doṣāṇāṃ darśanāccaiva jñānotpattistu jāyate ।। utpasyantīha śāstrāṇāṃ dvāpare paripanthinaḥ ।।
arthaśāstravikalpāśca hetuśāstravikalpanam ।। smṛtiśāstraprabhedāśca prasthānāni pṛthak pṛthak ।। manasā karmaṇā vācā kṛcchrādvārttā prasidhyati ।। lobho adhṛtirvaṇigyuddhaṃ tattvānāmaviniścayaḥ ।।
varṇāśramaparidhvaṃsaḥ kāmadveṣau tathaiva ca ।। niḥśeṣe dvāpare tasmiṃs tasya saṃdhyā tu pādataḥ ।। tathaiva saṃdhyā pādena aṃśastasyāṃ pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।। dvāparasyāṃśaśeṣe tu pratipattiḥ kaleratha ।।
ete svabhāvāḥ puṣyasya sādhayanti ca tāḥ prajāḥ ।। manasā karmaṇā vācā vārttāḥ sidhyanti vā na vā ।। anāvṛṣṭibhayaṃ caiva deśānāṃ ca viparyayaḥ ।। garbhastho mriyate kaścid yauvanasthastathā paraḥ ।।
alpatejobalāḥ pāpā mahākopā hyadhārmikāḥ ।। duriṣṭairduradhītaiśca durācārairdurāgamaiḥ ।। hiṃsā mānastatherṣyā ca krodho asūyākṣamādhṛtiḥ ।। saṃkṣobho jāyate atyarthaṃ kalimāsādya vai yugam ।।
utsīdanti tathā caiva vaiśyaiḥ sārdhaṃ tu kṣatriyāḥ ।। bhavatīha kalau tasmiñ chayanāsanabhojanaiḥ ।। kāṣāyiṇaśca niṣkacchās tathā kāpālinaśca ha ।। divyavṛttāśca ye kecid vṛttyarthaṃ śrutiliṅginaḥ ।।
adhīyate tadā vedāñ chūdrā dharmārthakovidāḥ ।। strībālagovadhaṃ kṛtvā hatvā caiva parasparam ।। duḥkhapracuratālpāyur deśotsādaḥ sarogatā ।। bhrūṇahatyā prajānāṃ na tathā hyevaṃ pravartate ।।
duḥkhenābhiplutānāṃ ca paramāyuḥ śataṃ nṛṇām ।। utsīdante tathā yajñāḥ kevalaṃ dharmahetavaḥ ।। yuge yuge tu hīyante trīṃstrīnpādāṃśca siddhayaḥ ।। saṃdhyāsvabhāvāḥ svāṃśeṣu pādenaivāvatasthire ।।
teṣāmadharmiṇāṃ śāstā bhṛgūṇāṃ ca kule sthitaḥ ।। kalisaṃdhyāṃśabhāgeṣu manoḥ svāyambhuve antare ।। aśvakarmā sa vai senāṃ hastyaśvarathasaṃkulām ।। sa tadā taiḥ parivṛto mlecchānsarvān nijaghnivān ।।
pāṣaṇḍānsa sadā sarvān niḥśeṣānakarotprabhuḥ ।। udīcyānmadhyadeśāṃśca pārvatīyāṃstathaiva ca ।। tathaiva dākṣiṇātyāṃśca draviḍānsiṃhalaiḥ saha ।। tuṣārānbarbarāñchvetān halikāndaradānkhasān ।।
pravṛttacakro balavāñ chūdrāṇāmantakṛdbabhau ।। mānavasya tu vaṃśe tu nṛdevasyeha jajñivān ।। sutaḥ sa vai candramasaḥ pūrve kaliyuge prabhuḥ ।। nijaghne sarvabhūtāni mānuṣāṇyeva sarvaśaḥ ।।
parasparanimittena kālenākasmikena ca ।। gaṅgāyamunayormadhye siddhiṃ prāptā samādhinā ।। utsādya pārthivānsarvāṃs teṣvatīteṣu vai tadā ।। sthitāsvalpāvaśiṣṭāsu prajāsviha kvacit kvacit ।।
upahiṃsanti cānyonyaṃ pralumpanti parasparam ।। prajāstā vai tadā sarvāḥ parasparabhayārditāḥ ।। svānsvānprāṇānavekṣanto niṣkāruṇyāt suduḥkhitāḥ ।। nirmaryādā nirānandā niḥsnehā nirapatrapāḥ ।।
hitvā dārāṃśca putrāṃśca viṣādavyākulaprajāḥ ।। āśrayanti sma pratyantān hitvā janapadānsvakān ।। cīrakṛṣṇājinadharā niṣkriyā niṣparigrahāḥ ।। evaṃ kaṣṭamanuprāptā hy alpaśeṣāḥ prajāstataḥ ।।
saṃśrayanti ca deśāṃstāṃś cakravatparivartanāḥ ।। mṛgānvarāhānvṛṣabhān ye cānye vanacāriṇaḥ ।। samudraṃ saṃśritā yāstu nadīścaiva prajāstu tāḥ ।। abhakṣyāhāradoṣeṇa ekavarṇagatāḥ prajāḥ ।।
tathā kaliyugasyānte śūdrībhūtāḥ prajāstathā ।। ṣaṭtriṃśacca sahasrāṇi mānuṣāṇi tu tāni vai ।। matsyāścaiva hatāḥ sarvaiḥ kṣudhāviṣṭaiśca sarvaśaḥ ।। saṃdhyāṃśe pratipanne tu niḥśeṣāstu tadā kṛtāḥ ।।
phalamūlāśanāḥ sarve aniketāstathaiva ca ।। parigraho na teṣvasti dhanaśuddhimavāpnuyuḥ ।। tāsāmalpāvaśiṣṭānām āhārādṛddhiriṣyate ।। tato varṣaśatasyānte alpaśiṣṭāḥ striyaḥ sutāḥ ।।
tatastāstu mriyante vai pūrvotpannāḥ prajāstu yāḥ ।। yathā svarge śarīrāṇi narake caiva dehinām ।। evaṃ kṛtasya saṃtānaḥ kaleścaiva kṣayastathā ।। tataścaivātmasambodhaḥ sambodhāddharmaśīlatā ।।
bhāvino arthasya ca balāt tataḥ kṛtamavartata ।। ete yugasvabhāvāstu mayoktāstu samāsataḥ ।। pravṛtte tu tatastasmin punaḥ kṛtayuge tu vai ।। tiṣṭhanti ceha ye siddhā adṛṣṭā viharanti ca ।।
kārtayugabhavaiḥ sārdhaṃ nirviśeṣāstadābhavan ।। teṣāṃ saptarṣayo dharmaṃ kathayantīha teṣu ca ।। evaṃ teṣu kriyāvatsu pravartantīha vai kṛte ।। te tu dharmavyavasthārthaṃ tiṣṭhantīha kṛte yuge ।।
yathā dāvapradagdheṣu tṛṇeṣvevāparaṃ tṛṇam ।। evaṃ yugādyugānāṃ vai saṃtānastu parasparam ।। sukhamāyurbalaṃ rūpaṃ dharmārthau kāma eva ca ।। ityeṣa pratisaṃdhirvaḥ kīrtitastu mayā dvijāḥ ।।
eṣāṃ caturyugāṇāṃ tu gaṇitā hyekasaptatiḥ ।। yugākhyāsu tu sarvāsu bhavatīha yadā ca yat ।। sarge sarge yathā bhedā hy utpadyante tathaiva ca ।। āsurī yātudhānī ca paiśācī yakṣarākṣasī ।।
ityetallakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ yugānāṃ vai yathākramam ।। kṣaṇaṃ na saṃtiṣṭhati jīvalokaḥ kṣayodayābhyāṃ parivartamānaḥ ।। manvantarāṇi yānyasmin kalpe vakṣyāmi tāni ca ।। vyatītānāgatāni syur yāni manvantareṣviha ।।
tasminyuge ca sambhūtir yāsāṃ yāvacca jīvitam ।। caturdaśasu tāvanto jñeyā manvantareṣviha ।। teṣāmāyurupakrāntaṃ yugadharmeṣu sarvaśaḥ ।। asthitiṃ ca kalau dṛṣṭvā bhūtānāmāyuṣaśca vai ।।
devāsuramanuṣyāśca yakṣagandharvarākṣasāḥ ।। ṣaṇṇavatyaṅgulotsedho hy aṣṭānāṃ devayoninām ।। etatsvābhāvikaṃ teṣāṃ pramāṇamadhikurvatām ।। devāsurapramāṇaṃ tu saptasaptāṅgulaṃ kramāt ।।
ā pādatalamastako navatālo bhavettu yaḥ ।। gavāṃ ca hastināṃ caiva mahiṣasthāvarātmanām ।। ṣaṭsaptatyaṅgulotsedhaḥ paśur ākakudo bhavet ।। aṅgulānāṃ sahasraṃ tu dvicatvāriṃśadaṅgulam ।।
mānuṣasya śarīrasya saṃniveśastu yādṛśaḥ ।। buddhyātiśayasaṃyukto devānāṃ kāya ucyate ।। ityeva hi parikrāntā bhāvā ye divyamānuṣāḥ ।। gāvo ajāśvāśca vijñeyā hastinaḥ pakṣiṇo mṛgāḥ ।।
yathākramopabhogāśca devānāṃ paśumūrtayaḥ ।। manojñaistatra tairbhogaiḥ sukhino hyupapedire ।। saṃyujya brahmaṇā hyantas tena santaḥ pracakṣate ।। brahmakṣatraviśo yuktāḥ śrautasmārtena karmaṇā ।।
śrautasmārto hi yo dharmo jñānadharmaḥ sa ucyate ।। kāraṇātsādhanāccaiva gṛhasthaḥ sādhurucyate ।। yatamāno yatiḥ sādhuḥ smṛto yogasya sādhanāt ।। kuśalākuśalau caiva dharmādharmau bravītprabhuḥ ।।
ayaṃ dharmo hyayaṃ neti bruvate maunamūrtinā ।। ādhāraṇe mahattve vā dharmaḥ sa tu nirucyate ।। adharmaścāniṣṭaphala ācāryairnopadiśyate ।। samyagvinītā mṛdavas tānācāryānpracakṣate ।।
dārāgnihotrasambandham ijyā śrautasya lakṣaṇam ।। pūrvebhyo vedayitveha śrautaṃ saptarṣayo abruvan ।। manvantarasyātītasya smṛtvā tanmanurabravīt ।। evaṃ vai dvividho dharmaḥ śiṣṭācāraḥ sa ucyate ।।
manvantareṣu ye śiṣṭā iha tiṣṭhanti dhārmikāḥ ।। tiṣṭhantīha ca dharmārthaṃ tāñchiṣṭānsampracakṣate ।। trayī vārttā daṇḍanītiḥ prajāvarṇāśramepsayā ।। pūrvaiḥpūrvairmatatvācca śiṣṭācāraḥ sa śāśvataḥ ।।
aṣṭau tāni caritrāṇi śiṣṭācārasya lakṣaṇam ।। manvantareṣu sarveṣu śiṣṭācārastataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। pratyaṅgāni pravakṣyāmi dharmasyeha tu lakṣaṇam ।। yathābhūtapravādastu ityetatsatyalakṣaṇam ।।
ityetattapaso rūpaṃ sughoraṃ tu durāsadam ।। ṛtvijāṃ dakṣiṇāyāśca saṃyogo yajña ucyate ।। vartate satataṃ hṛṣṭaḥ kriyā śreṣṭhā dayā smṛtā ।। aduṣṭo vāṅmanaḥkāyais titikṣuḥ sā kṣamā smṛtā ।।
parasvānām anādānam alobha iti saṃjñitam ।। nivṛttirbrahmacaryaṃ ca tadetacchamalakṣaṇam ।। viṣaye na pravartante damasyaitattu lakṣaṇam ।। na krudhyeta pratihataḥ sa jitātmā bhaviṣyati ।।
tattadguṇavate deyam ityetaddānalakṣaṇam ।। śiṣṭācārapravṛddhaśca dharmo ayaṃ sādhusaṃmataḥ ।। prītitāpaviṣādānāṃ vinivṛttir viraktatā ।। kuśalākuśalābhyāṃ tu prahāṇaṃ nyāsa ucyate ।।
cetanācetanaṃ jñātvā jñāne jñānī sa ucyate ।। ṛṣibhirdharmatattvajñaiḥ pūrvaiḥ svāyambhuve antare ।। tathaiva cāturhotrasya cāturvarṇyasya caiva hi ।। ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāni yathāvatpratidaivatam ।।
dravyastotraṃ guṇastotraṃ karmastotraṃ tathaiva ca ।। manvantareṣu sarveṣu yathā bhedā bhavanti hi ।। evaṃ mantraguṇānāṃ tu samutpattiścaturvidhā ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ tapyatāṃ teṣāṃ tapaḥ paramaduścaram ।।
asaṃtoṣādbhayādduḥkhān mohācchokācca pañcadhā ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ yādṛśatvaṃ hi tadvakṣyāmīha lakṣaṇam ।। tathā ṛṣīṇāṃ vakṣyāmi ārṣasyeha samudbhavam ।। avibhāgena devānām anirdeśye tamomaye ।।
tenārṣaṃ buddhipūrvaṃ tu cetanenāpyadhiṣṭhitam ।। kāryakāraṇabhāvena tathā tasya pravartate ।। kālena prāpaṇīyena bhedāśca kāraṇātmakāḥ ।। mahato asāvahaṃkāras tasmādbhūtendriyāṇi ca ।।
saṃsiddhikāraṇaṃ kāryaṃ sadya eva vivartate ।। tathā pravṛttāḥ kṣetrajñāḥ kālenaikena kāraṇāt ।। tathā nivṛtto hyavyaktaḥ khadyota iva saṃjvalan ।। mahatastamasaḥ pāre vailakṣaṇyādvibhāvyate ।।
buddhirvivardhatastasya prādurbhūtā caturvidhā ।। sāṃsiddhikānyathaitāni apratītāni tasya vai ।। puri śete yataḥ pūrvaṃ kṣetrajñānaṃ tathāpi ca ।। yasmāddharmātprasūte hi tasmādvai dhārmikastu saḥ ।।
evaṃ vivṛttaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ kṣetraṃ hyanabhisaṃdhitaḥ ।। kṣetrajñena parijñātaṃ bhogyo ayaṃ viṣayo mama ।। eṣa sannilayo yasmād brāhmaṇastutatas tv ṛṣiḥ ।। ṛṣate paramaṃ yasmāt paramarṣistataḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
yasmādeṣa svayaṃbhūtas tasmācca ṛṣitā matā ।। nivartamānaistairbuddhyā mahānparigataḥ paraḥ ।। īśvarāṇāṃ sutāsteṣāṃ mānasāścaurasāśca vai ।। ṛṣiputrā ṛṣīkāstu maithunādgarbhasambhavāḥ ।।
ṛṣikāṇāṃ sutā ye tu vijñeyā ṛṣiputrakāḥ ।। avyaktātmā mahātmā vā-haṃkārātmā tathaiva ca ।। ityevamṛṣijātistu pañcadhā nāmaviśrutā ।। manurdakṣo vasiṣṭhaśca pulastyaścāpi te daśa ।।
paratvenarṣayo yasmān matāstasmānmaharṣayaḥ ।। kāvyo bṛhaspatiścaiva kaśyapaścyavanastathā ।। kardamo vālakhilyāśca viśravāḥ śaktivardhanaḥ ।। teṣāṃ putrānṛṣīkāṃstu garbhotpannānnibodhata ।।
ṛṣirdīrghatamāścaiva bṛhadvakṣāḥ śaradvataḥ ।। śṛṅgī ca śaṅkhapāc caiva rājā vaiśravaṇastathā ।। īśvarā ṛṣayaścaiva ṛṣīkā ye ca viśrutāḥ ।। bhṛguḥ kāśyapaḥ pracetā dadhīco hyātmavānapi ।।
ārṣṭiṣeṇaścyavanaśca vītahavyaḥ savedhasaḥ ।। ekonaviṃśatirhyete bhṛgavo mantrakṛttamāḥ ।। kṛtavācastathā gargaḥ smṛtisaṃkṛtireva ca ।। yuvanāśvaḥ purukutsaḥ svaśravastu sadasyavān ।।
pṛṣadaśvo virūpaśca kāvyaścaivātha mudgalaḥ ।। apasyauṣaḥ sucittiśca vāmadevastathaiva ca ।। kakṣīvāṃśca trayastriṃśat smṛtā hyaṅgirasāṃ varāḥ ।। kāśyapaḥ sahavatsāro naidhruvo nitya eva ca ।।
atrir ardhasvanaścaiva śāvāsyo atha gaviṣṭhiraḥ ।। karṇakaśca ṛṣiḥ siddhas tathā pūrvātithiśca yaḥ ।। vasiṣṭhaścaiva śaktiśca tṛtīyaśca parāśaraḥ ।। ṣaṣṭhastu mitrāvaruṇaḥ sattamaḥ kuṇḍinastathā ।।
viśvāmitraśca gādheyo devarātastathā balaḥ ।। aṣṭako lohitaścaiva bhṛtakīlaśca māmbudhiḥ ।। śiśiraśca mahātejāḥ śālaṅkāyana eva ca ।। agastyo atha dṛḍhadyumna indrabāhustathaiva ca ।।
manurvaivasvataścaiva ailo rājā purūravāḥ ।। bhalandakaśca vāsāśvaḥ saṃkīlaścaiva te trayaḥ ।। iti dvinavatiḥ proktā mantrāyaiśca bahiṣkṛtāḥ ।। ṛṣīkāṇāṃ sutā hyete ṛṣiputrāḥ śrutarṣayaḥ ।।
kasminkāle vinirvṛttā katheyaṃ sūtanandana ।। idaṃ mune samākhyāhi mahābuddhe manogatam ।। kathaṃ śaravaṇe jāto devaḥ ṣaḍvadano vibho ।। uvāca bhagavānprīto brahmasūnurmahāmatim ।।
surānudvāsayāmāsa purebhyaḥ sa mahābalaḥ ।। bhītāṃśca tridaśāndṛṣṭvā brahmā teṣāmuvāca ha ।। tuhinācaladauhitras taṃ haniṣyati dānavam ।। svareto vahnivadane vyasṛjatkāraṇāntare ।।
vidārya jaṭharāṇyeṣām ajīrṇaṃ nirgataṃ mune ।। tasmāttu sa samudbhūto guho dinakaraprabhaḥ ।। evaṃ śrutvā tato vākyaṃ tam ūcur ṛṣisattamāḥ ।। vistareṇa hi no brūhi yāthātathyena śṛṇvatām ।।
yasyābhūttārakaḥ putraḥ surapramathano balī ।। guhajanma tu kārtsnyena asmākaṃ brūhi mānada ।। ṣaṣṭiṃ so ajanayatkanyā vairiṇyāmeva naḥ śrutam ।। saptaviṃśatiṃ somāya catasro ariṣṭanemaye ।।
dve kṛśāśvāya viduṣe prajāpatisutaḥ prabhuḥ ।। surabhirvinatā caiva tāmrā krodhavaśā irā ।। tāsāṃ sakāśāllokānāṃ jaṅgamasthāvarātmanām ।। devendropendrapūṣādyāḥ sarve te ditijā matāḥ ।।
dānavāśca danoḥ putrā gāvaśca surabhīsutāḥ ।। nāgāḥ kadrūsutā jñeyāḥ śeṣāścānye api jantavaḥ ।। hiraṇyakaśipuścakre jitvā rājyaṃ mahābalaḥ ।। nihatā viṣṇunā saṃkhye śeṣāścendreṇa dānavāḥ ।।
bhartāraṃ kaśyapaṃ devaṃ putramanyaṃ mahābalam ।। samare śakrahantāraṃ sa tasyā adadātprabhuḥ ।। varṣāṇāṃ lapsyase putram ityuktā sā tathākarot ।। upāsāmācarattasyāḥ sā cainamanvamanyata ।।
uvāca śakraṃ suprītā varadā tapasi sthitā ।। bhaviṣyati ca te bhrātā tena sārdhamimāṃ śriyam ।। ityuktvā nidrayāviṣṭā caraṇākrāntamūrdhajā ।। tattu randhraṃ samāsādya jaṭharaṃ pākaśāsanaḥ ।।
ekaikaṃ tu punaḥ khaṇḍaṃ cakāra maghavā tataḥ ।। vibudhyovāca mā śakra ghātayethāḥ prajāṃ mama ।। uvāca vākyaṃ saṃtrasto māturvai vadaneritam ।। saptasaptabhirevātas tava garbhaḥ kṛto mayā ।।
dāsyāmi teṣāṃ sthānāni divi daivatapūjite ।। punaśca devī bhartāram uvācāsitalocanā ।। yo nāstraśastrairvadhyatvaṃ gacchettridivavāsinām ।। daśa varṣasahasrāṇi tapaḥ kṛtvā tu lapsyase ।।
vajrāṅgo nāma putraste bhavitā putravatsale ।। daśa varṣasahasrāṇi sā tapo ghoramācarat ।। putramapratikarmāṇam ajeyaṃ vajraduśchidam ।। uvāca mātaraṃ bhaktyā mātaḥ kiṃ karavāṇyaham ।।
bahavo me hatāḥ putrāḥ sahasrākṣeṇa putraka ।। bāḍhamityeva tāmuktvā jagāma tridivaṃ balī ।। māturantikamāgacchad vyāghraḥ kṣudramṛgaṃ yathā ।। āgatau tatra yatrāstāṃ mātāputrāvabhītakau ।।
muñcainaṃ putra devendraṃ kimanena prayojanam ।। asmadvākyena yo mukto viddhi taṃ mṛtameva ca ।। jīvanneva mṛto vatsa divase divase sa tu ।। etacchrutvā tu vajrāṅgaḥ praṇato vākyamabravīt ।।
tvaṃ surāsuranātho asi mama ca prapitāmahaḥ ।। tapase me ratirdeva nirvighnaṃ caiva me bhavet ।। tasmiṃstūṣṇīṃ sthite daitye provācedaṃ pitāmahaḥ ।। anayā cittaśuddhyā te paryāptaṃ janmanaḥ phalam ।।
tāmasmai pradadau devaḥ patnyarthaṃ padmasambhavaḥ ।। vajrāṅgo api tayā sārdhaṃ jagāma tapase vanam ।। kālaṃ kamalapattrākṣaḥ śuddhabuddhir mahātapāḥ ।। nirāhāro ghoratapās taporāśirajāyata ।।
jalāntaraṃ praviṣṭasya tasya patnī mahāvratā ।। nirāhārā tapo ghoraṃ praviveśa mahādyutiḥ ।। bhūtvā tu markaṭastatra tadāśramapadaṃ mahān ।। tatastu megharūṣeṇa kampaṃ tasyākaronmahān ।।
apākarṣattato dūraṃ bhramaṃstasyā mahīmimām ।। tato gomāyurūpeṇa tasyādūṣayadāśramam ।। bhīṣikābhir anekābhis tāṃ kliśyanpākaśāsanaḥ ।। śailasya duṣṭatāṃ matvā śāpaṃ dātuṃ vyavasthitā ।।
uvāca tāṃ varārohāṃ varāṅgīṃ bhīrucetanaḥ ।। vibhramaṃ tu karotyeṣa ruṣitaḥ pākaśāsanaḥ ।। tuṣṭaḥ provāca vajrāṅgaṃ tamāgamya jalāśrayam ।। uvāca prāñjalirvākyaṃ sarvalokapitāmaham ।।
tapasyeva ratir me'stu śarīrasyāstu vartanam ।। vajrāṅgo api samāpte tu tapasi sthirasaṃyamaḥ ।। kṣudhāviṣṭaḥ sa śailasya gahanaṃ praviveśa ha ।। tāṃ vilokya sa daityendraḥ provāca parisāntvayan ।।
kaṃ vā kāmaṃ prayacchāmi śīghraṃ me brūhi bhāmini ।। raudreṇa devarājena naṣṭanātheva bhūriśaḥ ।। putraṃ me tārakaṃ dehi duḥkhaśokamahārṇavāt ।। śakto api devarājasya pratikartuṃ mahāsuraḥ ।।
jñātvā tu tasya saṃkalpaṃ brahmā krūrataraṃ punaḥ ।। uvāca tasmai bhagavān prabhurmadhurayā girā ।। āhārābhimukho daitya tanno brūhi mahāvrata ।। kṣaṇenaikena tallabhyaṃ tyaktvāhāramupasthitam ।।
yathā prāptaṃ parityajya kāmaṃ kamalalocana ।। cintayaṃstapasā yukto hṛdi brahmamukheritam ।। mahiṣī bhīṣitā dīnā rudatī śākhinastale ।। kimevaṃ vartase bhīru vada tvaṃ kiṃ cikīrṣasi ।।
vākyaṃ covāca tanvaṅgī bhītā sā hetusaṃhitam ।। raudreṇa devarājena naṣṭanātheva bhūriśaḥ ।। putraṃ me tārakaṃ dehi hy asmādduḥkhamahārṇavāt ।। tapo ghoraṃ kariṣyāmi jayāya tridivaukasām ।।
uvāca daityarājānaṃ prasannaścaturānanaḥ ।। putraste tārako nāma bhaviṣyati mahābalaḥ ।। ityukto daityanāthastu praṇipatya pitāmaham ।। tau dampatī kṛtārthau tu jagmatuḥ svāśramaṃ mudā ।।
pūrṇaṃ varṣasahasraṃ ca dadhārodara eva hi ।। jāyamāne tu daityendre tasmiṃllokabhayaṃkare ।। celurmahīdharāḥ sarve vavurvātāśca bhīṣaṇāḥ ।। candrasūryau jahuḥ kāntiṃ sanīhārā diśo abhavan ।।
ājagmurhṛṣitāstatra tathā cāsurayoṣitaḥ ।। tato mahotsavo jāto dānavānāṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। varāṅgī svasutaṃ dṛṣṭvā harṣeṇāpūritā tadā ।। jātamātrastu daityendras tārakaścaṇḍavikramaḥ ।।
sarvāsuramahārājye pṛthivītulanakṣamaiḥ ।। uvāca dānavaśreṣṭhān yuktiyuktamidaṃ vacaḥ ।। śreyase kriyatāṃ buddhiḥ sarvaiḥ kṛtyasya saṃvidhau ।। asmākaṃ jātidharmo vai virūḍhaṃ vairamakṣayam ।।
svabāhubalamāśritya sarva eva na saṃśayaḥ ।। ahamādau kariṣyāmi tato ghoraṃ diteḥ sutāḥ ।। sthiropāyo hi puruṣaḥ sthiraśrīrapi jāyate ।। tacchrutvā dānavāḥ sarve vākyaṃ tasyāsurasya tu ।।
so agacchatpāriyātrasya gireḥ kandaramuttamam ।। nānādhāturasasrāvacitraṃ nānāguhāgṛham ।। anekākārabahulaṃ pṛthakpakṣikulākulam ।। prāpya tatkandaraṃ daityaś cacāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ ।।
śataṃ śataṃ samānāṃ tu tapāṃsyetāni so akarot ।। māṃsasyāgnau juhāvāsau tato nirmāṃsatāṃ gataḥ ।। jajvaluḥ sarvabhūtāni tejasā tasya sarvataḥ ।। etasminnantare brahmā paramaṃ toṣamāgataḥ ।।
uvāca tārakaṃ devo girā madhurayā yutaḥ ।। varaṃ vṛṇīṣva ruciraṃ yatte manasi vartate ।। uvāca prāñjalirbhūtvā praṇataḥ pṛthuvikramaḥ ।। kṛtapratikṛtākāṅkṣī jigīṣuḥ prāyaśo janaḥ ।।
teṣāmahaṃ samuddhartā bhaveyamiti me matiḥ ।। syāmahaṃ paramo hyeṣa varo mama hṛdi sthitaḥ ।। tamuvāca tato daityaṃ viriñciḥ suranāyakaḥ ।। yatastato api varaya mṛtyuṃ yasmānna śaṅkase ।।
vavre mahāsuro mṛtyum avalepena mohitaḥ ।। jagāma tridivaṃ devo daityo api svakamālayam ।। parivavruḥ sahasrākṣaṃ divi devagaṇā yathā ।। ṛtavo mūrtimantaśca svakālaguṇabṛṃhitāḥ ।।
kāntirdyutirdhṛtirmedhā śrīravekṣya ca dānavam ।। kālāguruviliptāṅgaṃ mahāmukuṭabhūṣaṇam ।। vījayantyapsaraḥśreṣṭhā bhṛśaṃ muñcanti naiva tāḥ ।। kṛtānto agresarastasya babhūvurmunisattamāḥ ।।
babhāṣe sacivāndaityaḥ prabhūtavaradarpitaḥ ।। aniryāpya surairvairaṃ kā śāntirhṛdaye mama ।। viṣṇuḥ śriyaṃ na jahati tiṣṭhate ca gatabhramaḥ ।। sotpalā madirāmodā divi krīḍāyaneṣu ca ।।
janma tasya vṛthā bhūtam ajanmā tu viśiṣyate ।। kīrtiṃ hi vā nārjayate himābhāṃ pumānsa jāto api mṛto mataṃ me ।। dhvajaṃ ca me kāñcanapaṭṭanaddhaṃ chattraṃ ca me mauktikajālabaddham ।। senānīr daityarājasya tathā cakre balānvitaḥ ।।
turagāṇāṃ sahasreṇa cakrāṣṭakavibhūṣitam ।। nānākrīḍāgṛhayutaṃ gītavādyamanoharam ।। daśakoṭīśvarā daityā daityānāṃ caṇḍavikramāḥ ।। mahiṣaḥ kuñjaro meghaḥ kālanemirnimistathā ।।
anye api śataśastasya pṛthivīdalanakṣamāḥ ।। nānāyudhapraharaṇā nānāśastrāstrapāragāḥ ।। ketunā makareṇāpi senānīr grasano arihā ।। kharavidhūtalāṅgūlaṃ kujambhasyābhavaddhvaje ।।
dhvāṅkṣo dhvaje tu śumbhasya kṛṣṇāyomayamucchritam ।। śatena śīghravegāṇāṃ vyāghrāṇāṃ hemamālinām ।। śatenāpi ca siṃhānāṃ ratho jambhasya durjayaḥ ।। rathastu mahiṣasyoṣṭrair gajasya tu turaṃgamaiḥ ।।
parvatābhaiḥ samārūḍho nimirmattairmahāgajaiḥ ।। śatahastāyataiḥ kṛṣṇais turaṃgairhemabhūṣaṇaiḥ ।। sitacandanacārvaṅgo nānāpuṣpasrajojjvalaḥ ।। jambhakaḥ kiṅkiṇījālamālamuṣṭraṃ samāsthitaḥ ।।
anye api dānavā vīrā nānāvāhanagāminaḥ ।। nānāvidhottarāsaṅgā nānāmālyavibhūṣaṇāḥ ।। nānāvādyaparispandāś cāgresaramahārathāḥ ।। tadbalaṃ daityasiṃhasya bhīmarūpaṃ vyajāyata ।।
pratasthe amarayuddhāya bahupattipatāki tat ।। dṛṣṭvā sa dānavabalaṃ jagāmendrasya śaṃsitum ।। śaśaṃsa madhye devānāṃ tatkāryaṃ samupasthitam ।। bṛhaspatimuvācedaṃ vākyaṃ kāle mahābhujaḥ ।।
kāryaṃ kimatra tadbrūhi nītyupāyasamanvitam ।। ityuvāca mahābhāgo bṛhaspatirudāradhīḥ ।। jigīṣatāṃ suraśreṣṭha sthitireṣā sanātanī ।। nītau kramāddeśakālaripuyogyakramādidam ।।
saṃtāpitaḥ khalo yāti sādhyatāṃ bhraṣṭasaṃśayaḥ ।। jātidharmeṇa vā bhedyā dānaṃ prāptaśriye ca kim ।। durjaneṣu kṛtaṃ sāma mahadyāti ca vandhyatām ।। ṛjutāmāryabuddhitvaṃ dayānītivyatikramam ।।
tasmād durjanam ākrāntuṃ śreyānpauruṣasaṃśrayaḥ ।। durjanaḥ sujanatvāya kalpate na kadācana ।। evaṃ me budhyate buddhir yūyamatra vyavasyata ।। kartavyatāṃ sa saṃcintya provācāmarasaṃsadi ।।
bhavanto yajñabhoktāras tuṣṭātmāno atisāttvikāḥ ।। bhavataścānimittena bādhane dānaveśvarāḥ ।। kriyatāṃ samarodyogaḥ sainyaṃ saṃyojyatāṃ mama ।। vāhanāni ca yānāni yojayantu mamāmarāḥ ।।
ityuktāḥ samanahyanta devānāṃ ye pradhānataḥ ।। nānāścaryaguṇopetaṃ samprāptaṃ sarvadaivataiḥ ।। yamo mahiṣamāsthāya senāgre samavartata ।। kalpakāloddhatajvālāpūritāmbaralocanaḥ ।।
pavano aṅkuśapāṇistu vistāritamahājavaḥ ।। narayuktarathe devo rākṣaseśo viyaccaraḥ ।। mahāsiṃharavo devo dhanādhyakṣo gadāyudhaḥ ।। rājabhiḥ sahitāstasthur gandharvā hemabhūṣaṇāḥ ।।
nākapṛṣṭhaśikhaṇḍāstu vaiḍūryamakaradhvajāḥ ।। gṛdhradhvajā mahāvīryā nirmalāyovibhūṣaṇāḥ ।। mahāmegharavā nāgā bhīmolkāśanihetayaḥ ।। tāmrolūkadhvajā raudrā hemaratnavibhūṣaṇāḥ ।।
gārdhrapattradhvajaprāyam asthibhūṣaṇabhūṣitam ।। kiṃnarāḥ śvetavasanāḥ sitapattripatākinaḥ ।। muktājālapariṣkāro haṃso rajatanirmitaḥ ।। padmarāgamahāratnaviṭapaṃ dhanadasya tu ।।
vṛkeṇa kāṣṭhalohena yamasyāsīnmahādhvajaḥ ।। hemasiṃhadhvajau devau candrārkāvamitadyutī ।। hemamātaṃgaracitaṃ citraratnapariṣkṛtam ।। sanāgayakṣagandharvam ahoraganiśācarā ।।
koṭayastās trayastriṃśad devadevanikāyinām ।। kṛtābhirāgojjvalakuṅkumāṅkure kapolalīlālikadambasaṃkule ।। sahasradṛgbandisahasrasaṃstutas triviṣṭape aśobhata pākaśāsanaḥ ।। camūśca sā durjayapattrisaṃtatā vibhāti nānāyudhayodhadustarā ।।
tumulo atimahānāsīt senayorubhayorapi ।। tūryāṇāṃ caiva nirghoṣair mātaṃgānāṃ ca bṛṃhitaiḥ ।। jyāghoṣeṇa ca śūrāṇāṃ tumulo atimahānabhūt ।। roṣeṇātiparītānāṃ tyaktajīvitacetasām ।।
rathenāsaktapādāto rathena ca turaṃgamaḥ ।। mātaṃgenāparo hastī turaṃgairbahubhirgajaḥ ।। tataḥ prāsāśanigadābhindipālaparaśvadhaiḥ ।। cakraiśca śaṅkubhiścaiva tomarairaṅkuśaiḥ sitaiḥ ।।
bhallaiśca śatapattraiśca śukatuṇḍaiśca nirmalaiḥ ।। saṃpracchādya diśaḥ sarvās tamomayamivākarot ।। alakṣyaṃ visṛjantaste hetisaṃghātamuddhatam ।। tato dhvajairbhujaiśchattraiḥ śirobhiśca sakuṇḍalaiḥ ।।
ākāśasaraso bhraṣṭaiḥ paṅkajairiva bhūḥ stṛtā ।। gajāḥ śalanibhāḥ petur dharaṇyāṃ rudhirasravāḥ ।। petuḥ śakalatāṃ yātās turaṃgāśca sahasraśaḥ ।। vetālākrīḍamabhavat tatsaṃkularaṇājiram ।।
vavarṣa śaravarṣeṇa viśeṣeṇāgnivarcasā ।। kṛtapratikṛtākāṅkṣī dhanurānamya bhairavam ।। sa vicintya yamo bāṇān grasanasyātipauruṣam ।। kṛtāntaśaravṛṣṭiṃ tāṃ viyati pratisarpiṇīm ।।
viphalāṃ tāṃ samālokya yamastāṃ śarasaṃtatim ।। cikṣepa mudgaraṃ ghoraṃ tarasā tasya cāntakaḥ ।। jagrāha vāmahastena yāmyaṃ dānavanandanaḥ ।। pātayāmāsa vegena sa papāta mahītale ।।
prāsena tāḍayāmāsa grasanaṃ vadane dṛḍham ।। grasanaṃ patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā jambho bhīmaparākramaḥ ।। yamastena prahāreṇa susrāva rudhiraṃ mukhāt ।। vṛto yakṣāyutaśatair jambhaṃ pratyudyayau ruṣā ।।
uvāca prājño vākyaṃ tu yathā snigdhena bhāṣitam ।। maṇihemapariṣkārāṃ gurvīm arivimardinīm ।। gadāyāḥ pratighātārthaṃ jagaddalanabhairavam ।। sa gadāṃ viyati prāpya rarāsāmbudharo yathā ।।
tābhyāṃ niṣpeṣanirhrādajaḍīkṛtadigantaram ।। kṣaṇātpraśāntanirhrādaṃ jvaladulkāsamācitam ।। nihatyātha gadāṃ daṇḍas tato grasanamūrdhani ।। sa tu tena prahāreṇa dṛṣṭvā satimirā diśaḥ ।।
tato hāhāravo ghoraḥ senayorubhayorabhūt ।। apaśyatsvāṃ tanuṃ dhvastāṃ vilolābharaṇāmbarām ।। madvidhe vastuni puṃsi prabhoḥ paribhavodayāt ।। asaṃbhāvita evāstu janaḥ svacchandaceṣṭitaḥ ।।
evaṃ saṃcintya vegena samuttasthau mahābalaḥ ।। grasano ghorasaṃkalpaḥ saṃdaṣṭauṣṭhapuṭacchadaḥ ।। samāsādya yamaṃ yuddhe grasano bhrāmya mudgaram ।। vilokya mudgaraṃ dīptaṃ yamaḥ saṃbhrāntalocanaḥ ।।
tasminnapasṛte dūraṃ caṇḍānāṃ bhīmakarmaṇām ।। tatastāṃ nihatāṃ dṛṣṭvā ghorāṃ kiṃkaravāhinīm ।। grasanastu samālokya tāṃ kiṃkaramayīṃ camūm ।। nigrāhya grasanaḥ senāṃ visṛjannastravṛṣṭayaḥ ।।
kāṃścidbibheda śūlena kāṃścidbāṇairajihmagaiḥ ।। kecitprāsaprahāraiśca dāruṇaistāḍitāstadā ।। śilābhirapare jaghnur drumairanyairmahocchrayaiḥ ।। apare muṣṭibhiḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ kiṃkarāḥ praharanti ca ।।
utsṛjya gātraṃ bhūpṛṣṭhe niṣpipeṣa sahasraśaḥ ।। sa tu kiṃkarayuddhena grasanaḥ śramamāptavān ।। ājagāma samudyamya daṇḍaṃ mahiṣavāhanaḥ ।। acintayitvā tatkarma grasanasyāntako arihā ।।
sa ratho daṇḍamathitair vyāghrairardhair vikṛṣyate ।। samutsṛjya rathaṃ daityaḥ padātirdharaṇīṃ gataḥ ।। yamo api śastrāṇyutsṛjya bāhuyuddheṣvavartata ।। bhrāmayāmāsa vegena pracittamiva sambhramaḥ ।।
vegena bhrāmayāmāsa samutkṛṣya mahītalāt ।। daityendrasyātikāyatvāt tataḥ śrāntabhujo yamaḥ ।। tamālakṣya tato daityaḥ śrāntamantakamojasā ।। yāvadyamasya vadanāt susrāva rudhiraṃ bahu ।।
jayaṃ prāpyoddhataṃ daityo nādaṃ muktvā mahāsvanaḥ ।। dhanādhipasya jambhena sāyakairmarmabhedibhiḥ ।। tataḥ krodhaparītastu dhaneśo jambhadānavam ।। sārathiṃ ca śatenājau dhvajaṃ daśabhireva ca ।।
mārgaṇair barhipattrāṅgais tailadhautairajihmagaiḥ ।। jambhastu karma taddṛṣṭvā dhaneśasyātiduṣkaram ।। jagrāha niśitānbāṇāñ chatrumarmavibhedinaḥ ।। vivyādha dhanadaṃ tīkṣṇaiḥ śarairvakṣasi dānavaḥ ।।
cicheda jyāmathaikena tailadhautena dānavaḥ ।। vivyādhorasi vitteśaṃ daśabhiḥ krūrakarmakṛt ।। sa kṣaṇāddhairyamālambya dhanurākṛṣya bhairavam ।। diśaḥ khaṃ vidiśo bhūmīr anīkānyasurasya ca ।।
jambho api paramekaikaṃ śarairbahubhirāhave ।। tato dhaneśaḥ saṃkruddho dānavendrasya karmaṇā ।। taddṛṣṭvā duṣkṛtaṃ karma dhanādhyakṣasya dānavaḥ ।। dhanadānucarānyakṣān niṣpipeṣa sahasraśaḥ ।।
rathaṃ dhanapateḥ sarve parivārya vyavasthitāḥ ।। tena daityasahasrāṇi sūdayāmāsa satvaraḥ ।। jagrāha paraśuṃ daityo mardanaṃ daityavidviṣām ।। cicheda śataśo daityo hy ākhuḥ snigdhamivāmbaram ।।
