mahāhavavimardeṣu dṛptaśatruvināśinīm ।। nānācandanadigdhāṅgāṃ divyapuṣpavivāsitām ।। cikṣepa mūrdhni saṃkruddho jambhasya tu dhanādhipaḥ ।। daityo gadābhighātārthaṃ śastravṛṣṭiṃ mumoca ha ।।
hemakeyūranaddhābhyāṃ bāhubhyāṃ caṇḍavikramaḥ ।। prasphurantī papātogrā maholkevādrikandare ।। srotobhiścāsya rudhiraṃ susrāva gatacetasaḥ ।। dhanādhipasya saṃkruddho vākyenātīva kopitaḥ ।।
cicheda bāṇajālaṃ tad ardhacandraiḥ śitaistataḥ ।। sa taṃ daityaḥ śaravrātaṃ cicheda niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ ।। śaktiṃ jagrāha durdharṣāṃ hemaghaṇṭāṭṭahāsinīm ।। sa tāṃ nirūpya vegena kujambhāya mumoca ha ।।
vittehā svalpasattvasya puruṣasyeva bhāvitā ।। tato muhūrtādasvastho dānavo dāruṇākṛtiḥ ।। sa tena paṭṭiśenājau dhanadasya stanāntaram ।। nirbibhedābhijātasya hṛdayaṃ durjano yathā ।।
nipapāta rathopasthe jarjaro dhūrvaho yathā ।। khaḍgāstro nirṛtirdevo niśācarabalānugaḥ ।। atha dṛṣṭvā tu durdharṣaṃ kujambho rākṣaseśvaram ।। sa dṛṣṭvā coditāṃ senāṃ bhallanānāstrabhīṣaṇām ।।
khaḍgena kamalānīva vikośenāmbaratviṣā ।। tiryakpṛṣṭhamadhaścordhvaṃ dīrghabāhurmahāsinā ।। pracaṇḍakoparaktākṣo nyakṛntaddānavānraṇe ।। muktvā kujambho dhanadaṃ rākṣasendramabhidravan ।।
jīvagrāhānsa jagrāha baddhvā pāśaiḥ sahasraśaḥ ।। vāhanāni ca divyāni vimānāni sahasraśaḥ ।। niḥśvasandīrghamuṣṇaṃ ca roṣāttāmravilocanaḥ ।। mumoca dānavānīke taṃ bāṇaṃ śatrudāraṇam ।।
anantaraṃ sphuliṅgānāṃ koṭayo dīptavarcasām ।। tataḥ krameṇa durvāraṃ nānārūpaṃ tadābhavat ।। tato antarikṣe śaṃsanti tejaste tu pariṣkṛtam ।। abhidudrāva vegena padātirdhanadaṃ nadan ।।
babhūva sambhramāviṣṭaḥ palāyanaparāyaṇaḥ ।। papāta bhūtale dīptaṃ ravibimbamivāmbarāt ।। martuṃ saṃgrāmaśirasi yuktaṃ tadbhūṣaṇāgrataḥ ।। yuyutsavaḥ sthitā yakṣā mukuṭaṃ parivārya tam ।।
tānamarṣācca samprekṣya dānavaścaṇḍapauruṣaḥ ।। rakṣiṇo mukuṭasyātha niṣpipeṣa niśācarān ।। samāropyāmararipur jitvā dhanadamāhave ।। dhanādhipo vai vinikīrṇamūrdhajo jagāma dīnaḥ surabharturantikam ।।
māyāmamoghāmāśritya tāmasīṃ rākṣaseśvaraḥ ।। tato viphalanetrāṇi dānavānāṃ balāni tu ।। tato nānāstravarṣeṇa dānavānāṃ mahācamūm ।। vadhyamāneṣu daityeṣu kujambhe mūḍhacetasi ।।
astraṃ cakāra sāvitram ulkāsaṃghātamaṇḍitam ।। praṇāśamagamattīvraṃ tamo ghoramanantaram ।। praphullāruṇapadmaughaṃ śaradīvāmalaṃ saraḥ ।। cakruḥ krūreṇa manasā devānīkaiḥ sahādbhutam ।।
athādāya dhanurghoram iṣūṃścāśīviṣopamān ।। rākṣasendrastam āyāntaṃ vilokya sapadānugaḥ ।। tadādānaṃ ca saṃdhānaṃ na mokṣaścāpi lakṣyate ।। dhvajaṃ paramatīkṣṇena citrakarmāmaradviṣaḥ ।।
kujambhaḥ karma taddṛṣṭvā rākṣasendrasya saṃyuge ।। khaḍgaṃ jagrāha vegena śaradambaranirmalam ।। abhyadravadraṇe daityo rakṣo adhipatimojasā ।। sa tu tena prahāreṇa kṣīṇaḥ saṃbhrāntamānasaḥ ।।
sa muhūrtaṃ samāśvasto dānavendro atidurjayaḥ ।। keśeṣu nirṛtiṃ daityo jānunākramya dhiṣṭhitam ।। tasmiṃstadantare devo varuṇo apāṃpatirdrutam ।। tato baddhabhujaṃ daityaṃ viphalīkṛtapauruṣam ।।
sa tu tena prahāreṇa srotobhiḥ kṣatajaṃ vaman ।। tadavasthāgataṃ dṛṣṭvā kujambhaṃ mahiṣāsuraḥ ।। nirṛtiṃ varuṇaṃ caiva tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrotkaṭānanaḥ ।। tyaktvā rathapathaṃ bhītau mahiṣasyātiraṃhasā ।।
jagāma nirṛtiḥ kṣipraṃ śaraṇaṃ pākaśāsanam ।। tamantakamukhāsaktam ālokya himavaddyutiḥ ।। vāyavyaṃ cāstramatulaṃ candraścakre dvitīyakam ।। vyathitā dānavāḥ sarve śītocchinnā vipauruṣāḥ ।।
mahāhimanipātena śastraiścandrapracoditaiḥ ।। mahiṣo niṣprayatnastu śītenākampitānanaḥ ।। sarve te niṣpratīkārā daityāścandramasā jitāḥ ।। tatrābravītkālanemir daityānkopena dīpitaḥ ।।
ekaiko api jagatsarvaṃ śaktastulayituṃ bhujaiḥ ।। ekaikasyāpi paryāptā na sarve api divaukasaḥ ।। kiṃ prayātāśca tiṣṭhadhvaṃ samare amaranirjitāḥ ।। rājā cāntarito asmākaṃ tārako lokamārakaḥ ।।
śītena naṣṭaśrutayo bhraṣṭavākpāṭavāstathā ।। tāndṛṣṭvā naṣṭacetaskān daityāñchītena sāditān ।। āśritya dānavīṃ māyāṃ vitatya svaṃ mahāvapuḥ ।। nirmame dānavendreśaḥ śarīre bhāskarāyutam ।।
tato jvālākulaṃ sarvaṃ trailokyamabhavatkṣaṇāt ।। tataḥ krameṇa vibhraṣṭaṃ śītadurdinam ābabhau ।। uvācāruṇamudbhrāntaḥ kopāllokaikalocanaḥ ।। vimardastatra viṣamo bhavitā śūrasaṃkṣayaḥ ।।
ityuktaścodayāmāsa rathaṃ garuḍapūrvajaḥ ।। jagaddīpo atha bhagavāñ jagrāha vitataṃ dhanuḥ ।। saṃcārāstreṇa saṃdhāya bāṇamekaṃ sasarja saḥ ।। saṃcārāstreṇa rūpāṇāṃ kṣaṇāccakre viparyayam ।।
matvā surānsvakāneva jaghne ghorāstralāghavāt ।। kāṃścidgadābhirghorābhiḥ kāṃścidghoraiḥ paraśvadhaiḥ ।। kāṃścit pipeṣātha rathasya vegāt kāṃścitkrudhā coddhatamuṣṭipātaiḥ ।। rūpaṃ svaṃ tu prapadyanta hy asurāḥ suradharṣitāḥ ।।
nemidaityastu tāndṛṣṭvā kālanemimuvāca ha ।। bhavatā mohitenājau nihatā bhūrivikramāḥ ।। sarvāstravāraṇaṃ muñca brāhmamastraṃ tvarānvitaḥ ।। yojayāmāsa bāṇaṃ hi brahmāstravihitena tu ।।
tato astratejasā vyāptaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram ।। saṃcarāstraṃ ca saṃśāntaṃ svayamāyodhane babhau ।। mahendrajālamāśritya cakre svāṃ koṭiśastanum ।। tatāpa dānavānīkaṃ gatamajjaughaśoṇitam ।।
cakṣūṃṣi dānavendrāṇāṃ cakārāndhāni ca prabhuḥ ।। turagā niḥśvasantaśca gharmārtā rathino api ca ।। pracchāyaviṭapāṃścaiva girīṇāṃ gahvarāṇi ca ।। toyārthinaḥ puro dṛṣṭvā toyaṃ kallolamālinam ।।
aprāpya salilaṃ bhūmau vyāttāsyā gatacetasaḥ ।। rathā gajāśca patitās turagāśca samāpitāḥ ।। dānavānāṃ sahasrāṇi vyadṛśyanta mṛtāni tu ।। prakopodbhūtatāmrākṣaḥ kālanemī ruṣāturaḥ ।।
gambhīrāsphoṭanirhrādajagaddhṛdayaghaṭṭakaḥ ।। śītaṃ vavarṣa salilaṃ dānavendrabalaṃ prati ।। bījāṅkurā ivāmlānāḥ prāpya vṛṣṭiṃ dharātale ।। śastravṛṣṭiṃ vavarṣogrāṃ devānīkeṣu durjayām ।।
gatiṃ kāṃ ca na paśyanto gāvaḥ śītārditā iva ।। sveṣu bādhe vyalīyanta gajeṣu turageṣu ca ।। apare kuñcitairgātraiḥ svahastapihitānanāḥ ।। evaṃvidhe tu saṃgrāme tumule devasaṃkṣaye ।।
vibhujā bhinnamūrdhānas tathā chinnorujānavaḥ ।। nirbhinnāṅgaisturaṃgaistu gajaiścācalasaṃnibhaiḥ ।। evamājau balī daityaḥ kālanemirmahāsuraḥ ।। yakṣāṇāṃ pañca lakṣāṇi rakṣasāmayutāni ṣaṭ ।।
jaghne piśācamukhyānāṃ sapta lakṣāṇi nirbhayaḥ ।। jaghne sa koṭīḥ saṃkruddhaś citrāstrairastrakovidaḥ ।। saṃkruddhāvaśvinau devau citrāstrakavacojjvalau ।। tamāsādya raṇe ghoram ekaikaḥ ṣaṣṭibhiḥ śaraiḥ ।।
tābhyāṃ bāṇaprahāraiḥ sa kiṃcidāyastacetanaḥ ।। tena cakreṇa so aśvibhyāṃ cicheda rathakūbaram ।। vavarṣa bhiṣajo mūrdhni saṃchādyākāśagocaram ।। tacca karma tayordṛṣṭvā vismitaḥ kopamāviśat ।।
jagrāha mudgaraṃ bhīmaṃ kāladaṇḍavibhīṣaṇam ।। taṃ tu mudgaram āyāntam ālokyāmbaragocaram ।। tau rathau sa tu niṣpiṣya mudgaro acalasaṃnibhaḥ ।। tasya karmāśvinau dṛṣṭvā bhiṣajau citrayodhinau ।।
tato vajramayaṃ varṣaṃ prāvartad atidāruṇam ।। ratho dhvajo dhanuścakraṃ kavacaṃ cāpi kāñcanam ।। taddṛṣṭvā duṣkaraṃ karma so aśvibhyāṃ bhīmavikramaḥ ।। vajrāstraṃ śamayāmāsa dānavendro astratejasā ।।
jīvagrāhaṃ grāhayitum aśvinau tu pracakrame ।। prayātau vepamānau tu padā śastravivarjitau ।। prāpyendrasya rathaṃ krūro daityānīkapadānugaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā daityasya tatkrauryaṃ sarvabhūtāni menire ।।
celuḥ śikhariṇo mukhyāḥ peturulkā nabhastalāt ।। tāṃ bhūtavikṛtiṃ dṛṣṭvā bhagavāngaruḍadhvajaḥ ।। lakṣmīkarayugājasralālitāṅghrisaroruhaḥ ।। kaustubhodbhāsitoraskaḥ kāntakeyūrabhāsvaraḥ ।।
āhūte avasthite tasmin nāgāvasthitavarṣmaṇi ।। tatrāpaśyata devendram abhidrutamabhiplutaiḥ ।। yathā hi puruṣaṃ ghorair abhāgyairvaṃśaśālibhiḥ ।। athāpaśyanta daiteyā viyati jyotirmaṇḍalam ।।
prabhāvaṃ jñātumicchanto dānavāstasya tejasaḥ ।। tamāsthitaṃ ca meghaughadyutimakṣayamacyutam ।। ayaṃ vai devasarvasvaṃ jite asminnirjitāḥ surāḥ ।। enamāśritya lokeṣu yajñabhāgabhujo amarāḥ ।।
nijaghnurvividhairastrais te tam āyāntam āhave ।। ṣaṣṭyā vivyādha bāṇānāṃ kālanemirjanārdanam ।। jambhakaścaiva saptatyā śumbho daśabhireva ca ।। daśabhiścaiva yattāste jaghnuḥ sagaruḍaṃ raṇe ।।
ekaikaṃ dānavaṃ jaghne ṣaḍbhiḥ ṣaḍbhirajihmagaiḥ ।। viṣṇuṃ vivyādha hṛdaye krodhādraktavilocanaḥ ।। mayūkhānīva dīptāni kaustubhasya sphuṭatviṣaḥ ।। satataṃ bhrāmya vegena dānavāya vyasarjayat ।।
cicheda tilaśaḥ kruddho darśayanpāṇilāghavam ।। tena daityasya hṛdayaṃ tāḍayāmāsa gāḍhataḥ ।। śaktiṃ jagrāha tīkṣṇāgrāṃ hemaghaṇṭāṭṭahāsinīm ।। bhinnaḥ śaktyā bhujastasya srutaśoṇita ābabhau ।।
tato viṣṇuḥ prakupito jagrāha vipulaṃ dhanuḥ ।। daityasya hṛdayaṃ ṣaḍbhir vivyādha ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ ।। dvābhyāṃ jyādhanuṣī cāpi bhujaṃ savyaṃ ca pattriṇā ।। srutaraktāruṇaprāṃśuḥ pīḍākulitamānasaḥ ।।
tamākampitamālakṣya gadāṃ jagrāha keśavaḥ ।। sā papāta śirasyugrā vipulā kālaneminaḥ ।। srutaraktaugharandhrastu srutadhāturivācalaḥ ।। patitasya rathopasthe dānavasyācyuto arihā ।।
gacchāsura vimukto asi sāmprataṃ jīva nirbhayaḥ ।। apavāhya rathaṃ dūram anayatkālaneminaḥ ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā dānavāḥ kruddhāśceruḥ svaiḥ svairbalairvṛtāḥ । saraghā iva mākṣīkaharaṇe sarvatodiśam ।।
citrapañcapatāke tu prabhinnakaraṭāmukhe ।। āruhyājau nimirdaityo hariṃ pratyudyayau balī ।। saptaviṃśatisāhasrāḥ kirīṭakavacojjvalāḥ ।। śumbho api vipulaṃ meṣaṃ samāruhyāvrajadraṇam ।।
ājaghnuḥ samare kruddhā viṣṇumakliṣṭakāriṇam ।। śumbhaḥ śūlena tīkṣṇena prāsena grasanastathā ।। jaghnurnārāyaṇaṃ sarve śeṣāstīkṣṇaiśca mārgaṇaiḥ ।। gurūktānyupadiṣṭāni sacchiṣyasya śrutāviva ।।
śarāṃścāśīviṣākārāṃs tailadhautānajihmagān ।। abhyadravadraṇe kruddho daityānīke tu pauruṣāt ।। mathanaṃ daśabhirbāṇaiḥ śumbhaṃ pañcabhireva ca ।। jambhaṃ dvādaśabhistīkṣṇaiḥ sarvāṃścaikaikaśo aṣṭabhiḥ ।।
nardamānāḥ prayatnena cakruratyadbhutaṃ raṇam ।। saṃdhyamānaṃ śaraṃ haste cicheda mahiṣāsuraḥ ।। bhujaṃ tasyāhanadgāḍhaṃ śumbho bhūdharasaṃnibhaḥ ।। tāṃ prāhiṇotsa vegena mathanāya mahāhave ।।
tāṃ nāśamāgatāṃ dṛṣṭvā hīnāgre prārthanāmiva ।। taṃ mumocātha vegena nimimuddiśya dānavam ।। gadayā jambhadaityastu grasanaḥ paṭṭiśena tu ।। nirākṛtaṃ tamālokya durjane praṇayaṃ yathā ।।
jambhāya tāṃ samuddiśya prāhiṇodraṇabhīṣaṇaḥ ।। gṛhītāṃ tāṃ samālokya śikṣāmiva vivekibhiḥ ।। raudrāstramabhisaṃdhāya tasminbāṇaṃ mumoca ha ।। tato bāṇamayaṃ sarvam ākāśaṃ samadṛśyata ।।
dṛṣṭvā tadastramāhātmyaṃ senanīr grasano asuraḥ ।। tena tatpraśamaṃ yātaṃ raudrāstraṃ lokaghasmaram ।। kāladaṇḍāstramakarot sarvalokabhayaṃkaram ।। cakampe ca mahī devī daityā bhinnadhiyo abhavan ।।
cakrurastrāṇi divyāni nānārūpāṇi saṃyuge ।। aiṣīkamastraṃ ca cakāra jambhas tatkāladaṇḍāstranivāraṇāya ।। tāvatkṣaṇenaiva jaghāna koṭīr daityeśvarāṇāṃ sagajānsahāśvān ।। śāntaṃ tadālokya hariḥ svaśastraṃ svavikrame manyuparītamūrtiḥ ।।
cikṣepa senāpataye abhisaṃdhya kaṇṭhasthalaṃ vajrakaṭhoramugram ।। nāśaknuvanvārayituṃ pracaṇḍaṃ daivaṃ yathā karma mudhā prapannam ।। jagāma bhūyo api janārdanasya pāṇiṃ pravṛddhānalatulyadīpti ।। nirmaryādamayudhyanta hariṇā saha dānavāḥ ।।
tīkṣṇānanaiśca nārācaiś cakraiḥ śaktibhireva ca ।। ekaikaṃ śataśaścakre bāṇairagniśikhopamaiḥ ।। astrāṇyādātumabhavann asamarthā yadā raṇe ।। samantātkoṭiśo daityāḥ sarvataḥ pratyayodhayan ।।
uvāca ca garutmantaṃ tasminsutumule raṇe ।। yadyaśrānto asi tadyāhi mathanasya rathaṃ prati ।। ityukto garuḍastena viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā ।। daityastvabhimukhaṃ dṛṣṭvā śaṅkhacakragadādharam ।।
tatprahāramacintyaiva viṣṇustasminmahāhave ।। punardaśabhir ākṛṣṭais taṃ tatāḍa stanāntare ।। sa muhūrtaṃ samāśvāsya jagrāha parighaṃ tadā ।। viṣṇustena prahāreṇa kiṃcidāghūrṇito abhavat ।।
mathanaṃ sarathaṃ roṣān niṣpipeṣātha roṣataḥ ।। tasminnipatite bhūmau dānave vīryaśālini ।। tatasteṣu vipanneṣu dānaveṣvatimāniṣu ।। pratyudyayau hariṃ raudraḥ svabāhubalamāsthitaḥ ।।
śaktyā ca garuḍaṃ vīro mahiṣo abhyahanaddhṛdi ।। grastumaicchadraṇe daityaḥ sa garutmantamacyutam ।। vadanaṃ pūrayāmāsa divyairastrairmahābalaḥ ।। pidhāya vadanaṃ divyair divyāstraparimantritaiḥ ।।
parivartitakāyo adhaḥ papāta na mamāra ca ।। mahiṣāsura mattastvaṃ vadhaṃ nāstrairihārhasi ।। uttiṣṭha jīvitaṃ rakṣa gacchāsmātsaṃgarāddrutam ।। saṃdaṣṭauṣṭhapuṭaḥ kopād bhrukuṭīkuṭilānanaḥ ।।
sajyaṃ cakāra sa dhanuḥ śarāṃścāśīviṣopamān ।। bāṇairjvaladvahniśikhānikāśaiḥ kṣiptairasaṃkhyaiḥ parighātahīnaiḥ ।। tayā bhuśuṇḍyā ca pipeṣa meṣaṃ śumbhasya pattraṃ dharaṇīdharābham ।। tato mahīsthasya hariḥ śaraughān mumoca kālānalatulyabhāsaḥ ।।
viṣṇurvikṛṣṭaiḥ śravaṇāvasānaṃ daityasya vivyādha vivṛttanetraḥ ।। tato asya kiṃcic calitasya dhairyād uvāca śaṅkhāmbujaśārṅgapāṇiḥ ।। vadhaṃ na matto arhasi ceha mūḍha vṛthaiva kiṃ yuddhasamutsuko asi ।। gadāmathodyamya nimiḥ pracaṇḍāṃ jaghāna gāḍhāṃ garuḍaṃ śirastaḥ ।।
tau dānavābhyāṃ viṣamaiḥ prahārair nipetururvyāṃ ghanapāvakābhau ।। vāsāṃsi caivādudhuvuḥ pare tu dadhmuśca śaṅkhānakagomukhaughān ।। parāṅmukho raṇāttasmāt palāyata mahājavaḥ ।। hariṃ devaḥ sahasrākṣo mene bhagnaṃ durāhave ।।
athāyānnikaṭe viṣṇoḥ sureśaḥ pākaśāsanaḥ ।। kimebhiḥ krīḍase deva dānavairduṣṭamānasaiḥ ।। śaktenopekṣito nīco manyate balamātmanaḥ ।। athāgresarasaṃpattyā rathino jayamāpnuyuḥ ।।
hiraṇyakaśipurdaityo vīryaśālī madoddhataḥ ।। pūrve apyatibalā ye ca daityendrāḥ suravidviṣaḥ ।। yuge yuge ca daityānāṃ tvamevāntakaro hare ।। evamuktastato viṣṇur vyavardhata mahābhujaḥ ।।
athovāca sahasrākṣaṃ kālakṣamam adhokṣajaḥ ।। durjayastārako daityo muktvā saptadinaṃ śiśum ।। jambhastu vadhyatāṃ prāpto dānavaḥ krūravikramaḥ ।। avadhyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ tvāṃ vinā sa tu dānavaḥ ।।
tadvaikuṇṭhavacaḥ śrutvā sahasrākṣo amarārihā ।। yatsāraṃ sarvalokeṣu vīryasya tapaso api ca ।। vyālabhogāṅgasaṃnaddhā balino nīlakaṃdharāḥ ।। śūlajvālāvaliptāṅgā bhujamaṇḍalabhairavāḥ ।।
kapālīśādayo rudrā vidrāvitamahāsurāḥ ।। ajeśaḥ śāsanaḥ śāstā śaṃbhuścaṇḍo dhruvastathā ।। pālayanto balasyāgre dārayantaśca dānavān ।। himācalābhe mahati kāñcanāmburuhasraji ।।
airāvate caturdante mātaṅge acalasaṃsthite ।। tasthau himagireḥ śṛṅge bhānumāniva dīptimān ।। jugopāparamagnistu jvālāpūritadiṅmukhaḥ ।। ādityā vasavo viśve marutaścāśvināvapi ।।
nānāvidhāyudhāścitrā dadhānā hemabhūṣaṇāḥ ।। cerurdaityavadhe hṛṣṭāḥ sahendrāḥ surajātayaḥ ।। sitonnatadhvajapaṭakoṭimaṇḍitā babhūva sā ditisutaśokavardhinī ।। gajarūpī mahāmbhodasaṃghāto bhāti bhairavaḥ ।।
mamarda ca raṇe devāṃś cikṣepānyānkareṇa tu ।। tasya pātayataḥ senāṃ yakṣagandharvakiṃnarāḥ ।। pāśān paraśvadhāṃścakrān bhindipālān samudgarān ।। tānsarvānso agrasaddaityaḥ kavalāniva yūthapaḥ ।।
vicacāra raṇe devān duṣprekṣye gajadānavaḥ ।। tasmiṃstasminmahāśabdo hāhākārakṛto abhavat ।। rudrāḥ parasparaṃ procur ahaṃkārotthitārciṣaḥ ।। karṣatainaṃ śitaiḥ śūlair bhañjatainaṃ ca marmasu ।।
saṃmārjya vāmahastena saṃrambhavivṛtekṣaṇaḥ ।। dṛḍhena muṣṭibandhena śūlaṃ viṣṭabhya nirmalam ।। tato daśāpi te rudrā nirmalāyomayai raṇe ।। srutaśoṇitarandhrastu śitaśūlamukhārditaḥ ।।
protphullāruṇanīlābjasaṃghātaḥ sarvatodiśam ।। upasthitārtirdaityo atha pracalatkarṇapallavaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā saktaṃ tu rudrābhyāṃ nava rudrāstato adbhutam ।। nirbhayā balino yuddhe raṇabhūmau vyavasthitāḥ ।।
kapālinaṃ parityajya gataścāsurapuṃgavaḥ ।। mamarda caraṇāghātair dantaiścāpi kareṇa ca ।। tadā kapālī jagrāha karaṃ tasyāmaradviṣaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā śramāturaṃ daityaṃ kiṃcitsphuritajīvitam ।।
tataḥ patata evāsya carma cotkṛtya bhairavam ।। dṛṣṭvā vinihataṃ daityaṃ dānavendrā mahābalāḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā kapālino rūpaṃ gajacarmāmbarāvṛtam ।। evaṃ vilulite tasmin dānavendre mahābale ।।
kalpāntāmbudharābheṇa durdhareṇāpi dānavaḥ ।। nimirabhyapatattūrṇaṃ surasainyāni loḍayan ।। gandhena suramātaṅgā dudruvustasya hastinaḥ ।। tasthau dikpālakaiḥ sārdham aṣṭabhiḥ keśavena ca ।।
tāvacchakragajo yāto muktvā nādaṃ sa bhairavam ।। palāyite gaje tasminn ārūḍhaḥ pākaśāsanaḥ ।। śatakratustu vajreṇa nimiṃ vakṣasyatāḍayat ।। tatprahāramacintyaiva nimirnirbhayapauruṣaḥ ।।
sa hato mudgareṇātha śakrakuñjara āhave ।। lāghavātkṣipramutthāya tato amaramahāgajaḥ ।। tato vāyurvavau rūkṣo bahuśarkarapāṃsulaḥ ।। srutarakto babhau śailo ghanadhātuhrado yathā ।।
cikṣepa vegāddaityendro nipapātāsya mūrdhani ।। dantairbhittvā dharāṃ vegāt papātācalasaṃnibhaḥ ।। sarvataḥ surasainyānāṃ gajabṛṃhitabṛṃhitaiḥ ।। gajaṃ taṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā nimiṃ cāpi parāṅmukham ।।
jambho jajvāla kopena pītājya iva pāvakaḥ ।। tiṣṭhatetyabravīttāvat sārathiṃ cāpyacodayat ।। yathādityasahasrasyābhuditasyodayācale ।। śaśiśubhrātapatreṇa sa tena syandanena tu ।।
tam āyāntam abhiprekṣya dhanuṣyāhitasāyakaḥ ।। bāṇaṃ ca tailadhautāgram ardhacandramajihmagam ।। kṣipraṃ saṃtyajya taccāpaṃ jambho dānavanandanaḥ ।। śarāṃścāśīviṣākārāṃs tailadhautānajihmagān ।।
hṛdaye ca tribhiścāpi dvābhyāṃ ca skandhayor dvayoḥ ।। aprāptāndānavendrastu śarāñchakrabhujeritān ।। tatastu śarajālena devendro dānaveśvaram ।। daityo api bāṇajālaṃ tad vyadhamatsāyakaiḥ śitaiḥ ।।
śakro atha krodhasaṃrambhān na viśeṣayate yadā ।। tadutthatejasā vyāptam abhūdgamanagocaram ।। muñcadbhiradbhutākārair astravṛṣṭiṃ samantataḥ ।। jambhaṃ śaraṇamāgacchad aprameyaparākramam ।।
smaransādhusamācāraṃ bhītatrāṇaparo abhavat ।। tato ayomusalaiḥ sarvam abhavatpūritaṃ jagat ।। gandharvanagaraṃ teṣu gandharvāstravinirmitam ।। ekaikena prahāreṇa gajānaśvānmahārathān ।।
tataḥ surādhipastvāṣṭram astraṃ ca samudīrayat ।। tato yantramayān divyān āyudhānduṣpradharṣiṇaḥ ।। vitānakena tenātha praśamaṃ mausale gate ।। vyāmapramāṇairupalais tato varṣamavartata ।।
tenopalanipātena gatāni tilaśastataḥ ।। nipapātātivegenā-dārayatpṛthivīṃ tataḥ ।। tadopalamahāvarṣaṃ vyaśīryata samantataḥ ।। aiṣīkamastramakarod abhīto atiparākramaḥ ।।
vijṛmbhatyatha caiṣīke paramāstre atidurdhare ।। dahyamāneṣvanīkeṣu tejasā surasattamaḥ ।। tenāstreṇa tadastraṃ ca babhraṃśe tadanantaram ।। jajvāla kāyaṃ jambhasya sarathaṃ ca sasārathim ।।
vāruṇāstraṃ mumocātha śamanaṃ pāvakārciṣām ।। gambhīramurajadhvānair āpūritam ivāmbaram ।। patantībhirjagatsarvaṃ kṣaṇenāpūritaṃ babhau ।। vāyavyam astram akaron meghasaṃghātanāśanam ।।
babhūva vimalaṃ vyoma nīlotpaladalaprabham ।। na śekustatra te sthātuṃ raṇe atibalino api ye ।। mārutapratighātārthaṃ dānavānāṃ bhayāpahaḥ ।। tataḥ praśamite vāyau daityendre parvatākṛtau ।।
tayāśanyā patitayā daityasyācalarūpiṇaḥ ।। tataḥ sā dānavendrasya śailamāyā nyavartata ।। babhūva kuñjaro bhīmo mahāśailasamākṛtiḥ ।। babhañja pṛṣṭhataḥ kāṃścit kareṇāveṣṭya dānavaḥ ।।
astraṃ trailokyadurdharṣaṃ nārasiṃhaṃ mumoca ha ।। kṛṣṇadaṃṣṭrāṭṭahāsāni krakacābhanakhāni ca ।। tataścāśīviṣo ghoro abhavatphaṇaśatākulaḥ ।। tato astraṃ gāruḍaṃ cakre śakraścārubhujastadā ।।
kṛtastu khaṇḍaśo daityaḥ sāsya māyā vyanaśyata ।। vivṛttavadano grastum iyeṣa surapuṃgavān ।। surasenāviśadbhīmaṃ pātālottānatālukam ।। śakro dainyaṃ samāpannaḥ śrāntabāhuḥ savāhanaḥ ।।
kimanantaramatrāsti kartavyasyāvaśeṣitam ।। tato hariruvācedaṃ vajrāyudhamudāradhīḥ ।। vardhasvāśu mahāmāyāṃ puraṃdara ripuṃ prati ।। mā śakra mohamāgaccha kṣipramastraṃ smara prabho ।।
nārāyaṇāstraṃ prayato mumocāsuravakṣasi ।। trīṇi lakṣāṇi gandharvīkiṃnaroragarākṣasān ।। mahāstrabhinnahṛdayaḥ susrāva rudhiraṃ ca saḥ ।। tadastratejasā tasya rūpaṃ daityasya nāśitam ।।
gaganasthaḥ sa daityendraḥ śastrāsanamatīndriyam ।। prāsānparaśvadhāṃścakrān bāṇānvajrānsamudgarān ।। vavarṣa dānavo raudro hy abandhyānakṣayānapi ।। bāhubhirdharaṇiḥ pūrṇā śirobhiśca sakuṇḍalaiḥ ।।
bhagneṣādaṇḍacakrākṣai rathaiḥ sārathibhiḥ saha ।। rudhiraughahradāvartā śavarāśiśiloccayaiḥ ।। śṛgālagṛdhravāyasāḥ paraṃ pramodamādadhuḥ kvacidvikṛṣṭalocanaḥ śavasya rauti vāyasaḥ ।। mṛtasya māṃsamāharañchvajātayaśca saṃsthitāḥ kvacidvṛko gajāsṛjaṃ papau nilīyatāntrataḥ ।।
svakāminīyutairdrutaṃ pramodamattasaṃbhramair mamaitadānayānanaṃ khuro ayamastu me priyaḥ ।। parā priyā hyavāpa yadbhṛtoṣṇaśoṇitāsavaṃ vikṛṣya śavacarma tatprabaddhasāndrapallavam ।। vipāṭya mauktikaṃ paraṃ priyaprasādamicchate samāṃsaśoṇitāsavaṃ papuśca yakṣarākṣasāḥ ।। na pathyatāṃ prayāti me gataṃ śmaśānagocaraṃ narasya tajjahātyasau praśasya kiṃnarānanam ।।
iti priyāya vallabhā vadanti yakṣayoṣitaḥ pare kapālapāṇayaḥ piśācayakṣarākṣasāḥ ।। pitṝn pratarpya devatāḥ samarcayanti cāmiṣair gajoḍupe susaṃsthitāstaranti śoṇitaṃ hradam ।। iti pragāḍhasaṃkaṭe surāsure susaṃgare bhayaṃ samujhya durjayā bhaṭāḥ sphuṭanti māninaḥ ।। yamo api nirṛtiścāpi divyāstrāṇi mahābalāḥ ।।
astrāṇi vyarthatāṃ jagmur devānāṃ dānavānprati ।। gatiṃ na vividuścāpi śrāntā daityasya devatāḥ ।। parasparaṃ vyalīyanta gāvaḥ śītārditā iva ।। viṣṇunā coditaḥ śakraḥ sasmārāstraṃ mahaujasam ।।
dhanuṣyajayye viniyojya buddhimān abhūttato mantrasamādhimānasaḥ ।। vikṛṣya karṇāntam akuṇṭhadīdhitiṃ mumoca vīkṣyāmbaramārgamunmukhaḥ ।। pravepamānena mukhena śuṣyatā balena gātreṇa ca saṃbhramākulaḥ ।। puraṃdarasyāsanabandhutāṃ gato navārkabimbaṃ vapuṣā viḍambayan ।।
prakīrṇadhūmajvalanābhamūrdhajaṃ papāta jambhasya śiraḥ sakuṇḍalam ।। tataste bhagnasaṃkalpāḥ prayayuryatra tārakaḥ ।। sa jambhadānavendraṃ tu surai raṇamukhe hatam ।। sāviṣkāramanākāraṃ tārako bhāvamāviśat ।।
saṃrambhāddānavendrastu surai raṇamukhe gataḥ ।। trailokyaṛddhisampannaḥ suvistṛtamahānanaḥ ।। jambhāstrakṣatasarvāṅgaṃ tyaktvairāvatadantinam ।। taptahemapariṣkāraṃ mahāratnasamanvitam ।।
gandharvakiṃnarodgītam apsaronṛtyasaṃkulam ।। taṃ rathaṃ devarājasya parivārya samantataḥ ।। tataścacāla vasudhā tato rūkṣo marudvavau ।। tatastamaḥ samudbhūtaṃ nāto adṛśyanta tārakāḥ ।।
ekatastārako daityaḥ surasaṃghastu caikataḥ ।। carācarāṇi bhūtāni surāsuravibhedataḥ ।। tat tatrādṛśyad akhilaṃ khilībhūtavibhūtikam ।। sattvaujasāṃ tannikaraṃ babhūva surāsurāṇāṃ tapaso balena ।।
bāṇairanalakalpāgrair bibhidustārakaṃ hṛdi ।। navabhirnavabhirbāṇaiḥ surānvivyādha dānavaḥ ।। tato acchinnaṃ śaravrātaṃ saṃgrāme mumucuḥ surāḥ ।। tadaprāptaṃ viyatyeva nāśayāmāsa dānavaḥ ।।
sunirmalaṃ kramāyātaṃ kuputraḥ svaṃ mahākulam ।। bāṇairvyoma diśaḥ pṛthvīṃ pūrayāmāsa dānavaḥ ।। bāṇajālaiḥ sutīkṣṇāgraiḥ kaṅkabarhiṇavājitaiḥ ।। śāstrārthaiḥ saṃśayaprāptān yathārthānvai vikalpitaiḥ ।।
nārāyaṇaṃ ca saptatyā navatyā ca hutāśanam ।। dhanadaṃ caiva saptatyā varuṇaṃ ca tathāṣṭabhiḥ ।। vivyādha punarekaikaṃ daśabhirdaśabhiḥ śaraiḥ ।। garuḍaṃ daśabhiścaiva sa vivyādha patatribhiḥ ।।
tato vikavacā devā vidhanuṣkāḥ śaraiḥ kṛtāḥ ।। śarairakṣayairdānavendraṃ tatakṣus tadā dānavo amarṣasaṃraktanetraḥ ।। jaghānorasi kṣipramindraṃ subāhuṃ mahendro vyakampadrathopastha eva ।। śarābhyāṃ jaghānāṃsamūle salīlaṃ tataḥ keśavasyāpatacchārṅgamagre ।।
śarairagnikalpairjaleśasya kāyaṃ raṇe aśoṣayaddurjayo daityarājaḥ ।। pṛṣatkaiśca rūkṣairvikāraprayuktaṃ cakārānilaṃ līlayaivāsureśaḥ ।। kṣaṇāllabdhacittāḥ svayaṃ viṣṇuśakrānalādyāḥ susaṃhatya tīkṣṇaiḥ pṛṣatkaiḥ । pracakruḥ pracaṇḍena daityena sārdhaṃ mahāsaṃgaraṃ saṃgaragrāsakalpam ।।
yamo bāhudaṇḍaṃ rathāṅgāni vāyur niśācāriṇām īśvarasyāpi varma ।। daityanāthaḥ kṛtaṃ saṃkhye svabāhuyugabāndhavaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā mudgaram āyāntam anivāryamathāmbare ।। mudgaro api rathopasthe papāta paruṣasvanaḥ ।।
gṛhītvā paṭṭiśaṃ daityo jaghānorasi keśavam ।। khaḍgena rākṣasendrasya nicakarta ca vāhanam ।। vahniṃ ca bhindipālena tāḍayāmāsa mūrdhani ।। dhaneśaṃ ca dhanuṣkoṭyā kuṭṭayāmāsa kopanaḥ ।।
jaghānāstrairasaṃkhyeyair daityendro amitavikramaḥ ।। dānavendravasāsiktaṃ piśitāśanakonmukham ।। papāta cakraṃ daityasya hṛdaye bhāskaradyuti ।। tato vajraṃ mahendrastu pramumocārcitaṃ ciram ।।
tārakasya susaṃprāpya śarīraṃ śauryaśālinaḥ ।। vināśamagamanmuktaṃ vāyunāsuravakṣasi ।। vināśamāgataṃ dṛṣṭvā vāyuścāṅkuśamāhave ।। cikṣepa dānavendrāya pañcayojanavistṛtam ।।
jagrāha vāmahastena bālakandukalīlayā ।। daityendraṃ mūrdhni cikṣepa bhrāmya vegena durjayaḥ ।। kalpāntadahanālokām ajayyāṃ jvalanastataḥ ।। navā śirīṣamāleva sāsya vakṣasyarājata ।।
bhāsitāsitadigbhāgaṃ lokapālo api nirṛtiḥ ।। patitaścāgamatkhaḍgaḥ sa śīghraṃ śatakhaṇḍatām ।। mumoca pāśaṃ daityasya bhujabandhābhilāṣukaḥ ।। sphuṭitakrakacakrūradaśanālir mahāhanuḥ ।।
yakṣarākṣasagandharvā divyanānāstrapāṇayaḥ ।। na cāstrāṇyasya sajanti gātre vajrācalopame ।। jaghāna koṭiśo devān karapārṣṇibhireva ca ।। diśo bhītāni saṃtyajya raṇopakaraṇāni tu ।।
sakeśavāndṛḍhaiḥ pāśaiḥ paśumāraḥ paśūniva ।। siddhagandharvasaṃghuṣṭavipulācalamastakam ।। trailokyalakṣmīstaddeśe prāviśatsvapuraṃ yathā ।। kṣaṇaṃ vinodyamānastu pracalanmaṇikuṇḍalaḥ ।।
sa jānubhyāṃ mahīṃ gatvā pihitāsyaḥ svapāṇinā ।। daityendramarkavṛndānāṃ bibhrataṃ bhāsvaraṃ vapuḥ ।। sa vijñāpayati stheyaṃ kva bandibhiriti prabho ।। yatheṣṭaṃ sthīyatāmebhir gṛhaṃ me bhuvanatrayam ।।
evaṃ kṛte tato devā dūyamānena cetasā ।। tuṣṭuvuḥ spaṣṭavarṇārthair vacobhiḥ kamalāsanam ।। sambhūtasyānantaraṃ sattvamūrte saṃhārecchoste namo rudramūrte ।। dyāvāpṛthvyor ūrdhvakhaṇḍāvarāmyāṃ hy aṇḍādasmāttvaṃ vibhāgaṃ karoṣi ।।
vyaktaṃ devā janmanaḥ śāśvatasya dyauste mūrdhā locane candrasūryau ।। māyākāraḥ kāraṇaṃ tvaṃ prasiddho vedaiḥ śānto jyotiṣā tvaṃ vimuktaḥ ।। tvāmātmānaṃ labdhayogā gṛṇanti sāṃkhyairyāstāḥ sapta sūkṣmāḥ praṇītāḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā mūrtiṃ sthūlasūkṣmāṃ cakāra devairbhāvāḥ kāraṇaiḥ kaiściduktāḥ ।।
tvatsaṃkalpenāntamāyāptigūḍhaḥ kālo meyo dhvastasaṃkhyāvikalpaḥ ।। ye anye sūkṣmāḥ santi tebhyo abhigītaḥ sthūlā bhāvāścāvṛtāraśca teṣām ।। itthaṃ devo bhaktibhājāṃ śaraṇyas trātā goptā no bhavānantamūrtiḥ ।। tasthurmanobhir iṣṭārthasamprāptiprārthanāstataḥ ।।
amarānvaradenāha vāmahastena nirdiśan ।। na rājate tathā śakra mlānavaktraśiroruhā ।। bhasmaneva praticchanno dagdhadāvaściroṣitaḥ ।। daṇḍasyālambaneneva hy akṛcchrastu pade pade ।।
rākṣasendra kṣatārāte tvamarātikṣato yathā ।। vimuktarudhiraṃ pāśaṃ phaṇibhiḥ pravilokayan ।। kiṃ tvaṃ bibheṣi dhanada saṃnyasyaiva kuberatām ।। bhavantaḥ kena tatkṣiptaṃ tejastu bhavatāmapi ।।
alaṃ nīlotpalābhena cakreṇa madhusūdana ।। kriyate stimitākṣeṇa bhavatā viśvatomukha ।। vācāṃ pradhānabhūtatvān mārutaṃ tamacodayan ।। caturmukhaṃ tadā prāha carācaraguruṃ vibhum ।।
na tu vetsi carācarabhūtagataṃ bhavabhāvamatīva mahānucchritaḥ prabhavaḥ । punararthivaco abhivistṛtaśravaṇopamakautukabhāvakṛtaḥ ।। amarāsurametadaśeṣamapi tvayi tulyamaho janako asi yataḥ ।। bhavato varalābhanivṛttabhayaḥ kuliśāṅgasuto ditijo atibalaḥ ।।
kila deva tvayā sthitaye jagatāṃ mahadadbhutacitraviciguṇāḥ ।। api nākamabhūtkila yajñabhujāṃ bhavato viniyogavaśātsatatam ।। kṛtavānasi sarvaguṇātiśayaṃ yamaśeṣamahīdhararājatayā ।। adhivāsavihāravidhāvucito ditijane pavikṣataśṛṅgataṭaḥ ।।
surarāja sa tasya bhayena gataṃ vyadadhādaśarīra ito api vṛthā ।। bhavataiva vinirmitamādiyuge surahetisamūham anutthamidam ।। labdhapraveśāḥ kṛcchreṇa vayaṃ tasyāmaradviṣaḥ ।। vetrahastair ajalpantas tato apahasitāstu taiḥ ।।
cāṭuyuktamatho karma hy amarā bahu bhāṣata ।। vadateti ca daityasya preṣyairvihasitā bahu ।। kṛtāparādhasaṃtrāsaṃ na tyajanti kadācana ।। surāgam upadhā nityaṃ gīyate tasya veśmasu ।।
śaraṇāgatasaṃtyāgī tyaktasatyapariśrayaḥ ।। tasyāvinayamākhyātuṃ sraṣṭā tatra parāyaṇam ।। surānuvāca bhagavāṃs tataḥ smitamukhāmbujaḥ ।। yasya vadhyaḥ sa nādyāpi jātastribhuvane pumān ।।
tapasaḥ sāṃprataṃ rājā trailokyadahanātmakāt ।। sa saptadivaso bālaḥ śaṃkarādyo bhaviṣyati ।। sāṃprataṃ cāpyapatnīkaḥ śaṃkaro bhagavānprabhuḥ ।। uttāno varadaḥ pāṇir eṣa devyāḥ sadaiva tu ।।
tasyāḥ sakāśādyaḥ śarvas tv araṇyāṃ pāvako yathā ।। mayāpyupāyaḥ sa kṛto yathaivaṃ hi bhaviṣyati ।। stokakālaṃ pratīkṣadhvaṃ nirviśaṅkena cetasā ।। jagmustaṃ praṇipatyeśaṃ yathāyogaṃ divaukasaḥ ।।
niśāṃ sasmāra bhagavān svatanoḥ pūrvasaṃbhavām ।। tāṃ vivikte samālokya brahmovāca vibhāvarīm ।। tatkartavyaṃ tvayā devi śṛṇu kāryasya niścayam ।। tasyābhāvāya bhagavāñ janayiṣyati ceśvaraḥ ।।
śaṃkarasyābhavatpatnī satī dakṣasutā tu yā ।। bhavitā himaśailasya duhitā lokabhāvinī ।। tapasyanhimaśailasya kandare siddhasevite ।। tayoḥ sutaptatapasor bhavitā yo mahābalaḥ ।।
jātamātrā tu sā devī svalpasaṃjñā ca bhāminī ।। tayoḥ sutaptatapasoḥ saṃyogaḥ syācchubhānane ।। tato api saṃśayo bhūyas tārakaṃ prati dṛśyate ।। vighnastvayā vidhātavyo yathā tābhyāṃ tathā śṛṇu ।।
tato vihāya śarvastāṃ viśrānto narmapūrvakam ।। prayāsyati tapaścartuṃ tattasmāttapase punaḥ ।। sa bhaviṣyati hantā vai surārīṇāmasaṃśayam ।। yāvacca na satī dehasaṃkrāntaguṇasaṃcayā ।।
evaṃ kṛte tapastaptvā sṛṣṭisaṃhārakāriṇī ।। tadā svameva tadrūpaṃ śailajā pratipatsyate ।। rūpāṃśena tu saṃyuktā tvamumāyāṃ bhaviṣyasi ।। bhedairbahuvidhākāraiḥ sarvagā kāmasādhinī ।।
ākrāntirūrjitākārā rājabhiśca mahābhujaiḥ ।। kṣāntirmunīnāmakṣobhyā dayā niyamināmiti ।। paricchittistvamarthānāṃ tvamīhā prāṇihṛcchayā ।। tvaṃ ca kīrtimatāṃ kīrtis tvaṃ mūrtiḥ sarvadehinām ।।
tvaṃ kāntiḥ kṛtabhūṣāṇāṃ tvaṃ śāntirduḥkhakarmaṇām ।। jaladhīnāṃ mahāvelā tvaṃ ca līlā vilāsinām ।। tvaṃ kālarātrirniḥśeṣabhuvanāvalināśinī ।। ityanekavidhairdevi rūpairloke tvamarcitā ।।
te sarvakāmānāpsyanti niyatā nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। jagāma tvaritā tūrṇaṃ gṛhaṃ himagireḥ param ।। dadarśa menāmāpāṇḍucchavivaktrasaroruhām ।। mahauṣadhigaṇābaddhamantrarājaniṣevitām ।।
maṇidīpagaṇajyotir mahālokaprakāśite ।। śucinyaṃśukasaṃchannabhūśayyāstaraṇojjvale ।। tataḥ krameṇa divase gate dūraṃ vibhāvarī ।। prasuptaprāyapuruṣe nidrābhūtopacārike ।।
rajanīcarabhūtānāṃ saṃghairāvṛtacatvare ।। kiṃcidākulatāṃ prāpte menānetrāmbujadvaye ।। janmadāyā jaganmātuḥ krameṇa jaṭharāntare ।। arañjayacchaviṃ devyā guhāraṇye vibhāvarī ।।
brāhme muhūrte subhage vyasūyata guhāraṇim ।। abhavansukhinaḥ sarve sarvalokanivāsinaḥ ।। abhavatkrūrasattvānāṃ cetaḥ śāntaṃ ca dehinām ।। vanāśritāścauṣadhayaḥ svāduvanti phalāni ca ।।
mārutaśca sukhasparśo diśaśca sumanoharā ।। abhavatpṛthivī devī śālimālākulāpi ca ।। tasmingatāni sāphalyaṃ kāle nirmalacetasām ।। prabhāvastīrthamukhyānāṃ tadā puṇyatamo abhavat ।।
samahendraharibrahmavāyuvahnipurogamāḥ ।। jagurgandharvamukhyāśca nanṛtuścāpsarogaṇāḥ ।। tasminmahotsave prāpte divyaprabhṛtapāṇayaḥ ।। himaśailo abhavalloke tathā sarvaiścarācaraiḥ ।।
anubhūyotsavaṃ devā jagmuḥ svānālayānmudā ।। himaśailasutā devī svayaṃpūrvikayā tataḥ ।। krameṇa rūpasaubhāgyaprabodhairbhuvanatrayam ।। etasminnantare śakro nāradaṃ devasaṃmatam ।।
smṛtiṃ śakrasya vijñāya jātāṃ tu bhagavāṃstadā ।। taṃ sa dṛṣṭvā sahasrākṣaḥ samutthāya mahāsanāt ।। śakrapraṇītāṃ tāṃ pūjāṃ pratigṛhya yathāvidhi ।। pṛṣṭe ca kuśale śakraḥ provāca vacanaṃ prabhuḥ ।।
tatphalodbhavasaṃpattau tvaṃ bhavātandrito mune ।। nirvṛtiṃ paramāṃ yāti nivedyārthaṃ suhṛjjane ।। śīghraṃ tadudyamaḥ sarvair asmatpakṣairvidhīyatām ।। śakraṃ jagāma bhagavān himaśailaniveśanam ।।
vandito himaśailena nirgatena puro muniḥ ।। nivedite svayaṃ haime himaśaile na vistṛte ।। yathārhaṃ cārghyapādyaṃ ca śailastasmai nyavedayat ।। gṛhītārghaṃ munivaram apṛcchacchlakṣṇayā girā ।।
munirapyadrirājānam apṛcchatkuśalaṃ tadā ।। pṛthutvaṃ manasā tulyaṃ kandarāṇāṃ tathācala ।। prasannatā ca toyasya manaso apyadhikā ca te ।। na ca lakṣmīstathā svarge kutrādhikatayā sthitā ।।
pāvanaiḥ pāvito nityaṃ tvatkandarasamāśritaiḥ ।। piturgṛha ivāsannā devagandharvakiṃnarāḥ ।। adhyāste lokanātho api samādhānaparāyaṇaḥ ।। himaśailasya mahiṣī menā munididṛkṣayā ।।
lajjāpraṇayanamrāṅgī praviveśa niveśanam ।। dṛṣṭvā tu tejaso rāśiṃ muniṃ śailapriyā tadā ।। tāṃ vilokya mahābhāgo maharṣir amitadyutiḥ ।। tato vismitacittā tu himavadgiriputrikā ।।
ehi vatseti cāpyuktā ṛṣiṇā snigdhayā girā ।। uvāca mātā tāṃ devīm abhivandaya putrike ।। ityuktā tu tato mātrā vastrāntapihitānanā ।। tataḥ punaruvācedaṃ vākyaṃ mātā sutāṃ tadā ।।
ratnakrīḍanakaṃ ramyaṃ sthāpitaṃ yacciraṃ mayā ।। vavande mūrdhni saṃdhāya karapaṅkajakuḍmalam ।। codayāmāsa śanakais tasyāḥ saubhāgyaśaṃsinām ।। strīsvabhāvādyadduhituś cintāṃ hṛdi samudvahan ।।
anudgīrṇo akṣatirmene ramyametadupasthitam ।। smitānano mahābhāgo vākyaṃ provāca nāradaḥ ।। svachāyayā bhaviṣyeyaṃ kimanyadbahu bhāṣyate ।। nāradaṃ pratyuvācātha sāśrukaṇṭho mahāgiriḥ ।।
sṛṣṭyāṃ cāvaśyabhāvinyāṃ kenāpyatiśayātmanā ।। yo jāyate hi yadbījo janituḥ sa hyasārthakaḥ ।। svakarmaṇaiva jāyante vividhā bhūtajātayaḥ ।। mānuṣācca sarīsṛpyāṃ manuṣyatvena jāyate ।।
aputrajanminaḥ śeṣāḥ prāṇinaḥ samavasthitāḥ ।। krameṇāśramasaṃprāptir brahmacārivratādanu ।। saṃsārasya kuto vṛddhiḥ sarve syuryadatigrahāḥ ।। prāṇināṃ mohanārthāya narakatrāṇasaṃśrayāt ।।
śāstrālocanasāmarthyam ujjhitaṃ tāsu vedhasā ।। daśaputrasamā kanyā yā na syācchīlavarjitā ।। kanyā hi kṛpaṇā śocyā piturduḥkhavivardhinī ।। kiṃ punardurbhagā hīnā patiputradhanādibhiḥ ।।
aho muhyāmi śuṣyāmi glāmi sīdāmi nārada ।। anugraheṇa me chinddhi duḥkhaṃ kanyāśrayaṃ mune ।। tṛṣṇā muṣṇāti niṣṇātā phalalobhāśrayāśubhā ।। ihāmutra sukhāyoktaṃ satpatiprāptisaṃjñitam ।।
na prāpyate vinā puṇyaiḥ patirnāryā kadācana ।। dhanaṃ jīvitaparyāptaṃ patyau nāryāḥ pratiṣṭhitam ।। daivataṃ paramaṃ nāryāḥ patiruktaḥ sadaiva hi ।। etaddaurbhāgyamatulam asaṃkhyaṃ guru duḥsaham ।।
na sa jāta iti brūṣe tena me vyākulaṃ manaḥ ।। lakṣaṇaṃ hastapādādau vihitairlakṣaṇaiḥ kila ।। uttānahastatā proktā yācatāmeva nityadā ।। svachāyayāsyāścaraṇau tvayoktau vyabhicāriṇau ।।
śarīralakṣaṇāścānye pṛthakphalanivedinaḥ ।। taiśca sarvairvihīneyaṃ tvamāttha munipuṃgava ।। muhyāmi muniśārdūla hṛdayaṃ dīryatīva me ।। smitapūrvamuvācedaṃ nārado devacoditaḥ ।।
aparicchinnavākyārthe mohaṃ yāsi mahāgire ।। samāhito mahāśaila mayoktasya vicāraṇe ।। śaraṇyaḥ śāśvataḥ śāstā śaṃkaraḥ parameśvaraḥ ।। tasyaite parameśasya sarve krīḍanakā gire ।।
viṣṇuryuge yuge jāto nānājātirmahātanuḥ ।। ātmano na vināśo asti sthāvarānte api bhūdhara ।। naśyate deha evātra nātmano nāśa ucyate ।। sa janmamṛtyuduḥkhārto hy avaśaḥ parivartate ।।
bhaviṣyati patiḥ so asyā jagannātho nirāmayaḥ ।। śṛṇu tasyāpi vākyasya samyaktvena vicāraṇam ।। sarvāyurdhanasaubhāgyaparimāṇaprakāśakaḥ ।। naivāṅko lakṣaṇākāraḥ śarīre saṃvidhīyate ।।
yathāhamuktavānasyā hy uttānakaratāṃ sadā ।। surāsuramunivrātavaradeyaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। asyāḥ śṛṇu mamātrāpi vāgyuktiṃ śailasattama ।। surāsurāṇāṃ namatāṃ kirīṭamaṇikāntibhiḥ ।।
bhāryā jagadgurorhyeṣā vṛṣāṅkasya mahīdhara ।। śiveyaṃ pāvanāyaiva tvatkṣetre pāvakadyutiḥ ।। atyantaṃ hi mahatkāryaṃ devānāṃ himabhūdhara ।। ātmānaṃ sa punarjātaṃ mene menāpatistadā ।।
uvāca so api saṃhṛṣṭo nāradaṃ tu himācalaḥ ।। pātālādahamuddhṛtya saptalokādhipaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। himācale acalaguṇāṃ prāpito asmi samunnatim ।। yadi vācāmadhīśaḥ syāṃ tvadguṇānāṃ vicāraṇe ।।
tavāsmānprati cāpalyaṃ vyaktaṃ mama mahāmune ।। munīnāṃ devatānāṃ ca svayaṃkartāpi kalmaṣam ।। ityuktavati śailendre sa tadā harṣanirbhare ।। surakārye ya evārthas tavāpi sumahattaraḥ ।।
sa gatvā śakrabhavanam amareśaṃ dadarśa ha ।। pṛṣṭaḥ śakreṇa provāca himajāsaṃśrayāṃ kathām ।। kiṃ tu pañcaśarasyaiva samayo ayamupasthitaḥ ।। cūtāṅkurāstraṃ sasmāra bhagavānpākaśāsanaḥ ।।
prādurbhūtaṃ tu taṃ dṛṣṭvā śakraḥ provāca sādaram ।। manobhavo asi tena tvaṃ vetsi bhūtamanogatam ।। saṃyuto madhunā caiva ṛturājena durjaya ।। provāca pañcabāṇo atha vākyaṃ bhītaḥ śatakratum ।।
duḥsādhyaḥ śaṃkaro devaḥ kiṃ na vetsi jagatprabho ।। prāyaḥ prasādaḥ kopo api sarvo hi mahatāṃ mahān ।। adhyāśritaṃ ca yatsaukhyaṃ bhavatā naṣṭaceṣṭitam ।। prāgeva ceha dṛśyante bhūtānāṃ kāryasaṃbhavāḥ ।।
śrutvaitadvacanaṃ śakras tamuvācāmarairyutaḥ ।। kasyacic ca kvaciddṛṣṭaṃ sāmarthyaṃ na tu sarvataḥ ।। ratiyukto jagāmāśu prasthaṃ tu himabhūbhṛtaḥ ।। mahārthā ye hi niṣkampā manasteṣāṃ sudurjayam ।।
saṃsiddhiṃ prāpnuyuścaiva pūrvaṃ saṃśodhya mānasam ।। krodhaḥ krūratarāsaṅgād bhīṣaṇerṣyāṃ mahāsakhīm ।। tāmasya viniyokṣyāmi manaso vikṛtiṃ parām ।। avagantuṃ hi māṃ tatra na kaścidatipaṇḍitaḥ ।।
paścānmūlakriyārambhagambhīrāvartadustaraḥ ।। indriyagrāmamāvṛtya ramyasādhanasaṃvidhiḥ ।। jagāma jagatīsāraṃ saraladrumavedikam ।। nānāpuṣpalatājālaṃ gaganasthagaṇeśvaram ।।
tatrāpaśyattrinetrasya ramyaṃ kaṃciddvitīyakam ।। yakṣakuṅkumakiñjalkapuñjapiṅgajaṭāsaṭam ।। tato nimīlitonnidrapadmapatrābhalocanam ।। śravastarasasiṃhendracarmalambottarīyakam ।।
preṅkhatkapālaparyantatumbilambijaṭācayam ।। brahmāñjalisthapucchāgranibaddhoragabhūṣaṇam ।। tato bhramarajhaṅkāramālambidrumasānukam ।। śaṃkarastamathākarṇya madhuraṃ madanāśrayam ।।
tataḥ sā tasya śanakais tirobhūyātinirmalā ।। tatastanmayatāṃ yātaḥ pratyūhāpihitāśayaḥ ।। īṣatkopasamāviṣṭo dhairyamālambya dhūrjaṭiḥ ।। sa tayā māyayāviṣṭo jajvāla madanastataḥ ।।
hṛdayānnirgataḥ so atha vāsanāvyasanātmakaḥ ।। anuyāto atha hṛdyena mitreṇa madhunā saha ।। stabakaṃ madano ramyaṃ haravakṣasi satvaram ।। śivasya hṛdaye śuddhe nāśaśālī mahāśaraḥ ।।
tataḥ karaṇasaṃdeho viddhastu hṛdaye bhavaḥ ।। tataḥ prabhutvādbhāvānāṃ nāveśaṃ samapadyata ।। tataḥ kopānalodbhūtaghorahuṅkārabhīṣaṇe ।। rudrasya raudravapuṣo jagatsaṃhārabhairavam ।।
tannetravisphuliṅgena krośatāṃ nākavāsinām ।। sa tu taṃ bhasmasātkṛtvā haranetrodbhavo analaḥ ।। tato bhavo jagaddhetor vyabhavajjātavedasam ।। bhṛṅgeṣu kokilāsyeṣu vibhāgena smarānalam ।।
rāgasnehasamiddhāntardhāvaṃstīvrahutāśanaḥ ।। samprāpya snehasaṃpṛktaṃ kāmināṃ hṛdayaṃ kila ।। vilokya harahuṅkārajvālābhasmakṛtaṃ smaram ।। tato vilapya bahuśo madhunā parisāntvitā ।।
bhṛṅgānuyātāṃ saṃgṛhya puṣpitāṃ sahakārajām ।। nirbadhya tu jaṭājūṭaṃ kuṭilair alakai ratiḥ ।। jānubhyāmavanīṃ gatvā provācenduvibhūṣaṇam ।। namaḥ śivāyāstu surārcitāya tubhyaṃ sadā bhaktakṛpāparāya ।।
namo astu te gūḍhamahāvratāya namo astu māyāgahanāśrayāya ।। namo astu kālāya namaḥ kalāya namo astu te jñānavarapradāya ।। namo astvameyāndhakamardakāya namaḥ śaraṇyāya namo aguṇāya ।। namo astu nānājagatāṃ vidhātre namo astu te citraphalaprayoktre ।।
namo astu bhaktābhimatapradātre namaḥ sadā te bhavasaṅgahartre ।। śaśāṅkacihnāya sadaiva tubhyam ameyamānāya namaḥ stutāya ।। namo astu bhaktyābhimatapradāya namo astu sarvārtiharāya tubhyam ।। tvāmindumauliṃ śaraṇaṃ prapannā priyāprameyaṃ mahatāṃ maheśam ।।
priyaṃ vinā tvāṃ priyajīviteṣu tvatto aparaḥ ko bhuvaneṣvihāsti ।। tvamevameko bhuvanasya nātho dayālurunmūlitabhaktabhītiḥ ।। tutoṣa doṣākarakhaṇḍadhārī uvāca caināṃ madhuraṃ nirīkṣya ।। anaṅga iti lokeṣu sa vikhyātiṃ gamiṣyati ।।
jagāmopavanaṃ ramyaṃ ratistu himabhūbhṛtaḥ ।। maraṇavyavasāyāttu nivṛttā sā harājñayā ।। kṛtābharaṇasaṃskārāṃ kṛtakautukamaṅgalām ।। śarābhyāṃ saṃyutāṃ śailo gṛhītvā svasutāṃ tataḥ ।।
sakānanānyupākramya vanānyupavanāni ca ।। rūpeṇāsadṛśīṃ loke ramyeṣu vanasānuṣu ।। upasarpya tatastasyā nikaṭe so abhyapṛcchata ।। naitadalpamahaṃ manye kāraṇaṃ lokasundari ।।
rudatī śokajananaṃ śvasatī dainyavardhanam ।। girāvasminmahābhāga giriśastapasi sthitaḥ ।। dagdho asau jhaṣaketustu mama kānto ativallabhaḥ ।। stutavatyatha saṃstutyā tato māṃ giriśo abravīt ।।
lapsyate kāṅkṣitaṃ kāmaṃ nivartya maraṇāditaḥ ।। śarīraṃ parirakṣiṣye kaṃcitkālaṃ mahādyute ।। pāṇāvādāya hi sutāṃ gantumaicchatsvakaṃ puram ।। lajjamānā sakhimukhair uvāca pitaraṃ girim ।।
kathaṃ ca tādṛśaṃ prāptaṃ sukhaṃ me sa patirbhavet ।। durbhagatvaṃ vṛthā loko vahate sati sādhane ।। bhaviṣyāmi na saṃdeho niyamaiḥ śoṣaye tanum ।। sāhaṃ tapaḥ kariṣyāmi yadahaṃ prāpya durlabhā ।।
uvāca vācā śailendraḥ snehagadgadavarṇayā ।। soḍhuṃ kleśasvarūpasya tapasaḥ saumyadarśane ।। bhāvino arthā bhavantyeva haṭhenānicchato api vā ।। bhavanāyaiva gacchāmaś cintayiṣyāmi tatra vai ।।
tataḥ sa cintayāviṣṭo duhitāṃ praśaśaṃsa ca ।। umeti capale putri tvayoktā tanayā tataḥ ।। siddhiṃ ca mūrtimatyeṣā sādhayiṣyati cintitām ।। anujñāya sutāṃ śailo jagāmāśu svamandiram ।।
sakhībhyāmanuyātā tu niyatā nagarājajā ।। divyapuṣpalatākīrṇaṃ siddhagandharvasevitam ।। divyaprasravaṇopetaṃ dīrghikābhiralaṃkṛtam ।। jalajasthalajaiḥ puṣpaiḥ protphullairupaśobhitam ।।
vihaṅgasaṃghasaṃjuṣṭaṃ kalpapādapasaṃkaṭam ।। sarvartukusumopetaṃ manorathaśatojjvalam ।। nataṃ sūryasya rucibhir bhinnasaṃhṛtapallavam ।। saṃvītā valkalairdivyair darbhanirmitamekhalā ।।
śatamekena śīrṇena parṇenāvartayattadā ।। tata udvejitāḥ sarve prāṇinastattapo agninā ।। te samāgamya munayaḥ sarve samuditāstataḥ ।। kimarthaṃ tu suraśreṣṭha saṃsmṛtāstu vayaṃ tvayā ।।
tasyā hyabhimataṃ kāmaṃ bhavantaḥ kartumarhatha ।। tathetyuktvā tu śailendraṃ siddhasaṃghātasevitam ।। putri kiṃ te vyavasitaḥ kāmaḥ kamalalocane ।। tapasyato mahābhāgāḥ prāpya maune bhavādṛśān ।।
praśnonmukhatvādbhavatāṃ yuktamāsanamāditaḥ ।। ityuktvā sā tataścakre kṛtāsanaparigrahān ।। uvācādityasaṃkāśān munīnsapta satī śanaiḥ ।। bhāvaṃ tasyāstu maunāntaṃ tasyāḥ saptarṣayo yathā ।।
sāpi gauravagarbheṇa manasā cāruhāsinī ।। bhagavanto vijānanti prāṇināṃ mānasaṃ hitam ।। kecit tu nipuṇāstatra ghaṭante vibudhodyamaiḥ ।। apare tu paricchinnā nānākārābhyupakramāḥ ।।
mama tvākāśasambhūtapuṣpadāmā vibhūṣitam ।। ahaṃ kila bhavaṃ devaṃ patiṃ prāptuṃ samudyatā ।। surāsurairanirṇītaṃ paramārthakriyāśrayam ।। kathamārādhayedīśaṃ mādṛśī tādṛśaṃ śivam ।।
jñātumasyā vacaḥ procuḥ prakramātprakṛtārthakam ।। śarīrasyāsya saṃbhogaiś cetasaścāpi nirvṛtiḥ ।। kapālī bhikṣuko nagno virūpākṣaḥ sthirakriyaḥ ।। yatinā tena kaste artho mūrtānarthena kāṅkṣitaḥ ।।
tatkathaṃ te mahādevād bhayabhājo jugupsitāt ।। śvasadugrabhujaṃgendrakṛtabhūṣaṇabhīṣaṇāt ।। surendramukuṭavrātanighṛṣṭacaraṇo arihā ।। nātho yajñabhujāmasti tathendraḥ pākaśāsanaḥ ।।
vāyurasti jagaddhātā yaḥ prāṇaḥ sarvadehinām ।। ebhya ekatamaṃ kasmān na tvaṃ samprāptumicchasi ।। asminneva parāḥ sarvāḥ kalyāṇaprāptayastava ।। atastatprāptaye kleśaḥ sa vāpyatrāphalastava ।।
asya te vidhiyogasya dhātā kartātra caiva hi ।। uvāca koparaktākṣī sphuradbhirdaśanacchadaiḥ ।। viparītārthaboddhāraḥ satpathe kena yojitāḥ ।। na māṃ prativicāro asti yatrehāsadgrahāvitau ।।
nūnaṃ na vettha taṃ devaṃ śāśvataṃ jagataḥ prabhum ।। ajamīśānamavyaktam ameyamahimodayam ।। viduryaṃ na haribrahmapramukhā hi sureśvarāḥ ।। prakaṭaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ tadapyatra na vettha kim ।।
kasya bhūḥ kasya varuṇaḥ kaścandrārkavilocanaḥ ।। yaṃ bruvantīśvaraṃ devā vidhīndrādyā maharṣayaḥ ।। aditiḥ kasya māteyaṃ kasmājjāto janārdanaḥ ।। marīceḥ kaśyapaḥ putro hy aditirdakṣaputrikā ।।
brahmā hiraṇmayāttvaṇḍād divyasiddhivibhūtikam ।। prakṛtau tu tṛtīyāyāṃ madhudviḍjananakriyā ।। ajātako abhavadvedhā brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।। brahmaṇaḥ siddhasarvārtham aiśvaryaṃ lokakartṛtām ।।
kṛtvānyaṃ deham anyā dṛk tādṛk kṛtvā punarhariḥ ।। evameva hi saṃsāro yo janmamaraṇātmakaḥ ।। atha nārāyaṇo devaḥ svakāṃ chāyāṃ samāśrayat ।। sāpi karmaṇa evoktā preraṇā vivaśātmanām ।।
iṣṭānyeva yathārthāni viparītāni manyate ।। dharmādharmaphalāvāptau viṣṇureva nibodhitaḥ ।। na hyasya jīvitaṃ dīrghaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ dehe tu kutracit ।। dehināṃ dharma evaiṣa kvacijjāyetkacinmriyet ।।
kvacitsamāḥ śataṃ jīvet kvacidbālye vipadyate ।। jīvito na mriyatyagre tasmātso amara ucyate ।। etatsaṃśuddhamaiśvaryaṃ saṃsāre ko labhediha ।। tasmāddivaścarānsarvān malinānsvalpabhūtikān ।।
sthitaṃ ca tāratamyena prāṇināṃ paramaṃ tvidam ।। yasmānna kiṃcidaparaṃ sarvaṃ yasmātpravartate ।। eṣa me vyavasāyaśca dīrgho ativiparītakaḥ ।। evaṃ niśamya vacanaṃ devyā munivarāstadā ।।
ūcuśca paramaprītāḥ śailajāṃ madhuraṃ vacaḥ ।। prasādayati no bhāvaṃ bhavabhāvapratiśrayāt ।। tvanniścayasya dṛḍhatāṃ vettuṃ vayamihāgatāḥ ।। kvādityasya prabhā yāti ratnebhyaḥ kva dyutiḥ pṛthak ।।
yāmo naikābhyupāyane tamabhyarthayituṃ vayam ।। atastvameva sā buddhir yato nītistvameva hi ।। ityuktvā pūjitā yātā munayo girikanyayā ।। gaṅgāmbuplāvitātmānaṃ piṅgabaddhajaṭāsaṭam ।।
gireḥ samprāpya te prasthaṃ dadṛśuḥ śaṃkarāśramam ।। niḥśabdākṣobhasalilaprapātaṃ sarvatodiśam ।। sapta te munayaḥ pūjyā vinītāḥ kāryagauravāt ।। draṣṭuṃ vayamihāyātāḥ śaraṇyaṃ gaṇanāyakam ।।
tvameva no gatistattvaṃ yathā kālānatikramaḥ ।। ityukto munibhiḥ so atha gauravāttānuvāca saḥ ।। kṣaṇena bhavitā viprās tatra drakṣyatha śūlinam ।। gambhīrāmbudharaṃ prāvṛṭtṛṣitāścātakā yathā ।।
vīrāsanaṃ bibhedeśo mṛgacarmanivāsitam ।। uvāca vīrako devaṃ praṇāmaikasamāśrayaḥ ।। te abruvandevakāryeṇa tava darśanalālasāḥ ।। bhūbhaṅgasaṃjñayā teṣāṃ praveśājñāṃ dadau tadā ।।
ājuhāvāvidūrasthān darśanāya pinākinaḥ ।। viviśurvedikāṃ siddhāṃ giriśasya vibhūtibhiḥ ।। pinākipādayugalaṃ vandyaṃ nākanivāsinām ।। manmathāriṃ tato hṛṣṭāḥ samaṃ tuṣṭuvurādṛtāḥ ।।
bhavatprasādāmalavārisekataḥ phalena kācit tapasā niyujyate ।। sa daityarājo api mahāphalodayo vimūlitāśeṣasuro hi tārakaḥ ।। sa dhanyadhīrlokapitā caturmukho hariśca yatsaṃbhramavahnidīpitaḥ ।। tvameva caiko vividhākṛtakriyaḥ kileti vācā vidhurair vibhāṣyate ।।
na vetsi vā duḥkhamidaṃ prajātmakaṃ vihanyate te khalu sarvataḥ kriyā ।। svayogamāyāmahimāguhāśrayaṃ na vidyate nirmalabhūtigauravam ।। adarśanaṃ tena manoratho yathā prayāti sāphalyatayā manogatam ।। vinemuritthaṃ munayo visṛjya tāṃ giraṃ girīśaśrutibhūmisaṃnidhau ।।
utkṛṣṭakedāra ivāvanītale subījamuṣṭiṃ suphalāya karṣakāḥ ।। vācaṃ vācaspatistuṣṭaḥ provāca smitasundarīm ।। jātā prāleyaśailasya saṃketakanirūpaṇāḥ ।। teṣāṃ tvaranti cetāṃsi kiṃtu kāryaṃ vivakṣitam ।।
sevante te yato dharmaṃ tatprāmāṇyātpare sthitāḥ ।। ūcurmunivarāḥ prītāḥ svalpavarṇaṃ tvarānvitāḥ ।। tacchīghraṃ pāvayātmānam āhutyevānalārpaṇāt ।। jagaduddharaṇāyaiṣa kriyatāṃ vai samudyamaḥ ।।
asamartho abhavadvaktum uttaraṃ prārthayañchivam ।। duhitustānmunīṃścaiva caraṇāśrayam arthavit ।। tadevopasthitaṃ sarvaṃ prakrameṇaiva sāṃpratam ।। varastasyāpi cāhūya sutā deyā hyayācataḥ ।।
putrīvākyādyadatrāsti vidheyaṃ tadvidhīyatām ।। ūcuḥ punarudārārthaṃ nārīcittaprasādakam ।। ārādhyamānapādābjayugalatvātsunirvṛtaiḥ ।। ghoraṃ tapasyate bālā tena rūpeṇa nirvṛtiḥ ।।
tatra sāvahitā tāvat tasmāt saiva bhaviṣyati ।। jitārkajvalanajvālā tapastejomayī hyumā ।। ramyaṃ priyaṃ manohāri mā rūpaṃ tapasā daha ।। vayamarthitavantaste pitaraṃ pūrvamāgatāḥ ।।
pitrā saha gṛhaṃ gaccha vayaṃ yāmaḥ svamandiram ।। tvaramāṇā yayau veśma piturdivyārthaśobhitam ।। haradarśanasaṃjātamahotkaṇṭhā himādrijā ।। nānāmaṅgalasaṃdohān yathāvatkramapūrvakam ।।
upāsata giriṃ mūrtā ṛtavaḥ sārvakāmikāḥ ।। harmyeṣu śrīḥ svayaṃ devī kṛtanānāprasādhanā ।। cintāmaṇiprabhṛtayo ratnāḥ śailaṃ samantataḥ ।। oṣadhyo mūrtimatyaśca divyauṣadhisamanvitāḥ ।।
kiṃkarāstasya śailasya vyagrāścājñānuvartinaḥ ।। tatsarvaṃ himaśailasya mahimānamavardhayat ।। śaṃkarasyāpi vibudhā gandhamādanaparvate ।। śarvasyāpi jaṭājūṭe candrakhaṇḍaṃ pitāmahaḥ ।।
kapālamālāṃ vipulāṃ cāmuṇḍā mūrdhnyabandhayat ।। yo daityendrakulaṃ hatvā māṃ raktaistarpayiṣyati ।। bhujagābharaṇaṃ gṛhya sajjaṃ śaṃbhoḥ puro abhavat ।। dadhre sarabhasaṃ svidyad vistīrṇamukhapaṅkajam ।।
vṛṣaṃ vibhūṣayāmāsa harayānaṃ mahaujasam ।। svāṃ dyutiṃ lokanāthasya jagataḥ karmasākṣiṇaḥ ।। manujāsthimayīṃ mālām ābabandha ca pāṇinā ।। nānākāramahāratnabhūṣaṇaṃ dhanadāhṛtam ।।
karṇottaṃsaṃ cakāreśo vāsukiṃ takṣakaṃ svayam ।। tatastu te gaṇādhīśā vinayāttatra vīrakam ।। niṣpannābharaṇaṃ devaṃ prasādhyeśaṃ prasādhanaiḥ ।। tato vilokitātmānaṃ mahāmbudhijalodare ।।
śobhase deva rūpeṇa jagadānandadāyinā ।। kālo ayamiti cālakṣya prakāreṅgitasaṃjñayā ।। ratiḥ purastava prāptā nābhāti madanojjhitā ।। prayāṇaṃ girijāvaktradarśanotsukamānasaḥ ।।
mahāvṛṣaṃ gaṇatumulāhitekṣaṇaṃ sa bhūdharānaśaniriva prakampayan ।। dharārajaḥśabalitabhūṣaṇo abravīt prayāta mā kuruta patho asya saṃkaṭam ।। viyaccarā viyati kimasti kāntakaṃ prayāta no dharaṇidharāvidūrataḥ ।। gaṇeśvarāś capalatayā na gamyatāṃ sureśvaraiḥ sthiramatibhir nirīkṣyate ।।
vṛthā yamaḥ prakaṭitadantakoṭaraṃ tvamāyudhaṃ vahasi vihāya saṃbhramam ।। amī surāḥ pṛthaganuyāyibhirvṛtāḥ padātayo dviguṇapathān harapriyāḥ ।। surāḥ svakaṃ kimiti sarāgamūrjitaṃ vicāryate niyatalayatrayānugam ।। ajātijāḥ kimiti na ṣaḍjamadhyam apṛthusvaraṃ bahutaramatra vakṣyate ।।
viśaṅkitā bhavadatibhedaśīlinaḥ prayāntyamī drutapadameva gauḍakāḥ ।। prabhoḥ puro bhavati hi yasya cākṣataṃ samudgatārthakamiti tatpratīyate ।। prayuñjate giriśayaśovisāriṇaṃ prakīrṇakaṃ bahutaranāgajātayaḥ ।। na jātayo dhvanimurajāsamīritā na mūrchitāḥ kimiti ca mūrchanātmakāḥ ।।
śrutipriyakramagatibhedasādhanaṃ tatādikaṃ kimiti na tumbareritam । na hanyate bahuvidhavādyaḍambaraṃ prakīrṇavīṇāmurajādi nāma yat ।। niyāmitāḥ prayayuratīva harṣitāś carācaraṃ jagadakhilaṃ hyapūrayan ।। jagatyabhūttumula ivākulīkṛtaḥ pinākinā tvaritagatena bhūdharaḥ ।।
kvacit kvacid vimalavidūravedikaṃ kvacid galajjaladhararamyanirjharam ।। sitāsitāruṇarucidhātuvarṇikaṃ śriyojjvalaṃ pravitatamārgagopuram ।। vijṛmbhitāpratimadhvanivāridaṃ sugandhibhiḥ purapavanairmanoharam । haro mahāgirinagaraṃ samāsadatkṣaṇādiva pravarasurāsurastutaḥ ।।
vyagrapurandhrijanaṃ jayayuktaṃ dhāvitamārgajanākularathyam ।। suprakaṭā samadṛśyata kācit svābharaṇāṃśuvitānavigūḍhā ।। kāciduvāca kalaṃ gatamānā kātaratāṃ sakhi mā kuru mūḍhe ।। kācidapi svayameva patantī prāha parāṃ virahaskhalitāṅgīm ।।
kāpi kṛtavyavadhānamadṛṣṭvā yuktivaśādgiriśo hyayamūce ।। nāmabhir indujaṭaṃ nijasevāprāptaphalāya natāstu ghaṭante ।। dhāvati vajradharo amararājo mārgamamuṃ vivṛtīkaraṇāya ।। sapraṇayaṃ karaghaṭṭitavaktraḥ kiṃciduvāca mitaṃ śrutimūle ।।
śaṃkarasaṃśrayaṇād girijāyājanmaphalaṃ paramaṃ tviti cocuḥ ।। mahānīlamayastambhaṃ jvalatkāñcanakuṭṭimam ।। krīḍodyānasahasrāḍhyaṃ kāñcanāmbujadīrghikam ।। netrāṇi saphalānyadya manobhiriti te dadhuḥ ।।
kathaṃcitpramukhāstatra viviśurnākavāsinaḥ ।। cakāra vidhinā sarvaṃ vidhimantrapuraḥsaram ।। dātā mahībhṛtāṃ nātho hotā devaścaturmukhaḥ ।। carācarāṇi bhūtāni surāsuravarāṇi ca ।।
mumocābhinavānsarvān sasyaśālīnrasauṣadhīḥ ।। gṛhītvā varuṇaḥ sarvaratnānyābharaṇāni ca ।। tasthau sābharaṇo devo harṣadaḥ sarvadehinām ।। jātarūpavicitrāṇi prayataḥ samupasthitaḥ ।।
chatramindukarodbhāsi susitaṃ ca śatakratuḥ ।। jagurgandharvamukhyāśca nanṛtuścāpsarogaṇāḥ ।। mūrtāśca ṛtavastatra jaguśca nanṛtuśca vai ।। uttiṣṭhankramaśaścātra viśvabhugbhaganetrahā ।।
dattārgho girirājena suravṛndair vinoditaḥ ।। tato gandharvagītena nṛtyenāpsarasāmapi ।। jagāma mandaragiriṃ vāyuvegena śṛṅgiṇā ।। sabāndhavo bhavati ca kasya no mano vihvalaṃ ca jagati hi kanyakāpituḥ ।।
haro girau ciramanukalpitaṃ tadā visarjitāmaranivaho aviśatsvakam ।। purodyāneṣu ramyeṣu vivikteṣu vaneṣu ca ।। tato bahutithe kāle sutakāmā gireḥ sutā ।। kadācidgandhatailena gātramabhyajya śailajā ।।
tadudvartanakaṃ gṛhya naraṃ cakre gajānanam ।। jāhnavyāstu śivāsakhyās tataḥ so abhūdbṛhadvapuḥ ।। putretyuvāca te devī putretyūce ca jāhnavī ।। vināyakādhipatyaṃ ca dadāvasya pitāmahaḥ ।।
manojñamaṅkuraṃ rūḍham aśokasya śubhānanā ।। bṛhaspatimukhairviprair divaspatipurogamaiḥ ।। bhavāni bhavatī bhavyā sambhūtā lokabhūtaye ।। aputrāśca prajāḥ prāyo dṛśyante daivahetavaḥ ।।
ityuktā harṣapūrṇāṅgī provācomā śubhāṃ giram ।। bindau bindau ca toyasya vasetsaṃvatsaraṃ divi ।। eṣaiva mama maryādā niyatā lokabhāvinī ।। jagmuḥ svamandirāṇyeva bhavānīṃ vandya sādaram ।।
pāṇinālambya vāmena śanaiḥ prāveśayacchubhām ।। lambamauktikadāmānaṃ mālikākulavedikam ।। prakīrṇakusumāmodamattālikulakūjitam ।। sugandhidhūpasaṃghātamanaḥprārthyamalakṣitam ।।
haṃsasaṃghātasaṃghuṣṭaṃ sphaṭikastambhavedikam ।। śukairyatrābhihanyante padmarāgavinirmitāḥ ।। tatrākṣakrīḍayā devī vihartumupacakrame ।। vapuḥsahāyatāṃ prāptau vinodarasanirvṛtau ।।
prādurbhavanmahāśabdas tadgṛhodaragocaraḥ ।। papraccha taṃ śubhatanur haraṃ vismayapūrvakam ।। ete gaṇeśāḥ krīḍante śaile asminmatpriyāḥ sadā ।। yairahaṃ toṣitaḥ pūrvaṃ ta ete manujottamāḥ ।।
kāmarūpā mahotsāhā mahārūpaguṇānvitāḥ ।। carācarasya jagataḥ sṛṣṭisaṃharaṇakṣamāḥ ।। samāvṛto apyahaṃ nityaṃ naibhirvirahito rame ।। ityuktā tu tato devī tyaktvā tadvismayākulā ।।
yāvantaste kṛśā dīrghā hrasvāḥ sthūlā mahodarāḥ ।। anekaprāṇirūpāśca jvālāsyāḥ kṛṣṇapiṅgalāḥ ।। nānāvihaṅgavadanā nānāvidhamṛgānanāḥ ।। gokarṇā gajakarṇāśca bahuvaktrekṣaṇodarāḥ ।।
anekakusumāpīḍā nānāvyālavibhūṣaṇāḥ ।। vicitravāhanārūḍhā divyarūpā viyaccarāḥ ।। gaṇeśāṃstāṃstathā dṛṣṭvā devī provāca śaṃkaram ।। ekaikaśo mama brūhi dhiṣṭhitā ye pṛthakpṛthak ।।
jagadāpūritaṃ sarvair ebhirbhīmairmahābalaiḥ ।। ete viśanti muditā nānāhāravihāriṇaḥ ।। raktapāḥ sarvabhakṣāśca vāyupā hyambubhojanāḥ ।। na hyeṣāṃ vai anantatvād guṇānvaktuṃ hi śakyate ।।
mānaśilena kalkena capalo rañjitānanaḥ ।। pāṣāṇaśakalottānakāṃsyatālapravartakaḥ ।। ya eṣa gaṇagīteṣu dattakarṇo muhurmuhuḥ ।। nānāścaryaguṇādhāro gaṇeśvaragaṇārcitaḥ ।।
kadāham īdṛśaṃ putraṃ drakṣyāmyānandadāyinam ।। tvayā mātrā kṛtārtho astu vīrako api sumadhyame ।। vīrakānayanāyāśu duhitā himabhūbhṛtaḥ ।। vijayovāca gaṇapaṃ gaṇamadhye pravartitā ।।
kimuttaraṃ vadatyarthe nṛtyaraṅge tu śailajā ।। āhūtastu tayodbhūtamūlaprastāvaśaṃsakaḥ ।। prāsādaśikharātphullaraktāmbujanibhadyutiḥ ।। girijovāca sasnehaṃ girā madhuravarṇayā ।।
ehyehi yāto asi me putratāṃ devadevena datto adhunā vīraka ।। ityevamaṅke nidhāyātha taṃ paryacumbatkapole kalavādinam ।। mūrdhnyupāghrāya saṃmārjya gātrāṇi bhūṣayāmāsa divyaiḥ svayaṃ bhūṣaṇaiḥ kiṅkiṇīmekhalānūpurair māṇikyakeyūrahārorumūlaguṇaiḥ ।। komalaiḥ pallavaiścitritaiścārubhir divyamantrodbhavais tasya śubhaistato bhūribhiścākaronmiśrasiddhārthakair aṅgarakṣāvidhim ।।
evamādāya covāca kṛtvā srajaṃ mūrdhni gorocanāpatrabhaṅgojjvalam ।। gaccha gacchādhunā krīḍa sārdhaṃ gaṇairapramatto nage śvabhravarja śanairvyālamālākulāḥ śailasānudrumadantibhir bhinnasārāḥ pare saṅginaḥ ।। jāhnavīyaṃ jalaṃ kṣubdhatoyākulaṃ kūlaṃ mā viśethā bahuvyāghraduṣṭe vane ।। vatsāsaṃkhyeṣu durgā gaṇeśeṣvetasminvīrake putrabhāvopatuṣṭāntaḥkaraṇā tiṣṭhatu ।।
svasya pitṛjanaprārthitaṃ bhavyamāyātibhāvinyasau bhavyatā ।। so api nirvartya sarvān gaṇān sasmayamāha bālatvalīlārasāviṣṭadhīḥ ।। eṣa mātrā svayaṃ me kṛtabhūṣaṇo atra eṣa paṭaḥ pāṭalairbindubhiḥ sinduvārasya puṣpairiyaṃ mālatīmiśritā mālikā me śirasyāhitā ।। ko ayamātodyadhārī gaṇastasya dāsyāmi hastādidaṃ krīḍanam ।।
dakṣiṇātpaścimaṃ paścimāduttaramuttarātpūrvamabhyetya sakhyā yutā prekṣatī taṃ gavākṣāntarādvīrakaṃ śailaputrī bahiḥ krīḍanaṃ yajjaganmāturapyeṣa cittabhramaḥ ।। putralubdho janastatra ko mohamāyāti na svalpacetā jaḍo māṃsaviṇmūtrasaṃghātadehaḥ ।। draṣṭumabhyantare nākavāseśvarair indumauliṃ praviṣṭeṣu kakṣāntaram ।। vāhanātyāvarohā gaṇāstairyuto lokapālāstramūrto hyayaṃ khaḍgo vikhaḍgakaro nirmamaḥ kṛtāntaḥ kasya kenāhato brūta maune bhavanto astradaṇḍena kiṃ duḥspṛhāḥ ।।
bhīmamūrtyānanenāsti kṛtyaṃ girau ya eṣo astrajñena kiṃ vadhyate ।। mā vṛthā lokapālānugacittatā evam evaitad ityūcurasmai tadā devatāḥ ।। devadevānugaṃ vīrakaṃ lakṣaṇā prāha devī vanaṃ parvatā nirjharāṇyagnidevyānyatho bhūtapā nirjharāmbhonipāteṣu nimajjata ।। puṣpajālāvanaddheṣu dhāmasvapi prottuṅganānādrikuñjeṣvanugarjantu hemārutāsphoṭasaṃkṣepaṇāt kāmataḥ ।।
kāñcanottuṅgaśṛṅgāvarohakṣitau hemareṇūtkarāsaṅgadyutiṃ khecarāṇāṃ vanādhāyini ramye bahurūpasaṃpatprakare gaṇānvāsitaṃ mandarakandare sundaramandārapuṣpapravālāmbuje siddhanārībhir āpītarūpāmṛtaṃ vistṛtair netrapātrair anunmeṣibhir vīrake śailaputrī nimeṣāntarād asmaratputragṛdhrī vinodārthinī ।। so api tādṛkkṣaṇāvāptapuṇyodayo yo api janmāntarasyātmajatvaṃ gataḥ krīḍatastasya tṛptiḥ kathaṃ jāyate yo api bhāvijagadvedhasā tejasaḥ kalpitaḥ pratikṣaṇaṃ divyagītakṣaṇo nṛtyalolo gaṇeśaiḥ praṇataḥ ।। kṣaṇaṃ phullanānātamālālikāle kṣaṇaṃ vṛkṣamūle vilolo marāle ।। nikuñjeṣu vidyādharairgītaśīlaḥ pinākīva līlāvilāsaiḥ salīlaḥ ।।
deśāntaraṃ tadā paścād dūramastāvanīdharam ।। mitratvamasya sudṛḍhaṃ hṛdaye paricintyatām ।। nākarotsevituṃ merur upahāraṃ patiṣyataḥ ।। dināntānugato bhānuḥ svajanatvamapūrayat ।।
yācantyāgamanaṃ śīghraṃ nivāryātmani bhāvitām ।। kuṭilasyeva hṛdaye kāluṣyaṃ dūṣayanmanaḥ ।। śayanaṃ śaśisaṃghātaśubhravastrottaracchadam ।। ratnakiṅkiṇikājālaṃ lambamuktākalāpakam ।।
mandire mandasaṃcāraḥ śanairgirisutāyutaḥ ।। śaśimaulisitajyotsnā śucipūritagocaraḥ ।। tamuvāca tato devaḥ krīḍākelikalāyutam ।। bhujaṃgīvāsitā śuddhā saṃśliṣṭā candane tarau ।।
rajanīvāsite pakṣe dṛṣṭidoṣaṃ dadāsi me ।। uvāca koparaktākṣī bhrukuṭīkuṭilānanā ।। avaśyamarthī prāpnoti khaṇḍanāṃ janamaṇḍale ।। tasyā me niyatastveṣa hy avamānaḥ pade pade ।।
saviṣayastvaṃ gataḥ khyātiṃ vyaktadoṣākarāśrayaḥ ।। ādityaśca vijānāti bhagavāndvādaśātmakaḥ ।। yastvaṃ māmāha kṛṣṇeti mahākāleti viśrutaḥ ।। jīvantyā nāsti me kṛtyaṃ dhūrtena paribhūtayā ।।
uvācāviṣṭasaṃbhrāntipraṇayonmiśrayā girā ।। tvadbhaktibuddhyā kṛtavāṃs tavāhaṃ nāmasaṃśrayam ।। yadyevaṃ kupitā bhīru tvaṃ tavāhaṃ na vai punaḥ ।। śirasā praṇataścāhaṃ racitaste mayāñjaliḥ ।।
tasmānna jātu ruṣṭasya narmaspṛṣṭo janaḥ kila ।। kopaṃ tīvraṃ na tatyāja satī marmaṇi ghaṭṭitā ।। viparyastālakā vegād yātumaicchata śailajā ।। satyaṃ sarvairavayavaiḥ sutāsi sadṛśī pituḥ ।।
tathā duravagāhyebhyo hṛdayebhyastavāśayaḥ ।। saṃkrāntiṃ sarvadaiveti tanvaṅgi himaśailarāṭ ।। kopakampitamūrdhā ca prasphuraddaśanacchadā ।। tavāpi duṣṭasaṃparkāt saṃkrāntaṃ sarvameva hi ।।
hṛtkāluṣyaṃ śaśāṅkāttu durbodhitvaṃ vṛṣādapi ।। nirghṛṇatvaṃ kapālitvād dayā te vigatā ciram ।। ityuktvā mandirāttasmān nirjagāma himādrijā ।। kva mātargacchasi tyaktvā rudanto dhāvitāḥ punaḥ ।।
provāca mātaḥ kiṃtvetat kva yāsi kupitāntarā ।। no cetpatiṣye śikharāt taponiṣṭhe tvayojjhitaḥ ।। uvāca vīrakaṃ mātā śokaṃ putraka mā kṛthāḥ ।। yuktaṃ te putra vakṣyāmi yena kāryeṇa tacchṛṇu ।।
sārhaṃ tapaḥ kariṣyāmi yena gaurītvamāpnuyām ।। dvārarakṣā tvayā kāryā nityaṃ randhrānvavekṣiṇā ।। dṛṣṭvā parāṃstriyaṃ cātra vadethā mama putraka ।। evamastviti devīṃ sa vīrakaḥ prāha sāṃpratam ।।
jagāma kakṣāṃ saṃdraṣṭuṃ praṇipatya ca mātaram ।। kusumamodinīṃ nāma tasya śailasya devatām ।। kva putri gacchasītyuccair āliṅgyovāca devatā ।। punaścovāca girijā devatāṃ mātṛsaṃmatām ।।
sarvataḥ saṃnidhānaṃ te mama cātīva vatsalā ।। anyastrīsaṃpraveśastu tvayā rakṣyaḥ prayatnataḥ ।। pinākinaḥ praviṣṭāyāṃ vaktavyaṃ me tvayānaghe ।। ityuktā sā tathetyuktvā jagāma svagiriṃ śubham ।।
antarikṣaṃ samāviśya meghamālāmiva prabhā ।। grīṣme pañcāgnisaṃtaptā varṣāsu ca jaloṣitā ।। evaṃ sādhayatī tatra tapasā saṃvyavasthitā ।। andhakasya suto dṛptaḥ piturvadhamanusmaran ।।
āḍirnāmāntaraprekṣī satataṃ candramaulinaḥ ।। sa tatrāgatya dadṛśe vīrakaṃ dvāryavasthitam ।। hate tadāndhake daitye giriśenāmaradviṣi ।। tamāgatyābravīdbrahmā tapasā paritoṣitaḥ ।।
brahmāṇamāha daityastu nirmṛtyutvamahaṃ vṛṇe ।। yatastato api daityendra mṛtyuḥ prāpyaḥ śarīriṇā ।। rūpasya parivarto me yadā syātpadmasaṃbhava ।। ityuktastu tadovāca tuṣṭaḥ kamalasaṃbhavaḥ ।।
tadā te bhavitā mṛtyur anyathā na bhaviṣyati ।। tasminkāle tu saṃsmṛtya tadvadhopāyamātmanaḥ ।। bhujaṃgarūpī randhreṇa praviveśa dṛśaḥ patham ।। alakṣito gaṇeśena praviṣṭo atha purāntakam ।।
umārūpī chalayituṃ giriśaṃ mūḍhacetanaḥ ।। sarvāvayavasampūrṇaṃ sarvābhijñānasaṃvṛtam ।। tīkṣṇāgrān buddhimohena giriśaṃ hantumudyataḥ ।। pāpo ramyākṛtiścitrabhūṣaṇāmbarabhūṣitaḥ ।।
manyamāno girisutāṃ sarvairavayavāntaraiḥ ।। yā tvaṃ madāśayaṃ jñātvā prāpteha varavarṇinī ।। prāptā prasannavadanā yuktamevaṃvidhaṃ tvayi ।। na cābudhyadabhijñānaṃ prāyastripuraghātinaḥ ।।
ratiśca tatra me nābhūt tataḥ prāptā tvadantikam ।। hṛdayena samādhāya devaḥ prahasitānanaḥ ।। aprāptakāmā samprāptā kimetatsaṃśayo mama ।। nāpaśyadvāmapārśve tu tadaṅge padmalakṣaṇam ।।
abudhyaddānavīṃ māyām ākāraṃ gūhayaṃstataḥ ।। abudhyadvīrako naiva dānavendraṃ niṣūditam ।। aparicchinnatattvārthā śailaputryai nyavedayat ।। aśapadvīrakaṃ putraṃ hṛdayena vidūyatā ।।
vihitāvasaraḥ strīṇāṃ śaṃkarasya rahovidhau ।। gaṇeśa kṣārasadṛśī śilā mātā bhaviṣyati ।। so abhavatprakrameṇaiva vicitrākhyānasaṃśrayaḥ ।। nirjagāma mukhātkrodhaḥ siṃharūpī mahābalaḥ ।।
proddhūtalambalāṅgūlo daṃṣṭrotkaṭamukhātaṭaḥ ।। tasyāśu vartituṃ devī vyavasyata satī tadā ।। āgamyovāca deveśo girijāṃ spaṣṭayā girā ।। viramyatām atikleśāt tapaso asmānmadājñayā ।।
vākyaṃ vācā cirodgīrṇavarṇanirṇītavāñchitam ।। sa māṃ śyāmalavarṇeti bahuśaḥ proktavānbhavaḥ ।। bharturbhūtapateraṅgam ekato nirviśe aṅgavat ।। evaṃ bhava tvaṃ bhūyaśca bhartṛdehārdhadhāriṇī ।।
tatastatyāja bhṛṅgāṅgaṃ phullanīlotpalatvacam ।। nānābharaṇapūrṇāṅgī pītakauśeyadhāriṇī ।। niśe bhūdharajādehasamparkāt tvaṃ mamājñayā ।। ya eṣa siṃhaḥ prodbhūto devyāḥ krodhādvarānane ।।
gaccha vindhyācalaṃ tatra surakāryaṃ kariṣyasi ।। dattaste kiṃkaro devi mayā māyāśatairyutaḥ ।। umāpi prāptasaṃkalpā jagāma giriśāntikam ।। rurodha vīrako devīṃ hemavetralatādharaḥ ।।
prayojanaṃ na te astīha gaccha yāvanna bhetsyase ।। praviṣṭo na ca dṛṣṭo asau sa vai devena ghātitaḥ ।। dvāreṣu nāvadhānaṃ te yasmātpaśyāmi vai tataḥ ।। ataste atra na dāsyāmi praveśaṃ gamyatāṃ drutam ।।
praveśaṃ labhate nānyā nārī kamalalocane ।। na sā nārīti daityo asau vāyurme yāmabhāṣata ।। akāryaṃ kriyate mūḍhaiḥ prāyaḥ krodhasamīritaiḥ ।। viparītārthabuddhīnāṃ sulabho vipadodayaḥ ।।
lajjāsajjavikāreṇa vadanenāmbujatviṣā ।। śaṃkarasyāsmi dayitā sutā tuhinabhūbhṛtaḥ ।। tuṣṭena gauratā dattā mameyaṃ padmajanmanā ।। jñātvā nārīpraveśaṃ tu śaṃkare rahasi sthite ।।
śīghrameṣyasi mānuṣyāt sa tvaṃ kāmasamanvitaḥ ।। uvācoditapūrṇendudyutiṃ ca himaśailajām ।। nagasute śaraṇāgatavatsale tava nato asmi natārtivināśini ।। viṣabhujaṃganiṣaṅgavibhūṣite girisute bhavatīmahamāśraye ।।
jagati kāṃ ca na vāñchati śaṃkaro bhuvanadhṛttanaye bhavatīṃ yathā ।। vidalitāndhakabāndhavasaṃhatiḥ suravaraiḥ prathamaṃ tvamabhiṣṭutā ।। vimalaśaktimukhānalapiṅgalāyatabhujaughavipiṣṭamahāsurā ।। praṇatacintitadānavadānavapramathanaikaratistarasā bhuvi ।।
tadajite apratime praṇamāmyahaṃ bhuvanabhāvini te bhavavallabhe ।। phaṇasahasrabhṛtaśca bhujaṃgamās tvadabhidhāsyati mayyabhayaṃkarāḥ ।। karaṇajātamihāstu mamācalaṃ nutilavāptiphalāśayahetutaḥ ।। tvayi mamāstu matiḥ satataṃ śive śaraṇago asmi nato asmi namo astu te ।।
praviveśa śubhaṃ bhartur bhavanaṃ bhūdharātmajā ।। cittavyāmohanākārāṃ karīndronmattagāminīm ।। madhye kṣāmāṃ tathākṣīṇalāvaṇyāmṛtavarṣiṇīm ।। sakāmaḥ śaṅkito dīno raudro vīro bhayānakaḥ ।।
jighāṃsurdevavākyena bhairavaṃ kṛtavānvapuḥ ।। tasyā rūpasahasrāṇi dadarśa girigocaraḥ ।। pārvatyā cātha niḥśaṅkaḥ śaṃkaro vābhavattataḥ ।। virahotkaṇṭhitāṃ bhāryāṃ prāpya bhūyo himātmajām ।।
nānākaraṇabaddhotthā krīḍāsīt saṃtatā tayoḥ ।। vyasarjayat svakānyeva gṛhāṇyādarapūrvakam ।। nibhṛtaḥ krīḍatītyuktā yayuste ca yathāgatam ।। jvalanaṃ codayāmāsur jñātuṃ śaṃkaraceṣṭitam ।।
dadṛśe śayane śarvaṃ rataṃ girijayā saha ।। tamuvāca mahādevaḥ kiṃcitkopasamanvitaḥ ।। lajjayā viratisthāyāṃ tvamardhaṃ piba pāvaka ।। ityuktaḥ prāñjalirvahnir apibadvīryamāhitam ।।
vipāṭya jaṭharaṃ teṣāṃ vīryaṃ māheśvaraṃ tataḥ ।। tasminsaro mahajjātaṃ vimalaṃ bahuyojanam ।। tacchrutvā tu tato devī hemadrumamahājalam ।। tatra kṛtvā jalakrīḍāṃ tadabjakṛtaśekharā ।।
pātukāmā ca tattoyaṃ svādu nirmalapaṅkajam ।। padmapatre tu tadvāri gṛhītvopasthitā gṛham ।। tatastā ūcurakhilaṃ kṛttikā himaśailajām ।। bhavellokeṣu vikhyātaḥ sarveṣvapi śubhānane ।।
sarvairavayavairyukto bhavatībhyaḥ suto bhavet ।। uttamānyuttamāṅgāni yadyevaṃ tu bhaviṣyati ।। tatastā harṣasampūrṇāḥ padmapatrasthitaṃ payaḥ ।। pīte tu salile tasmiṃs tatastasminsarovare ।।
niścakrāmādbhuto bālaḥ sarvalokavibhāsakaḥ ।। gṛhītanirmalodagraśaktiśūlaḥ ṣaḍānanaḥ ।। etasmātkāraṇāddaivaḥ kumāraścāpi so abhavat ।। skandācca vadane vahneḥ śukrātsuvadano arihā ।।
śākhābhidhāḥ samākhyātāḥ ṣaṭsu vaktreṣu vistṛtāḥ ।। skando viśākhaḥ ṣaḍvaktraḥ kārtikeyaśca viśrutaḥ ।। sambhūtāvarkasadṛśau viśāle śarakānane ।। bālakābhyāṃ cakāraikaṃ matvā cāmarabhūtaye ।।
sarvairamarasaṃghātair brahmendropendrabhāskaraiḥ ।। chatraiścāmarajālaiśca bhūṣaṇaiśca vilepanaiḥ ।। sutāmasmai dadau śakro devaseneti viśrutām ।। yakṣāṇāṃ daśalakṣāṇi dadāvasmai dhanādhipaḥ ।।
evaṃ surāstu te sarve parivāramanuttamam ।। dadurmuditacetaskāḥ skandāyādityavarcase ।। stotreṇānena varadaṃ ṣaṇmukhaṃ mukhyaśaḥ surāḥ ।। navārkavidyuddyutaye namo astute namo astu te ṣaṇmukha kāmarūpa ।।
namo astu te arkapratimaprabhāya namo astu guhyāya guhāya tubhyam ।। namo viśālāmalalocanāya namo viśākhāya mahāvratāya ।। namo mayūrojjvalavāhanāya namo astu keyūradharāya tubhyam ।। namaste namaste varavīryaśāline kṛpāparo no bhava bhavyamūrte ।।
nirīkṣya netrairamalaiḥ sureśāñ śatrūnhaniṣyāmi gatajvarāḥ stha ।। yadyapyasādhyaṃ hṛdyaṃ vo hṛdaye cintitaṃ param ।। sarva eva mahātmānaṃ guhaṃ tadgatamānasāḥ ।। tameva jahi hṛdyo artha eṣo asmākaṃ bhayāpaha ।।
jagāma jagatāṃ nāthaḥ stūyamāno amareśvaraiḥ ।। tataśca preṣayāmāsa śakro labdhasamāśrayaḥ ।। sa tu gatvābravīddaityaṃ nirbhayo bhīmadarśanaḥ ।। tārakāsura tacchrutvā ghaṭaśaktyā yathecchayā ।।
tasyāhaṃ śāsakaste adya rājāsmi bhuvanatraye ।। uvāca dūtaṃ duṣṭātmā naṣṭaprāyavibhūtikaḥ ।। nistrapatvānna te lajjā vidyate śakra durmate ।। nālabdhasaṃśrayaḥ śakro vaktumevaṃ hi cārhati ।।
nimittāni ca duṣṭāni so apaśyadduṣṭaceṣṭitaḥ ।। bhujanetraprakampaṃ ca vaktraśoṣamanobhramam ।। duṣṭāṃśca prāṇino raudrān so apaśyadduṣṭavedinaḥ ।। yāvadgajaghaṭāghaṇṭāraṇatkāraravotkaṭām ।।
cañcalasyandanodagradhvajarājivirājitām ।। tāṃ bhūṣaṇanibaddhāṃ ca kiṃnarodgatināditām ।। vikośāstrapariṣkārāṃ varmanirmaladarśanām ।। senāṃ nākasadāṃ daityaḥ prāsādastho vyalokayat ।।
apūrvaḥ ko bhavedyoddhā yo mayā na vinirjitaḥ ।। siddhabandibhirudghuṣṭam idaṃ hṛdayadāraṇam ।। jayātulaśaktidīdhitipiñjara bhujadaṇḍacaṇḍaraṇarabhasa । suravadana kumudakānana-vikāsanendo kumāra jaya ditijakulamahodadhivaḍavānala ।।
ṣaṇmukha madhuraravamayūraratha suramukuṭakoṭighaṭṭitacaraṇanakhāṅkuramahāsana । jaya lalitacūḍākalāpanavavimaladalakamalakānta daityavaṃśaduḥsahadāvānala ।। jaya viśākha vibho jaya sakalalokatāraka jaya devasenānāyaka । skanda jaya gaurīnandana ghaṇṭāpriya priya viśākha vibho dhṛtapatākaprakīrṇapaṭala ।
kanakabhūṣaṇa bhāsuradinakaracchāya ।। jaya janitasaṃbhrama līlālūnākhilārāte jaya sakalalokatāraka ditijāsuravaratārakāntaka । skanda jaya bāla saptavāsara jaya bhuvanāvaliśokavināśana ।। sasmāra brahmaṇo vākyaṃ vadhaṃ bālādupasthitam ।।
mandirānnirjagāmāśu śokagrastena cetasā ।। yodhā dhāvata gṛhīta yojayadhvaṃ varūthinīm ।। kiṃ bāla yoddhukāmo asi krīḍa kandukalīlayā ।। bālatvādatha te buddhir evaṃ svalpārthadarśinī ।।
śṛṇu tāraka śāstrārthas tava caiva nirūpyate ।। śiśutvaṃ māvamaṃsthā me śiśuḥ kālabhujaṃgamaḥ ।। alpākṣaro na mantraḥ kiṃ susphuro daitya dṛśyate ।। kumārastaṃ nirasyātha vajreṇāmoghavarcasā ।।
kareṇa tacca jagrāha kārtikeyo amarārihā ।। tayā hatastato daityaś cakampe acalarāḍiva ।। cintayāmāsa buddhyā vai prāptaḥ kālo na saṃśayaḥ ।। sarve daityeśvarā jaghnuḥ kumāraṃ raṇadāruṇam ।।
raṇaśauṇḍāstu daityendrāḥ punaḥ prāsaiḥ śilīmukhaiḥ ।। kumārasya vyathā nābhūd daityāstranihatasya tu ।। devānnipīḍitāndṛṣṭvā kumāraḥ kopamāviśat ।। tatastair niṣpratīkarais tāḍitāḥ surakaṇṭakāḥ ।।
vidruteṣvatha daityeṣu hateṣu ca samantataḥ ।। jagrāha ca gadāṃ divyāṃ hemajālapariṣkṛtām ।। śarairmayūrapatraiśca cakāra vimukhānsurān ।। bibheda tārakaḥ kruddhaḥ sa sainye asuranāyakaḥ ।।
jagrāha śaktiṃ vimalāṃ raṇe kanakabhūṣaṇām ।। tato javānmahāsenas tārakaṃ dānavādhipam ।। hato asyadya mayā śaktyā smara śastraṃ suśikṣitam ।। bibheda daityahṛdayaṃ vajraśailendrakarkaśam ।।
vikīrṇamukuṭoṣṇīṣo visrastākhilabhūṣaṇaḥ ।। nābhūt kaścit tadā duḥkhī narakeṣvapi pāpakṛt ।। jagmuḥ svāneva bhavanān bhūridhāmāna utsukāḥ ।। tuṣṭāḥ samprāptasarvecchāḥ saha siddhaistapodhanaiḥ ।।
śṛṇuyācchrāvayedvāpi sa bhavetkīrtimānnaraḥ ।। bhūtebhyo nirbhayaścāpi sarvaduḥkhavivarjitaḥ ।। sa muktaḥ kilbiṣaiḥ sarvair mahādhanapatirbhavet ।। tanukṣaye ca sāyujyaṃ ṣaṇmukhasya vrajennaraḥ ।।
narasiṃhasya māhātmyaṃ tathā pāpavināśanam ।। daityānāmādipuruṣaś cakāra sa mahattapaḥ ।। jalavāsī samabhavat snānamaunadhṛtavrataḥ ।। brahmā prīto abhavattasya tapasā niyamena ca ।।
vimānenārkavarṇena haṃsayuktena bhāsvatā ।। rudrairviśvasahāyaiśca yakṣarākṣasapannagaiḥ ।। nakṣatraiśca muhūrtaiśca khecaraiśca mahāgrahaiḥ ।। rājarṣibhiḥ puṇyakṛdbhir gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ ।।
brahmā brahmavidāṃ śreṣṭho daityaṃ vacanamabravīt ।। varaṃ varaya bhadraṃ te yatheṣṭaṃ kāmamāpnuhi ।। na mānuṣāḥ piśācā vā hanyurmāṃ devasattama ।। yadi me bhagavānprīto vara eṣa vṛto mayā ।।
na śuṣkeṇa na cārdreṇa na divā na niśātha vā ।। salilaṃ cāntarikṣaṃ ca nakṣatrāṇi diśo daśa ।। dhanadaśca dhanādhyakṣo yakṣaḥ kiṃpuruṣādhipaḥ ।। sarvānkāmānsadā vatsa prāpsyasi tvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।।
vairājaṃ brahmasadanaṃ brahmarṣigaṇasevitam ।। varapradānaṃ śrutvaiva pitāmahamupasthitāḥ ।। tatprasīdāśu bhagavan vadho apyasya vicintyatām ।। sraṣṭā tvaṃ havyakavyānām avyaktaprakṛtir budhaḥ ।।
āśvāsayāmāsa surān suśītairvacanāmbubhiḥ ।। tapaso ante asya bhagavān vadhaṃ viṣṇuḥ kariṣyati ।। svāni sthānāni divyāni viprajagmurmudānvitāḥ ।। hiraṇyakaśipurdaityo varadānena darpitaḥ ।।
satyadharmaparāndāntān dharṣayāmāsa dānavaḥ ।। trailokyaṃ vaśamānīya svarge vasati dānavaḥ ।। yajñiyānakaroddaityān ayajñiyāśca devatāḥ ।। sendrā devagaṇā yakṣāḥ siddhadvijamaharṣayaḥ ।।
devadevaṃ yajñamayaṃ vāsudevaṃ sanātanam ।। trāyasva jahi daityendraṃ hiraṇyakaśipuṃ prabho ।। tvaṃ hi naḥ paramo devo brahmādīnāṃ surottama ।। tathaiva tridivaṃ devāḥ pratipadyata mā ciram ।।
avadhyamamarendrāṇāṃ dānavendraṃ nihanmyaham ।। vadhaṃ saṃkalpayāmāsa hiraṇyakaśipoḥ prabhuḥ ।। athauṃkārasahāyastu bhagavānviṣṇuravyayaḥ ।। tejasā bhāskarākāraḥ śaśī kāntyeva cāparaḥ ।।
nārasiṃhena vapuṣā pāṇiṃ saṃspṛśya pāṇinā ।। sarvakāmayutāṃ śubhrāṃ hiraṇyakaśipoḥ sabhām ।। vaihāyasīṃ kāmagamāṃ pañcayojanavistṛtām ।। veśmaharmyavatīṃ ramyāṃ jvalantīmiva tejasā ।।
divyaratnamayairvṛkṣaiḥ phalapuṣpapradairyutām ।। avatānaistathā gulmair mañjarīśatadhāribhiḥ ।। raśmivatī bhāsvarā ca divyagandhamanoramā ।। na kṣutpipāse glāniṃ vā prāpya tāṃ prāpnuvanti te ।।
stambhairna vibhṛtā sā vai śāśvatī cākṣapā sadā ।। dīpyate nākapṛṣṭhasthā bhāsayantīva bhāskaram ।। rasayuktaṃ prabhūtaṃ ca bhakṣyabhojyamanantakam ।। uṣṇe śītāni toyāni śīte coṣṇāni santi ca ।।
latāvitānasaṃchannā nadīṣu ca saraḥsu ca ।। gandhavanti ca puṣpāṇi rasavanti phalāni ca ।। apaśyatsarvatīrthāni sabhāyāṃ tasya sa prabhuḥ ।। raktaiḥ kuvalayairnīlaiḥ kumudaiḥ saṃvṛtāni ca ।।
kāraṇḍavaiścakravākaiḥ sārasaiḥ kurarairapi ।। bahuhaṃsopagītāni sārasābhirutāni ca ।। dṛṣṭavānparvatāgreṣu nānāpuṣpadharā latāḥ ।। cūtā nīpāḥ prasthapuṣpāḥ kadambā bakulā dhavāḥ ।।
sālāstālāstamālāśca campakāśca manoramāḥ ।। vidrumāśca drumāścaiva jvalitāgnisamaprabhāḥ ।। añjanāśokavarṇāśca bahavaścitrakā drumāḥ ।। nīpāḥ sumanasaścaiva nimbā aśvatthatindukāḥ ।।
āmalakyastathā jambūlakucāḥ śailavālukāḥ ।। kālīyakā drukālāśca hiṅgavaḥ pāriyātrakāḥ ।। raktāḥ kuraṇṭakāścaiva nīlāścāgarubhiḥ saha ।। saptaparṇāśca bilvāśca madhupairāvṛtāstathā ।।
madhūkāḥ saptaparṇāśca bahavaḥ kṣīrakā drumāḥ ।। ete cānye ca bahavas tatra kānanajā drumāḥ ।। cakorāḥ śatapatrāśca mattakokilasārikāḥ ।। raktapītāruṇāstatra pādapāgragatāḥ khagāḥ ।।
tasyāṃ sabhāyāṃ daityendro hiraṇyakaśipustadā ।। anarghyamaṇivajrārciḥ śikhājvalitakuṇḍalaḥ ।। divākaranibhe divye divyāstaraṇasaṃstṛte ।। hiraṇyakaśipurdaitya āste jvalitakuṇḍalaḥ ।।
divyatānena gītāni jagur gandharvasattamāḥ ।। divyātha saurabheyī ca samīcī puñjikasthalī ।। cārukeśī ghṛtācī ca menakā corvaśī tathā ।। upatiṣṭhanti rājānaṃ hiraṇyakaśipuṃ prabhum ।।
upāsate diteḥ putrāḥ sarve labdhavarāstathā ।। balirvirocanastatra narakaḥ pṛthivīsutaḥ ।। surahantā sunāmā ca pramatiḥ sumatirvaraḥ ।। viśvarūpaḥ surūpaśca svabalaśca mahābalaḥ ।।
ghaṭāsyo akampanaścaiva prajanaścendratāpanaḥ ।। sragviṇo vāgminaḥ sarve sadaiva caritavratāḥ ।। ete cānye ca bahavo hiraṇyakaśipuṃ prabhum ।। vimānairvividhākārair bhrājamānairivāgnibhiḥ ।।
bhūṣitāṅgā diteḥ putrās tamupāsanta sarvaśaḥ ।। hiraṇyavapuṣaḥ sarve divākarasamaprabhāḥ ।। aiśvaryaṃ daityasiṃhasya yathā tasya mahātmanaḥ ।। sa dadarśa mṛgādhipaḥ sabhāyāṃ suracitaratnagavākṣaśobhitāyām ।।
divasakaramahāprabhājvalantaṃ ditijasahasraśatairniṣevyamāṇam ।। narasiṃhavapuśchannaṃ bhasmacchannamivānalam ।। divyena cakṣuṣā siṃham apaśyaddevamāgatam ।। vismitā dānavāḥ sarve hiraṇyakaśipuśca saḥ ।।
na śrutaṃ na ca no dṛṣṭaṃ nārasiṃhamidaṃ vapuḥ ।। daityāntakaraṇaṃ ghoraṃ saṃśatīva mano mama ।। himavānpāriyātraśca ye cānye kulaparvatāḥ ।। dhanado varuṇaścaiva yamaḥ śakraḥ śacīpatiḥ ।।
nāgā yakṣāḥ piśācāśca rākṣasā bhīmavikramāḥ ।। sthāvarāṇi ca sarvāṇi jaṅgamāni tathaiva ca ।। vimānaśatasaṃkīrṇā tathaiva bhavataḥ sabhā ।। dṛśyante nārasiṃhe asmiṃs tathedamakhilaṃ jagat ।।
utpātakālaśca dhṛtirmatiśca ratiśca satyaṃ ca tapo damaśca ।। krodhaśca kāmaśca tathaiva harṣo dharmaśca mohaḥ pitaraśca sarve ।। uvāca dānavānsarvān gaṇāṃśca sa gaṇādhipaḥ ।। yadi vā saṃśayaḥ kaścid vadhyatāṃ vanagocaraḥ ।।
parikṣipanto muditās trāsayāmāsurojasā ।। babhañja tāṃ sabhāṃ divyāṃ vyāditāsya ivāntakaḥ ।। cikṣepāstrāṇi siṃhasya roṣādvyākulalocanaḥ ।। kālacakraṃ tathāghoraṃ viṣṇucakraṃ tathā param ।।
vicitrāmaśanīṃ caiva śuṣkārdraṃ cāśanidvayam ।। mohanaṃ śoṣaṇaṃ caiva saṃtāpanavilāpanam ।। tathāpratihatāṃ śaktiṃ krauñcamastraṃ tathaiva ca ।। kampanaṃ śātanaṃ caiva tvāṣṭraṃ caiva subhairavam ।।
saṃvartanaṃ mohanaṃ ca tathā māyādharaṃ param ।। astraṃ pāśupataṃ caiva yasyāpratihatā gatiḥ ।। nārāyaṇāstramaindraṃ ca sārpamastraṃ tathādbhutam ।। mahābalaṃ bhāvanaṃ ca prasthāpanavikampane ।।
asṛjannarasiṃhasya dīptasyāgnerivāhutim ।। vivasvān gharmasamaye himavantamivāṃśubhiḥ ।। kṣaṇena plāvayāmāsa mainākamiva sāgaraḥ ।। vajrairaśanibhiścaiva sāgnibhiśca mahādrumaiḥ ।।
śataghnībhiśca dīptābhir daṇḍairapi sudāruṇaiḥ ।। samantato abhyudyatabāhukāyāḥ sthitāstriśīrṣā iva nāgapāśāḥ ।। muktāvalīdāmasanāthakakṣā haṃsā ivābhānti viśālapakṣāḥ ।। tānyuttamāṅgānyabhito vibhānti prabhātasūryāṃśusamaprabhāṇi ।।
kṣipadbhir ugrair jvalitair mahābalair mahāstrapūgaiḥ susamāvṛto babhau । giriryathā saṃtatavarṣibhir ghanaiḥ kṛtāndhakārāntarakaṃdaro drumaiḥ ।। tairhanyamāno api mahāstrajālair mahābalair daityagaṇaiḥ sametaiḥ । nākampatājau bhagavānpratāpasthitaḥ prakṛtyā himavānivācalaḥ ।।
saṃtrāsitāstena nṛsiṃharūpiṇā diteḥ sutāḥ pāvakatulyatejasā । bhayādviceluḥ pavanoddhutāṅgā yathormayaḥ sāgaravārisaṃbhavāḥ ।। īhāmṛgamukhāścānye varāhamukhasaṃsthitāḥ ।। ardhacandrārdhavaktrāśca agnidīptamukhāstathā ।।
siṃhāsyā lelihānāśca kākagṛdhramukhāstathā ।। mahāgrāhamukhāścānye dānavā baladarpitāḥ ।। avadhyasya mṛgendrasya na vyathāṃ cakrurāhave ।। mṛgendrasyopari kruddhā niḥśvasanta ivoragāḥ ।।
vilayaṃ jagmurākāśe khadyotā iva parvate ।। mṛgendrāyāsṛjannāśu jvalitāni samantataḥ ।। yugānte saṃprakāśadbhiś candrādityagrahairiva ।। grastānyudīrṇāni tadā pāvakārciḥsamāni vai ।।
meghodaradarīṣveva candrasūryagrahā iva ।। śaktiṃ prajvalitāṃ ghorāṃ dhautaśastrataḍitprabhām ।। huṃkāreṇaiva raudreṇa babhañja bhagavāṃstadā ।। savisphuliṅgā jvalitā maholkeva divaścyutā ।।
nīlotpalapalāśānāṃ mālevojjvaladarśanā ।। tatsainyam utsāritavāṃs tṛṇāgrāṇīva mārutaḥ ।। nagamātraiḥ śilākhaṇḍair giriśṛṅgairmahāprabhaiḥ ।। diśo daśa vikīrṇā vai khadyotaprakarā iva ।।
chādayāṃcakrire meghā dhārābhiriva parvatam ।। bhīmavego acalaśreṣṭhaṃ samudra iva mandaram ।। dhārābhirakṣamātrābhiḥ prādurāsītsamantataḥ ।। āvṛtya sarvato vyoma diśaścopadiśastathā ।।
na spṛśanti ca tā devaṃ nipatantyo aniśaṃ bhuvi ।। mṛgendrapratirūpasya sthitasya yudhi māyayā ।। so asṛjaddānavo māyām agnivāyusamīritām ।। mahatā toyavarṣeṇa śamayāmāsa pāvakam ।।
asṛjadghorasaṃkāśaṃ tamastīvraṃ samantataḥ ।। svatejasā parivṛto divākara ivābabhau ।। lalāṭasthāṃ triśūlāṅkāṃ gaṅgāṃ tripathagāmiva ।। hiraṇyakaśipuṃ daityaṃ vivarṇāḥ śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ ।।
tasminkruddhe tu daityendre tamobhūtamabhūjjagat ।। parāvahaḥ saṃvahaśca mahābalaparākramāḥ ।। ityevaṃ kṣubhitāḥ sapta maruto gaganecarāḥ ।। te sarve gagane dṛṣṭā vyacaranta yathāsukham ।।
sagrahaḥ saha nakṣatrair ākāpatirariṃdamaḥ ।। kṛṣṇaṃ kabandhaṃ ca tathā lakṣyate sumahaddivi ।। gaganasthaśca bhagavān abhīkṣṇaṃ paridṛśyate ।। somasya gaganasthasya grahāstiṣṭhanti śṛṅgagāḥ ।।
śanaiścaro lohitāṅgo jvalanāṅgasamadyutiḥ ।। śṛṅgāṇi śanakairghorā yugāntāvartino grahāḥ ।। carācaravināśāya rohiṇīṃ nābhyanandata ।। ulkāḥ prajvalitāścandre vicaranti yathāsukham ।।
apatangaganādulkā vidyudrūpā mahāsvanāḥ ।। latāśca saphalāḥ sarvā ye cāhurdaityanāśanam ।। unmīlanti nimīlanti hasanti ca rudanti ca ।। pratimāḥ sarvadevānāṃ vedayanti mahadbhayam ।।
cakruḥ subhairavaṃ tatra mahāyuddhamupasthitam ।। na prakāśanti ca diśo raktareṇusamākulāḥ ।। vāyuvegena hanyante bhajyante praṇamanti ca ।। aparāhṇagate sūrye lokānāṃ yugasaṃkṣaye ।।
bhāṇḍāgārāyudhāgāre niviṣṭamabhavanmadhu ।। dṛśyante vividhotpātā ghorā ghoranidarśanāḥ ।। daityendrasya vināśāya dṛśyante kālanirmitāḥ ।। mahīdharā nāgagaṇā nipeturamitaujasaḥ ।।
catuḥśīrṣāḥ pañcaśīrṣāḥ saptaśīrṣāśca pannagāḥ ।। elāmukhaḥ kāliyaśca mahāpadmaśca vīryavān ।। śeṣo ananto mahābhāgo duṣprakampyaḥ prakampitaḥ ।। tadā kruddhena mahatā kampitāni samantataḥ ।।
hiraṇyakaśipurdaityas tadā saṃspṛṣṭavānmahīm ।। nadī bhāgīrathī caiva sarayūḥ kauśikī tathā ।। suveṇā ca mahābhāgā nadī godāvarī tathā ।। kamalaprabhavaścaiva śoṇo maṇinibhodakaḥ ।।
gomatī gokulākīrṇā tathā pūrvasarasvatī ।। jambūdvīpaṃ ratnavaṭaṃ sarvaratnopaśobhitam ।। mahānadaṃ ca lauhityaṃ śailakānanaśobhitam ।। māgadhāśca mahāgrāmā muṇḍāḥ śuṅgāstathaiva ca ।।
bhavanaṃ vainateyasya daityendreṇābhikampitam ।। raktatoyo mahābhīmo lauhityo nāma sāgaraḥ ।। suvarṇavedikaḥ śrīmān meghapaṅktiniṣevitaḥ ।। śālaistālaistamālaiśca karṇikāraiśca puṣpitaiḥ ।।
tamālavanagandhaśca parvato malayaḥ śubhaḥ ।। bhojāḥ pāṇḍyāśca vaṅgāśca kaliṅgāstāmraliptakāḥ ।। kṣobhitāstena daityena sadevāścāpsarogaṇāḥ ।। siddhacāraṇasaṃghaśca viprakīrṇaṃ manoharam ।।
jātarūpamayaiḥ śṛṅgair apsarogaṇanāditam ।। rarāja sumahāśṛṅgair gaganaṃ vilikhanniva ।। vidyutvānsarvataḥ śrīmān āyataḥ śatayojanam ।। ṛṣabhaḥ parvataścaiva śrīmānvṛṣabhasaṃjñitaḥ ।।
viśālākṣaśca durdharṣaḥ sarpāṇāmālayaḥ purī ।। mahāseno giriścaiva pāriyātraśca parvataḥ ।। prāgjyautiṣapuraṃ cāpi jātarūpamayaṃ śubham ।। meghaśca parvataśreṣṭho meghagambhīraniḥsvanaḥ ।।
taruṇādityasaṃkāśo merustatra mahāgiriḥ ।। hemagarbho mahāśailas tathā hemasakho giriḥ ।। hemapuṣkarasaṃchannaṃ tena vaikhānasaṃ saraḥ ।। triśṛṅgaparvataścaiva kumārī ca saridvarā ।।
uśīrabinduśca giriś candraprasthastathādrirāṭ ।। devābhraparvataścaiva tathā vai reṇuko giriḥ ।। ete cānye ca girayo deśā janapadāstathā ।। kapilaśca mahīputro vyāghravāṃścaiva kampitaḥ ।।
gaṇastathā paro raudro meghanāmāṅkuśāyudhaḥ ।। gadī śūlī karālaśca hiraṇyakaśipustadā ।। jīmūtaghananirghoṣo jīmūta iva vegavān ।। tadoṃkārasahāyena vidārya nihato yudhi ।।
nadyaśca śailāśca mahārṇavāśca gatāḥ prasādaṃ ditiputranāśāt ।। tuṣṭuvurnāmabhirdivyair ādidevaṃ sanātanam ।। etadevārcayiṣyanti parāvaravido janāḥ ।। bhavānkartā vikartā ca lokānāṃ prabhavo avyayaḥ ।।
paraṃ ca dharmaṃ paramaṃ ca viśvaṃ tvāmāhuragryaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇam ।। paraṃ rahasyaṃ paramāṃ gatiṃ ca tvāmāhuragryaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇam ।। paraṃ parasyāpi paraṃ ca bhūtaṃ tvāmāhuragryaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇam ।। paraṃ parasyāpi paraṃ mahadyat tvāmāhuragryaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇam ।।
paraṃ parasyāpi paraṃ ca dāntaṃ tvāmāhuragryaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇam ।। stutvā nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ brahmalokaṃ gataḥ prabhuḥ ।। kṣīrodasyottaraṃ kūlaṃ jagāma harirīśvaraḥ ।। paurāṇaṃ rūpamāsthāya prayayau garuḍadhvajaḥ ।।
avyaktaprakṛtirdevaḥ svasthānaṃ gatavānprabhuḥ ।। punastasyaiva māhātmyam anyadvistarato vada ।। kathaṃ ca vaiṣṇavī sṛṣṭiḥ padmamadhye abhavatpurā ।। vismayotphullanayanaḥ punaḥ papraccha keśavam ।।
jalārṇavagatasyeha nābhau jātaṃ janārdana ।। puṣkare ca kathaṃ bhūtā devāḥ sarṣigaṇāḥ purā ।। śṛṇvatastasya me kīrtiṃ na tṛptirupajāyate ।। kiyantaṃ vā svapiti ca ko asya kālasya saṃbhavaḥ ।।
kathaṃ cotthāya bhagavān sṛjate nikhilaṃ jagat ।। kathaṃ nirmitavāṃścaiva citraṃ lokaṃ sanātanam ।। dagdhe devāsuranare pranaṣṭoragarākṣase ।। kevalaṃ gahvarībhūte mahābhūtaviparyaye ।।
āste suravaraśreṣṭho vidhimāsthāya yogavit ।। vaktumarhasi dharmiṣṭha yaśo nārāyaṇātmakam ।। śraddhayā copaviṣṭānāṃ bhagavanvaktumarhasi ।। tadvaṃśyānvayabhūtasya nyāyyaṃ ravikularṣabha ।।
brāhmaṇānāṃ ca vadatāṃ śrutvā vai sumahātmanām ।। parāśarasutaḥ śrīmān gururdvaipāyano abravīt ।। yadvijñātuṃ mayā śakyam ṛṣimātreṇa sattamāḥ ।। viśvāyanaśca yadbrahmā na vedayati tattvataḥ ।।
tadadhyātmavidāṃ cintyaṃ narakaṃ ca vikarmiṇām ।। tadbhūtamadhibhūtaṃ ca tatparaṃ paramarṣīṇām ।। yaḥ kartā kārako buddhir manaḥ kṣetrajña eva ca ।। prāṇaḥ pañcavidhaścaiva dhruva akṣara eva ca ।।
ucyate vividhairdevaiḥ sa evāyaṃ na tatparam ।। so asmānkārayate sarvān so atyeti vyākulīkṛtān ।। yo vaktā yacca vaktavyaṃ yaccāhaṃ tadbravīmi vaḥ ।। viśvaṃ viśvapatiryaśca sa tu nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
yatkiṃcic caramacaraṃ yadasti cānyat tatsarvaṃ puruṣavaraḥ prabhuḥ purāṇaḥ ।। tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā dviguṇā ravinandana ।। svadharmaniratāḥ santo jāyante yatra mānavāḥ ।। kṛṣyāmabhiratā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ śuśrūṣavaḥ sthitāḥ ।।
sadbhirācaritaṃ karma kriyate khyāyate ca vai ।। prāṇināṃ dharmasaṅgānām api vai nīcajanmanām ।। tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā dviguṇā parikīrtyate ।। yatra satyaṃ ca sattvaṃ ca tretādharmo vidhīyate ।।
cāturvarṇyasya vaikṛtyād yānti daurbalyamāśramāḥ ।। dvāparasya tu yā ceṣṭā tāmapi śrotumarhasi ।। tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā dviguṇā yugamucyate ।। sarve naiṣkṛtikāḥ kṣudrā jāyante ravinandana ।।
viparyayācchanairdharmaḥ kṣayameti kalau yuge ।। vratopavāsāstyajyante dvāpare yugaparyaye ।। saṃdhyayā saha saṃkhyātaṃ krūraṃ kaliyugaṃ smṛtam ।। kāminastapasā hīnā jāyante tatra mānavāḥ ।।
nāstikā brahmabhaktā vā jāyante tatra mānavāḥ ।। viprāḥ śūdrasamācārāḥ santi sarve kalau yuge ।। varṇānāṃ caiva saṃdeho yugānte ravinandana ।। evaṃ sahasraparyantaṃ tadaharbrāhmamucyate ।।
śarīranirvṛtiṃ dṛṣṭvā lokasaṃhārabuddhitaḥ ।। daityānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca yakṣarākṣasapakṣiṇām ।। tiryagyonigatānāṃ ca sattvānāṃ kṛmiṇāṃ tathā ।। jagatsaṃharaṇārthāya kurute vaiśasaṃ mahat ।।
bhūtvā vahnirnirdahansarvalokān bhūtvā megho bhūya ugro apyavarṣat ।। gabhastibhiḥ pradīptābhiḥ saṃśoṣayati sāgarān ।। parvatānāṃ ca salilaṃ sarvamādāya raśmibhiḥ ।। pātālajalamādāya pibate rasamuttamam ।।
tatsarvamaravindākṣa ādatte puruṣottamaḥ ।। prāṇāpānasamānādyān vāyūn ākarṣate hariḥ ।। gandho ghrāṇaṃ śarīraṃ ca pṛthivīṃ saṃśritā guṇāḥ ।। rūpaṃ cakṣurvipākaśca jyotirevāśritā guṇāḥ ।।
śabdaḥ śrotraṃ ca khānyeva gagane saṃśritā guṇāḥ ।। mano buddhiśca sarveṣāṃ kṣetrajñaśceti yaḥ śrutaḥ ।। tato bhagavatastasya raśmibhiḥ parivāritaḥ ।। teṣāṃ saṃgharṣaṇodbhūtaḥ pāvakaḥ śatadhā jvalan ।।
saparvatadrumāngulmāṃl latāvallīstṛṇāni ca ।। yāni cāśrayaṇīyāni tāni sarvāṇi so adahat ।। bhūyo nirvāpayāmāsa yugāntena ca karmaṇā ।। divyatoyena haviṣā tarpayāmāsa medinīm ।।
śivena puṇyena mahī nirvāṇamagamatparam ।। ekārṇavajalībhūtā sarvasattvavivarjitā ।। naṣṭārkapavanākāśe sūkṣme jagati saṃvṛte ।। dagdhvā saṃplāvya ca tathā svapityekaḥ sanātanaḥ ।।
