ekārṇavajalavyāpī yogī yogamupāśritaḥ ।। na cainaṃ kaścidavyaktaṃ vyaktaṃ veditumarhati ।। asau kiyantaṃ kālaṃ ca ekārṇavavidhiṃ prabhuḥ ।। kariṣyatīti bhagavān iti kaścin na budhyate ।।
tasya na jñāyate kiṃcit tamṛte devasattamam ।। pitāmahaṃ śrutinilayaṃ mahāmuniṃ praśāmya bhūyaḥ śayanaṃ hyarocayat ।। pracchādya salilenorvīṃ haṃso nārāyaṇastadā ।। virajaskaṃ mahābāhum akṣayaṃ brahma yadviduḥ ।।
manaḥ sāttvikamādhāya yatra tatsatyamāsata ।। rahasyāraṇyakoddiṣṭaṃ yaccaupaniṣadaṃ smṛtam ।। yaścānyaḥ puruṣākhyaḥ syāt sa eṣa puruṣottamaḥ ।। asmādeva purā bhūtā yajñebhyaḥ śrūyatāṃ tathā ।।
hotāramapi cādhvaryuṃ bāhubhyāmasṛjatprabhuḥ ।। tau mitrāvaruṇau pṛṣṭhāt pratiprastārameva ca ।। acchāvākamathorubhyāṃ neṣṭāraṃ caiva pārthiva ।। grāvastutaṃ tu pādābhyām unnetāraṃ ca yājuṣam ।।
pravaktṝnsarvayajñānām ṛtvijo asṛjaduttamān ।। vedāścaitanmayāḥ sarve sāṅgopaniṣadakriyāḥ ।। śrūyatāṃ tadyathā viprā mārkaṇḍeyakutūhalam ।। bahuvarṣasahasrāyus tasyaiva varatejasā ।।
āśramāṇi ca puṇyāni devatāyatanāni ca ।। japahomaparaḥ śāntas tapo ghoraṃ samāsthitaḥ ।। sa niṣkrāmanna cātmānaṃ jānīte devamāyayā ।। sarvatastamasācchannaṃ mārkaṇḍeyo anvavaikṣata ।।
devadarśanasaṃhṛṣṭo vismayaṃ paramaṃ gataḥ ।। kiṃ nu syānmama cinteyaṃ mohaḥ svapno anubhūyate ।। na hīdṛśaṃ jagatkleśam ayuktaṃ satyamarhati ।। katamaḥ syādayaṃ loka iti cintāmavasthitaḥ ।।
salile ardhamatho magnaṃ jīmūtamiva sāgare ।। śarvaryāṃ jāgratamiva bhāsantaṃ svena tejasā ।। tathaiva sa muniḥ kukṣiṃ punareva praveśitaḥ ।। tathaiva tu punarbhūyo vijānansvapnadarśanam ।।
puṇyatīrthajalopetāṃ vividhānyāśramāṇi ca ।। apaśyaddevakukṣisthān yājakāñchataśo dvijān ।। catvāraścāśramāḥ samyag yathoddiṣṭā mayā tava ।। carataḥ pṛthivīṃ sarvāṃ na kukṣyantaḥ samīkṣitaḥ ।।
suptaṃ nyagrodhaśākhāyāṃ bālamekaṃ niraikṣata ।। avyagraḥ krīḍate loke sarvabhūtavivarjite ।। bālamādityasaṃkāśaṃ nāśaknodabhivīkṣitum ।। pūrvadṛṣṭamidaṃ mene śaṅkito devamāyayā ।।
plavaṃstathārtim agamad bhayātsaṃtrastalocanaḥ ।। babhāṣe meghatulyena svareṇa puruṣottamaḥ ।। mārkaṇḍeyo munistvāha bālaṃ taṃ śramapīḍitaḥ ।। divyaṃ varṣasahasrākhyaṃ dharṣayanniva me vayaḥ ।।
māṃ brahmāpi hi deveśo dīrghāyuriti bhāṣate ।। mārkaṇḍeyeti māmuktvā mṛtyumīkṣitumarhati ।। tathaiva bhagavānbhūyo babhāṣe madhusūdanaḥ ।। āyuṣpradātā paurāṇaḥ kiṃ māṃ tvaṃ nopasarpasi ।।
pūrvamārādhayāmāsa tapastīvraṃ samāśritaḥ ।। uktavānahamātmasthaṃ maharṣim amitaujasam ।। draṣṭumekārṇavagataṃ krīḍantaṃ yogavartmanā ।। mūrdhni baddhāñjalipuṭo mārkaṇḍeyo mahātapāḥ ।।
tasmai bhagavate bhaktyā namaskāramathākarot ।। yadekārṇavamadhyasthaḥ śeṣe tvaṃ bālarūpavān ।। tarkaye tvāṃ mahātmānaṃ ko hyanyaḥ sthātumarhati ।। ahaṃ sahasraśīrṣākhyo yaḥ padairabhisaṃjñitaḥ ।।
ahamagnirhavyavāho yādasāṃ patiravyayaḥ ।। ahaṃ yogī yugākhyasya yugāntāvarta eva ca ।। bhujaṃgānāmahaṃ śeṣas tārkṣyo vai sarvapakṣiṇām ।। ahaṃ dharmastapaścāhaṃ sarvāśramanivāsinām ।।
yattatsatyaṃ ca paramam ahamekaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। ahamijyā kriyā cāham ahaṃ vidyādhipaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। ahamāpaḥ samudrāśca nakṣatrāṇi diśo daśa ।। kṣīrodasāgare cāhaṃ samudre vaḍavāmukhaḥ ।।
ahaṃ purāṇaḥ paramaṃ tathaivāhaṃ parāyaṇam ।। yatkiṃcitpaśyase vipra yacchṛṇoṣi ca kiṃcana ।। viśvaṃ sṛṣṭaṃ mayā pūrvaṃ sṛjyaṃ cādyāpi paśya mām ।। tadetadakhilaṃ sarvaṃ mārkaṇḍeyāvadhāraya ।।
mama brahmā śarīrastho devaiśca ṛṣibhiḥ saha ।। ahamekākṣaro mantras tryakṣaraścaiva tārakaḥ ।। evamādipurāṇeśo vadanneva mahāmatiḥ ।। tato bhagavataḥ kukṣiṃ praviṣṭo munisattamaḥ ।।
śanaiścaranprabhurapi haṃsasaṃjñito asṛjajjagadviharati kālaparyaye ।। chādayitvātmano dehaṃ yādasāṃ kulasaṃbhavam ।। mahatāṃ pañcabhūtānāṃ viśvo viśvamacintayat ।। nirākāśe toyamaye sūkṣme jagati gahvare ।।
anantarormibhiḥ sūkṣmam atha chidramabhūtpurā ।। sa labdhvāntaramakṣobhyo vyavardhata samīraṇaḥ ।। kṛṣṇavartmā samabhavat prabhurvaiśvānaro mahān ।। kṣayājjalanidheśchidram abhavadvistṛtaṃ nabhaḥ ।।
ākāśaṃ chidrasambhūtaṃ vāyurākāśasaṃbhavaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā prīto mahādevo mahābhūtavibhāvanaḥ ।। brahmaṇo janmasahitaṃ bahurūpo vyacintayat ।। bahujanmā hi viśvātmā brahmaṇo havirucyate ।।
jñānaṃ vṛṣṭaṃ tu viśvārthe yogināṃ yāti mukhyatām ।। pade brahmaṇi viśveśaṃ nyayojayata yogavit ।। jale krīḍaṃśca vidhivan modate sarvalokakṛt ।। sahasraparṇaṃ virajaṃ bhāskarābhaṃ hiraṇmayam ।।
virājate kamalamudāravarcasaṃ mahātmanastanuruhacārudarśanam ।। sraṣṭāraṃ sarvalokānāṃ brahmāṇaṃ sarvatomukham ।। sarvatejoguṇamayaṃ pārthivairlakṣaṇairvṛtam ।। nārāyaṇasamudbhūtaṃ pravadanti maharṣayaḥ ।।
ye padmasāraguravas tāndivyān parvatānviduḥ ।। kailāsaṃ muñjavantaṃ ca tathānyaṃ gandhamādanam ।। udayaṃ piñjaraṃ caiva vindhyavantaṃ ca parvatam ।। āśrayāḥ puṇyaśīlānāṃ sarvakāmaphalapradāḥ ।।
jambūdvīpasya saṃsthānaṃ yajñiyā yatra vai kriyāḥ ।। divyāstīrthaśatādhārāḥ suramyāḥ saritaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। asaṃkhyeyāḥ pṛthivyāste viśve vai dhātuparvatāḥ ।। te durgamāḥ śailacitā mlecchadeśā vikalpitāḥ ।।
daityānāmuragāṇāṃ ca pataṅgānāṃ ca pārthiva ।। mahāpātakakarmāṇo majjante yatra mānavāḥ ।। proktātha dikṣu sarvāsu catvāraḥ salilākarāḥ ।। prādurbhāvo apyayaṃ tasmān nāmnā puṣkarasaṃjñitaḥ ।।
yājñikairvedadṛṣṭāntair yajñe padmavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।। parvatānāṃ nadīnāṃ ca hradānāṃ caiva nirmitaḥ ।। śanaiḥ svayaṃbhūḥ śayanaṃ sṛjattadā jaganmayaṃ padmavidhiṃ mahārṇave ।। tenaiva ca sahodbhūto hy asuro nāma kaiṭabhaḥ ।।
ekārṇave jagatsarvaṃ kṣobhayantau mahābalau ।। kirīṭakuṇḍalodagrau keyūravalayojjvalau ।। mahāgireḥ saṃhananau jaṅgamāviva parvatau ।। vidyudābhau gadāgrābhyāṃ karābhyāmatibhīṣaṇau ।।
kampayantāviva hariṃ śayānaṃ madhusūdanam ।। yogināṃ śreṣṭhamāsādya dīptaṃ dadṛśatustadā ।। daivatāni ca viśvāni mānasānasurānṛṣīn ।। dīptau mumūrṣū saṃkruddhau roṣavyākulitekṣaṇau ।।
ādhāya niyamaṃ mohād āste tvaṃ vigatajvaraḥ ।। āvābhyāṃ paramīśābhyām aśaktastvamihārṇave ।। kaḥ sraṣṭā kaśca te goptā kena nāmnā vidhīyase ।। tatsaṃyogena bhavatoḥ karma nāmāvagacchatām ।।
āvābhyāṃ chādyate viśvaṃ tamasā rajasātha vai ।। chādyamānau dharmaśīlau dustarau sarvadehinām ।। āvāmarthaśca kāmaśca yajñaḥ svargaparigrahaḥ ।। yeṣāṃ yatkāṅkṣitaṃ caiva tattadāvāṃ vicintaya ।।
taṃ samādhāya guṇavat sattvaṃ cāsmi samāśritaḥ ।। rajasastamasaścaiva yaḥ sraṣṭā viśvasaṃbhavaḥ ।। sa eva hi yuvāṃ nāṃśe vaśī devo haniṣyati ।। bāhuṃ nārāyaṇo brahmā kṛtavānātmamāyayā ।।
ceratustau vigalitau śakunāviva pīvarau ।। padmanābhaṃ hṛṣīkeśaṃ praṇipatya sthitāvubhau ।। tvamāvāṃ pāhi hetvartham idaṃ nau buddhikāraṇam ।। tatastvāmāgatāvāvām abhitaḥ prasamīkṣitum ।।
amoghadarśano asi tvaṃ namaste samitiṃjaya ।। dattāyuṣkau punarbhūyo raho jīvitum icchathaḥ ।। tamicchāvo vadhaścaiva tvatto no astu mahāvrata ।। bhaviṣyato na saṃdehaḥ satyametadbravīmi vām ।।
rajastamovargabhavāyanau yamau mamantha tāvūrutalena vai prabhuḥ ।। ūrdhvabāhurmahātejās tapo ghoraṃ samāśritaḥ ।। babhāse sarvadharmasthaḥ sahasrāṃśurivāṃśubhiḥ ।। ājagāma mahātejā yogācāryo mahāyaśāḥ ।।
ubhāvapi mahātmānau stuvantau kṣetratatparau ।। parāvaraviśeṣajñau pūjitau ca maharṣibhiḥ ।। grāmaṇīḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ brahmā trailokyapūjitaḥ ।। trīnimān kṛtavāṃllokān yatheyaṃ brahmaṇaḥ śrutiḥ ।।
tasyāgre vāgyatastasthau brahmā tāmasamavyayam ।। kiṃ kurmastava sāhāyyaṃ bravītu bhagavānṛṣiḥ ।। vadate bhavatastattvaṃ tatkuruṣva mahāmate ।। śuśrūṣurasmi yuvayoḥ kiṃ karomi kṛtāñjaliḥ ।।
yatsatyaṃ yadṛtaṃ tattu paraṃ padamanusmara ।। gatvā ca tatra brahmatvam agamajjñānatejasā ।। saṃkalpayitvā manasā tameva ca mahāmanāḥ ।। pitāmahasamājñāto brahmāṇaṃ samupasthitaḥ ।।
prāptaśca paramaṃ sthānaṃ sa tayoḥ pārśvamāgataḥ ।। mokṣapravṛttikuśalaṃ bhūrbhuvaṃ nāmato vibhum ।। evaṃ putrāstrayo apyeta uktāḥ śaṃbhormahātmanaḥ ।। nārāyaṇaśca bhagavān kapilaśca yatīśvaraḥ ।।
tato ghoratamaṃ bhūyaḥ saṃśritaḥ paramaṃ vratam ।। śarīrārdhāttato bhāryāṃ samutpāditavāñchubhām ।। sadṛśīmātmano devīṃ samarthāṃ lokasarjane ।। tato jagāda tripadāṃ gāyatrīṃ vedapūjitām ।।
aparāṃścaiva caturo vedāngāyatrisaṃbhavān ।। viśve prajānāṃ patayo yebhyo lokā viniḥsṛtāḥ ।। sarvamantrahitaṃ puṇyaṃ nāmnā dharmaṃ sa sṛṣṭavān ।। vasiṣṭhaṃ gautamaṃ caiva bhṛgumaṅgirasaṃ manum ।।
trayodaśaguṇaṃ dharmam ālabhanta maharṣayaḥ ।। tāmrā krodhātha suratā vinatā kadrureva ca ।। marīceḥ kaśyapaḥ putras tapasā nirmitaḥ kila ।। nakṣatrāṇi ca somāya tadā vai dattavānṛṣiḥ ।।
lakṣmīrmarutvatī sādhyā viśveśā ca matā śubhā ।। etāḥ pañca variṣṭhā vai suraśreṣṭhāya pārthiva ।। yā tu rūpavatī patnī brahmaṇaḥ kāmarūpiṇī ।। tatastāmagamadbrahmā maithunaṃ lokapūjitaḥ ।।
jajñire ca sutāstasyāṃ vipulā dhūmasaṃnibhāḥ ।। te rudanto dravantaśca garhayantaḥ pitāmaham ।। nirṛtiścaiva śaṃbhurvai tṛtīyaścāparājitaḥ ।। ahirbudhnyaśca bhagavān kapālī cāpi piṅgalaḥ ।।
tasyāmeva surabhyāṃ ca gāvo yajñeśvarāśca vai ।। ajāścaiva tu haṃsāśca tathaivāmṛtamuttamam ।। dharmāllakṣmīstathā kāmaṃ sādhyā sādhyānvyajāyata ।। aruṇaṃ cāruṇiṃ caiva viśvāvasubaladhruvau ।।
vatsaraṃ caiva bhūtiṃ ca sarvāsuraniṣūdanam ।। vāsavānugatā devī janayāmāsa vai surān ।। viśvāvasuṃ tṛtīyaṃ ca caturthaṃ somamīśvaram ।। saptamaṃ ca tathā vāyum aṣṭamaṃ nirṛtiṃ vasum ।।
viśve devāśca viśvāyāṃ dharmājjātā iti śrutiḥ ।। cākṣuṣastu manuścaiva tathā madhumahoragau ।। garuḍaścātisattvaujā bhāskarapratimadyutiḥ ।। marutvatī marutvato devānajanayatsutān ।।
amaraṃ śaravṛṣṭiṃ ca sukarṣaṃ ca mahābhujam ।। aśvamitraṃ citraraśmiṃ tathā niṣadhanaṃ nṛpa ।। bṛhantaṃ vai bṛhadrūpaṃ tathā vai pūtanānugam ।। aditiḥ kaśyapājjajña ādityāndvādaśaiva hi ।।
pūṣā mitraśca dhanado dhātā parjanya eva ca ।। ādityasya sarasvatyāṃ jajñāte dvau sutau varau ।। danustu dānavāñjajñe ditirdaityānvyajāyata ।। anāyuṣāyāstanayā vyādhayaḥ sumahābalāḥ ।।
tāmrā tvapsarasāṃ mātā puṇyānāṃ bhāratodbhava ।। jajñe yakṣagaṇāṃścaiva rākṣasāṃśca viśāṃpate ।। suparṇānpakṣiṇaścaiva vinatā ca vyajāyata ।। evaṃ vṛddhiṃ samagaman viśve lokāḥ paraṃtapa ।।
prādurbhāvaḥ pauṣkaraste mayā dvaipāyaneritaḥ ।। kathitaste anupūrveṇa saṃstutaḥ paramarṣibhiḥ ।। avāpya lokānsa hi vītarāgaḥ paratra ca svargaphalāni bhuṅkte ।। prasādayati yaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ taṃ kṛṣṇo anuprasīdati ।।
kṣīṇāyurlabhate cāyuḥ putrakāmaḥ sutaṃ tathā ।। prāpnoti vividhaṃ puṇyaṃ viṣṇubhakto dhanāni ca ।। sarvaṃ vihāya ya imaṃ paṭhetpauṣkarakaṃ hareḥ ।। kīrtitaste mahābhāga vyāsaśrutinidarśanāt ।।
vaikuṇṭhatvaṃ ca deveṣu kṛṣṇatvaṃ mānuṣeṣu ca ।। saṃpratyatītānbhavyāṃśca śṛṇu rājanyathātatham ।। nārāyaṇo hyanantātmā prabhavo avyaya eva ca ।। brahmā vāyuśca somaśca dharmaḥ śakro bṛhaspatiḥ ।।
eṣa viṣṇuriti khyāta indrasyāvarajo vibhuḥ ।। vadhārthaṃ suraśatrūṇāṃ daityadānavarakṣasām ।। so asṛjatpūrvapuruṣaḥ purākalpe prajāpatīn ।। tebhyo abhavanmahātmabhyo bahudhā brahma śāśvatam ।।
kīrtanīyasya lokeṣu kīrtyamānaṃ nibodha me ।। āsīttrailokyavikhyātaḥ saṅgrāmastārakāmayaḥ ।। ghnanti devagaṇānsarvān sayakṣoragarākṣasān ।। trātāraṃ manasā jagmur devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum ।।
sārkacandragrahagaṇaṃ chādayanto nabhastalam ।। anyonyavegābhihatāḥ pravavuḥ saha mārutāḥ ।। ravaiḥ sughorairutpātair dahyamānam ivāmbaram ।। divyāni ca vimānāni prapatantyutpatanti ca ।।
arūpavanti rūpāṇi tasminnutpātalakṣaṇe ।। timiraughaparikṣiptā na rejuśca diśo daśa ।। dyaurna bhātyabhibhūtārkā ghoreṇa tamasāvṛtā ।। vapuḥ saṃdarśayāmāsa divyaṃ kṛṣṇavapurhariḥ ।।
tejasā vapuṣā caiva kṛṣṇaṃ kṛṣṇamivācalam ।। dhūmāndhakāravapuṣaṃ yugāntāgnimivotthitam ।। babhau cāmīkaraprakhyair āyudhairupaśobhitam ।। nandakānanditakaraṃ śarāśīviṣadhāriṇam ।।
viṣṇuśailaṃ kṣamāmūlaṃ śrīvṛkṣaṃ śārṅgaśṛṅgiṇam ।। sarvalokamanaḥkāntaṃ sarvasattvamanoharam ।। vidyāhaṃkārasārāḍhyaṃ mahābhūtaprarohaṇam ।। daityalokamahāskandhaṃ martyalokaprakāśitam ।।
mṛgendrapāśairvitataṃ pakṣajantuniṣevitam ।। avyaktānantasalilaṃ vyaktāhaṃkāraphenilam ।। vimānavihagavyātaṃ toyadāḍambarākulam ।। traiguṇyaviṣayāvartaṃ sarvalokatimiṅgilam ।।
dvādaśārkamahādvīpaṃ rudraikādaśapattanam ।। saṃdhyāsaṃkhyormisalilaṃ suparṇānilasevitam ।। pitāmahamahāvīryaṃ sarvastrīratnaśobhitam ।। kālayogimahāparvapralayotpattiveginam ।।
devādhidevaṃ varadaṃ bhaktānāṃ bhaktivatsalam ।। haryaśvarathasaṃyukte suparṇadhvajasevite ।। anantaraśmibhiryukte vistīrṇe merugahvare ।। bhayeṣvabhayadaṃ vyomni devā daityaparājitāḥ ।।
te kṛtāñjalayaḥ sarve devāḥ śakrapurogamāḥ ।। sa teṣāṃ tāṃ giraṃ śrutvā viṣṇurdaivatadaivatam ।। ākāśe tu sthito viṣṇur uttamaṃ vapurāsthitaḥ ।। śāntiṃ vrajata bhadraṃ vo mā bhaiṣṭa marutāṃ gaṇāḥ ।।
te tasya satyasaṃdhasya viṣṇorvākyena toṣitāḥ ।। tatastamaḥ saṃhṛtaṃ tad vineśuśca balāhakāḥ ।। śuddhaprabhāṇi jyotīṃṣi somaścakruḥ pradakṣiṇām ।। virajaskābhavanmārgā nākavargādayastrayaḥ ।।
āsañchubhānīndriyāṇi narāṇāmantarātmasu ।। yajñeṣu ca haviḥ pākaṃ śivamāpa ca pāvakaḥ ।। viṣṇordattapratijñasya śrutvārinidhane giram ।। udyogaṃ vipulaṃ cakrur yuddhāya vijayāya ca ।।
catuścakraṃ suvipulaṃ sukalpitamahāyugam ।। ruciraṃ ratnajālaiśca hemajālaiśca śobhitam ।। divyāstratūṇīradharaṃ payodharavināditam ।। gadāparighasampūrṇaṃ mūrtimantamivārṇavam ।।
sapatākadhvajopetaṃ sādityamiva mandaram ।। yuktamṛkṣasahasreṇa samṛddhāmbudanāditam ।। adhyatiṣṭhadraṇākāṅkṣī meruṃ dīpta ivāṃśumān ।। śailākāramasaṃbādhaṃ nīlāñjanacayopamam ।।
timirodgārikiraṇaṃ garjantamiva toyadam ।। āyasaiḥ parighaiḥ pūrṇaṃ kṣepaṇīyaiśca mudgaraiḥ ।। śobhitaṃ trāsayānaiśca tomaraiśca paraśvadhaiḥ ।। yuktaṃ kharasahasreṇa so adhyārohadrathottamam ।।
pramukhe tasya sainyasya dīptaśṛṅga ivācalaḥ ।। syandanaṃ vāhayāmāsa sapatnānīkamardanaḥ ।। varāhaḥ pramukhe tasthau sapraroha ivācalaḥ ।। sphuraddantoṣṭhanayanaḥ saṅgrāmaṃ so abhyakāṅkṣata ।।
vyūhituṃ dānavavyūhaṃ paricakrāma vīryavān ।। śvetaśailapratīkāśo yuddhāyābhimukhe sthitaḥ ।। yuddhāyābhimukhastasthau dharādharavikampanaḥ ।। sabalā dānavāścaiva saṃnahyante yathākramam ।।
lambastu navameghābhaḥ pralambāmbarabhūṣaṇaḥ ।। svarbhānurāsyayodhī tu daśanoṣṭhekṣaṇāyudhaḥ ।। anye hayagatāstatra gajaskandhagatāḥ pare ।। kecitkharoṣṭrayātāraḥ kecicchvāpadavāhanāḥ ।।
ekapādārdhapādāśca nanṛturyuddhakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।। hṛṣṭaśārdūlanirghoṣā nedurdānavapuṃgavāḥ ।। bāhubhiḥ parighākārais tarjayanti sma devatāḥ ।। cikrīḍuste śataghnībhiḥ śatadhāraiśca mudgaraiḥ ।।
cakraiśca daityapravarāś cakrur ānanditaṃ balam ।। devānabhimukhe tasthau meghānīkamivoddhatam ।। balaṃ raṇaughābhyudaye abhyudīrṇaṃ yuyutsayonmattam ivābabhāse ।। surāṇāmapi sainyasya vistāraṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ śṛṇu ।।
sabalāḥ sānugāścaiva saṃnahyanta yathākramam ।। grāmaṇīḥ sarvadevānām āruroha suradvipam ।। sucārucakracaraṇo hemavajrapariṣkṛtaḥ ।। dīptimadbhiḥ sadasyaiśca brahmarṣibhirabhiṣṭutaḥ ।।
yukto balāhakagaṇaiḥ parvatairiva kāmagaiḥ ।। havirdhāneṣu gāyanti viprā makhamukhe sthitāḥ ।। sundaryaḥ parinṛtyanti śataśo apsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ ।। yukto hayasahasreṇa manomārutaraṃhasā ।।
kṛtsnaḥ parivṛto merur bhāskarasyeva tejasā ।। tasthau suragaṇānīke daityānnādena bhīṣayan ।। śaṅkhamuktāṅgadadharo bibhrattoyamayaṃ vapuḥ ।। vāyvīritair jalākāraiḥ kurvaṃllīlāḥ sahasraśaḥ ।।
maṇiśyāmottamavapur haribhārārpito varaḥ ।। yuddhavelāmabhilaṣan bhinnavela ivārṇavaḥ ।। yuktaśca śaṅkhapadmābhyāṃ nidhīnāmadhipaḥ prabhuḥ ।। vimānayodhī dhanado vimāne puṣpake sthitaḥ ।।
ukṣāṇamāsthitaḥ saṃkhye sākṣādiva śivaḥ svayam ।। varuṇaḥ paścimaṃ pakṣam uttaraṃ naravāhanaḥ ।। svāsu dikṣu svarakṣanta tasya devabalasya te ।। śriyā jājvalyamānena dīpyamānaiśca raśmibhiḥ ।।
tridivadvāracakreṇa tapatā lokamavyayam ।। cacāra madhye lokānāṃ dvādaśātmā dineśvaraḥ ।। himavattoyapūrṇābhir bhābhirāhlādayañjagat ।। śaśacchāyāṅkitatanuṃ naiśasya tamasaḥ kṣayam ।।
oṣadhīnāṃ sahasrāṇāṃ nidhānamamṛtasya ca ।। dadṛśurdānavāḥ somaṃ himapraharaṇaṃ sthitam ।। saptadhātugato lokāṃs trīndadhāra cacāra ca ।। saptasvaragato yaśca nityaṃ gīrbhirudīryate ।।
yamāhurākāśagamaṃ śīghragaṃ śabdayoginam ।। vavau pravyathayandaityān pratilomaṃ satoyadaḥ ।। cikrīḍurasibhiḥ śubhrair nirmuktairiva pannagaiḥ ।। śarabhūtā divīndrāṇāṃ cerurvyāttānanā divi ।।
upatasthuḥ suragaṇāḥ prahartuṃ dānavaṃ balam ।। yugāntakṛṣṇavartmābho viśvasya jagataḥ prabhuḥ ।। bhūmyāpovyomabhūtātmā śyāmaḥ śāntikaro arihā ।। arkaṃ nāgādivodyantam udyamyottamatejasā ।।
kareṇa kālīṃ vapuṣā śatrukālapradāṃ gadām ।। dadhārāyudhajātāni śārṅgādīni mahābalaḥ ।। pavanādhikasaṃpātaṃ gaganakṣobhaṇaṃ khagam ।। amṛtārambhanirmuktaṃ mandarādrim ivocchritam ।।
mahendreṇāmṛtasyārthe vajreṇa kṛtalakṣaṇam ।। vicitrapatravasanaṃ dhātumantamivācalam ।। bhogibhogāvasaktena maṇiratnena bhāsvatā ।। yugānte sendracāpābhyāṃ toyadābhyāmivāmbaram ।।
ketuveṣapraticchannaṃ mahākāyaniketanam ।। suvarṇavarṇavapuṣā suparṇaṃ khecarottamam ।। gīrbhiḥ paramamantrābhis tuṣṭuvuśca janārdanam ।। dvijarājaparikṣiptaṃ devarājavirājitam ।।
pavanāviddhanirghoṣaṃ saṃpradīptahutāśanam ।। balaṃ balavadudvṛttaṃ yuddhāya samavartata ।। svastyastu dānavānīka uśanā vākyamādade ।। surāṇāmasurāṇāṃ ca parasparajayaiṣiṇām ।।
samīyuryudhyamānā vai parvatā iva parvataiḥ ।। dharmādharmasamāyuktaṃ darpeṇa vinayena ca ।। utpatadbhiśca gaganam asihastaiḥ samantataḥ ।। cāpairvisphāryamāṇaiśca pātyamānaiśca mudgaraiḥ ।।
jagatastrāsajananaṃ yugasaṃvartakopamam ।। dānavāḥ samare jaghnur devānindrapurogamān ।। viṣaṇṇavadanā devā jagmurārtiṃ parāṃ mṛdhe ।। bhinnoraskā ditisutair vemū raktaṃ vraṇairbahu ।।
praviṣṭā dānavīṃ māyāṃ na śekuste viceṣṭitum ।। balaṃ surāṇāmasurair niṣprayatnāyudhaṃ kṛtam ।। śakro daityabalaṃ ghoraṃ viveśa bahulocanaḥ ।। tāmasenāstrajālena tamobhūtamathākarot ।।
ghoreṇa tamasāviṣṭāḥ puruhūtasya tejasā ।। vapūṃṣi daityasiṃhānāṃ tamobhūtānyapātayan ।। petuste dānavagaṇāś chinnapakṣā ivādrayaḥ ।। dānavaṃ devakadanaṃ tamobhūtamivābhavat ।।
yugāntodyotajananīṃ sṛṣṭāmaurveṇa vahninā ।। daityāścādityavapuṣaḥ sadya uttasthurāhave ।। bhejire candraviṣayaṃ śītāṃśusalilapradam ।। śaśaṃsurvajriṇaṃ devāḥ saṃtaptāḥ śaraṇaiṣiṇaḥ ।।
codito devarājena varuṇo vākyamabravīt ।। ūrvaḥ sapūrvatejasvī sadṛśo brahmaṇo guṇaiḥ ।। upatasthurmunigaṇā divyā devarṣibhiḥ saha ।। ṛṣiṃ vijñāpayāmāsuḥ purā paramatejasam ।।
ṛṣivaṃśeṣu bhagavaṃś chinnamūlamidaṃ padam ।। kaumāraṃ vratamāsthāya kleśamevānuvartase ।। ekadehāni tiṣṭhanti viviktāni vinā prajāḥ ।। bhavāṃstu tapasā śreṣṭho prajāpātasamadyutiḥ ।।
tvayā dharmo arjitastena dvitīyāṃ kuru vai tanum ।। jagarhe tānṛṣigaṇān vacanaṃ cedamabravīt ।। ārṣaṃ vai sevataḥ karma vanyamūlaphalāśinaḥ ।। brahmacaryaṃ sucaritaṃ brahmāṇamapi cālayet ।।
asmākaṃ tu varaṃ vṛttir vanāśramanivāsinām ।। aśmakuṭṭā hyaśanakāḥ pañcātapasahāśca ye ।। brahmacaryaṃ puraskṛtya prārthayanti parāṃ gatim ।। evamāhuḥ pare loke brahmacaryavido janāḥ ।।
ye sthitā brahmacarye tu brāhmaṇā divi saṃsthitāḥ ।। nāsti loke yaśomūlaṃ brahmacaryātparaṃ tapaḥ ।। brahmacaryaṃ samādhatte kimataḥ paramaṃ tapaḥ ।। abrahmacarye caryā ca trayaṃ syād dambhasaṃjñakam ।।
nanviyaṃ brahmaṇā sṛṣṭā manasā mānasī prajā ।। sṛjadhvaṃ mānasānputrān prājāpatyena karmaṇā ।। na dārayogo bījaṃ vā vratamuktaṃ tapasvinām ।। vyāhṛtaṃ sadbhiratyartham asadbhiriva me matam ।।
dārayogaṃ vinā srakṣye putram ātmatanūruham ।। vanyenānena vidhinā didhakṣantamiva prajāḥ ।। mamanthaikena darbheṇa sutasya prabhavāraṇim ।। jagato dahanākāṅkṣī putro agniḥ samapadyata ।।
didhakṣanniva lokāṃstrīñ jajñe paramakopanaḥ ।। kṣudhā me bādhate tāta jagadbhakṣye tyajasva mām ।। nirdahansarvabhūtāni vavṛdhe so antako analaḥ ।। uvāca vāryatāṃ putro jagataśca dayāṃ kuru ।।
tathyametadvacaḥ putra śṛṇu tvaṃ vadatāṃ vara ।। matimetāṃ dadātīha paramānugrahāya vai ।। bhagavaṃstarpitaḥ putraḥ kairhavyaiḥ prāpsyate sukham ।। vidhāsyatīha bhagavān vīryatulyaṃ mahaujasaḥ ।।
mama yonirjalaṃ vipra tasya pītavataḥ sukham ।। taddhavistava putrasya visṛjāmyālayaṃ ca tat ।। sahitau vicariṣyāvo niṣputrāṇāmṛṇāpahaḥ ।। dahanaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ sadevāsurarakṣasām ।।
praviveśārṇavamukhaṃ prakṣipya pitari prabhām ।। aurvasyāgneḥ prabhāṃ jñātvā svāṃ svāṃ gatimupāśritāḥ ।। uccaiḥ praṇatasarvāṅgo vākyametaduvāca ha ।। tapasā te muniśreṣṭha parituṣṭaḥ pitāmahaḥ ।।
bhṛtya ityavagantavyaḥ sādhyo yadiha karmaṇā ।। yadi sīdenmuniśreṣṭha tavaiva syātparājayaḥ ।। nāsti me tapasānena bhayamadyeha suvrata ।। nirindhanāmagnimayīṃ durdharṣāṃ pāvakairapi ।।
saṃrakṣatyātmapakṣaṃ ca vipakṣaṃ ca pradhakṣyati ।। jagāma tridivaṃ hṛṣṭaḥ kṛtārtho dānaveśvaraḥ ।। aurveṇa nirmitā pūrvaṃ pāvakenorvasūnunā ।। śāpo hyasyāḥ purā dattaḥ sṛṣṭā yenaiva tejasā ।।
dīyatāṃ me sakhā śakra toyayonirniśākaraḥ ।। māyāmetāṃ haniṣyāmi tvatprasādānna saṃśayaḥ ।। saṃdideśāgrataḥ somaṃ yuddhāya śiśirāyudham ।। asurāṇāṃ vināśāya jayārthaṃ ca divaukasām ।।
tvanmayaṃ sarvalokeṣu rasaṃ rasavido viduḥ ।। parivartasyahorātraṃ kālaṃ jagati yojayan ।। na viduḥ soma devāpi ye ca nakṣatrayonayaḥ ।। tamaḥ protsārya mahasā bhāsayasyakhilaṃ jagat ।।
adhikṛt kālayogātmā iṣṭo yajñaraso avyayaḥ ।। śītāṃśuramṛtādhāraś capalaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ ।। saumyastvaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ timiraghnastvam ṛkṣarāṭ ।। śamaya tvāsurīṃ māyāṃ yayā dahyāma saṃyuge ।।
eṣa varṣāmi śiśiraṃ daityamāyāpakarṣaṇam ।। vimāyānvimadāṃścaiva daityasiṃhānmahāhave ।। plāvayāmāsa sainyāni surāṇāṃ śāntivṛddhaye ।। veṣṭayanti sma tānghorān daityānmeghagaṇā iva ।।
